Namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassa

# Khuddakanikāye

## Jātakapāḷi

#### (Paṭhamo bhāgo)

### 1. Ekakanipāto

#### 1. Apaṇṇakavaggo

#### 1. Apaṇṇakajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
Apaṇṇakaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0001" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0001" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0001" /> ṭhānameke, dutiyaṃ āhu takkikā;
```

```
Etadaññāya medhāvī, taṃ gaṇhe yadapaṇṇakanti <note>taṃ gaṇheyya apaṇṇakaṃ (ka.)</note>.
```

Apaṇṇakajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Vaṇṇupathajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
Akilāsuno <pb ed="V" n="1.0002" /> vaṇṇupathe <note>vaṇṇapathe (ka.)</note> khaṇantā, udaṅgaṇe tattha papaṃ avinduṃ;
```

```
Evaṃ munī vīriya <note>muni viriya (pī.), muni vīriya (syā. ka.)</note> balūpapanno, akilāsu vinde hadayassa santinti.
```

Vaṇṇupathajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Serivavāṇijajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
Idha <pb ed="T" n="1.0002" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0002" /> ce naṃ <note>idha ce hi naṃ (sī. pī.)</note> virādhesi, saddhammassa niyāmataṃ <note>niyāmakaṃ (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Ciraṃ tvaṃ anutappesi <note>anutapessasi (sī. pī.), anutappissasi (?)</note>, serivāyaṃva vāṇijoti.
```

Serivavāṇijajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 4. Cūḷaseṭṭhijātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
Appakenapi medhāvī, pābhatena vicakkhaṇo;
```

```
Samuṭṭhāpeti attānaṃ, aṇuṃ aggiṃva sandhamanti.
```

Cūḷa <note>culla (sī.), cullaka (syā. pī.)</note> seṭṭhijātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 5. Taṇḍulanāḷijātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
<note>kimagghatī taṇḍulanāḷikā ca, bārāṇasī antarabāhirāni; assapañcasate tāni, ekā taṇḍulanāḷikāti; (syā.)</note> Kimagghati taṇḍulanāḷikāya, assāna mūlāya vadehi rāja <note>nāḷikā ca (sī.), nāḷikāya (ka. sī. aṭṭha.)</note>;
```

```
Bārāṇasiṃ santarabāhirato <note>bāhirantaṃ (sī.)</note>, ayamagghati taṇḍulanāḷikāti <note>kimagghatī vaṇḍulanāḷikā ca, bārāṇasī antarabāhirāni; assapañcasate tāni, ekā taṇḍulanāḷikāti; (syā.)</note>.
```

Taṇḍulanāḷijātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 6. Devadhammajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
Hiriottappasampannā<pb ed="T" n="1.0003" />, sukkadhammasamāhitā;
```

```
Santo sappurisā loke, devadhammāti vuccareti.
```

Devadhammajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 7. Kaṭṭhahārijātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
Putto tyāhaṃ mahārāja, tvaṃ maṃ posa janādhipa;
```

```
Aññepi devo poseti, kiñca <note>kiñci (ka.)</note> devo sakaṃ pajanti.
```

Kaṭṭhahāri <note>kaṭṭhavāhana (ka.)</note> jātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 8. Gāmaṇijātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
Api <pb ed="V" n="1.0003" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0003" /> ataramānānaṃ, phalāsāva samijjhati;
```

```
Vipakkabrahmacariyosmi, evaṃ jānāhi gāmaṇīti.
```

Gāmaṇijātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Maghadevajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
Uttamaṅgaruhā mayhaṃ, ime jātā vayoharā;
```

```
Pātubhūtā devadūtā, pabbajjāsamayo mamāti.
```

Maghadeva <note>makhādeva (sī. pī.), devadūta (ka.)</note> jātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 10. Sukhavihārijātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
Yañca <pb ed="T" n="1.0004" /> aññe na rakkhanti, yo ca aññe na rakkhati;
```

```
Sa ve rāja sukhaṃ seti, kāmesu anapekkhavāti.
```

Sukhavihārijātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Apaṇṇakavaggo paṭhamo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Varāpaṇṇaka vaṇṇupatha serivaro, suvicakkhaṇa taṇḍulanāḷikassā;
```

```
Hiri puttavaruttagāmaṇinā, yo ca na rakkhati tena dasāti.
```

#### 2. Sīlavaggo

#### 11. Lakkhaṇamigajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
Hoti sīlavataṃ attho, paṭisanthāra <note>paṭisandhāra (ka.)</note> vuttinaṃ;
```

```
Lakkhaṇaṃ passa āyantaṃ, ñātisaṅghapurakkhataṃ <note>purakkhitaṃ (syā.), purekkhitaṃ (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Atha passasimaṃ kāḷaṃ, suvihīnaṃva ñātibhīti.
```

Lakkhaṇamigajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 12. Nigrodhamigajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
Nigrodhameva <pb ed="T" n="1.0005" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0004" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0004" /> seveyya, na sākhamupasaṃvase;
```

```
Nigrodhasmiṃ mataṃ seyyo, yañce sākhasmi <note>sākhasmiṃ (sī. pī.)</note> jīvitanti.
```

Nigrodhamigajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 13. Kaṇḍijātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
Dhiratthu kaṇḍinaṃ sallaṃ, purisaṃ gāḷhavedhinaṃ;
```

```
Dhiratthu taṃ janapadaṃ, yatthitthī pariṇāyikā;
```

```
Te cāpi dhikkitā <note>dhikkatā (?)</note> sattā, ye itthīnaṃ vasaṃgatāti.
```

Kaṇḍijātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 14. Vātamigajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
Na kiratthi rasehi pāpiyo, āvāsehi va <note>vā (sabbattha)</note> santhavehi vā;
```

```
Vātamigaṃ gahananissitaṃ <note>gehanissitaṃ (sī. pī.)</note>, vasamānesi rasehi sañjayoti.
```

Vātamigajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 15. Kharādiyajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
Aṭṭhakkhuraṃ kharādiye, migaṃ vaṅkātivaṅkinaṃ;
```

```
Sattahi <pb ed="T" n="1.0006" /> kālātikkantaṃ <note>sattahi kalāha’tikkantaṃ (sī.), sattakāleha’tikkantaṃ (syā.), sattahi kālāha’tikkantaṃ (pī.)</note>, na naṃ ovaditussaheti.
```

Kharādiyajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 16. Tipallatthamigajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
Migaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0005" /> tipallattha <note>tipallatta (ka.)</note> manekamāyaṃ, aṭṭhakkhuraṃ aḍḍharattāpapāyiṃ <note>aḍḍharattāvapāyiṃ (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Ekena sotena chamāssasanto, chahi kalāhitibhoti <note>kalāhatibhoti (sī. syā. pī.)</note> bhāgineyyoti.
```

Tipallatthamigajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 17. Mālutajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
Kāḷe <pb ed="V" n="1.0005" /> vā yadi vā juṇhe, yadā vāyati māluto;
```

```
Vātajāni hi sītāni, ubhotthamaparājitāti.
```

Mālutajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 18. Matakabhattajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
Evaṃ ce sattā jāneyyuṃ, dukkhāyaṃ jātisambhavo;
```

```
Na pāṇo pāṇinaṃ haññe, pāṇaghātī hi socatīti.
```

Matakabhattajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 19. Āyācitabhattajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
Sace <pb ed="T" n="1.0007" /> mucce <note>muñce (sī. syā. pī.)</note> pecca mucce <note>muñce (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, muccamāno hi bajjhati;
```

```
Na hevaṃ dhīrā muccanti, mutti bālassa bandhananti.
```

Āyācitabhattajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 20. Naḷapānajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
Disvā padamanuttiṇṇaṃ, disvānotaritaṃ padaṃ;
```

```
Naḷena vāriṃ pissāma <note>pivissāma (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, neva <note>na ca (ka.)</note> maṃ tvaṃ vadhissasīti.
```

Naḷapānajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Sīlavaggo dutiyo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Atha <pb ed="M" n="1.0006" /> lakkhaṇa sākha dhiratthu puna, na kiratthi rasehi kharādiyā;
```

```
Atibhoti vara <note>rasa (sabbattha)</note> māluta pāṇa, muccena naḷaavhayanena bhavanti dasāti.
```

#### 3. Kuruṅgavaggo

#### 21. Kuruṅgamigajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
Ñātametaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0006" /> kuruṅgassa, yaṃ tvaṃ sepaṇṇi siyyasi <note>seyyasi (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Aññaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0008" /> sepaṇṇi gacchāmi, na me te ruccate phalanti.
```

Kuruṅgamigajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 22. Kukkurajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
Ye kukkurā rājakulamhi vaddhā, koleyyakā vaṇṇabalūpapannā;
```

```
Teme na vajjhā mayamasma vajjhā, nāyaṃ saghaccā dubbalaghātikāyanti.
```

Kukkurajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 23. Gojānīyajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
Api passena semāno, sallebhi sallalīkato;
```

```
Seyyova vaḷavā gojo <note>bhojjo (sī.), bhojjho (syā. pī.)</note>, yuñja maññeva sārathīti.
```

Gojānīya <note>bhojājānīya (sī. syā. pī.)</note> jātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 24. Ājaññajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
Yadā yadā yattha yadā, yattha yattha yadā yadā;
```

```
Ājañño kurute vegaṃ, hāyanti tattha vāḷavāti.
```

Ājaññajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 25. Titthajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
Aññamaññehi <pb ed="T" n="1.0009" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0007" /> titthehi, assaṃ pāyehi sārathi;
```

```
Accāsanassa puriso, pāyāsassapi tappatīti.
```

Titthajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 26. Mahiḷāmukhajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
Purāṇacorāna <pb ed="V" n="1.0007" /> vaco nisamma, mahiḷāmukho pothayamanvacārī;
```

```
Susaññatānañhi vaco nisamma, gajuttamo sabbaguṇesu aṭṭhāti.
```

Mahiḷāmukhajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 27. Abhiṇhajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
Nālaṃ kabaḷaṃ padātave, na ca piṇḍaṃ na kuse na ghaṃsituṃ;
```

```
Maññāmi abhiṇhadassanā, nāgo snehamakāsi <note>sinehamakāsi (sī. syā. pī.)</note> kukkureti.
```

Abhiṇhajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 28. Nandivisālajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
Manuññameva <pb ed="T" n="1.0010" /> bhāseyya, nāmanuññaṃ kudācanaṃ;
```

```
Manuññaṃ bhāsamānassa, garuṃ bhāraṃ udaddhari;
```

```
Dhanañca naṃ alābhesi, tena cattamano ahūti.
```

Nandivisālajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 29. Kaṇhajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
Yato yato garu dhuraṃ, yato gambhīravattanī;
```

```
Tadāssu kaṇhaṃ yuñjanti, svāssu taṃ vahate dhuranti.
```

Kaṇhajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 30. Munikajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
Mā <pb ed="M" n="1.0008" /> munikassa pihayi, āturannāni bhuñjati;
```

```
Appossukko bhusaṃ khāda, etaṃ dīghāyulakkhaṇanti.
```

Munikajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Kuruṅgavaggo tatiyo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Kuruṅgassa <pb ed="V" n="1.0008" /> kukkuragojavaro, puna vāḷavassasirivhayano <note>sirivayano (sabbattha)</note>;
```

```
Mahiḷāmukhanāmanuññavaro, vahate dhura munikena dasāti.
```

#### 4. Kulāvakavaggo

#### 31. Kulāvakajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
Kulāvakā <pb ed="T" n="1.0011" /> mātali simbalismiṃ, īsāmukhena parivajjayassu;
```

```
Kāmaṃ cajāma asuresu pāṇaṃ, mā me dijā vikkulavā <note>māyime dijā vikulāvā (sī. syā. pī.)</note> ahesunti.
```

Kulāvakajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 32. Naccajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
Rudaṃ manuññaṃ rucirā ca piṭṭhi, veḷuriyavaṇṇūpanibhā <note>vaṇṇūpaṭibhā (syā.), vaṇṇasannibhā (ka.)</note> ca gīvā;
```

```
Byāmamattāni ca pekhuṇāni, naccena te dhītaraṃ no dadāmīti.
```

Naccajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 33. Sammodamānajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
Sammodamānā <pb ed="M" n="1.0009" /> gacchanti, jālamādāya pakkhino;
```

```
Yadā te vivadissanti, tadā ehinti me vasanti.
```

Sammodamānajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 34. Macchajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="T" n="1.0012" /> maṃ sītaṃ na maṃ uṇhaṃ, na maṃ jālasmi bādhanaṃ;
```

```
Yañca maṃ maññate macchī, aññaṃ so ratiyā gatoti.
```

Macchajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 35. Vaṭṭakajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
Santi <pb ed="V" n="1.0009" /> pakkhā apatanā, santi pādā avañcanā;
```

```
Mātāpitā ca nikkhantā, jātaveda paṭikkamāti.
```

Vaṭṭakajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 36. Sakuṇajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
Yaṃ nissitā jagatiruhaṃ vihaṅgamā, svāyaṃ aggiṃ pamuñcati;
```

```
Disā bhajatha vakkaṅgā <note>vaṅkaṅgā (syā.)</note>, jātaṃ saraṇato bhayanti.
```

Sakuṇajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 37. Tittirajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
Ye vuḍḍha <note>vaddha (sī. pī.)</note> mapacāyanti, narā dhammassa kovidā;
```

```
Diṭṭheva dhamme pāsaṃsā, samparāye ca suggatīti.
```

Tittirajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 38. Bakajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
Nāccantaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0013" /> nikatippañño, nikatyā sukhamedhati;
```

```
Ārādheti nikatippañño <note>ārādhe nikatippañño (pī.)</note>, bako kakkaṭakāmivāti.
```

Bakajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 39. Nandajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
Maññe <pb ed="M" n="1.0010" /> sovaṇṇayo rāsi, soṇṇamālā ca nandako;
```

```
Yattha dāso āmajāto, ṭhito thullāni <note>thūlāni (ka.)</note> gajjatīti.
```

Nandajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 40. Khadiraṅgārajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
Kāmaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0010" /> patāmi nirayaṃ, uddhaṃpādo avaṃsiro;
```

```
Nānariyaṃ karissāmi, handa piṇḍaṃ paṭiggahāti.
```

Khadiraṅgārajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Kulāvakavaggo catuttho.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Sirimātali dhītara pakkhivaro, ratiyāgato mātāpitā ca puna;
```

```
Jagatīruha vuḍḍha sukakkaṭako, tathā nandakapiṇḍavarena dasāti.
```

#### 5. Atthakāmavaggo

#### 41. Losakajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
Yo <pb ed="T" n="1.0014" /> atthakāmassa hitānukampino, ovajjamāno na karoti sāsanaṃ;
```

```
Ajiyā pādamolamba <note>pādamolumba (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, mittako viya socatīti.
```

Losakajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 42. Kapotajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
Yo <pb ed="M" n="1.0011" /> atthakāmassa hitānukampino, ovajjamāno na karoti sāsanaṃ;
```

```
Kapotakassa vacanaṃ akatvā, amittahatthatthagatova setīti.
```

Kapotajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 43. Veḷukajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
Yo atthakāmassa hitānukampino, ovajjamāno na karoti sāsanaṃ;
```

```
Evaṃ so nihato seti, veḷukassa yathā pitāti.
```

Veḷukajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 44. Makasajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
Seyyo <pb ed="T" n="1.0015" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0011" /> amitto matiyā upeto, na tveva mitto mativippahīno;
```

```
Makasaṃ vadhissanti hi eḷamūgo, putto pitu abbhidā uttamaṅganti.
```

Makasajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 45. Rohiṇijātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
Seyyo amitto medhāvī, yañce bālānukampako;
```

```
Passa rohiṇikaṃ jammiṃ, mātaraṃ hantvāna socatīti.
```

Rohiṇijātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 46. Ārāmadūsakajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
Na ve anatthakusalena, atthacariyā sukhāvahā;
```

```
Hāpeti atthaṃ dummedho, kapi ārāmiko yathāti.
```

Ārāmadūsakajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 47. Vāruṇidūsakajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="M" n="1.0012" /> ve anatthakusalena, atthacariyā sukhāvahā;
```

```
Hāpeti atthaṃ dummedho, koṇḍañño vāruṇiṃ yathāti.
```

Vāruṇidūsakajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 48. Vedabbajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
Anupāyena <pb ed="T" n="1.0016" /> yo atthaṃ, icchati so vihaññati;
```

```
Cetā haniṃsu vedabbaṃ <note>vedabbhaṃ (sī. pī.)</note>, sabbe te byasanamajjhagūti.
```

Vedabba <note>vedabbha (sī. pī.)</note> jātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 49. Nakkhattajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
Nakkhattaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0012" /> paṭimānentaṃ, attho bālaṃ upaccagā;
```

```
Attho atthassa nakkhattaṃ, kiṃ karissanti tārakāti.
```

Nakkhattajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 50. Dummedhajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
Dummedhānaṃ sahassena, yañño me upayācito;
```

```
Idāni khohaṃ yajissāmi, bahu <note>bahū (sī. pī.), bahuṃ (ka.)</note> adhammiko janoti.
```

Dummedhajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Atthakāmavaggo pañcamo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Atha mittaka mātu kapotavaro, tathā veḷūka eḷamūgo rohiṇī;
```

```
Kapi <pb ed="T" n="1.0017" /> vāruṇi cetacarā ca puna, tathā tāraka yaññavarena dasāti.
```

Paṭhamo paṇṇāsako.

#### 6. Āsīsavaggo

#### 51.Mahāsīlavajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
Āsīsetheva <pb ed="M" n="1.0013" /> <note>āsiṃsetheva (sī. syā. pī.)</note> puriso, na nibbindeyya paṇḍito;
```

```
Passāmi vohaṃ attānaṃ, yathā icchiṃ tathā ahūti.
```

Mahāsīlavajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 52. Cūḷajanakajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
Vāyametheva puriso, na nibbindeyya paṇḍito;
```

```
Passāmi vohaṃ attānaṃ, udakā thalamubbhatanti.
```

Cūḷajanakajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 53. Puṇṇapātijātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
Tatheva <pb ed="V" n="1.0013" /> puṇṇā pātiyo, aññāyaṃ vattate kathā;
```

```
Ākāraṇena <note>ākārakena (sī. syā. pī.)</note> jānāmi, na cāyaṃ bhaddikā surāti.
```

Puṇṇapātijātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 54. Kiṃphalajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
Nāyaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0018" /> rukkho durāruho, napi gāmato ārakā;
```

```
Ākāraṇena jānāmi, nāyaṃ sāduphalo dumoti.
```

Kiṃphalajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 55. Pañcāvudhajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
Yo alīnena cittena, alīnamanaso naro;
```

```
Bhāveti kusalaṃ dhammaṃ, yogakkhemassa pattiyā;
```

```
Pāpuṇe anupubbena, sabbasaṃyojanakkhayanti.
```

Pañcāvudhajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 56. Kañcanakkhandhajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
Yo <pb ed="M" n="1.0014" /> pahaṭṭhena cittena, pahaṭṭhamanaso naro;
```

```
Bhāveti kusalaṃ dhammaṃ, yogakkhemassa pattiyā;
```

```
Pāpuṇe anupubbena, sabbasaṃyojanakkhayanti.
```

Kañcanakkhandhajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 57. Vānarindajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
Yassete caturo dhammā, vānarinda yathā tava;
```

```
Saccaṃ dhammo dhiti <note>dhitī (sī. pī.)</note> cāgo, diṭṭhaṃ so ativattatīti.
```

Vānarindajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 58. Tayodhammajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
Yassete <pb ed="T" n="1.0019" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0014" /> ca <note>yassa ete (sī. pī.)</note> tayo dhammā, vānarinda yathā tava;
```

```
Dakkhiyaṃ sūriyaṃ paññā, diṭṭhaṃ so ativattatīti.
```

Tayodhammajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 59. Bherivādakajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
Dhame dhame nātidhame, atidhantañhi pāpakaṃ;
```

```
Dhantena hi sataṃ laddhaṃ, atidhantena nāsitanti.
```

Bherivādakajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 60. Saṅkhadhamajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
Dhame dhame nātidhame, atidhantañhi pāpakaṃ;
```

```
Dhantenādhigatā bhogā, te tāto vidhamī dhamanti.
```

Saṅkhadhamajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Āsīsavaggo chaṭṭho.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Yathā <pb ed="M" n="1.0015" /> icchiṃ tathāhudakā thalā, sura sāduphalo ca alīnamano;
```

```
Sampahaṭṭhamano <pb ed="T" n="1.0020" /> caturo ca tayo, sataladdhaka bhogadhanena dasāti.
```

#### 7. Itthivaggo

#### 61. Asātamantajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
Asā lokitthiyo nāma, velā tāsaṃ na vijjati;
```

```
Sārattā ca pagabbhā ca, sikhī sabbaghaso yathā;
```

```
Tā hitvā pabbajissāmi, vivekamanubrūhayanti.
```

Asātamantajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 62. Aṇḍabhūtajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
Yaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0015" /> brāhmaṇo avādesi, vīṇaṃ samukhaveṭhito;
```

```
Aṇḍabhūtā bhatā bhariyā, tāsu ko jātu vissaseti.
```

Aṇḍabhūtajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 63. Takkapaṇḍitajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
Kodhanā akataññū ca, pisuṇā mittabhedikā <note>pisuṇā ca vibhedikā (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Brahmacariyaṃ cara bhikkhu, so sukhaṃ na vihāhasīti <note>pihāhisīti (sī. syā. pī.), vihāyasi (ka.)</note>.
```

Takkapaṇḍitajātakaṃ <note>takkajātakaṃ (sī. syā. pī. aṭṭha.)</note> tatiyaṃ.

#### 64. Durājānajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
Mā <pb ed="T" n="1.0021" /> su nandi icchati maṃ, mā su soci na micchati <note>na icchati (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Thīnaṃ bhāvo durājāno, macchassevodake gatanti.
```

Durājānajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 65. Anabhiratijātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
Yathā <pb ed="M" n="1.0016" /> nadī ca pantho ca, pānāgāraṃ sabhā papā;
```

```
Evaṃ lokitthiyo nāma, nāsaṃ kujjhanti paṇḍitāti.
```

Anabhiratijātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 66. Mudulakkhaṇajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
Ekā icchā pure āsi, aladdhā mudulakkhaṇaṃ;
```

```
Yato laddhā aḷārakkhī, icchā icchaṃ vijāyathāti.
```

Mudulakkhaṇajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 67. Ucchaṅgajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
Ucchaṅge deva me putto, pathe dhāvantiyā pati;
```

```
Tañca desaṃ na passāmi, yato sodariyamānayeti <note>sodariyaṃ naye (ka.)</note>.
```

Ucchaṅgajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 68. Sāketajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
Yasmiṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0022" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0016" /> mano nivisati, cittañcāpi <note>cittaṃ vāpi (katthaci)</note> pasīdati;
```

```
Adiṭṭhapubbake pose, kāmaṃ tasmimpi vissaseti.
```

Sāketajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 69. Visavantajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
Dhiratthu taṃ visaṃ vantaṃ, yamahaṃ jīvitakāraṇā;
```

```
Vantaṃ paccāvamissāmi <note>paccāharissāmi (ka.)</note>, mataṃ me jīvitā varanti.
```

Visavantajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 70. Kuddālajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
Na taṃ jitaṃ sādhu jitaṃ, yaṃ jitaṃ avajīyati;
```

```
Taṃ kho jitaṃ sādhu jitaṃ, yaṃ jitaṃ nāvajīyatīti.
```

Kuddālajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Itthivaggo sattamo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Sikhīsabbaghasopi <pb ed="M" n="1.0017" /> ca vīṇavaro, pisuṇā mittabhedikā nandī nadī;
```

```
Mudulakkhaṇa sodariyā ca mano, visa sādhujitena bhavanti dasāti.
```

#### 8. Varuṇavaggo

#### 71. Varuṇajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
Yo <pb ed="T" n="1.0023" /> pubbe karaṇīyāni, pacchā so kātumicchati;
```

```
Varuṇakaṭṭha <note>varaṇakaṭṭha (sī. pī.)</note> bhañjova, sa pacchā manutappatīti.
```

Varuṇajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 72. Sīlavahatthijātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
Akataññussa <pb ed="V" n="1.0017" /> posassa, niccaṃ vivaradassino;
```

```
Sabbaṃ ce pathaviṃ <note>paṭhaviṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> dajjā, neva naṃ abhirādhayeti.
```

Sīlavahatthijātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 73. Saccaṃkirajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
Saccaṃ kirevamāhaṃsu, narā ekacciyā idha;
```

```
Kaṭṭhaṃ niplavitaṃ <note>viplāvitaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> seyyo, na tvevekacciyo naroti.
```

Saccaṃkirajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 74. Rukkhadhammajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
Sādhū sambahulā ñātī, api rukkhā araññajā;
```

```
Vāto <pb ed="T" n="1.0024" /> vahati ekaṭṭhaṃ, brahantampi vanappatinti.
```

Rukkhadhammajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 75. Macchajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
Abhitthanaya <pb ed="M" n="1.0018" /> pajjunna, nidhiṃ kākassa nāsaya;
```

```
Kākaṃ sokāya randhehi, mañca sokā pamocayāti.
```

Macchajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 76. Asaṅkiyajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
Asaṅkiyomhi gāmamhi, araññe natthi me bhayaṃ;
```

```
Ujuṃ maggaṃ samārūḷho, mettāya karuṇāya cāti.
```

Asaṅkiyajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 77. Mahāsupinajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
Usabhā <pb ed="V" n="1.0018" /> rukkhā gāviyo gavā ca, asso kaṃso siṅgālī <note>sigāsī (sī. syā. pī.)</note> ca kumbho;
```

```
Pokkharaṇī ca apākacandanaṃ, lābūni sīdanti silā plavanti.
```

```
Maṇḍūkiyo kaṇhasappe gilanti, kākaṃ supaṇṇā parivārayanti;
```

```
Tasā <pb ed="T" n="1.0025" /> vakā eḷakānaṃ bhayāhi, vipariyāso <note>vipariyāyo (syā. ka.)</note> vattati nayidha matthīti.
```

Mahāsupinajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 78. Illisajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
Ubho khañjā ubho kuṇī, ubho visamacakkhukā <note>cakkhulā (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Ubhinnaṃ piḷakā <note>pīḷakā (syā.)</note> jātā, nāhaṃ passāmi illisanti.
```

Illisajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 79. Kharassarajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
Yato <pb ed="M" n="1.0019" /> viluttā ca hatā ca gāvo, daḍḍhāni gehāni jano ca nīto;
```

```
Athāgamā puttahatāya putto, kharassaraṃ ḍiṇḍimaṃ <note>deṇḍimaṃ (sī. syā. pī.), ḍindimaṃ (ka.)</note> vādayantoti.
```

Kharassarajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 80. Bhīmasenajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
Yaṃ te pavikatthitaṃ pure, atha te pūtisarā sajanti pacchā;
```

```
Ubhayaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0026" /> na sameti bhīmasena, yuddhakathā ca idañca te vihaññanti.
```

Bhīmasenajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Varuṇavaggo <note>varaṇavaggo (sī. pī.)</note> aṭṭhamo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Varuṇā akataññūvare tu saccavaraṃ, savanappatinā ca abhitthanaya;
```

```
Karuṇāya silāplava illisato, puna ḍiṇḍimapūtisarena dasāti.
```

#### 9. Apāyimhavaggo

#### 81. Surāpānajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
Apāyimha <pb ed="V" n="1.0019" /> anaccimha, agāyimha rudimha ca;
```

```
Visaññikaraṇiṃ pitvā <note>pītvā (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, diṭṭhā nāhumha vānarāti.
```

Surāpānajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 82. Mittavindakajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
Atikkamma <pb ed="T" n="1.0027" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0020" /> ramaṇakaṃ, sadāmattañca dūbhakaṃ;
```

```
Svāsi pāsāṇamāsīno, yasmā jīvaṃ na mokkhasīti.
```

Mittavindakajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 83. Kālakaṇṇijātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
Mitto have sattapadena hoti, sahāyo pana dvādasakena hoti;
```

```
Māsaḍḍhamāsena ca ñāti hoti, tatuttariṃ attasamopi hoti;
```

```
Sohaṃ kathaṃ attasukhassa hetu, cirasanthutaṃ <note>cirasandhavaṃ (ka.), cirasatthunaṃ (pī.)</note> kāḷakaṇṇiṃ jaheyyanti.
```

Kālakaṇṇijātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 84. Atthassadvārajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
Ārogyamicche paramañca lābhaṃ, sīlañca vuddhānumataṃ sutañca;
```

```
Dhammānuvattī ca alīnatā ca, atthassa dvārā pamukhā chaḷeteti.
```

Atthassadvārajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 85. Kiṃpakkajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
Āyatiṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0028" /> dosaṃ nāññāya, yo kāme paṭisevati;
```

```
Vipākante hananti naṃ, kiṃpakkamiva bhakkhitanti.
```

Kiṃpakkajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 86. Sīlavīmaṃsakajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
Sīlaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0020" /> kireva kalyāṇaṃ, sīlaṃ loke anuttaraṃ;
```

```
Passa ghoraviso nāgo, sīlavāti na haññatīti.
```

Sīlavīmaṃsakajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 87. Maṅgalajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
Yassa <pb ed="M" n="1.0021" /> maṅgalā samūhatāse <note>samūhatā (sī. syā. pī. su. ni. 362</note>, uppātā <note>uppādā (pī.)</note> supinā ca lakkhaṇā ca;
```

```
So <note>sa (sī. pī. ka.)</note> maṅgaladosavītivatto, yugayogādhigato na jātumetīti.
```

Maṅgalajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 88. Sārambhajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
Kalyāṇimeva muñceyya, na hi muñceyya pāpikaṃ;
```

```
Mokkho kalyāṇiyā sādhu, mutvā tappati pāpikanti.
```

Sārambhajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 89. Kuhakajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
Vācāva <pb ed="T" n="1.0029" /> kira te āsi, saṇhā sakhilabhāṇino;
```

```
Tiṇamatte asajjittho, no ca nikkhasataṃ haranti.
```

Kuhakajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 90. Akataññujātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
Yo pubbe katakalyāṇo, katattho nāvabujjhati;
```

```
Pacchā kicce samuppanne, kattāraṃ nādhigacchatīti.
```

Akataññujātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Apāyimhavaggo navamo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Apāyimha ca dūbhakaṃ sattapadaṃ, chaḷadvara ca āyatinā ca puna;
```

```
Ahisīlava maṅgali pāpikassā, sataṃnikkha katatthavarena dasāti.
```

#### 10. Littavaggo

#### 91. Littajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
Littaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0021" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0022" /> paramena tejasā, gilamakkhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0030" /> puriso na bujjhati;
```

```
Gila re gila pāpadhuttaka, pacchā te kaṭukaṃ bhavissatīti.
```

Littajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 92. Mahāsārajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
Ukkaṭṭhe sūramicchanti, mantīsu akutūhalaṃ;
```

```
Piyañca annapānamhi, atthe jāte ca paṇḍitanti.
```

Mahāsārajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 93. Visāsabhojanajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§93.</p>

```
Na vissase avissatthe, vissatthepi na vissase;
```

```
Vissāsā bhayamanveti, sīhaṃva migamātukāti <note>migamātuyā (ka.)</note>.
```

Visāsabhojanajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 94. Lomahaṃsajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§94.</p>

```
Sotatto sosindo <note>sosīto (sī. syā. pī.), sosino (ka.)</note> ceva, eko bhiṃsanake vane;
```

```
Naggo na caggimāsīno, esanāpasuto munīti.
```

Lomahaṃsajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 95. Mahāsudassanajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§95.</p>

```
Aniccā <pb ed="T" n="1.0031" /> vata saṅkhārā, uppādavayadhammino;
```

```
Uppajjitvā nirujjhanti, tesaṃ vūpasamo sukhoti.
```

Mahāsudassanajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 96. Telapattajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§96.</p>

```
Samatittikaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0022" /> anavasekaṃ, telapattaṃ yathā parihareyya;
```

```
Evaṃ sacittamanurakkhe, patthayāno disaṃ agatapubbanti.
```

Telapattajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 97. Nāmasiddhijātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§97.</p>

```
Jīvakañca <pb ed="M" n="1.0023" /> mataṃ disvā, dhanapāliñca duggataṃ;
```

```
Panthakañca vane mūḷhaṃ, pāpako punarāgatoti.
```

Nāmasiddhijātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 98. Kūṭavāṇijajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§98.</p>

```
Sādhu <pb ed="T" n="1.0032" /> kho paṇḍito nāma, na tveva atipaṇḍito;
```

```
Atipaṇḍitena puttena, manamhi upakūḷitoti <note>upakūlitoti (sī.), upakuṭṭhitoti (syā.), upakuṭito (ka.)</note>.
```

Kūṭavāṇijajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 99. Parosahassajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§99.</p>

```
Parosahassampi samāgatānaṃ, kandeyyuṃ te vassasataṃ apaññā;
```

```
Ekova seyyo puriso sapañño, yo bhāsitassa vijānāti atthanti.
```

Parosahassajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 100. Asātarūpajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§100.</p>

```
Asātaṃ sātarūpena, piyarūpena appiyaṃ;
```

```
Dukkhaṃ sukhassa rūpena, pamattamativattatīti.
```

Asātarūpajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Littavaggo dasamo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Gilamakkhakutūhala <pb ed="T" n="1.0033" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0023" /> mātukassā, muninā ca aniccata pattavaraṃ;
```

```
Dhanapālivaro atipaṇḍitako, saparosahassaasātadasāti.
```

Majjhimo paṇṇāsako.

#### 11. Parosatavaggo

#### 101. Parosatajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§101.</p>

```
Parosataṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0024" /> cepi samāgatānaṃ, jhāyeyyuṃ te vassasataṃ apaññā;
```

```
Ekova seyyo puriso sapañño, yo bhāsitassa vijānāti atthanti.
```

Parosatajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 102. Paṇṇikajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§102.</p>

```
Yo dukkhaphuṭṭhāya bhaveyya tāṇaṃ, so me pitā dubbhi <note>dūbhi (sī. pī.)</note> vane karoti;
```

```
Sā kassa kandāmi vanassa majjhe, yo tāyitā so sahasaṃ <note>sahasā (sī. syā. pī.)</note> karotīti.
```

Paṇṇikajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 103. Verijātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§103.</p>

```
Yattha <pb ed="T" n="1.0034" /> verī nivisati <note>nivasati (sī. ka.)</note>, na vase tattha paṇḍito;
```

```
Ekarattaṃ dirattaṃ vā, dukkhaṃ vasati verisūti.
```

Verijātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 104. Mittavindakajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§104.</p>

```
Catubbhi aṭṭhajjhagamā, aṭṭhāhipi ca soḷasa;
```

```
Soḷasāhi ca bāttiṃsa <note>battiṃsa (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, atricchaṃ cakkamāsado;
```

```
Icchāhatassa posassa, cakkaṃ bhamati matthaketi.
```

Mittavindakajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 105. Dubbalakaṭṭhajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§105.</p>

```
Bahumpetaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0024" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0025" /> vane kaṭṭhaṃ, vāto bhañjati dubbalaṃ;
```

```
Tassa ce bhāyasī nāga, kiso nūna bhavissasīti.
```

Dubbalakaṭṭhajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 106. Udañcanījātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§106.</p>

```
Sukhaṃ vata maṃ jīvantaṃ <note>sukhakaṃ vata jīvaṃ (ka.)</note>, pacamānā udañcanī;
```

```
Corī jāyappavādena, telaṃ loṇañca yācatīti.
```

Udañcanījātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 107. Sālittakajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§107.</p>

```
Sādhu <pb ed="T" n="1.0035" /> kho sippakaṃ nāma, api yādisa kīdisaṃ;
```

```
Passa khañjappahārena, laddhā gāmā catuddisāti.
```

Sālittakajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 108. Bāhiyajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§108.</p>

```
Sikkheyya sikkhitabbāni, santi tacchandino <note>sacchandino (sī. pī.)</note> janā;
```

```
Bāhiyā hi <note>pi (sī. syā. pī.)</note> suhannena, rājānamabhirādhayīti.
```

Bāhiyajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 109. Kuṇḍapūvajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§109.</p>

```
Yathanno puriso hoti, tathannā tassa devatā;
```

```
Āharetaṃ kuṇḍapūvaṃ <note>kaṇaṃ pūvaṃ (sī. pī.)</note>, mā me bhāgaṃ vināsayāti.
```

Kuṇḍapūvajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 110. Sabbasaṃhārakapañhajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§110.</p>

```
Sabbasaṃhārako <pb ed="V" n="1.0025" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0026" /> <note>sabbasāhārako (ka.)</note> natthi, suddhaṃ kaṅgu pavāyati;
```

```
Alikaṃ bhāyatiyaṃ dhuttī, saccamāha mahallikāti.
```

Sabbasaṃhārakapañhajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Parosatavaggo ekādasamo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Saparosata tāyita verī <pb ed="T" n="1.0036" /> puna, bhamacakkatha nāgasirivhayano;
```

```
Sukhakañca vata sippaka bāhiyā, kuṇḍapūva mahallikakā ca dasāti.
```

#### 12. Haṃcivaggo

#### 111. Gadrabhapañhajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§111.</p>

```
Haṃci <note>haṃsi (sī. syā.), hañci (?)</note> tuvaṃ evamaññasi seyyo, puttena pitāti rājaseṭṭha;
```

```
Handassatarassa te ayaṃ, assatarassa hi gadrabho pitāti.
```

Gadrabhapañhajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 112. Amarādevīpañhajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§112.</p>

```
Yena sattubilaṅgā ca, diguṇapalāso ca pupphito;
```

```
Yena dadāmi <note>yenā’dāmi (sī. syā.)</note> tena vadāmi, yena na dadāmi <note>yena nā’dāmi (sī. syā.)</note> na tena vadāmi;
```

```
Esa <pb ed="T" n="1.0037" /> maggo yavamajjhakassa, etaṃ channapathaṃ vijānāhīti.
```

Amarādevīpañhajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 113. Siṅgālajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§113.</p>

```
Saddahāsi <pb ed="M" n="1.0027" /> siṅgālassa <note>sigālassa (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, surāpītassa brāhmaṇa;
```

```
Sippikānaṃ sataṃ natthi, kuto kaṃsasatā duveti.
```

Siṅgālajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 114. Mitacintijātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§114.</p>

```
Bahucintī <pb ed="V" n="1.0026" /> appacintī, ubho jāle abajjhare;
```

```
Mitacintī pamocesī, ubho tattha samāgatāti.
```

Mitacintijātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 115. Anusāsikajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§115.</p>

```
Yāyañña <note>yāyaññe (ka.)</note> manusāsati, sayaṃ loluppacārinī;
```

```
Sāyaṃ vipakkhikā seti, hatā cakkena sāsikāti <note>sālikāti (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

Anusāsikajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 116. Dubbacajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§116.</p>

```
Atikaramakarācariya<pb ed="T" n="1.0038" />, mayhampetaṃ na ruccati;
```

```
Catutthe laṅghayitvāna, pañcamāyasi āvutoti.
```

Dubbacajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 117. Tittirajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§117.</p>

```
Accuggatātilapatā <note>atibalatā (sī. syā. pī.), atilapakā (katthaci)</note>, ativelaṃ pabhāsitā;
```

```
Vācā hanati dummedhaṃ, tittiraṃvātivassitanti.
```

Tittirajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 118. Vaṭṭakajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§118.</p>

```
Nācintayanto puriso, visesamadhigacchati;
```

```
Cintitassa phalaṃ passa, muttosmi vadhabandhanāti.
```

Vaṭṭakajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 119. Akālarāvijātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§119.</p>

```
Amātāpitarasaṃvaddho <pb ed="M" n="1.0028" /> <note>pitari (sī. pī.), pitu (syā.)</note>, anācerakule vasaṃ;
```

```
Nāyaṃ kālaṃ akālaṃ vā, abhijānāti kukkuṭoti.
```

Akālarāvijātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 120. Bandhanamokkhajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§120.</p>

```
Abaddhā <pb ed="T" n="1.0039" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0027" /> tattha bajjhanti, yattha bālā pabhāsare;
```

```
Baddhāpi tattha muccanti, yattha dhīrā pabhāsareti.
```

Bandhanamokkhajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Haṃcivaggo <note>haṃsivaggo (sī. syā.)</note> dvādasamo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Atha gadrabha sattuva kaṃsasataṃ, bahucinti sāsikāyātikara;
```

```
Ativela visesamanācariyova, dhīrāpabhāsaratena dasāti.
```

#### 13. Kusanāḷivaggo

#### 121. Kusanāḷijātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§121.</p>

```
Kare sarikkho atha vāpi seṭṭho, nihīnako vāpi kareyya eko;
```

```
Kareyyumete <note>kareyyuṃ te (sī. pī.)</note> byasane uttamatthaṃ, yathā ahaṃ kusanāḷi rucāyanti.
```

Kusanāḷijātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 122. Dummedhajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§122.</p>

```
Yasaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0040" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0029" /> laddhāna dummedho, anatthaṃ carati attano;
```

```
Attano ca paresañca, hiṃsāya paṭipajjatīti.
```

Dummedhajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 123. Naṅgalīsajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§123.</p>

```
Asabbatthagāmiṃ vācaṃ, bālo sabbattha bhāsati;
```

```
Nāyaṃ dadhiṃ vedi na <note>na vedi (ka.)</note> naṅgalīsaṃ, dadhippayaṃ <note>dadhimpayaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> maññati naṅgalīsanti.
```

Naṅgalīsajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 124. Ambajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§124.</p>

```
Vāyametheva <pb ed="V" n="1.0028" /> puriso, na nibbindeyya paṇḍito;
```

```
Vāyāmassa phalaṃ passa, bhuttā ambā anītihanti.
```

Ambajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 125. Kaṭāhakajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§125.</p>

```
Bahumpi so vikattheyya, aññaṃ janapadaṃ gato;
```

```
Anvāgantvāna dūseyya, bhuñja bhoge kaṭāhakāti.
```

Kaṭāhakajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 126. Asilakkhaṇajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§126.</p>

```
Tadevekassa <pb ed="T" n="1.0041" /> <note>tathevekassa (sī. syā. pī. aṭṭha. mūlapāṭho)</note> kalyāṇaṃ, tadevekassa pāpakaṃ;
```

```
Tasmā sabbaṃ na kalyāṇaṃ, sabbaṃ vāpi na pāpakanti.
```

Asilakkhaṇajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 127. Kalaṇḍukajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§127.</p>

```
Te desā tāni vatthūni, ahañca vanagocaro;
```

```
Anuvicca kho taṃ gaṇheyyuṃ, piva <note>pipa (sī. pī.)</note> khīraṃ kalaṇḍukāti.
```

Kalaṇḍukajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 128. Biḷāravatajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§128.</p>

```
Yo <pb ed="M" n="1.0030" /> ve dhammaṃ dhajaṃ <note>dhammadhajaṃ (syā. pī. ka.)</note> katvā, nigūḷho pāpamācare;
```

```
Vissāsayitvā bhūtāni, biḷāraṃ nāma taṃ vatanti.
```

Biḷāravatajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 129. Aggikabhāradvājajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§129.</p>

```
Nāyaṃ sikhā puññahetu, ghāsahetu ayaṃ sikhā;
```

```
Nāṅguṭṭhagaṇanaṃ yāti, alaṃ te hotu aggikāti.
```

Aggikabhāradvājajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 130. Kosiyajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§130.</p>

```
Yathā <pb ed="T" n="1.0042" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0029" /> vācā ca bhuñjassu, yathā bhuttañca byāhara;
```

```
Ubhayaṃ te na sameti, vācā bhuttañca kosiyeti.
```

Kosiyajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Kusanāḷivaggo <note>sarikkhavaggo (ka.)</note> terasamo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Kusanāḷisirivhayano ca yasaṃ, dadhi mamba kaṭāhakapañcamako;
```

```
Atha pāpaka khīra biḷāravataṃ, sikhi kosiyasavhayanena dasāti.
```

#### 14. Asampadānavaggo

#### 131. Asampadānajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§131.</p>

```
Asampadānenitarītarassa, bālassa mittāni kalī bhavanti;
```

```
Tasmā harāmi bhusaṃ aḍḍhamānaṃ, mā me mitti jīyittha sassatāyanti.
```

Asampadānajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 132. Bhīrukajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§132.</p>

```
Kusalūpadese <pb ed="T" n="1.0043" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0031" /> dhitiyā daḷhāya ca, anivattitattābhayabhīrutāya <note>avatthitattābhayabhīrutāya (sī. syā. pī.)</note> ca;
```

```
Na rakkhasīnaṃ vasamāgamimhase, sa sotthibhāvo mahatā bhayena meti.
```

Bhīruka <note>pañcagaruka (sī. pī.), pañcabhīruka (syā.), abhayabhīruta§(?)</note> jātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 133. Ghatāsanajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§133.</p>

```
Khemaṃ yahiṃ tattha arī udīrito <note>ari uddharito (ka.)</note>, dakassa majjhe jalate ghatāsano;
```

```
Na ajja vāso mahiyā mahīruhe, disā bhajavho saraṇājja no bhayanti.
```

Ghatāsanajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 134. Jhānasodhanajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§134.</p>

```
Ye <pb ed="V" n="1.0030" /> saññino tepi duggatā, yepi asaññino tepi duggatā;
```

```
Etaṃ ubhayaṃ vivajjaya, taṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0044" /> samāpattisukhaṃ anaṅgaṇanti.
```

Jhānasodhanajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 135. Candābhajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§135.</p>

```
Candābhaṃ sūriyābhañca, yodha paññāya gādhati.
```

```
Avitakkena jhānena, hoti ābhassarūpagoti.
```

Candābhajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 136. Suvaṇṇahaṃsajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§136.</p>

```
Yaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0032" /> laddhaṃ tena tuṭṭhabbaṃ, atilobho hi pāpako;
```

```
Haṃsarājaṃ gahetvāna, suvaṇṇā parihāyathāti.
```

Suvaṇṇahaṃsajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 137. Babbujātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§137.</p>

```
Yattheko labhate babbu, dutiyo tattha jāyati;
```

```
Tatiyo ca catuttho ca, idaṃ te babbukā bilanti.
```

Babbujātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 138. Godhajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§138.</p>

```
Kiṃ te jaṭāhi dummedha, kiṃ te ajinasāṭiyā;
```

```
Abbhantaraṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0045" /> te gahanaṃ, bāhiraṃ parimajjasīti.
```

Godhajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 139. Ubhatobhaṭṭhajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§139.</p>

```
Akkhī bhinnā paṭo naṭṭho, sakhigehe ca bhaṇḍanaṃ;
```

```
Ubhato paduṭṭhā kammantā <note>paduṭṭhakammanto (sī.), paduṭṭho kammanto (pī.)</note>, udakamhi thalamhi cāti.
```

Ubhatobhaṭṭhajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 140. Kākajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§140.</p>

```
Niccaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0031" /> ubbiggahadayā, sabbalokavihesakā;
```

```
Tasmā nesaṃ vasā natthi, kākānamhāka <note>kākānasmāka (sī. syā. pī.)</note> ñātinanti.
```

Kākajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Asampadānavaggo cuddasamo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Itarītara <pb ed="M" n="1.0033" /> rakkhasi khemiyo ca, parosatapañhena ābhassaro puna;
```

```
Atha haṃsavaruttamababbujaṭaṃ, paṭanaṭṭhaka kākavarena dasāti.
```

#### 15. Kakaṇṭakavaggo

#### 141. Godhajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§141.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="T" n="1.0046" /> pāpajanasaṃsevī, accantasukhamedhati;
```

```
Godhākulaṃ <note>godhakkulaṃ (ka.)</note> kakaṇṭāva <note>kakaṇṭakā (ka.)</note>, kaliṃ pāpeti attananti.
```

Godhajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 142. Siṅgālajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§142.</p>

```
Etañhi te durājānaṃ, yaṃ sesi matasāyikaṃ;
```

```
Yassa te kaḍḍhamānassa, hatthā daṇḍo na muccatīti.
```

Siṅgālajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 143. Virocajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§143.</p>

```
Lasī ca te nipphalitā, matthako ca padālito <note>vidālito (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Sabbā te phāsukā bhaggā, ajja kho tvaṃ virocasīti.
```

Virocajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 144. Naṅguṭṭhajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§144.</p>

```
Bahumpetaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0032" /> asabbhi <note>bahupetamasabbhi (ka.)</note> jātaveda, yaṃ taṃ vāladhinābhipūjayāma;
```

```
Maṃsārahassa <pb ed="T" n="1.0047" /> natthajja maṃsaṃ, naṅguṭṭhampi bhavaṃ paṭiggahātūti.
```

Naṅguṭṭhajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 145. Rādhajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§145.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="M" n="1.0034" /> tvaṃ rādha vijānāsi, aḍḍharatte anāgate;
```

```
Abyayataṃ <note>abyāyataṃ (sī. syā. pī.), abyattataṃ (?)</note> vilapasi, virattā kosiyāyaneti.
```

Rādhajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 146. Samuddakākajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§146.</p>

```
Api nu hanukā santā, mukhañca parisussati;
```

```
Oramāma na pārema, pūrateva mahodadhīti.
```

Samuddakākajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 147. Puppharattajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§147.</p>

```
Nayidaṃ dukkhaṃ aduṃ dukkhaṃ, yaṃ maṃ tudati vāyaso;
```

```
Yaṃ sāmā puppharattena, kattikaṃ nānubhossatīti.
```

Puppharattajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 148. Siṅgālajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§148.</p>

```
Nāhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0048" /> punaṃ na ca punaṃ, na cāpi apunappunaṃ;
```

```
Hatthibondiṃ pavekkhāmi, tathā hi bhayatajjitoti.
```

Siṅgālajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 149. Ekapaṇṇajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§149.</p>

```
Ekapaṇṇo ayaṃ rukkho, na bhūmyā caturaṅgulo;
```

```
Phalena visakappena, mahāyaṃ kiṃ bhavissatīti.
```

Ekapaṇṇajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 150. Sañjīvajātakaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§150.</p>

```
Asantaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0033" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0035" /> yo paggaṇhāti, asantaṃ cūpasevati;
```

```
Tameva ghāsaṃ kurute, byaggho sañjīvako yathāti.
```

Sañjīvajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Kakaṇṭaka <note>pāpasevana (ka.)</note> vaggo pannarasamo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Sukhamedhati daṇḍavaro ca puna, lasi vāladhi pañcamarādhavaro;
```

```
Samahodadhi <pb ed="T" n="1.0049" /> kattika bondi puna, caturaṅgulabyagghavarena dasāti.
```

(Uparimo paṇṇāsako.) <note>( ) sīhaḷapotthakeyeva dissati</note>

Atha vagguddānaṃ –

```
Apaṇṇakaṃ sīlavaggakuruṅga, kulāvakaṃ atthakāmena pañcamaṃ;
```

```
Āsīso itthivaruṇaṃ apāyi, littavaggena te dasa;
```

```
Parosataṃ haṃci kusanāḷi <note>haṃsi sarikkhaṃ (sabbattha)</note>, asampadaṃ kakaṇṭakavaggo.
```

Ekanipātamhilaṅkatanti.

<trailer rend="centre">Ekakanipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.</trailer>

### 2. Dukanipāto

#### 1. Daḷhavaggo

#### 151. Rājovādajātakaṃ (2-1-1)

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
Daḷhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0050" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0034" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0036" /> daḷhassa khipati, balliko <note>malliko (sī. pī.)</note> mudunā muduṃ;
```

```
Sādhumpi sādhunā jeti, asādhumpi asādhunā;
```

```
Etādiso ayaṃ rājā, maggā uyyāhi sārathi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
Akkodhena jine kodhaṃ, asādhuṃ sādhunā jine;
```

```
Jine kadariyaṃ dānena, saccenālikavādinaṃ;
```

```
Etādiso ayaṃ rājā, maggā uyyāhi sārathīti.
```

Rājovādajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 152. Asamekkhitakammantaṃ, turitābhinipātinaṃ.

```
Sāni kammāni tappenti, uṇhaṃvajjhohitaṃ mukhe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
Sīho ca sīhanādena, daddaraṃ abhinādayi;
```

```
Sutvā sīhassa nigghosaṃ, siṅgālo <note>sigālo (sī. syā. pī.)</note> daddare vasaṃ;
```

```
Bhīto santāsamāpādi, hadayañcassa apphalīti.
```

Siṅgālajātakaṃ <note>sigālajātakaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> dutiyaṃ.

#### 153. Sūkarajātakaṃ (2-1-3)

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
Catuppado <pb ed="T" n="1.0051" /> ahaṃ samma, tvampi samma catuppado;
```

```
Ehi samma <note>sīha (sī. pī.)</note> nivattassu, kiṃ nu bhīto palāyasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
Asuci <pb ed="V" n="1.0035" /> pūtilomosi, duggandho vāsi sūkara;
```

```
Sace yujjhitukāmosi, jayaṃ samma dadāmi teti.
```

Sūkarajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 154. Uragajātaka (2-1-4)

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
Idhūragānaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0037" /> pavaro paviṭṭho, selassa vaṇṇena pamokkhamicchaṃ;
```

```
Brahmañca vaṇṇaṃ <note>vakkaṃ (ka.)</note> apacāyamāno, bubhukkhito no vitarāmi <note>visahāmi (ka. si. syā. pī.)</note> bhottuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
So brahmagutto cirameva jīva, dibyā ca te pātubhavantu bhakkhā;
```

```
Yo brahmavaṇṇaṃ apacāyamāno, bubhukkhito no vitarāsi <note>sabbatthapi samānaṃ</note> bhottunti.
```

Uragajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 155. Bhaggajātakaṃ (2-1-5)

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
Jīva <pb ed="T" n="1.0052" /> vassasataṃ bhagga <note>gagga (sī. pī.)</note>, aparāni ca vīsatiṃ <note>vīsati (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Mā maṃ pisācā khādantu, jīva tvaṃ sarado sataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
Tvampi vassasataṃ jīva, aparāni ca vīsatiṃ;
```

```
Visaṃ pisācā khādantu, jīva tvaṃ sarado satanti.
```

Bhaggajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 156. Alīnacittajātakaṃ (2-1-6)

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
Alīnacittaṃ nissāya, pahaṭṭhā mahatī camū;
```

```
Kosalaṃ senāsantuṭṭhaṃ, jīvaggāhaṃ agāhayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
Evaṃ nissayasampanno, bhikkhu āraddhavīriyo;
```

```
Bhāvayaṃ kusalaṃ dhammaṃ, yogakkhemassa pattiyā;
```

```
Pāpuṇe anupubbena, sabbasaṃyojanakkhayanti.
```

Alīnacittajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 157. Guṇajātakaṃ (2-1-7)

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
Yena <pb ed="M" n="1.0038" /> kāmaṃ paṇāmeti, dhammo balavataṃ migī;
```

```
Unnadantī vijānāhi, jātaṃ saraṇato bhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
Api <pb ed="V" n="1.0036" /> cepi dubbalo mitto, mittadhammesu tiṭṭhati;
```

```
So ñātako ca bandhu ca, so mitto so ca me sakhā;
```

```
Dāṭhini <pb ed="T" n="1.0053" /> mātimaññittho <note>maññivo (syā.), maññavho (ka.)</note>, siṅgālo mama pāṇadoti.
```

Guṇajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 158. Suhanujātakaṃ (2-1-8)

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
Nayidaṃ visamasīlena, soṇena suhanū saha;
```

```
Suhanūpi tādisoyeva, yo soṇassa sagocaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
Pakkhandinā pagabbhena, niccaṃ sandānakhādinā;
```

```
Sameti pāpaṃ pāpena, sameti asatā asanti.
```

Suhanujātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 159. Morajātakaṃ (2-1-9)

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
Udetayaṃ cakkhumā ekarājā, harissavaṇṇo pathavippabhāso <note>paṭhavippabhāso (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Taṃ taṃ namassāmi harissavaṇṇaṃ pathavippabhāsaṃ, tayājja guttā viharemu divasaṃ.
```

```
Ye brāhmaṇā vedagū sabbadhamme, te me namo te ca maṃ pālayantu;
```

```
Namatthu buddhānaṃ <note>buddhāna (?)</note> namatthu bodhiyā, namo vimuttānaṃ <note>vimuttāna (?)</note> namo vimuttiyā;
```

```
Imaṃ so parittaṃ katvā, moro carati esanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
Apetayaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0054" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0039" /> cakkhumā ekarājā, harissavaṇṇo pathavippabhāso;
```

```
Taṃ taṃ nammassāmi harissavaṇṇaṃ pathavippabhāsaṃ, tayājja guttā viharemu rattiṃ.
```

```
Ye brāhmaṇā vedagū sabbadhamme, te me namo te ca maṃ pālayantu;
```

```
Namatthu buddhānaṃ namatthu bodhiyā, namo vimuttānaṃ namo vimuttiyā;
```

```
Imaṃ so parittaṃ katvā, moro vāsamakappayīti.
```

Morajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 160. Vinīlajātakaṃ (2-1-10)

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
Evameva nūna <note>nu (ka.)</note> rājānaṃ, vedehaṃ mithilaggahaṃ;
```

```
Assā vahanti ājaññā, yathā haṃsā vinīlakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
Vinīla <pb ed="V" n="1.0037" /> duggaṃ bhajasi, abhūmiṃ tāta sevasi;
```

```
Gāmantakāni <note>gāmantikāni (sī.), gāmantarāni (ka.)</note> sevassu, etaṃ mātālayaṃ tavāti.
```

Vinīlajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Daḷhavaggo paṭhamo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Varaballika <pb ed="T" n="1.0055" /> daddara sūkarako, uragūttama pañcamabhaggavaro;
```

```
Mahatīcamu yāva siṅgālavaro, suhanuttama mora vinīlaṃ dasāti.
```

#### 2. Santhavavaggo

#### 161. Indasamānagottajātakaṃ (2-2-1)

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="M" n="1.0040" /> santhavaṃ <note>sandhavaṃ (ka.)</note> kāpurisena kayirā, ariyo anariyena pajānamatthaṃ;
```

```
Cirānuvutthopi karoti pāpaṃ, gajo yathā indasamānagottaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
Yaṃ tveva jaññā sadiso mamanti, sīlena paññāya sutena cāpi;
```

```
Teneva mettiṃ kayirātha saddhiṃ, sukho have sappurisena saṅgamoti.
```

Indasamānagottajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 162. Santhavajātakaṃ (2-2-2)

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="T" n="1.0056" /> santhavasmā paramatthi pāpiyo, yo santhavo <note>sandhavo (ka.)</note> kāpurisena hoti;
```

```
Santappito sappinā pāyasena <note>pāyāsena (ka.)</note>, kicchākataṃ paṇṇakuṭiṃ adayhi <note>adaḍḍhahi (sī. syā.), adaṭṭhahi (pī.), adaddahi (?)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
Na santhavasmā paramatthi seyyo, yo santhavo sappurisena hoti;
```

```
Sīhassa byagghassa ca dīpino ca, sāmā mukhaṃ lehati santhavenāti.
```

Santhavajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 163. Susīmajātakaṃ (2-2-3)

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
Kāḷā migā setadantā tavīme <note>tava ime (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, parosataṃ hemajālābhichannā <note>hemajālābhisañchannā (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Te te dadāmīti susīma brūsi, anussaraṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0057" /> pettipitāmahānaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
Kāḷā <pb ed="V" n="1.0038" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0041" /> migā setadantā mamīme <note>mama ime (sī. pī.)</note>, parosataṃ hemajālābhicchannā;
```

```
Te te dadāmīti vadāmi māṇava, anussaraṃ pettipitāmahānanti.
```

Susīmajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 164. Gijjhajātakaṃ (2-2-4)

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
Yaṃ nu gijjho yojanasataṃ, kuṇapāni avekkhati;
```

```
Kasmā jālañca pāsañca, āsajjāpi na bujjhasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
Yadā parābhavo hoti, poso jīvitasaṅkhaye;
```

```
Atha jālañca pāsañca, āsajjāpi na bujjhatīti.
```

Gijjhajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 165. Nakulajātakaṃ (2-2-5)

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
Sandhiṃ katvā amittena, aṇḍajena jalābuja;
```

```
Vivariya dāṭhaṃ sesi <note>sayasi (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, kuto te bhayamāgataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
Saṅketheva <note>saṅkateva (ka.)</note> amittasmiṃ, mittasmimpi na vissase;
```

```
Abhayā bhayamuppannaṃ, api mūlāni kantatīti <note>mūlaṃ nikantatīti (sī.)</note>.
```

Nakulajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 166. Upasāḷakajātakaṃ (2-2-6)

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
Upasāḷakanāmāni <note>upasāḷhakanāmānaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, sahassāni catuddasa;
```

```
Asmiṃ padese daḍḍhāni, natthi loke anāmataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
Yamhi <pb ed="T" n="1.0058" /> saccañca dhammo ca, ahiṃsā saṃyamo damo;
```

```
Etaṃ ariyā sevanti, etaṃ loke anāmatanti.
```

Upasāḷakajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 167. Samiddhijātakaṃ (2-2-7)

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
Abhutvā <pb ed="M" n="1.0042" /> bhikkhasi bhikkhu, na hi bhutvāna bhikkhasi;
```

```
Bhutvāna bhikkhu bhikkhassu, mā taṃ kālo upaccagā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
Kālaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0039" /> vohaṃ na jānāmi, channo kālo na dissati;
```

```
Tasmā abhutvā bhikkhāmi, mā maṃ kālo upaccagāti.
```

Samiddhijātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 168. Sakuṇagghijātakaṃ (2-2-8)

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
Seno balasā patamāno, lāpaṃ gocaraṭhāyinaṃ;
```

```
Sahasā ajjhappattova, maraṇaṃ tenupāgami.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
Sohaṃ nayena sampanno, pettike gocare rato;
```

```
Apetasattu modāmi, sampassaṃ atthamattanoti.
```

Sakuṇagghijātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 169. Arakajātakaṃ (2-2-9)

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
Yo ve mettena cittena, sabbalokānukampati;
```

```
Uddhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0059" /> adho ca tiriyaṃ, appamāṇena sabbaso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
Appamāṇaṃ hitaṃ cittaṃ, paripuṇṇaṃ subhāvitaṃ;
```

```
Yaṃ pamāṇakataṃ kammaṃ, na taṃ tatrāvasissatīti.
```

Arakajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 170. Kakaṇṭakajātakaṃ (2-2-10)

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
Nāyaṃ pure uṇṇamati <note>unnamati (syā.)</note>, toraṇagge kakaṇṭako;
```

```
Mahosadha vijānāhi, kena thaddho kakaṇṭako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
Aladdhapubbaṃ laddhāna, aḍḍhamāsaṃ kakaṇṭako;
```

```
Atimaññati rājānaṃ, vedehaṃ mithilaggahanti.
```

Kakaṇṭakajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Santhavavaggo dutiyo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Atha <pb ed="M" n="1.0043" /> indasamāna sapaṇṇakuṭi, susimuttama gijjha jalābujako;
```

```
Upasāḷaka bhikkhu salāpavaro, atha mettavaro dasapuṇṇamatīti.
```

#### 3. Kalyāṇavaggo

#### 171. Kalyāṇadhammajātakaṃ (2-3-1)

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
Kalyāṇadhammoti <pb ed="T" n="1.0060" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0040" /> yadā janinda, loke samaññaṃ anupāpuṇāti;
```

```
Tasmā na hiyyetha <note>hīyetha (sī.)</note> naro sapañño, hiriyāpi santo dhuramādiyanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
Sāyaṃ samaññā idha majja pattā, kalyāṇadhammoti janinda loke;
```

```
Tāhaṃ samekkhaṃ idha pabbajissaṃ, na hi matthi chando idha kāmabhogeti.
```

Kalyāṇadhammajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 172. Daddarajātakaṃ (2-3-2)

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
Ko nu saddena mahatā, abhinādeti daddaraṃ;
```

```
Taṃ sīhā nappaṭinadanti <note>kiṃ sīhā nappaṭinadanti (sī. pī.), na sīhā paṭinadanti (ka.)</note>, ko nāmeso migādhibhū.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
Adhamo migajātānaṃ, siṅgālo tāta vassati;
```

```
Jātimassa jigucchantā, tuṇhī sīhā samacchareti.
```

Daddarajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 173. Makkaṭajātakaṃ (2-3-3)

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
Tāta <pb ed="T" n="1.0061" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0044" /> māṇavako eso, tālamūlaṃ apassito;
```

```
Agārakañcidaṃ atthi, handa demassagārakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
Mā kho tvaṃ tāta pakkosi, dūseyya no agārakaṃ;
```

```
Netādisaṃ mukhaṃ hoti, brāhmaṇassa susīlinoti.
```

Makkaṭajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 174. Dubbhiyamakkaṭajātakaṃ (2-3-4)

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
Adamha te vāri pahūtarūpaṃ, ghammābhitattassa pipāsitassa;
```

```
So dāni pitvāna <note>pītvāna (sī. pī.)</note> kiriṅkarosi <note>kikiṃkarosi (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, asaṅgamo pāpajanena seyyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
Ko te suto vā diṭṭho vā, sīlavā nāma makkaṭo;
```

```
Idāni kho taṃ ohacchaṃ <note>ūhacca (sī. pī.), ohaccaṃ (syā.), uhajjaṃ (ka.)</note>, esā asmāka dhammatāti.
```

Dubbhiyamakkaṭajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 175. Ādiccupaṭṭhānajātakaṃ (2-3-5)

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
Sabbesu <pb ed="V" n="1.0041" /> kira bhūtesu, santi sīlasamāhitā;
```

```
Passa sākhāmigaṃ jammaṃ, ādiccamupatiṭṭhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
Nāssa sīlaṃ vijānātha, anaññāya pasaṃsatha;
```

```
Aggihuttañca <pb ed="T" n="1.0062" /> uhannaṃ <note>ūhantaṃ (sī.), ūhanaṃ (syā.), ūhanti (pī.), uhadaṃ (ka.)</note>, dve ca bhinnā kamaṇḍalūti.
```

Ādiccupaṭṭhānajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 176. Kaḷāyamuṭṭhijātakaṃ (2-3-6)

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
Bālo <pb ed="M" n="1.0045" /> vatāyaṃ dumasākhagocaro, paññā janinda nayimassa vijjati;
```

```
Kaḷāyamuṭṭhiṃ <note>kalāyamuṭṭhiṃ (sī. pī.)</note> avakiriya kevalaṃ, ekaṃ kaḷāyaṃ patitaṃ gavesati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
Evameva mayaṃ rāja, ye caññe atilobhino;
```

```
Appena bahuṃ jiyyāma, kaḷāyeneva vānaroti.
```

Kaḷāyamuṭṭhijātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 177. Tindukajātakaṃ (2-3-7)

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
Dhanuhatthakalāpehi, nettiṃ savaradhāribhi;
```

```
Samantā parikiṇṇamha, kathaṃ mokkho bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
Appeva bahukiccānaṃ, attho jāyetha koci naṃ;
```

```
Atthi rukkhassa acchinnaṃ, khajjathaññeva tindukanti.
```

Tindukajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 178. Kacchapajātakaṃ (2-3-8)

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
Janittaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0063" /> me bhavittaṃ me, iti paṅke avassayiṃ;
```

```
Taṃ maṃ paṅko ajjhabhavi, yathā dubbalakaṃ tathā;
```

```
Taṃ taṃ vadāmi bhaggava, suṇohi vacanaṃ mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
Gāme vā yadi vā raññe, sukhaṃ yatrādhigacchati;
```

```
Taṃ janittaṃ bhavittañca, purisassa pajānato;
```

```
Yamhi jīve tamhi gacche, na niketahato siyāti.
```

Kacchapajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 179. Satadhammajātakaṃ (2-3-9)

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
Tañca <pb ed="V" n="1.0042" /> appañca ucchiṭṭhaṃ, tañca kicchena no adā;
```

```
Sohaṃ brāhmaṇajātiko, yaṃ bhuttaṃ tampi uggataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
Evaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0046" /> dhammaṃ niraṃkatvā <note>nirākatvā (?) ni + ā + kara + tvā</note>, yo adhammena jīvati;
```

```
Satadhammova lābhena, laddhenapi na nandatīti.
```

Satadhammajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 180. Duddadajātakaṃ (2-3-10)

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
Duddadaṃ dadamānānaṃ, dukkaraṃ kamma kubbataṃ;
```

```
Asanto nānukubbanti, sataṃ dhammo durannayo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
Tasmā satañca asataṃ, nānā hoti ito gati;
```

```
Asanto <pb ed="T" n="1.0064" /> nirayaṃ yanti, santo saggaparāyaṇāti <note>parāyanā (syā. ka.)</note>.
```

Duddadajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Kalyāṇavaggo tatiyo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Susamaññamigādhibhū māṇavako, vāripahūtarūpādiccupaṭṭhānā;
```

```
Sakaḷāyasatindukapaṅka puna, satadhamma sududdadakena dasāti.
```

#### 4. Asadisavaggo

#### 181. Asadisajātakaṃ (2-4-1)

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
Dhanuggaho asadiso, rājaputto mahabbalo;
```

```
Dūrepātī akkhaṇavedhī, mahākāyappadālano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
Sabbāmitte raṇaṃ katvā, na ca kañci viheṭhayi;
```

```
Bhātaraṃ sotthiṃ katvāna, saṃyamaṃ ajjhupāgamīti.
```

Asadisajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 182. Saṅgāmāvacarajātakaṃ (2-4-2)

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
Saṅgāmāvacaro <pb ed="V" n="1.0043" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0047" /> sūro, balavā iti vissuto;
```

```
Kiṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0065" /> nu toraṇamāsajja, paṭikkamasi kuñjara.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
Omadda khippaṃ palighaṃ, esikāni ca abbaha <note>ubbaha (syā.), abbhuha (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Toraṇāni ca madditvā, khippaṃ pavisa kuñjarāti.
```

Saṅgāmāvacarajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 183. Vālodakajātakaṃ (2-4-3)

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
Vālodakaṃ apparasaṃ nihīnaṃ, pitvā <note>pītvā (sī. pī.)</note> mado jāyati gadrabhānaṃ;
```

```
Imañca pitvāna rasaṃ paṇītaṃ, mado na sañjāyati sindhavānaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
Appaṃ pivitvāna nihīnajacco, so majjatī tena janinda puṭṭho <note>phuṭṭho (sī. syā.), muṭṭho (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Dhorayhasīlī ca kulamhi jāto, na majjatī aggarasaṃ pivitvāti.
```

Vālodakajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 184. Giridattajātakaṃ (2-4-4)

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
Dūsito giridattena <note>giridantena (pī.)</note>, hayo sāmassa paṇḍavo;
```

```
Porāṇaṃ pakatiṃ hitvā, tassevānuvidhiyyati <note>nuvidhīyati (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
Sace <pb ed="T" n="1.0066" /> ca tanujo poso, sikharākāra <note>siṅgārākāra (syā.)</note> kappito;
```

```
Ānane naṃ <note>taṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> gahetvāna, maṇḍale parivattaye;
```

```
Khippameva pahantvāna, tassevānuvidhiyyatīti.
```

Giridattajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 185. Anabhiratijātakaṃ (2-4-5)

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
Yathodake <pb ed="M" n="1.0048" /> āvile appasanne, na passati sippikasambukañca;
```

```
Sakkharaṃ vālukaṃ macchagumbaṃ, evaṃ āvilamhi <note>āvile hi (sī.)</note> citte;
```

```
Na passati attadatthaṃ paratthaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
Yathodake <pb ed="V" n="1.0044" /> acche vippasanne, so passati sippikasambukañca;
```

```
Sakkharaṃ vālukaṃ macchagumbaṃ, evaṃ anāvilamhi citte;
```

```
So passati attadatthaṃ paratthanti.
```

Anabhiratijātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 186. Dadhivāhanajātakaṃ (2-4-6)

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
Vaṇṇagandharasūpeto<pb ed="T" n="1.0067" />, amboyaṃ ahuvā pure;
```

```
Tameva pūjaṃ labhamāno, kenambo kaṭukapphalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
Pucimandaparivāro, ambo te dadhivāhana;
```

```
Mūlaṃ mūlena saṃsaṭṭhaṃ, sākhā sākhā <note>sākhaṃ (syā. ka.)</note> nisevare <note>nivīsare (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Asātasannivāsena, tenambo kaṭukapphaloti.
```

Dadhivāhanajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 187. Catumaṭṭhajātakaṃ (2-4-7)

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
Ucce viṭabhimāruyha, mantayavho rahogatā;
```

```
Nīce oruyha mantavho, migarājāpi sossati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
Yaṃ suvaṇṇo suvaṇṇena <note>yaṃ supaṇṇo supaṇṇena (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, devo devena mantaye;
```

```
Kiṃ tettha catumaṭṭhassa, bilaṃ pavisa jambukāti.
```

Catumaṭṭhajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 188. Sīhakotthujātakaṃ (2-4-8)

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
Sīhaṅgulī <pb ed="M" n="1.0049" /> sīhanakho, sīhapādapatiṭṭhito;
```

```
So sīho sīhasaṅghamhi, eko nadati aññathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
Mā <pb ed="T" n="1.0068" /> tvaṃ nadi rājaputta, appasaddo vane vasa;
```

```
Sarena kho <note>mā (ka.)</note> taṃ jāneyyuṃ, na hi te pettiko saroti.
```

Sīhakotthujātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 189. Sīhacammajātakaṃ (2-4-9)

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
Netaṃ sīhassa naditaṃ, na byagghassa na <note>byagghassa na ca (ka.)</note> dīpino;
```

```
Pāruto sīhacammena, jammo nadati gadrabho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
Cirampi <pb ed="V" n="1.0045" /> kho taṃ khādeyya, gadrabho haritaṃ yavaṃ;
```

```
Pāruto sīhacammena, ravamānova dūsayīti.
```

Sīhacammajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 190. Sīlānisaṃsajātakaṃ (2-4-10)

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
Passa saddhāya sīlassa, cāgassa ca ayaṃ phalaṃ;
```

```
Nāgo nāvāya vaṇṇena, saddhaṃ vahatupāsakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
Sabbhireva samāsetha, sabbhi kubbetha santhavaṃ;
```

```
Satañhi sannivāsena, sotthiṃ gacchati nhāpitoti.
```

Sīlānisaṃsajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Asadisavaggo catuttho.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Dhanuggaha <pb ed="T" n="1.0069" /> kuñjara apparaso, giridattamanāvilacittavaraṃ;
```

```
Dadhivāhana jambūka sīhanakho, haritayava nāgavarena dasāti.
```

#### 5. Ruhakavaggo

#### 191. Ruhakajātakaṃ (2-5-1)

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
Api <pb ed="M" n="1.0050" /> <note>ambho (syā. ka. sī.)</note> ruhaka chinnāpi, jiyā sandhīyate puna;
```

```
Sandhīyassu purāṇiyā, mā kodhassa vasaṃ gami.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
Vijjamānesu vākesu <note>vijjamānāsu maruvāsu (sī.), vijjamānāsu marūdvāsu (pī.)</note>, vijjamānesu kārisu;
```

```
Aññaṃ jiyaṃ karissāmi, alaññeva purāṇiyāti.
```

Ruhakajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 192. Sirikāḷakaṇṇijātakaṃ (2-5-2)

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
Itthī siyā rūpavatī, sā ca sīlavatī siyā;
```

```
Puriso taṃ na iccheyya, saddahāsi mahosadha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
Saddahāmi <pb ed="V" n="1.0046" /> mahārāja, puriso dubbhago siyā;
```

```
Sirī <pb ed="T" n="1.0070" /> ca kāḷakaṇṇī ca, na samenti kudācananti.
```

Sirikāḷakaṇṇijātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 193. Cūḷapadumajātakaṃ (2-5-3)

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
Ayameva sā ahamapi <note>ahampi (sī. syā. pī.), ahasmi (ka.)</note> so anañño, ayameva so hatthacchinno anañño;
```

```
Yamāha ‘‘komārapatī mama’’nti, vajjhitthiyo natthi itthīsu saccaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
Imañca jammaṃ musalena hantvā, luddaṃ chavaṃ paradārūpaseviṃ;
```

```
Imissā ca naṃ pāpapatibbatāya, jīvantiyā chindatha kaṇṇanāsanti.
```

Cūḷapadumajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 194. Maṇicorajātakaṃ (2-5-4)

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="M" n="1.0051" /> santi devā pavasanti nūna, na hi nūna santi idha lokapālā;
```

```
Sahasā karontānamasaññatānaṃ, na hi nūna santī paṭisedhitāro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
Akāle vassatī tassa, kāle tassa na vassati;
```

```
Saggā <pb ed="T" n="1.0071" /> ca cavati ṭhānā, nanu so tāvatā hatoti.
```

Maṇicorajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 195. Pabbatūpattharajātakaṃ (2-5-5)

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
Pabbatūpatthare <note>pabbatapatthare (sī. syā. pī.)</note> ramme, jātā pokkharaṇī sivā;
```

```
Taṃ siṅgālo apāpāyi <note>apāpāsi (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, jānaṃ sīhena rakkhitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
Pivanti ce <note>pivanti ve (sī.), pivantiva (pī.), pivanteva (?)</note> mahārāja, sāpadāni mahānadiṃ;
```

```
Na tena anadī hoti, khamassu yadi te piyāti.
```

Pabbatūpatthara <note>pabbatapatthara (sī. syā. pī.)</note> jātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 196. Valāhakassajātakaṃ (2-5-6)

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
Ye na kāhanti ovādaṃ, narā buddhena desitaṃ;
```

```
Byasanaṃ te gamissanti, rakkhasīhiva vāṇijā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
Ye <pb ed="V" n="1.0047" /> ca kāhanti ovādaṃ, narā buddhena desitaṃ;
```

```
Sotthiṃ pāraṃ gamissanti, valāheneva <note>vālāheneva (sī. pī.)</note> vāṇijāti.
```

Valāhakassa <note>vālāhassa (sī. pī.)</note> jātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 197. Mittāmittajātakaṃ (2-5-7)

<p rend="hangnum">§93.</p>

```
Na naṃ umhayate disvā, na ca naṃ paṭinandati;
```

```
Cakkhūni cassa na dadāti, paṭilomañca vattati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§94.</p>

```
Ete <pb ed="T" n="1.0072" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0052" /> bhavanti ākārā, amittasmiṃ patiṭṭhitā;
```

```
Yehi amittaṃ jāneyya, disvā sutvā ca paṇḍitoti.
```

Mittāmittajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 198. Rādhajātakaṃ (2-5-8)

<p rend="hangnum">§95.</p>

```
Pavāsā āgato tāta, idāni nacirāgato;
```

```
Kaccinnu tāta te mātā, na aññamupasevati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§96.</p>

```
Na kho panetaṃ subhaṇaṃ, giraṃ saccupasaṃhitaṃ;
```

```
Sayetha poṭṭhapādova, mummure <note>mummure (syā.), maṃ pure (ka.) mummurasaddo thusaggimhi kukkuḷe ca vattatīti sakkatābhidhānesu</note> upakūthitoti <note>upakūsitoti (sī. syā. pī.), upakūlito (ka.)</note>.
```

Rādhajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 199. Gahapatijātakaṃ (2-5-9)

<p rend="hangnum">§97.</p>

```
Ubhayaṃ me na khamati, ubhayaṃ me na ruccati;
```

```
Yācāyaṃ koṭṭhamotiṇṇā, nāddasaṃ iti bhāsati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§98.</p>

```
Taṃ taṃ gāmapati brūmi, kadare appasmi jīvite;
```

```
Dve māse saṅgaraṃ katvā <note>kāraṃ katvāna (sī. pī.), saṃkaraṃ katvā (ka.)</note>, maṃsaṃ jaraggavaṃ kisaṃ;
```

```
Appattakāle codesi, tampi mayhaṃ na ruccatīti.
```

Gahapatijātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 200. Sādhusīlajātakaṃ (2-5-10)

<p rend="hangnum">§99.</p>

```
Sarīradabyaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0073" /> vuḍḍhabyaṃ <note>vaddhabyaṃ (sī. pī.)</note>, sojaccaṃ sādhusīliyaṃ;
```

```
Brāhmaṇaṃ teva pucchāma, kannu tesaṃ vanimhase <note>vaṇimhase (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§100.</p>

```
Attho <pb ed="V" n="1.0048" /> atthi sarīrasmiṃ, vuḍḍhabyassa namo kare;
```

```
Attho atthi sujātasmiṃ, sīlaṃ asmāka ruccatīti.
```

Sādhusīlajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Ruhakavaggo pañcamo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Apiruhaka <pb ed="M" n="1.0053" /> rūpavatī musalo, pavasanti sapañcamapokkharaṇī;
```

```
Atha muttimavāṇija umhayate, ciraāgata koṭṭha sarīra dasāti.
```

#### 6. Nataṃdaḷhavaggo

#### 201. Bandhanāgārajātakaṃ (2-6-1)

<p rend="hangnum">§101.</p>

```
Na taṃ daḷhaṃ bandhanamāhu dhīrā, yadāyasaṃ dārujapabbajañca <note>babbajañca (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Sārattarattā maṇikuṇḍalesu, puttesu <pb ed="T" n="1.0074" /> dāresu ca yā apekkhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§102.</p>

```
Etaṃ daḷhaṃ bandhanamāhu dhīrā, ohārinaṃ sithilaṃ duppamuñcaṃ;
```

```
Etampi chetvāna vajanti dhīrā, anapekkhino kāmasukhaṃ pahāyāti.
```

Bandhanāgārajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 202. Keḷisīlajātakaṃ (2-6-2)

<p rend="hangnum">§103.</p>

```
Haṃsā koñcā mayūrā ca, hatthayo <note>hatthino (sī.), hatthiyo (syā. pī.)</note> pasadā migā;
```

```
Sabbe sīhassa bhāyanti, natthi kāyasmi tulyatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§104.</p>

```
Evameva manussesu, daharo cepi paññavā;
```

```
So hi tattha mahā hoti, neva bālo sarīravāti.
```

Keḷisīlajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 203. Khaṇḍajātakaṃ (2-6-3)

<p rend="hangnum">§105.</p>

```
Virūpakkhehi me mettaṃ, mettaṃ erāpathehi me;
```

```
Chabyāputtehi me mettaṃ, mettaṃ kaṇhāgotamakehi ca.
```

```
Apādakehi <pb ed="V" n="1.0049" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0054" /> me mettaṃ, mettaṃ dvipādakehi me;
```

```
Catuppadehi me mettaṃ, mettaṃ bahuppadehi me.
```

```
Mā <pb ed="T" n="1.0075" /> maṃ apādako hiṃsi, mā maṃ hiṃsi dvipādako;
```

```
Mā maṃ catuppado hiṃsi, mā maṃ hiṃsi bahuppado.
```

```
Sabbe sattā sabbe pāṇā, sabbe bhūtā ca kevalā;
```

```
Sabbe bhadrāni passantu, mā kañci <note>kiñci (syā. ka.)</note> pāpamāgamā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§106.</p>

```
Appamāṇo buddho, appamāṇo dhammo;
```

```
Appamāṇo saṅgho, pamāṇavantāni sarīsapāni <note>sirisapāni (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Ahivicchikasatapadī, uṇṇanābhi <note>uṇṇānābhi (sī. syā. pī.)</note> sarabūmūsikā.
```

```
Katā me rakkhā katā me parittā, paṭikkamantu bhūtāni;
```

```
Sohaṃ namo bhagavato, namo sattannaṃ sammāsambuddhānanti.
```

Khaṇḍajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 204. Vīrakajātakaṃ (2-6-4)

<p rend="hangnum">§107.</p>

```
Api vīraka passesi, sakuṇaṃ mañjubhāṇakaṃ;
```

```
Mayūragīvasaṅkāsaṃ, patiṃ mayhaṃ saviṭṭhakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§108.</p>

```
Udakathalacarassa pakkhino, niccaṃ āmakamacchabhojino;
```

```
Tassānukaraṃ saviṭṭhako, sevāle paliguṇṭhito matoti.
```

Vīrakajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 205. Gaṅgeyyajātakaṃ (2-6-5)

<p rend="hangnum">§109.</p>

```
Sobhati maccho gaṅgeyyo, atho sobhati yāmuno <note>sobhanti macchā gaṅgeyyā, atho sobhanti yāmunā (syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Catuppadoyaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0076" /> puriso, nigrodhaparimaṇḍalo;
```

```
Īsakāyata <note>īsamāyata (ka.)</note> gīvo ca, sabbeva atirocati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§110.</p>

```
Yaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0055" /> pucchito na taṃ akkhāsi <note>akkhā (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, aññaṃ akkhāsi <note>akkhāti (syā. pī.)</note> pucchito;
```

```
Attappasaṃsako poso, nāyaṃ asmāka ruccatīti.
```

Gaṅgeyyajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 206. Kuruṅgamigajātakaṃ (2-6-6)

<p rend="hangnum">§111.</p>

```
Iṅgha <pb ed="V" n="1.0050" /> vaddhamayaṃ <note>vaddhamayaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> pāsaṃ, chinda dantehi kacchapa;
```

```
Ahaṃ tathā karissāmi, yathā nehiti luddako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§112.</p>

```
Kacchapo pāvisī vāriṃ, kuruṅgo pāvisī vanaṃ;
```

```
Satapatto dumaggamhā, dūre putte apānayīti.
```

Kuruṅgamigajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 207. Assakajātakaṃ (2-6-7)

<p rend="hangnum">§113.</p>

```
Ayamassakarājena, deso vicarito mayā;
```

```
Anukāmaya kāmena <note>anukāmayavanukāmena (sī. pī.)</note>, piyena patinā saha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§114.</p>

```
Navena sukhadukkhena, porāṇaṃ apidhīyati <note>apithīyati (sī. pī.), apithiyyati (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Tasmā assakaraññāva, kīṭo piyataro mamāti.
```

Assakajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 208. Susumārajātakaṃ (2-6-8)

<p rend="hangnum">§115.</p>

```
Alaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0077" /> metehi ambehi, jambūhi panasehi ca;
```

```
Yāni pāraṃ samuddassa, varaṃ mayhaṃ udumbaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§116.</p>

```
Mahatī vata te bondi, na ca paññā tadūpikā;
```

```
Susumāra <note>suṃsumāra (sī. syā. pī.)</note> vañcito mesi, gaccha dāni yathāsukhanti.
```

Susumārajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 209. Kukkuṭajātakaṃ (2-6-9)

<p rend="hangnum">§117.</p>

```
Diṭṭhā <pb ed="M" n="1.0056" /> mayā vane rukkhā, assakaṇṇā vibhīṭakā <note>vibhedakā (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Na tāni evaṃ sakkanti, yathā tvaṃ rukkha sakkasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§118.</p>

```
Purāṇakukkuṭo <note>kakkaro (sī. syā. pī.)</note> ayaṃ, bhetvā pañjaramāgato;
```

```
Kusalo vāḷapāsānaṃ, apakkamati bhāsatīti.
```

Kukkuṭa <note>kakkara (sī. syā. pī.)</note> jātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 210. Kandagalakajātakaṃ (2-6-10)

<p rend="hangnum">§119.</p>

```
Ambho <pb ed="V" n="1.0051" /> ko nāma yaṃ rukkho, sinnapatto <note>sīnapatto (sī. pī.)</note> sakaṇṭako;
```

```
Yattha ekappahārena, uttamaṅgaṃ vibhijjitaṃ <note>visāṭikaṃ (sī. syā. pī.), vighāṭitaṃ (sī. niyya)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§120.</p>

```
Acāri vatāyaṃ vitudaṃ vanāni, kaṭṭhaṅgarukkhesu asārakesu;
```

```
Athāsadā <pb ed="T" n="1.0078" /> khadiraṃ jātasāraṃ <note>jātisāraṃ (ka.)</note>, yatthabbhidā garuḷo uttamaṅganti.
```

Kandagalaka <note>kandalaka (ka.)</note> jātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Nataṃdaḷhavaggo chaṭṭho.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Daḷhabandhana haṃsavaro ca puna, virūpakkha saviṭṭhaka macchavaro;
```

```
Sakuruṅga saassaka ambavaro, puna kukkuṭako garuḷena dasāti.
```

#### 7. Bīraṇathambhavaggo

#### 211. Somadattajātakaṃ (2-7-1)

<p rend="hangnum">§121.</p>

```
Akāsi yoggaṃ dhuvamappamatto, saṃvaccharaṃ bīraṇathambhakasmiṃ;
```

```
Byākāsi saññaṃ parisaṃ vigayha, na niyyamo tāyati appapaññaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§122.</p>

```
Dvayaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0057" /> yācanako tāta, somadatta nigacchati;
```

```
Alābhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0079" /> dhanalābhaṃ vā, evaṃ dhammā hi yācanāti.
```

Somadattajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 212. Ucchiṭṭhabhattajātakaṃ (2-7-2)

<p rend="hangnum">§123.</p>

```
Añño uparimo vaṇṇo, añño vaṇṇo ca heṭṭhimo;
```

```
Brāhmaṇī tveva pucchāmi, kiṃ heṭṭhā kiñca uppari.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§124.</p>

```
Ahaṃ naṭosmi bhaddante, bhikkhakosmi idhāgato;
```

```
Ayañhi koṭṭhamotiṇṇo, ayaṃ so yaṃ <note>tvaṃ (ka.)</note> gavesasīti.
```

Ucchiṭṭhabhattajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 213. Bharujātakaṃ (2-7-3)

<p rend="hangnum">§125.</p>

```
Isīnamantaraṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0052" /> katvā, bharurājāti <note>kururājāti (ka.)</note> me sutaṃ;
```

```
Ucchinno saha raṭṭhehi <note>raṭṭhena (sī. pī.)</note>, sarājā vibhavaṅgato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§126.</p>

```
Tasmā hi chandāgamanaṃ, nappasaṃsanti paṇḍitā;
```

```
Aduṭṭhacitto bhāseyya, giraṃ saccupasaṃhitanti.
```

Bharujātakaṃ <note>kururātakaṃ (ka.)</note> tatiyaṃ.

#### 214. Puṇṇanadījātakaṃ (2-7-4)

<p rend="hangnum">§127.</p>

```
Puṇṇaṃ nadiṃ yena ca peyyamāhu, jātaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0080" /> yavaṃ yena ca guyhamāhu;
```

```
Dūraṃ gataṃ yena ca avhayanti, so tyāgato <note>tyābhato (syā. ka.) paheḷigāthābhāvo manasi kātabbo</note> handa ca bhuñja brāhmaṇa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§128.</p>

```
Yato maṃ saratī rājā, vāyasampi pahetave;
```

```
Haṃsā koñcā mayūrā ca <note>haṃsakoñcamayūrānaṃ (ka. aṭṭha. pāṭhantaraṃ)</note>, asatīyeva pāpiyāti.
```

Puṇṇanadījātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 215. Kacchapajātakaṃ (2-7-5)

<p rend="hangnum">§129.</p>

```
Avadhī <pb ed="M" n="1.0058" /> vata attānaṃ, kacchapo byāharaṃ giraṃ <note>kacchapova pabyāharaṃ (syā.), kacchapo so pabyāharaṃ (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Suggahītasmiṃ kaṭṭhasmiṃ, vācāya sakiyāvadhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§130.</p>

```
Etampi disvā naravīriyaseṭṭha, vācaṃ pamuñce kusalaṃ nātivelaṃ;
```

```
Passasi bahubhāṇena, kacchapaṃ byasanaṃ gatanti.
```

Kacchapajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 216. Macchajātakaṃ (2-7-6)

<p rend="hangnum">§131.</p>

```
Na māyamaggi tapati, na sūlo sādhutacchito;
```

```
Yañca maṃ maññate macchī, aññaṃ so ratiyā gato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§132.</p>

```
So <pb ed="T" n="1.0081" /> maṃ dahati rāgaggi, cittaṃ cūpatapeti maṃ;
```

```
Jālino muñcathāyirā maṃ, na kāme haññate kvacīti.
```

Macchajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 217. Seggujātakaṃ (2-7-7)

<p rend="hangnum">§133.</p>

```
Sabbo <pb ed="V" n="1.0053" /> loko attamano ahosi, akovidā gāmadhammassa seggu;
```

```
Komāri ko nāma <note>komārikā nāma (ka.), komāriko nāma (syā. pī.)</note> tavajja dhammo, yaṃ tvaṃ gahitā pavane parodasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§134.</p>

```
Yo dukkhaphuṭṭhāya bhaveyya tāṇaṃ, so me pitā dubbhi vane karoti;
```

```
Sā kassa kandāmi vanassa majjhe, yo tāyitā so sahasaṃ karotīti.
```

Seggujātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 218. Kūṭavāṇijajātakaṃ (2-7-8)

<p rend="hangnum">§135.</p>

```
Saṭhassa <pb ed="M" n="1.0059" /> sāṭheyyamidaṃ sucintitaṃ, paccoḍḍitaṃ paṭikūṭassa kūṭaṃ;
```

```
Phālañce khādeyyuṃ <note>adeyyuṃ (sī. pī.)</note> mūsikā, kasmā kumāraṃ kulalā na <note>no (sī. syā. pī.)</note> hareyyuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§136.</p>

```
Kūṭassa <pb ed="T" n="1.0082" /> hi santi <note>santīdha (ka.)</note> kūṭakūṭā, bhavati <note>bhavanti (ka.)</note> cāpi nikatino nikatyā;
```

```
Dehi puttanaṭṭha phālanaṭṭhassa phālaṃ, mā te puttamahāsi phālanaṭṭhoti.
```

Kūṭavāṇijajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 219. Garahitajātakaṃ (2-7-9)

<p rend="hangnum">§137.</p>

```
Hiraññaṃ me suvaṇṇaṃ me, esā rattiṃ divā kathā;
```

```
Dummedhānaṃ manussānaṃ, ariyadhammaṃ apassataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§138.</p>

```
Dve dve gahapatayo gehe, eko tattha amassuko;
```

```
Lambatthano veṇikato, atho aṅkitakaṇṇako;
```

```
Kīto dhanena bahunā, so taṃ vitudate jananti.
```

Garahitajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 220. Dhammadhajajātakaṃ (2-7-10)

<p rend="hangnum">§139.</p>

```
Sukhaṃ jīvitarūposi, raṭṭhā vivanamāgato;
```

```
So ekako rukkhamūle <note>araññasmiṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, kapaṇo viya jhāyasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§140.</p>

```
Sukhaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0054" /> jīvitarūposmi, raṭṭhā vivanamāgato;
```

```
So ekako rukkhamūle, kapaṇo viya jhāyāmi;
```

```
Sataṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0083" /> dhammaṃ anussaraṃti.
```

Dhammadhajajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Bīraṇathambhavaggo sattamo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Atha <pb ed="M" n="1.0060" /> bīraṇathambhavaro ca naṭo, bharurājavaruttamapuṇṇanadī;
```

```
Bahubhāṇi aggipavane mūsikā, sahalambatthano kapaṇena dasāti.
```

#### 8. Kāsāvavaggo

#### 221. Kāsāvajātakaṃ (2-8-1)

<p rend="hangnum">§141.</p>

```
Anikkasāvo kāsāvaṃ, yo vatthaṃ paridahissati <note>paridahessati (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Apeto damasaccena, na so kāsāvamarahati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§142.</p>

```
Yo ca vantakasāvassa, sīlesu susamāhito;
```

```
Upeto damasaccena, sa ve kāsāvamarahatīti.
```

Kāsāvajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 222. Cūḷanandiyajātakaṃ (2-8-2)

<p rend="hangnum">§143.</p>

```
Idaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0084" /> tadācariyavaco, pārāsariyo yadabravi <note>porāṇācariyobravi (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Māsu tvaṃ akari <note>akarā (sī. pī.)</note> pāpaṃ, yaṃ tvaṃ pacchā kataṃ tape.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§144.</p>

```
Yāni karoti puriso, tāni attani passati;
```

```
Kalyāṇakārī kalyāṇaṃ, pāpakārī ca pāpakaṃ;
```

```
Yādisaṃ vapate bījaṃ, tādisaṃ harate phalanti.
```

Cūḷanandiyajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 223. Puṭabhattajātakaṃ (2-8-3)

<p rend="hangnum">§145.</p>

```
Name <pb ed="V" n="1.0055" /> namantassa bhaje bhajantaṃ, kiccānukubbassa kareyya kiccaṃ;
```

```
Nānatthakāmassa kareyya atthaṃ, asambhajantampi na sambhajeyya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§146.</p>

```
Caje <pb ed="M" n="1.0061" /> cajantaṃ vanathaṃ na kayirā, apetacittena na sambhajeyya;
```

```
Dijo dumaṃ khīṇaphalanti ñatvā, aññaṃ samekkheyya mahā hi lokoti.
```

Puṭabhattajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 224. Kumbhilajātakaṃ (2-8-4)

<p rend="hangnum">§147.</p>

```
Yassete <pb ed="T" n="1.0085" /> caturo dhammā, vānarinda yathā tava;
```

```
Saccaṃ dhammo dhiti cāgo, diṭṭhaṃ so ativattati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§148.</p>

```
Yassa cete na vijjanti, guṇā paramabhaddakā;
```

```
Saccaṃ dhammo dhiti cāgo, diṭṭhaṃ so nātivattatīti.
```

Kumbhilajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 225. Khantivaṇṇajātakaṃ (2-8-5)

<p rend="hangnum">§149.</p>

```
Atthi me puriso deva, sabbakiccesu byāvaṭo <note>vāvaṭo (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Tassa cekoparādhatthi, tattha tvaṃ kinti maññasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§150.</p>

```
Amhākampatthi puriso, ediso idha vijjati;
```

```
Dullabho aṅgasampanno, khantirasmāka ruccatīti.
```

Khantivaṇṇajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 226. Kosiyajātakaṃ (2-8-6)

<p rend="hangnum">§151.</p>

```
Kāle nikkhamanā sādhu, nākāle sādhu nikkhamo;
```

```
Akālena hi nikkhamma, ekakampi bahujjano;
```

```
Na kiñci atthaṃ joteti, dhaṅkasenāva kosiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§152.</p>

```
Dhīro ca vidhividhānaññū, paresaṃ vivarānugū;
```

```
Sabbāmitte <pb ed="T" n="1.0086" /> vasīkatvā, kosiyova sukhī siyāti.
```

Kosiyajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 227. Gūthapāṇajātakaṃ (2-8-7)

<p rend="hangnum">§153.</p>

```
Sūro <pb ed="V" n="1.0056" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0062" /> sūrena saṅgamma, vikkantena pahārinā;
```

```
Ehi nāga nivattassu, kiṃ nu bhīto palāyasi;
```

```
Passantu aṅgamagadhā, mama tuyhañca vikkamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§154.</p>

```
Na taṃ pādā vadhissāmi, na dantehi na soṇḍiyā;
```

```
Mīḷhena taṃ vadhissāmi, pūti haññatu pūtināti.
```

Gūthapāṇajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 228. Kāmanītajātakaṃ (2-8-8)

<p rend="hangnum">§155.</p>

```
Tayo giriṃ antaraṃ kāmayāmi, pañcālā kuruyo kekake ca <note>kurayo kekaye ca (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Tatuttariṃ <note>taduttariṃ (ka.)</note> brāhmaṇa kāmayāmi, tikiccha maṃ brāhmaṇa kāmanītaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§156.</p>

```
Kaṇhāhidaṭṭhassa karonti heke, amanussapaviṭṭhassa <note>amanussavaddhassa (sī. pī.), amanussaviṭṭhassa (syā.)</note> karonti paṇḍitā;
```

```
Na kāmanītassa karoti koci, okkantasukkassa <pb ed="T" n="1.0087" /> hi kā tikicchāti.
```

Kāmanītajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 229. Palāyitajātakaṃ (2-8-9)

<p rend="hangnum">§157.</p>

```
Gajaggameghehi hayaggamālibhi, rathūmijātehi sarābhivassebhi <note>sarābhivassabhi (syā. sī. aṭṭha.), sarābhivassibhi (?)</note>;
```

```
Tharuggahāvaṭṭa <note>dhanuggahāvaṭṭa (ka.)</note> daḷhappahāribhi, parivāritā takkasilā samantato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§158.</p>

```
<note>abhidhāvathā ca patathā ca, vividhavinaditā ca dantibhi; vattatajja tumulo ghoso, yathā vijjutā jaladharassa gajjatoti; (sī. pī. ka.)</note> Abhidhāvatha <pb ed="M" n="1.0063" /> cūpadhāvatha ca <note>abhidhāvathā cuppatathā ca (syā.)</note>, vividhā vināditā <note>vināditattha (ka.)</note> vadantibhi;
```

```
Vattatajja tumulo ghoso yathā, vijjulatā jaladharassa gajjatoti <note>abhidhāvathā ca patathā ca, vividhavinaditā ca dantibhi; vattatajja tumulo ghoso, yathā vijjutā jaladharassa gajjatoti; (sī. pī. ka.)</note>.
```

Palāyitajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 230. Dutiyapalāyitajātakaṃ (2-8-10)

<p rend="hangnum">§159.</p>

```
Dhajamaparimitaṃ anantapāraṃ, duppasahaṃdhaṅkehi sāgaraṃva <note>sāgaramiva (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Girimivaanilena duppasayho <note>duppasaho (sī. pī. ka.)</note>, duppasaho ahamajjatādisena.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§160.</p>

```
Mā <pb ed="T" n="1.0088" /> bāliyaṃ vilapi <note>vippalapi (bahūsu)</note> na hissa tādisaṃ, viḍayhase <note>viḷayhase (sī. pī.)</note> na hi labhase nisedhakaṃ;
```

```
Āsajjasi gajamiva ekacārinaṃ, yo taṃ padā naḷamiva pothayissatīti.
```

Dutiyapalāyitajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Kāsāvavaggo aṭṭhamo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

