Varavatthavaco <pb ed="V" n="1.0057" /> dumakhīṇaphalaṃ, caturodhammavaraṃ purisuttama;
```

```
Dhaṅkamagadhā ca tayogirināma, gajaggavaro dhajavarena dasāti.
```

#### 9. Upāhanavaggo

#### 231. Upāhanajātakaṃ (2-9-1)

<p rend="hangnum">§161.</p>

```
Yathāpi <pb ed="M" n="1.0064" /> kītā purisassupāhanā, sukhassa atthāya dukhaṃ udabbahe;
```

```
Ghammābhitattā thalasā papīḷitā, tasseva pāde purisassa khādare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§162.</p>

```
Evameva <pb ed="T" n="1.0089" /> yo dukkulīno anariyo, tammāka <note>tamhāka (sī.), tumhāka (syā. pī.)</note> vijjañca sutañca ādiya;
```

```
Tameva so tattha sutena khādati, anariyo vuccati dupāhanūpamoti <note>pānadūpamoti (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

Upāhanajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 232. Vīṇāguṇajātakaṃ (2-9-2)

<p rend="hangnum">§163.</p>

```
Ekacintito yamattho, bālo apariṇāyako;
```

```
Na hi khujjena vāmena, bhoti saṅgantumarahasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§164.</p>

```
Purisūsabhaṃ maññamānā, ahaṃ khujjamakāmayiṃ;
```

```
Soyaṃ saṃkuṭito seti, chinnatanti yathā viṇāti <note>thuṇāti (sī.)</note>.
```

Vīṇāguṇajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 233. Vikaṇṇajātakaṃ (2-9-3)

<p rend="hangnum">§165.</p>

```
Kāmaṃ yahiṃ icchasi tena gaccha, viddhosi mammamhi <note>mamasmi (ka.)</note> vikaṇṇakena;
```

```
Hatosi bhattena suvāditena <note>savāditena (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, lolo ca macche anubandhamāno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§166.</p>

```
Evampi <pb ed="M" n="1.0065" /> lokāmisaṃ opatanto, vihaññatī <pb ed="T" n="1.0090" /> cittavasānuvattī;
```

```
So haññati ñātisakhāna majjhe, macchānugo soriva suṃsumāroti <note>susumāro (ka.)</note>.
```

Vikaṇṇajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 234. Asitābhūjātakaṃ (2-9-4)

<p rend="hangnum">§167.</p>

```
Tvameva <pb ed="V" n="1.0058" /> dānimakara <note>makari (syā.), makarā (ka. sī.)</note>, yaṃ kāmo byagamā tayi;
```

```
Soyaṃ appaṭisandhiko, kharachinnaṃva renukaṃ <note>rerukaṃ (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§168.</p>

```
Atricchaṃ <note>atricchā (sī. syā. pī.)</note> atilobhena, atilobhamadena ca;
```

```
Evaṃ hāyati atthamhā, ahaṃva asitābhuyāti.
```

Asitābhūjātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 235. Vacchanakhajātakaṃ (2-9-5)

<p rend="hangnum">§169.</p>

```
Sukhā gharā vacchanakha, sahiraññā sabhojanā;
```

```
Yattha bhutvā pivitvā ca, sayeyyātha anussuko.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§170.</p>

```
Gharā nānīhamānassa, gharā nābhaṇato musā;
```

```
Gharā nādinnadaṇḍassa, paresaṃ anikubbato <note>anikrubbato (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Evaṃ chiddaṃ durabhisambhavaṃ <note>durabhibhavaṃ (sī. pī.)</note>, ko gharaṃ paṭipajjatīti.
```

Vacchanakhajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 236. Bakajātakaṃ (2-9-6)

<p rend="hangnum">§171.</p>

```
Bhaddako <pb ed="T" n="1.0091" /> vatayaṃ pakkhī, dijo kumudasannibho;
```

```
Vūpasantehi pakkhehi, mandamandova jhāyati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§172.</p>

```
Nāssa sīlaṃ vijānātha, anaññāya pasaṃsatha;
```

```
Amhe dijo na pāleti, tena pakkhī na phandatīti.
```

Bakajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 237. Sāketajātakaṃ (2-9-7)

<p rend="hangnum">§173.</p>

```
Ko <pb ed="M" n="1.0066" /> nu kho bhagavā hetu, ekacce idha puggale;
```

```
Atīva hadayaṃ nibbāti, cittañcāpi pasīdati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§174.</p>

```
Pubbeva sannivāsena, paccuppannahitena vā;
```

```
Evaṃ taṃ jāyate pemaṃ, uppalaṃva yathodaketi.
```

Sāketajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 238. Ekapadajātakaṃ (2-9-8)

<p rend="hangnum">§175.</p>

```
Iṅgha <pb ed="V" n="1.0059" /> ekapadaṃ tāta, anekatthapadassitaṃ <note>padanissitaṃ (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Kiñci saṅgāhikaṃ brūsi, yenatthe sādhayemase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§176.</p>

```
Dakkheyyekapadaṃ tāta, anekatthapadassitaṃ;
```

```
Tañca sīlena saññuttaṃ, khantiyā upapāditaṃ;
```

```
Alaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0092" /> mitte sukhāpetuṃ, amittānaṃ dukhāya cāti.
```

Ekapadajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 239. Haritamaṇḍūkajātakaṃ (2-9-9)

<p rend="hangnum">§177.</p>

```
Āsīvisampi maṃ <note>āsīvisaṃ mamaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> santaṃ, paviṭṭhaṃ kumināmukhaṃ;
```

```
Ruccate haritāmātā, yaṃ maṃ khādanti macchakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§178.</p>

```
Vilumpateva puriso, yāvassa upakappati;
```

```
Yadā caññe vilumpanti, so vilutto vilumpatīti <note>viluppatīti (?)</note>.
```

Haritamaṇḍūkajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 240. Mahāpiṅgalajātakaṃ (2-9-10)

<p rend="hangnum">§179.</p>

```
Sabbo jano hiṃsito piṅgalena, tasmiṃ mate paccayā <note>paccayaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> vedayanti;
```

```
Piyo nu te āsi akaṇhanetto, kasmā nu tvaṃ rodasi dvārapāla.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§180.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="M" n="1.0067" /> me piyo āsi akaṇhanetto, bhāyāmi paccāgamanāya tassa;
```

```
Ito gato hiṃseyya maccurājaṃ, so hiṃsito āneyya puna idha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§181.</p>

```
Daḍḍho vāhasahassehi, sitto ghaṭasatehi so;
```

```
Parikkhatā <pb ed="T" n="1.0093" /> ca sā bhūmi, mā bhāyi nāgamissatīti.
```

Mahāpiṅgalajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Upāhanavaggo navamo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Varupāhana khujja vikaṇṇakako, asitābhuya pañcamavacchanakho;
```

```
Dija pemavaruttamaekapadaṃ, kumināmukha piṅgalakena dasāti.
```

#### 10. Siṅgālavaggo

#### 241. Sabbadāṭhijātakaṃ (2-10-1)

<p rend="hangnum">§182.</p>

```
Siṅgālo <pb ed="V" n="1.0060" /> mānathaddho ca, parivārena atthiko;
```

```
Pāpuṇi mahatiṃ bhūmiṃ, rājāsi sabbadāṭhinaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§183.</p>

```
Evameva manussesu, yo hoti parivāravā;
```

```
So hi tattha mahā hoti, siṅgālo viya dāṭhinanti.
```

Sabbadāṭhijātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 242. Sunakhajātakaṃ (2-10-2)

<p rend="hangnum">§184.</p>

```
Bālo <pb ed="T" n="1.0094" /> vatāyaṃ sunakho, yo varattaṃ <note>yo ca yottaṃ (ka.)</note> na khādati;
```

```
Bandhanā ca pamuñceyya, asito ca gharaṃ vaje.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§185.</p>

```
Aṭṭhitaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0068" /> me manasmiṃ me, atho me hadaye kataṃ;
```

```
Kālañca paṭikaṅkhāmi, yāva passupatū jano <note>pasupatujjano (syā. ka.)</note>.
```

Sunakhajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 243. Guttilajātakaṃ (2-10-3)

<p rend="hangnum">§186.</p>

```
Sattatantiṃ sumadhuraṃ, rāmaṇeyyaṃ avācayiṃ;
```

```
So maṃ raṅgamhi avheti, saraṇaṃ me hohi kosiya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§187.</p>

```
Ahaṃ taṃ saraṇaṃ samma <note>ahaṃ te saraṇaṃ homi (vi. va. 328)</note>, ahamācariyapūjako;
```

```
Na taṃ jayissati sisso, sissamācariya jessasīti.
```

Guttilajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 244. Vigaticchajātakaṃ (2-10-4)

<p rend="hangnum">§188.</p>

```
Yaṃ passati na taṃ icchati, yañca na passati taṃ kiricchati;
```

```
Maññāmi ciraṃ carissati, na hi taṃ lacchati yaṃ sa icchati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§189.</p>

```
Yaṃ labhati na tena tussati, yañca pattheti laddhaṃ hīḷeti;
```

```
Icchā hi anantagocarā, vigaticchāna <note>vīticchānaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> namo karomaseti.
```

Vigaticcha <note>vīticcha (sī. pī.)</note> jātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 245. Mūlapariyāyajātakaṃ (2-10-5)

<p rend="hangnum">§190.</p>

```
Kālo <pb ed="T" n="1.0095" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0061" /> ghasati bhūtāni, sabbāneva sahattanā;
```

```
Yo ca kālaghaso bhūto, sa bhūtapacaniṃ paci.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§191.</p>

```
Bahūni narasīsāni, lomasāni brahāni ca;
```

```
Gīvāsu paṭimukkāni, kocidevettha kaṇṇavāti.
```

Mūlapariyāyajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 246. Bālovādajātakaṃ (2-10-6)

<p rend="hangnum">§192.</p>

```
Hantvā chetvā <note>jhatvā (sī. pī.), ghatvā (syā.)</note> vadhitvā ca, deti dānaṃ asaññato;
```

```
Edisaṃ bhattaṃ bhuñjamāno, sa pāpamupalimpati <note>sa pāpena upalippati (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§193.</p>

```
Puttadārampi <pb ed="M" n="1.0069" /> ce hantvā, deti dānaṃ asaññato;
```

```
Bhuñjamānopi sappañño, na pāpamupalimpatīti.
```

Bālovādajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 247. Pādañjalījātakaṃ (2-10-7)

<p rend="hangnum">§194.</p>

```
Addhā pādañjalī sabbe, paññāya atirocati;
```

```
Tathā hi oṭṭhaṃ bhañjati, uttariṃ nūna passati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§195.</p>

```
Nāyaṃ dhammaṃ adhammaṃ vā, atthānatthañca bujjhati;
```

```
Aññatra <pb ed="T" n="1.0096" /> oṭṭhanibbhogā, nāyaṃ jānāti kiñcananti.
```

Pādañjalījātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 248. Kiṃsukopamajātakaṃ (2-10-8)

<p rend="hangnum">§196.</p>

```
Sabbehi kiṃsuko diṭṭho, kiṃnvettha vicikicchatha;
```

```
Na hi sabbesu ṭhānesu, sārathī paripucchito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§197.</p>

```
Evaṃ sabbehi ñāṇehi, yesaṃ dhammā ajānitā;
```

```
Te ve dhammesu kaṅkhanti, kiṃsukasmiṃva bhātaroti.
```

Kiṃsukopamajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 249. Sālakajātakaṃ (2-10-9)

<p rend="hangnum">§198.</p>

```
Ekaputtako <pb ed="V" n="1.0062" /> bhavissasi, tvañca no hessasi issaro kule;
```

```
Oroha dumasmā sālaka, ehi dāni gharakaṃ vajemase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§199.</p>

```
Nanu maṃ suhadayoti <note>nanu maṃ hadayeti (sī. pī.)</note> maññasi, yañca maṃ hanasi veḷuyaṭṭhiyā;
```

```
Pakkambavane ramāmase, gaccha tvaṃ gharakaṃ yathāsukhanti.
```

Sālakajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 250. Kapijātakaṃ (2-10-10)

<p rend="hangnum">§200.</p>

```
Ayaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0097" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0070" /> isī upasamasaṃyame rato, sa tiṭṭhati <note>santiṭṭhati (sī. pī.)</note> sisirabhayena aṭṭito;
```

```
Handa ayaṃ pavisatumaṃ agārakaṃ, vinetu sītaṃ darathañca kevalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§201.</p>

```
Nāyaṃ isī upasamasaṃyame rato, kapī ayaṃ dumavarasākhagocaro;
```

```
So dūsako rosako cāpi jammo, sacevajemampi <note>sace + āvaje + imampi</note> dūseyyagāranti <note>dūsaye gharanti (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

Kapijātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Siṅgālavaggo dasamo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Atha rājā siṅgālavaro sunakho, tathā kosiya icchati kālaghaso;
```

```
Atha dānavaroṭṭhapi sārathinā, punambavanañca sisirakapi dasāti.
```

Atha vagguddānaṃ –

```
Daḷhañca <pb ed="T" n="1.0098" /> vaggaṃ aparena santhavaṃ, kalyāṇavaggāsadiso ca rūhakaṃ;
```

```
Nataṃdaḷha bīraṇathambhakaṃ puna, kāsāvupāhana siṅgālakena dasāti.
```

<trailer rend="centre">Dukanipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.</trailer>

### 3. Tikanipāto

#### 1. Saṅkappavaggo

#### 251. Saṅkapparāgajātakaṃ (3-1-1)

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
Saṅkapparāgadhotena<pb ed="T" n="1.0099" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0063" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0071" />, vitakkanisitena ca;
```

```
Nālaṅkatena bhadrena <note>nevālaṅkatabhadrena (syā.)</note>, usukārākatena ca <note>na usukārakatena ca (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
Na kaṇṇāyatamuttena, nāpi morūpasevinā;
```

```
Tenamhi hadaye viddho, sabbaṅgaparidāhinā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
Āvedhañca na passāmi, yato ruhiramassave;
```

```
Yāva ayoniso cittaṃ, sayaṃ me dukkhamābhatanti.
```

Saṅkapparāgajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 252. Tilamuṭṭhijātakaṃ (3-1-2)

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
Ajjāpi me taṃ manasi <note>sarasi (ka.)</note>, yaṃ maṃ tvaṃ tilamuṭṭhiyā;
```

```
Bāhāya maṃ gahetvāna, laṭṭhiyā anutāḷayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
Nanu jīvite na ramasi, yenāsi brāhmaṇāgato;
```

```
Yaṃ maṃ bāhā gahetvāna, tikkhattuṃ anutāḷayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
Ariyo anariyaṃ kubbantaṃ <note>kubbānaṃ (sī. pī.), kubbaṃ (syā.)</note>, yo daṇḍena nisedhati;
```

```
Sāsanaṃ taṃ na taṃ veraṃ, iti naṃ paṇḍitā vidūti.
```

Tilamuṭṭhijātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 253. Maṇikaṇṭhajātakaṃ (3-1-3)

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
Mamannapānaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0100" /> vipulaṃ uḷāraṃ, uppajjatīmassa maṇissa hetu;
```

```
Taṃ te na dassaṃ atiyācakosi, na cāpi te assamamāgamissaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
Susū <pb ed="V" n="1.0064" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0072" /> yathā sakkharadhotapāṇī, tāsesi maṃ selaṃ yācamāno;
```

```
Taṃ te na dassaṃ atiyācakosi, na cāpi te assamamāgamissaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
Na taṃ yāce yassa piyaṃ jigīse <note>jigiṃse (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, desso hoti atiyācanāya;
```

```
Nāgo maṇiṃ yācito brāhmaṇena, adassanaṃyeva tadajjhagamāti.
```

Maṇikaṇṭhajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 254. Kuṇḍakakucchisindhavajātakaṃ (3-1-4)

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
Bhutvā tiṇaparighāsaṃ, bhutvā ācāmakuṇḍakaṃ;
```

```
Etaṃ te bhojanaṃ āsi, kasmā dāni na bhuñjasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
Yattha posaṃ na jānanti, jātiyā vinayena vā;
```

```
Bahuṃ <note>pahū (sī. pī.), pahuṃ (syā. ka.)</note> tattha mahābramhe, api ācāmakuṇḍakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
Tvañca <pb ed="T" n="1.0101" /> kho maṃ pajānāsi, yādisāyaṃ hayuttamo;
```

```
Jānanto jānamāgamma, na te bhakkhāmi kuṇḍakanti.
```

Kuṇḍakakucchisindhavajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 255. Sukajātakaṃ (3-1-5)

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
Yāva so mattamaññāsi, bhojanasmiṃ vihaṅgamo;
```

```
Tāva addhānamāpādi, mātarañca aposayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
Yato ca kho bahutaraṃ, bhojanaṃ ajjhavāhari <note>ajjhupāhari (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Tato tattheva saṃsīdi, amattaññū hi so ahu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
Tasmā mattaññutā sādhu, bhojanasmiṃ agiddhatā <note>agiddhitā (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Amattaññū hi sīdanti, mattaññū ca na sīdareti.
```

Sukajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 256. Jarūdapānajātakaṃ (3-1-6)

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
Jarūdapānaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0073" /> khaṇamānā, vāṇijā udakatthikā;
```

```
Ajjhagamuṃ ayasaṃ lohaṃ <note>ajjhagaṃsu ayolohaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, tipusīsañca vāṇijā;
```

```
Rajataṃ jātarūpañca, muttā veḷūriyā bahū.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
Te ca tena asantuṭṭhā, bhiyyo bhiyyo akhāṇisuṃ;
```

```
Te tatthāsīviso <note>tattha āsīviso (ka.), tatthapāsīviso (syā.)</note> ghoro, tejassī tejasā hani.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
Tasmā <pb ed="T" n="1.0102" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0065" /> khaṇe nātikhaṇe, atikhātaṃ <note>atikhaṇaṃ (ka.)</note> hi pāpakaṃ;
```

```
Khātena ca <note>khaṇena ca (ka.), khaṇanena (syā.)</note> dhanaṃ laddhaṃ, atikhātena <note>atikhaṇena (ka.)</note> nāsitanti.
```

Jarūdapānajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 257. Gāmaṇicandajātakaṃ (3-1-7)

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
Nāyaṃ gharānaṃ kusalo, lolo ayaṃ valīmukho;
```

```
Kataṃ kataṃ kho dūseyya, evaṃdhammamidaṃ kulaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
Nayidaṃ cittavato lomaṃ, nāyaṃ assāsiko migo;
```

```
Siṭṭhaṃ <note>satthaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> me janasandhena, nāyaṃ kiñci vijānati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
Na mātaraṃ pitaraṃ vā, bhātaraṃ bhaginiṃ sakaṃ;
```

```
Bhareyya tādiso poso, siṭṭhaṃ dasarathena meti.
```

Gāmaṇicanda <note>gāmaṇicaṇḍa (sī. pī.)</note> jātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 258. Mandhātujātakaṃ (3-1-8)

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
Yāvatā candimasūriyā, pariharanti disā bhanti virocanā <note>virocamānā (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Sabbeva dāsā mandhātu, ye pāṇā pathavissitā <note>paṭhavinissitā (sī. pī.), paṭhavissitā (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
Na kahāpaṇavassena, titti kāmesu vijjati;
```

```
Appassādā dukhā kāmā, iti viññāya paṇḍito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
Api <pb ed="M" n="1.0074" /> dibbesu kāmesu, ratiṃ so nādhigacchati;
```

```
Taṇhakkhayarato <pb ed="T" n="1.0103" /> hoti, sammāsambuddhasāvakoti.
```

Mandhātujātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 259. Tirīṭavacchajātakaṃ (3-1-9)

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
Nayimassa vijjāmayamatthi kiñci, na bandhavo no pana te sahāyo;
```

```
Atha kena vaṇṇena tirīṭavaccho <note>tirīṭivaccho (syā. ka.)</note>, tedaṇḍiko bhuñjati aggapiṇḍaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
Āpāsu <note>āvāsu (ka.)</note> me yuddhaparājitassa, ekassa katvā vivanasmi ghore;
```

```
Pasārayī kicchagatassa pāṇiṃ, tenūdatāriṃ dukhasaṃpareto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
Etassa <pb ed="V" n="1.0066" /> kiccena idhānupatto, vesāyino visayā jīvaloke;
```

```
Lābhāraho tāta tirīṭavaccho, dethassa bhogaṃ yajathañca <note>yajatañca (sī. pī.), yajitañca (syā.)</note> yaññanti.
```

Tirīṭavacchajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 260. Dūtajātakaṃ (3-1-10)

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
Yassatthā <pb ed="T" n="1.0104" /> dūramāyanti, amittamapi yācituṃ;
```

```
Tassūdarassahaṃ dūto, mā me kujjha <note>kujjhi (sī. pī.)</note> rathesabha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
Yassa divā ca ratto ca, vasamāyanti māṇavā;
```

```
Tassūdarassahaṃ dūto, mā me kujjha <note>kujjhi (sī. pī.)</note> rathesabha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
Dadāmi <pb ed="M" n="1.0075" /> te brāhmaṇa rohiṇīnaṃ, gavaṃ sahassaṃ saha puṅgavena;
```

```
Dūto hi dūtassa kathaṃ na dajjaṃ, mayampi tasseva bhavāma dūtāti.
```

Dūtajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Saṅkappavaggo paṭhamo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Usukāravaro tilamuṭṭhi maṇi, hayarāja vihaṅgama āsiviso;
```

```
Janasandha kahāpaṇavassa puna, tiriṭaṃ puna dūtavarena dasāti.
```

#### 2. Padumavaggo

#### 261. Padumajātakaṃ (3-2-1)

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
Yathā <pb ed="T" n="1.0105" /> kesā ca massū ca, chinnaṃ chinnaṃ virūhati;
```

```
Evaṃ rūhatu te nāsā, padumaṃ dehi yācito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
Yathā sāradikaṃ bījaṃ, khette vuttaṃ virūhati;
```

```
Evaṃ rūhatu te nāsā, padumaṃ dehi yācito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
Ubhopi palapantete <note>vilapantete (syā. ka.)</note>, api padmāni dassati;
```

```
Vajjuṃ vā te na vā vajjuṃ, natthi nāsāya rūhanā;
```

```
Dehi samma padumāni, ahaṃ yācāmi yācitoti.
```

Padumajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 262. Mudupāṇijātakaṃ (3-2-2)

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
Pāṇi <pb ed="V" n="1.0067" /> ce muduko cassa, nāgo cassa sukārito;
```

```
Andhakāro ca vasseyya, atha nūna tadā siyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
Analā <pb ed="M" n="1.0076" /> mudusambhāsā, duppūrā tā <note>duppūrattā (ka.)</note> nadīsamā;
```

```
Sīdanti naṃ viditvāna, ārakā parivajjaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
Yaṃ etā upasevanti, chandasā vā dhanena vā;
```

```
Jātavedova saṃ ṭhānaṃ, khippaṃ anudahanti nanti.
```

Mudupāṇijātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 263. Cūḷapalobhanajātakaṃ (3-2-3)

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
Abhijjamāne <pb ed="T" n="1.0106" /> vārismiṃ, sayaṃ <note>ayaṃ (ka.)</note> āgamma iddhiyā;
```

```
Missībhāvitthiyā gantvā, saṃsīdasi <note>saṃsīdati (ka.)</note> mahaṇṇave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
Āvaṭṭanī mahāmāyā, brahmacariyavikopanā;
```

```
Sīdanti naṃ viditvāna, ārakā parivajjaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
Yaṃ etā upasevanti, chandasā vā dhanena vā;
```

```
Jātavedova saṃ ṭhānaṃ, khippaṃ anudahanti nanti.
```

Cūḷapalobhana <note>cullapalobhana (sī. syā. pī.)</note> jātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 264. Mahāpanādajātakaṃ (3-2-4)

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
Panādo nāma so rājā, yassa yūpo suvaṇṇayo;
```

```
Tiriyaṃ soḷasubbedho <note>soḷasapabbedho (sī. pī.)</note>, uddhamāhu <note>uccamāhu (sī. syā. pī.)</note> sahassadhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
Sahassakaṇḍo satageṇḍu <note>satabhedo (sī. pī.), satabheṇḍu (sī. nissaya)</note>, dhajāsu haritāmayo;
```

```
Anaccuṃ tattha gandhabbā, cha sahassāni sattadhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
Evametaṃ <note>evameva (ka.)</note> tadā āsi, yathā bhāsasi bhaddaji;
```

```
Sakko ahaṃ tadā āsiṃ, veyyāvaccakaro tavāti.
```

Mahāpanādajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 265. Khurappajātakaṃ (3-2-5)

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
Disvā <pb ed="V" n="1.0068" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0077" /> khurappe dhanuveganunne, khagge <pb ed="T" n="1.0107" /> gahīte tikhiṇe teladhote;
```

```
Tasmiṃ bhayasmiṃ maraṇe viyūḷhe, kasmā nu te nāhu chambhitattaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
Disvā khurappe dhanuveganunne, khagge gahīte tikhiṇe teladhote;
```

```
Tasmiṃ bhayasmiṃ maraṇe viyūḷhe, vedaṃ alatthaṃ vipulaṃ uḷāraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
So vedajāto ajjhabhaviṃ amitte, pubbeva me jīvitamāsi cattaṃ;
```

```
Na hi jīvite ālayaṃ kubbamāno, sūro kayirā sūrakiccaṃ kadācīti.
```

Khurappajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 266. Vātaggasindhavajātakaṃ (3-2-6)

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
Yenāsi kisiyā paṇḍu, yena bhattaṃ na ruccati;
```

```
Ayaṃ so āgato bhattā <note>tāto (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, kasmā dāni palāyasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
Sace <note>na kho (syā. ka.)</note> panādikeneva, santhavo nāma jāyati;
```

```
Yaso hāyati itthīnaṃ, tasmā tāta palāyahaṃ <note>palāyihaṃ (syā.), palāyitaṃ (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
Yassassinaṃ kule jātaṃ, āgataṃ yā na icchati;
```

```
Socati <pb ed="T" n="1.0108" /> cirarattāya, vātaggamiva bhaddalīti <note>kundalīti (sī. pī.), gadrabhīti (syā.)</note>.
```

Vātaggasindhavajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 267. Kakkaṭakajātakaṃ (3-2-7)

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
Siṅgīmigo <pb ed="M" n="1.0078" /> āyatacakkhunetto, aṭṭhittaco vārisayo alomo;
```

```
Tenābhibhūto kapaṇaṃ rudāmi, mā heva maṃ pāṇasamaṃ jaheyya <note>jaheyyā (pī.) jahā’yye (?)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
Ayya na taṃ jahissāmi, kuñjaraṃ saṭṭhihāyanaṃ <note>kuñjara saṭṭhihāyana (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Pathabyā cāturantāya, suppiyo hosi me tuvaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
Ye kuḷīrā samuddasmiṃ, gaṅgāya yamunāya <note>nammadāya (sī. pī.)</note> ca;
```

```
Tesaṃ tvaṃ vārijo seṭṭho, muñca rodantiyā patinti.
```

Kakkaṭaka <note>kuḷīra (ka.)</note> jātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 268. Ārāmadūsakajātakaṃ (3-2-8)

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
Yo <pb ed="V" n="1.0069" /> ve sabbasametānaṃ, ahuvā seṭṭhasammato;
```

```
Tassāyaṃ edisī paññā, kimeva itarā pajā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
Evameva tuvaṃ brahme, anaññāya vinindasi;
```

```
Kathaṃ mūlaṃ adisvāna <note>kathaṃhi mūlaṃ aditvā (syā. pī.)</note>, rukkhaṃ jaññā patiṭṭhitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
Nāhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0109" /> tumhe vinindāmi, ye caññe vānarā vane;
```

```
Vissasenova gārayho, yassatthā rukkharopakāti.
```

Ārāmadūsakajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 269. Sujātajātakaṃ (3-2-9)

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
Na hi vaṇṇena sampannā, mañjukā piyadassanā;
```

```
Kharavācā piyā hoti, asmiṃ loke paramhi ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
Nanu passasimaṃ kāḷiṃ, dubbaṇṇaṃ tilakāhataṃ;
```

```
Kokilaṃ saṇhavācena, bahūnaṃ pāṇinaṃ piyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
Tasmā <pb ed="M" n="1.0079" /> sakhilavācassa, mantabhāṇī anuddhato;
```

```
Atthaṃ dhammañca dīpeti, madhuraṃ tassa bhāsitanti.
```

Sujātajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 270. Ulūkajātakaṃ (3-2-10)

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
Sabbehi kira ñātīhi, kosiyo issaro kato;
```

```
Sace ñātīhi anuññāto <note>ñātīhanuññāto (sī. pī.)</note>, bhaṇeyyāhaṃ ekavācikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
Bhaṇa samma anuññāto, atthaṃ dhammañca kevalaṃ;
```

```
Santi hi daharā pakkhī, paññavanto jutindharā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
Na me ruccati bhaddaṃ vo <note>bhadante (ka.)</note>, ulūkassābhisecanaṃ;
```

```
Akkuddhassa <pb ed="T" n="1.0110" /> mukhaṃ passa, kathaṃ kuddho karissatīti.
```

Ulūkajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Padumavaggo dutiyo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Padumuttama <pb ed="V" n="1.0070" /> nāgasirivhayano, sa-mahaṇṇava yūpa khurappavaro;
```

```
Atha bhaddalī kuñjara rukkha puna, kharavāca ulūkavarena dasāti.
```

#### 3. Udapānavaggo

#### 271. Udapānadūsakajātakaṃ (3-3-1)

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
Āraññikassa isino, cirarattaṃ tapassino;
```

```
Kicchākataṃ udapānaṃ, kathaṃ samma avāhasi <note>avāhayi (sī. pī.), apāhasi (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
Esa dhammo siṅgālānaṃ, yaṃ pitvā ohadāmase;
```

```
Pitupitāmahaṃ dhammo, na taṃ <note>na naṃ (sī. pī.)</note> ujjhātumarahasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
Yesaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0111" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0080" /> vo ediso dhammo, adhammo pana kīdiso;
```

```
Mā vo dhammaṃ adhammaṃ vā, addasāma kudācananti.
```

Udapānadūsakajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 272. Byagghajātakaṃ (3-3-2)

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
Yena mittena saṃsaggā, yogakkhemo vihiyyati;
```

```
Pubbevajjhābhavaṃ tassa, rukkhe akkhīva paṇḍito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
Yena mittena saṃsaggā, yogakkhemo pavaḍḍhati;
```

```
Kareyyattasamaṃ vuttiṃ, sabbakiccesu paṇḍito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
Etha byagghā nivattavho, paccupetha <note>paccametha (sī. pī.)</note> mahāvanaṃ;
```

```
Mā vanaṃ chindi nibyagghaṃ, byagghā māhesu nibbanāti.
```

Byagghajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 273. Kacchapajātakaṃ (3-3-3)

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
Ko nu uddhitabhattova <note>udditabhattova (sī.), vaḍḍhitabhattova (syā.)</note>, pūrahatthova brāhmaṇo;
```

```
Kahaṃ nu bhikkhaṃ acari, kaṃ saddhaṃ upasaṅkami.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
Ahaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0071" /> kapismi dummedho, anāmāsāni āmasiṃ;
```

```
Tvaṃ maṃ mocaya bhaddante, mutto gaccheyya pabbataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
Kacchapā kassapā honti, koṇḍaññā honti makkaṭā;
```

```
Muñca kassapa koṇḍaññaṃ, kataṃ methunakaṃ tayāti.
```

Kacchapajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 274. Lolajātakaṃ (3-3-4)

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
Kāyaṃ balākā sikhinī, corī laṅghipitāmahā;
```

```
Oraṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0112" /> balāke āgaccha, caṇḍo me vāyaso sakhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
Nāhaṃ balākā sikhinī, ahaṃ lolosmi vāyaso;
```

```
Akatvā vacanaṃ tuyhaṃ, passa lūnosmi āgato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
Punapāpajjasī <pb ed="M" n="1.0081" /> samma, sīlañhi tava tādisaṃ;
```

```
Na hi mānusakā bhogā, subhuñjā honti pakkhināti.
```

Lolajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 275. Rucirajātakaṃ (3-3-5)

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
Kāyaṃ balākā rucirā, kākanīḷasmimacchati;
```

```
Caṇḍo kāko sakhā mayhaṃ, yassa <note>tassa (sī. pī.)</note> cetaṃ kulāvakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
Nanu maṃ samma jānāsi, dija sāmākabhojana;
```

```
Akatvā vacanaṃ tuyhaṃ, passa lūnosmi āgato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
Punapāpajjasī samma, sīlañhi tava tādisaṃ;
```

```
Na hi mānusakā bhogā, subhuñjā honti pakkhināti.
```

Rucirajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 276. Kurudhammajātakaṃ (3-3-6)

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
Tava saddhañca sīlañca, viditvāna janādhipa;
```

```
Vaṇṇaṃ añjanavaṇṇena, kāliṅgasmiṃ nimimhase <note>vinimhase (syā.), vanimhase (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
Annabhaccā <pb ed="T" n="1.0113" /> cabhaccā ca, yodha uddissa gacchati;
```

```
Sabbe te appaṭikkhippā, pubbācariyavaco idaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
Dadāmi <pb ed="V" n="1.0072" /> vo brāhmaṇā nāgametaṃ, rājārahaṃ rājabhoggaṃ yasassinaṃ;
```

```
Alaṅkataṃ hemajālābhichannaṃ, sasārathiṃ gacchatha yena kāmanti.
```

Kurudhammajātakaṃ <note>kurudhammajātakaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 277. Romakajātakaṃ (3-3-7)

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
Vassāni <pb ed="M" n="1.0082" /> paññāsa samādhikāni, vasimha selassa guhāya romaka;
```

```
Asaṅkamānā abhinibbutattā <note>abhinibbutacittā (syā. ka.)</note>, hatthatta <note>hatthattha (syā.)</note> māyanti mamaṇḍajā pure.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
Te dāni vakkaṅga kimatthamussukā, bhajanti aññaṃ girikandaraṃ dijā;
```

```
Na nūna maññanti mamaṃ yathā pure, cirappavutthā atha vā na te ime.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
Jānāma taṃ na mayaṃ sampamūḷhā <note>na maya’masma mūḷhā (sī. pī.)</note>, soyeva tvaṃ te mayamasma nāññe;
```

```
Cittañca <pb ed="T" n="1.0114" /> te asmiṃ jane paduṭṭhaṃ, ājīvikā <note>ājīvaka (sī. syā.), ājīvika (pī.)</note> tena tamuttasāmāti.
```

Romakajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 278. Mahiṃsarājajātakaṃ (3-3-8)

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
Kimattha <note>kamattha (sī. pī.)</note> mabhisandhāya, lahucittassa dubbhino <note>dūbhino (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Sabbakāmadadasseva <note>duhasseva (sī. syā. pī.), rahasseva (ka.)</note>, imaṃ dukkhaṃ titikkhasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
Siṅgena nihanāhetaṃ, padasā ca adhiṭṭhaha;
```

```
Bhiyyo <note>bhīyo (sī.)</note> bālā pakujjheyyuṃ, no cassa paṭisedhako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
Mamevāyaṃ maññamāno, aññepevaṃ <note>aññampevaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> karissati;
```

```
Te naṃ tattha vadhissanti, sā me mutti bhavissatīti.
```

Mahiṃsarājajātakaṃ <note>mahisajātakaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 279. Satapattajātakaṃ (3-3-9)

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
Yathā <pb ed="M" n="1.0083" /> māṇavako panthe, siṅgāliṃ vanagocariṃ;
```

```
Atthakāmaṃ pavedentiṃ <note>pavadantiṃ (pī.)</note>, anatthakāmāti maññati;
```

```
Anatthakāmaṃ satapattaṃ, atthakāmoti maññati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
Evameva idhekacco, puggalo hoti tādiso;
```

```
Hitehi vacanaṃ vutto, paṭigaṇhāti vāmato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
Ye <pb ed="T" n="1.0115" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0073" /> ca kho naṃ pasaṃsanti, bhayā ukkaṃsayanti vā <note>ca (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Tañhi so maññate mittaṃ, satapattaṃva māṇavoti.
```

Satapattajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 280. Puṭadūsakajātakaṃ (3-3-10)

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
Addhā hi nūna migarājā, puṭakammassa kovido;
```

```
Tathā hi puṭaṃ dūseti, aññaṃ nūna karissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
Na me mātā vā pitā vā, puṭakammassa kovido;
```

```
Kataṃ kataṃ kho dūsema, evaṃ dhammamidaṃ kulaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
Yesaṃ vo ediso dhammo, adhammo pana kīdiso;
```

```
Mā vo dhammaṃ adhammaṃ vā, addasāma kudācananti.
```

Puṭadūsakajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Udapānavaggo <note>araññavaggo (sī. pī. ka.)</note> tatiyo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Udapānavaraṃ vanabyaggha kapi, sikhinī ca balāka ruciravaro;
```

```
Sujanādhiparomakadūsa puna, satapattavaro puṭakamma dasāti.
```

#### 4. Abbhantaravaggo

#### 281. Abbhantarajātakaṃ (3-4-1)

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
Abbhantaro <pb ed="T" n="1.0116" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0084" /> nāma dumo, yassa dibyamidaṃ phalaṃ;
```

```
Bhutvā dohaḷinī nārī, cakkavattiṃ vijāyati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
Tvampi <note>tvañca (sī. pī.), tvaṃ hi (ka.)</note> bhadde mahesīsi, sā cāpi <note>cāsi (sī. pī.)</note> patino piyā;
```

```
Āharissati te rājā, idaṃ abbhantaraṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§93.</p>

```
Bhatturatthe parakkanto, yaṃ ṭhānamadhigacchati;
```

```
Sūro attapariccāgī, labhamāno bhavāmahanti.
```

Abbhantarajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 282. Seyyajātakaṃ (3-4-2)

<p rend="hangnum">§94.</p>

```
Seyyaṃso <pb ed="V" n="1.0074" /> seyyaso hoti, yo seyyamupasevati;
```

```
Ekena sandhiṃ katvāna, sataṃ vajjhe <note>macce (ka.), bajjhe (ka. aṭṭha.)</note> amocayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§95.</p>

```
<note>kasmā…pe… saggaṃ na gaccheyya (katthaci)</note> Tasmā sabbena lokena, sandhiṃ katvāna ekato <note>ekako (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Pecca saggaṃ nigaccheyya <note>kasmā…pe… saggaṃ na gaccheyya (katthaci)</note>, idaṃ suṇātha kāsiyā <note>kāsayo (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§96.</p>

```
Idaṃ vatvā mahārājā, kaṃso bārāṇasiggaho;
```

```
Dhanuṃ kaṇḍañca <note>tūṇiñca (sī. pī.)</note> nikkhippa, saṃyamaṃ ajjhupāgamīti.
```

Seyyajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 283. Vaḍḍhakīsūkarajātakaṃ (3-4-3)

<p rend="hangnum">§97.</p>

```
Varaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0117" /> varaṃ tvaṃ nihanaṃ pure cari, asmiṃ padese abhibhuyya sūkare;
```

```
So dāni eko byapagamma jhāyasi, balaṃ nu te byaggha na cajja vijjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§98.</p>

```
Ime <pb ed="M" n="1.0085" /> sudaṃ <note>imassu tā (syā. ka.)</note> yanti disodisaṃ pure, bhayaṭṭitā leṇagavesino puthu;
```

```
Te dāni saṅgamma vasanti ekato, yatthaṭṭhitā duppasahajjame <note>duppasahajjime (syā.)</note> mayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§99.</p>

```
Namatthu saṅghāna samāgatānaṃ, disvā sayaṃ sakhya vadāmi abbhutaṃ;
```

```
Byagghaṃ migā yattha jiniṃsu dāṭhino, sāmaggiyā dāṭhabalesu muccareti.
```

Vaḍḍhakīsūkarajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 284. Sirijātakaṃ (3-4-4)

<p rend="hangnum">§100.</p>

```
Yaṃ ussukā saṅgharanti, alakkhikā bahuṃ dhanaṃ;
```

```
Sippavanto asippā ca, lakkhivā tāni bhuñjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§101.</p>

```
Sabbattha <pb ed="T" n="1.0118" /> katapuññassa, aticcaññeva pāṇino;
```

```
Uppajjanti bahū bhogā, appanāyatanesupi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§102.</p>

```
Kukkuṭo <note>kukkuṭa (sī. pī.), kukkuṭā (sī. nissaya, saddanīti)</note> maṇayo daṇḍo, thiyo ca puññalakkhaṇā;
```

```
Uppajjanti apāpassa, katapuññassa jantunoti.
```

Sirijātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 285. Maṇisūkarajātakaṃ (3-4-5)

<p rend="hangnum">§103.</p>

```
Dariyā <pb ed="V" n="1.0075" /> satta vassāni, tiṃsamattā vasāmase;
```

```
Haññāma <note>hañchema (sī. pī.), hañchāma (?)</note> maṇino ābhaṃ, iti no mantanaṃ ahu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§104.</p>

```
Yāvatā maṇiṃ ghaṃsāma <note>yāva yāva nighaṃsāma (sī. pī.)</note>, bhiyyo vodāyate maṇi;
```

```
Idañca dāni pucchāma, kiṃ kiccaṃ idha maññasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§105.</p>

```
Ayaṃ maṇi veḷūriyo, akāco vimalo <note>vipulo (ka.)</note> subho;
```

```
Nāssa sakkā siriṃ hantuṃ, apakkamatha sūkarāti.
```

Maṇisūkara <note>maṇighaṃsa (ka.)</note> jātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 286. Sālūkajātakaṃ (3-4-6)

<p rend="hangnum">§106.</p>

```
Mā <pb ed="M" n="1.0086" /> sālūkassa pihayi, āturannāni bhuñjati;
```

```
Appossukko bhusaṃ khāda, etaṃ dīghāyulakkhaṇaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§107.</p>

```
Idāni so idhāgantvā, atithī yuttasevako;
```

```
Atha dakkhasi sālūkaṃ, sayantaṃ musaluttaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§108.</p>

```
Vikantaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0119" /> <note>vikattaṃ (sī.), vikantiyamānaṃ chindiyamānaṃti attho</note> sūkaraṃ disvā, sayantaṃ musaluttaraṃ;
```

```
Jaraggavā vicintesuṃ, varamhākaṃ bhusāmivāti.
```

Sālūkajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 287. Lābhagarahajātakaṃ (3-4-7)

<p rend="hangnum">§109.</p>

```
Nānummatto nāpisuṇo, nānaṭo nākutūhalo;
```

```
Mūḷhesu labhate lābhaṃ, esā te anusāsanī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§110.</p>

```
Dhiratthu taṃ yasalābhaṃ, dhanalābhañca brāhmaṇa;
```

```
Yā vutti vinipātena, adhammacaraṇena <note>adhammacariyāya (sī. syā.)</note> vā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§111.</p>

```
Api ce pattamādāya, anagāro paribbaje;
```

```
Esāva jīvikā seyyo <note>seyyā (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, yā cādhammena esanāti.
```

Lābhagarahajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 288. Macchuddānajātakaṃ (3-4-8)

<p rend="hangnum">§112.</p>

```
Agghanti <pb ed="V" n="1.0076" /> macchā adhikaṃ sahassaṃ, na so atthi yo imaṃ saddaheyya;
```

```
Mayhañca assu idha satta māsā, ahampi taṃ macchuddānaṃ kiṇeyyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§113.</p>

```
Macchānaṃ bhojanaṃ datvā, mama dakkhiṇamādisi;
```

```
Taṃ dakkhiṇaṃ sarantiyā, kataṃ apacitiṃ tayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§114.</p>

```
Paduṭṭhacittassa <pb ed="T" n="1.0120" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0087" /> na phāti hoti, na cāpi taṃ <note>naṃ (sī. syā.)</note> devatā pūjayanti;
```

```
Yo bhātaraṃ pettikaṃ sāpateyyaṃ, avañcayī dukkaṭakammakārīti.
```

Macchuddānajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 289. Nānāchandajātakaṃ (3-4-9)

<p rend="hangnum">§115.</p>

```
Nānāchandā mahārāja, ekāgāre vasāmase;
```

```
Ahaṃ gāmavaraṃ icche, brāhmaṇī ca gavaṃ sataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§116.</p>

```
Putto ca ājaññarathaṃ, kaññā ca maṇikuṇḍalaṃ;
```

```
Yā cesā puṇṇikā jammī, udukkhalaṃbhikaṅkhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§117.</p>

```
Brāhmaṇassa gāmavaraṃ, brāhmaṇiyā gavaṃ sataṃ;
```

```
Puttassa ājaññarathaṃ, kaññāya maṇikuṇḍalaṃ;
```

```
Yañcetaṃ puṇṇikaṃ jammiṃ, paṭipādethudukkhalanti.
```

Nānāchandajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 290. Sīlavīmaṃsakajātakaṃ (3-4-10)

<p rend="hangnum">§118.</p>

```
Sīlaṃ kireva kalyāṇaṃ, sīlaṃ loke anuttaraṃ;
```

```
Passa ghoraviso nāgo, sīlavāti na haññati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§119.</p>

```
Sohaṃ sīlaṃ samādissaṃ, loke anumataṃ sivaṃ;
```

```
Ariyavuttisamācāro<pb ed="T" n="1.0121" />, yena vuccati sīlavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§120.</p>

```
Ñātīnañca piyo hoti, mittesu ca virocati;
```

```
Kāyassa bhedā sugatiṃ, upapajjati sīlavāti.
```

Sīlavīmaṃsakajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Abbhantaravaggo catuttho.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Duma <pb ed="V" n="1.0077" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0088" /> kaṃsavaruttamabyagghamigā, maṇayo maṇi sālukamavhayano;
```

```
Anusāsaniyopi ca macchavaro, maṇikuṇḍalakena kirena dasāti.
```

#### 5. Kumbhavaggo

#### 291. Surāghaṭajātakaṃ (2-5-1)

<p rend="hangnum">§121.</p>

```
Sabbakāmadadaṃ kumbhaṃ, kuṭaṃ laddhāna dhuttako;
```

```
Yāva naṃ anupāleti, tāva so sukhamedhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§122.</p>

```
Yadā matto ca ditto ca, pamādā kumbhamabbhidā;
```

```
Tadā naggo ca pottho ca, pacchā bālo vihaññati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§123.</p>

```
Evameva yo dhanaṃ laddhā, pamatto <note>amattā (sī.), amatto (pī.)</note> paribhuñjati;
```

```
Pacchā <pb ed="T" n="1.0122" /> tappati dummedho, kuṭaṃ bhitvāva <note>kuṭaṃ bhinnova (sī. pī.), kuṭabhinnova (?)</note> dhuttakoti.
```

Surāghaṭa <note>bhadraghaṭa (sī. pī.), bhadraghaṭabhedaka (syā.)</note> jātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 292. Supattajātakaṃ (3-5-2)

<p rend="hangnum">§124.</p>

```
Bārāṇasyaṃ <note>bārāṇassaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> mahārāja, kākarājā nivāsako <note>nivāsiko (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Asītiyā sahassehi, supatto parivārito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§125.</p>

```
Tassa dohaḷinī bhariyā, suphassā bhakkhitumicchati <note>macchamicchati (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Rañño mahānase pakkaṃ, paccagghaṃ rājabhojanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§126.</p>

```
Tesāhaṃ pahito dūto, rañño camhi idhāgato;
```

```
Bhattu apacitiṃ kummi, nāsāyamakaraṃ <note>makariṃ (sī. nissaya)</note> vaṇanti.
```

Supattajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 293. Kāyanibbindajātakaṃ (3-5-3)

<p rend="hangnum">§127.</p>

```
Phuṭṭhassa <pb ed="M" n="1.0089" /> me aññatarena byādhinā, rogena bāḷhaṃ dukhitassa ruppato;
```

```
Parisussati khippamidaṃ kaḷevaraṃ, pupphaṃ yathā paṃsuni ātape kataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§128.</p>

```
Ajaññaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0078" /> jaññasaṅkhātaṃ, asuciṃ sucisammataṃ;
```

```
Nānākuṇapaparipūraṃ, jaññarūpaṃ apassato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§129.</p>

```
Dhiratthumaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0123" /> āturaṃ pūtikāyaṃ, jegucchiyaṃ assuciṃ byādhidhammaṃ;
```

```
Yatthappamattā adhimucchitā pajā, hāpenti maggaṃ sugatūpapattiyāti.
```

Kāyanibbinda <note>kāyavicchanda (sī.), kāyavicchinda (pī.)</note> jātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 294. Jambukhādakajātakaṃ (3-5-4)

<p rend="hangnum">§130.</p>

```
Koyaṃ bindussaro vaggu, saravantāna <note>pavadantāna (sī. pī.)</note> muttamo;
```

```
Accuto jambusākhāya, moracchāpova kūjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§131.</p>

```
Kulaputtova jānāti <note>kulaputto pajānāti (syā. ka.)</note>, kulaputtaṃ <note>kulaputte (sī. pī.)</note> pasaṃsituṃ;
```

```
Byagghacchāpasarīvaṇṇa, bhuñja samma dadāmi te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§132.</p>

```
Cirassaṃ vata passāmi, musāvādī samāgate;
```

```
Vantādaṃ kuṇapādañca, aññamaññaṃ pasaṃsaketi.
```

Jambukhādakajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 295. Antajātakaṃ (3-5-5)

<p rend="hangnum">§133.</p>

```
Usabhasseva te khandho, sīhasseva vijambhitaṃ;
```

```
Migarāja namo tyatthu, api kiñci labhāmase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§134.</p>

```
Kulaputtova jānāti, kulaputtaṃ pasaṃsituṃ;
```

```
Mayūragīvasaṅkāsa, ito pariyāhi vāyasa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§135.</p>

```
Migānaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0124" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0090" /> siṅgālo <note>kotthuko (sī. pī.), koṭṭhuko (syā.)</note> anto, pakkhīnaṃ pana vāyaso;
```

```
Eraṇḍo anto rukkhānaṃ, tayo antā samāgatāti.
```

Antajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 296. Samuddajātakaṃ (3-5-6)

<p rend="hangnum">§136.</p>

```
Ko nāyaṃ <note>ko nvāyaṃ (syā.)</note> loṇatoyasmiṃ, samantā paridhāvati;
```

```
Macche makare ca vāreti, ūmīsu ca vihaññati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§137.</p>

```
Anantapāyī sakuṇo, atittoti disāsuto;
```

```
Samuddaṃ pātumicchāmi, sāgaraṃ saritaṃ patiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§138.</p>

```
So <pb ed="V" n="1.0079" /> ayaṃ hāyati ceva, pūrate ca mahodadhi;
```

```
Nāssa nāyati pītanto, apeyyo kira sāgaroti.
```

Samuddajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 297. Kāmavilāpajātakaṃ (3-5-7)

<p rend="hangnum">§139.</p>

```
Ucce sakuṇa ḍemāna, pattayāna vihaṅgama;
```

```
Vajjāsi kho tvaṃ vāmūruṃ, ciraṃ kho sā karissati <note>sarissati (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§140.</p>

```
Idaṃ kho sā na jānāti, asiṃ sattiñca oḍḍitaṃ;
```

```
Sā caṇḍī kāhati kodhaṃ, taṃ me tapati no idaṃ <note>no idha (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§141.</p>

```
Esa <pb ed="T" n="1.0125" /> uppalasannāho, nikkhañcussīsakohitaṃ <note>nikkhamussīsake kataṃ (sī. pī.), nikkhañcussīsake kataṃ (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Kāsikañca muduṃ vatthaṃ, tappetu dhanikā piyāti <note>dhanakāmiyāti (syā. pī.), dhanakāmikāti (sī.)</note>.
```

Kāmavilāpajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 298. Udumbarajātakaṃ (3-5-8)

<p rend="hangnum">§142.</p>

```
Udumbarā cime pakkā, nigrodhā ca kapitthanā;
```

```
Ehi nikkhama bhuñjassu, kiṃ jighacchāya miyyasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§143.</p>

```
Evaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0091" /> so suhito hoti, yo vuḍḍhamapacāyati;
```

```
Yathāhamajja suhito, dumapakkāni māsito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§144.</p>

```
Yaṃ vanejo vanejassa, vañceyya kapino kapi;
```

```
Daharo kapi <note>daharopi taṃ na (sī. pī.), daharopi na (syā.)</note> saddheyya, na hi jiṇṇo jarākapīti.
```

Udumbarajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 299. Komāraputtajātakaṃ (3-5-9)

<p rend="hangnum">§145.</p>

```
Pure tuvaṃ sīlavataṃ sakāse, okkantikaṃ <note>okkandikaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> kīḷasi assamamhi;
```

```
Karohare <note>karohi re (ka.)</note> makkaṭiyāni makkaṭa, na taṃ mayaṃ sīlavataṃ ramāma.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§146.</p>

```
Sutā <pb ed="T" n="1.0126" /> hi mayhaṃ paramā visuddhi, komāraputtassa bahussutassa;
```

```
Mā dāni maṃ maññi tuvaṃ yathā pure, jhānānuyutto viharāmi <note>jhānānuyuttā viharāma (sī. pī.)</note> āvuso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§147.</p>

```
Sacepi selasmi vapeyya bījaṃ, devo ca vasse na hi taṃ virūḷhe <note>neva hi taṃ ruheyya (sī. pī.), na hi taṃ virūhe (?)</note>;
```

```
Sutā hi te sā paramā visuddhi, ārā tuvaṃ makkaṭa jhānabhūmiyāti.
```

Komāraputtajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 300. Vakajātakaṃ (3-5-10)

<p rend="hangnum">§148.</p>

```
Parapāṇarodhā <pb ed="V" n="1.0080" /> <note>parapāṇaghāte (syā.), parapāṇarocaṃ (ka.)</note> jīvanto, maṃsalohitabhojano;
```

```
Vako vataṃ samādāya, upapajji uposathaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§149.</p>

```
Tassa sakko vataññāya, ajarūpenupāgami;
```

```
Vītatapo ajjhappatto, bhañji lohitapo tapaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§150.</p>

```
Evameva <pb ed="M" n="1.0092" /> idhekacce, samādānamhi dubbalā;
```

```
Lahuṃ karonti attānaṃ, vakova ajakāraṇāti.
```

Vakajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Kumbhavaggo pañcamo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Varakumbha <pb ed="T" n="1.0127" /> supattasirivhayano, sucisammata bindusaro cusabho;
```

```
Saritaṃpati caṇḍi jarākapinā, atha makkaṭiyā vakakena dasāti.
```

Atha vagguddānaṃ –

```
Saṅkappo padumo ceva, udapānena tatiyaṃ;
```

```
Abbhantaraṃ ghaṭabhedaṃ, tikanipātamhilaṅkatanti.
```

<trailer rend="centre">Tikanipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.</trailer>

### 4. Catukkanipāto

#### 1. Kāliṅgavaggo

#### 301. Cūḷakāliṅgajātakaṃ (4-1-1)

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
Vivarathimāsaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0128" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0081" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0093" /> <note>vivaratha imāsaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> dvāraṃ, nagaraṃ pavisantu <note>pavisituṃ mayā; (ka.)</note> aruṇarājassa;
```

```
Sīhena susiṭṭhena, surakkhitaṃ <note>susatthena, surakkhitaṃ (sī. pī.), susiṭṭhena (ka.)</note> nandisenena.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
Jayo kaliṅgānamasayhasāhinaṃ, parājayo anayo <note>ajayo (syā.), anvito (ka.)</note> assakānaṃ;
```

```
Icceva te bhāsitaṃ brahmacāri, na ujjubhūtā vitathaṃ bhaṇanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
Devā musāvādamupātivattā, saccaṃ dhanaṃ paramaṃ tesu <note>tathaṃ pemakaraṃ nu (ka.), tathaṃ paramaṃ karaṃ nu (syā.)</note> sakka;
```

```
Taṃ te musā bhāsitaṃ devarāja, kiṃ vā paṭicca maghavā mahinda.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
Nanu te sutaṃ brāhmaṇa bhaññamāne, devā na issanti purisaparakkamassa;
```

```
Damo samādhi manaso abhejjo <note>adejjo (sī. pī.), abhijjo (ka.)</note>, abyaggatā <pb ed="T" n="1.0129" /> nikkamanañca <note>nikkhamanañca (sī.)</note> kāle;
```

```
Daḷhañca viriyaṃ purisaparakkamo ca, teneva āsi vijayo assakānanti.
```

Cūḷakāliṅgajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 302. Mahāassārohajātakaṃ (4-1-2)

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
Adeyyesu dadaṃ dānaṃ, deyyesu nappavecchati;
```

```
Āpāsu byasanaṃ patto, sahāyaṃ nādhigacchati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
Nādeyyesu <pb ed="M" n="1.0094" /> dadaṃ dānaṃ, deyyesu yo pavecchati;
```

```
Āpāsu byasanaṃ patto, sahāyamadhigacchati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
Saññogasambhogavisesadassanaṃ, anariyadhammesu saṭhesu nassati;
```

```
Katañca ariyesu ca ajjavesu, mahapphalaṃ hoti aṇumpi tādisu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
Yo pubbe katakalyāṇo, akā loke sudukkaraṃ;
```

```
Pacchā kayirā na vā kayirā, accantaṃ pūjanārahoti.
```

Mahāassārohajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 303. Ekarājajātakaṃ (4-1-3)

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
Anuttare <pb ed="T" n="1.0130" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0082" /> kāmaguṇe samiddhe, bhutvāna pubbe vasī ekarāja;
```

```
So dāni dugge narakamhi khitto, nappajjahe vaṇṇabalaṃ purāṇaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
Pubbeva khantī ca tapo ca mayhaṃ, sampatthitā dubbhisena <note>dabbasenā (sī. pī.)</note> ahosi;
```

```
Taṃ dāni laddhāna kathaṃ nu rāja, jahe ahaṃ vaṇṇabalaṃ purāṇaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
Sabbā kirevaṃ pariniṭṭhitāni, yasassinaṃ paññavantaṃ visayha;
```

```
Yaso ca laddhā purimaṃ uḷāraṃ, nappajjahe vaṇṇabalaṃ purāṇaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
Panujja dukkhena sukhaṃ janinda, sukhena vā dukkhamasayhasāhi;
```

```
Ubhayattha santo abhinibbutattā, sukhe ca dukkhe ca bhavanti tulyāti.
```

Ekarājajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 304. Daddarajātakaṃ (4-1-4)

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
Imāni <pb ed="T" n="1.0131" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0095" /> maṃ daddara tāpayanti, vācāduruttāni manussaloke;
```

```
Maṇḍūkabhakkhā udakantasevī, āsīvisaṃ maṃ avisā sapanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
Sakā raṭṭhā pabbājito, aññaṃ janapadaṃ gato;
```

```
Mahantaṃ koṭṭhaṃ kayirātha, duruttānaṃ <note>duruttāni (ka.)</note> nidhetave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
Yattha posaṃ na jānanti, jātiyā vinayena vā;
```

```
Na tattha mānaṃ kayirātha, vasamaññātake jane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
Videsavāsaṃ vasato, jātavedasamenapi <note>jātavedabhayenapi (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Khamitabbaṃ sapaññena, api dāsassa tajjitanti.
```

Daddarajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 305. Sīlavīmaṃsanajātakaṃ (4-1-5)

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
Natthi loke raho nāma, pāpakammaṃ pakubbato;
```

```
Passanti vanabhūtāni, taṃ bālo maññatī raho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
Ahaṃ raho na passāmi, suññaṃ vāpi na vijjati;
```

```
Yattha aññaṃ <note>suññaṃ (syā. ka.)</note> na passāmi, asuññaṃ hoti taṃ mayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
Dujjacco ca sujacco <note>ajacco (pī.)</note> ca, nando ca sukhavaḍḍhito <note>sukhavacchako (sī.), sukhavacchano (syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Vejjo <pb ed="T" n="1.0132" /> ca addhuvasīlo <note>atha sīlo (ka.)</note> ca, te dhammaṃ jahu matthikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
Brāhmaṇo <pb ed="V" n="1.0083" /> ca kathaṃ jahe, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
```

```
Yo dhammamanupāleti, dhitimā saccanikkamoti.
```

Sīlavīmaṃsanajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 306. Sujātajātakaṃ (4-1-6)

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
Kimaṇḍakā <pb ed="M" n="1.0096" /> ime deva, nikkhittā kaṃsamallake;
```

```
Upalohitakā vaggū, taṃ <note>te (pī.)</note> me akkhāhi pucchito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
Yāni pure tuvaṃ devi, bhaṇḍu nantakavāsinī;
```

```
Ucchaṅgahatthā pacināsi, tassā te koliyaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
Uḍḍayhate na ramati, bhogā vippajahanti taṃ <note>vippajahanti’maṃ (?)</note>;
```

```
Tatthevimaṃ paṭinetha, yattha kolaṃ pacissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
Honti hete mahārāja, iddhippattāya <note>iddhimattāya (ka.)</note> nāriyā;
```

```
Khama deva sujātāya, māssā <note>māsu (ka.)</note> kujjha rathesabhāti.
```

Sujātajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 307. Palāsajātakaṃ (4-1-7)

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
Acetanaṃ brāhmaṇa assuṇantaṃ, jāno ajānantamimaṃ palāsaṃ;
```

```
Āraddhaviriyo dhuvaṃ appamatto, sukhaseyyaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0133" /> pucchasi kissa hetu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
Dūre suto ceva brahā ca rukkho, dese ṭhito bhūtanivāsarūpo;
```

```
Tasmā namassāmi imaṃ palāsaṃ, ye cettha bhūtā te <note>te ca (sī. pī.)</note> dhanassa hetu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
So te karissāmi yathānubhāvaṃ, kataññutaṃ brāhmaṇa pekkhamāno;
```

```
Kathañhi āgamma sataṃ sakāse, moghāni te assu pariphanditāni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
Yo <pb ed="M" n="1.0097" /> tindukarukkhassa paro <note>puro (ka.)</note> pilakkho <note>pilakkhu (sī. pī.), milakkhu (ka.)</note>, parivārito pubbayañño uḷāro;
```

```
Tassesa mūlasmiṃ nidhi nikhāto, adāyādo gaccha taṃ uddharāhīti.
```

Palāsajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 308. Sakuṇajātakaṃ (4-1-8)

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
Akaramhasa te kiccaṃ, yaṃ balaṃ ahuvamhase;
```

```
Migarāja namo tyatthu, api kiñci labhāmase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
Mama <pb ed="V" n="1.0084" /> lohitabhakkhassa, niccaṃ luddāni kubbato;
```

```
Dantantaragato santo, taṃ bahuṃ yampi jīvasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
Akataññumakattāraṃ<pb ed="T" n="1.0134" />, katassa appaṭikārakaṃ;
```

```
Yasmiṃ kataññutā natthi, niratthā tassa sevanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
Yassa sammukhaciṇṇena, mittadhammo na labbhati;
```

```
Anusūya <note>anusuyya (sī. pī.)</note> manakkosaṃ, saṇikaṃ tamhā apakkameti.
```

Sakuṇajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 309. Chavakajātakaṃ (4-1-9)

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
Sabbamidaṃ carimaṃ kataṃ <note>carimavataṃ (sī. pī.)</note>, ubho dhammaṃ na passare;
```

```
Ubho pakatiyā cutā, yo cāyaṃ mantejjhāpeti <note>mantajjhāyati (sī.), sajjhāpayati (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Yo ca mantaṃ adhīyati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
Sālīnaṃ odanaṃ bhuñje, suciṃ maṃsūpasecanaṃ;
```

```
Tasmā etaṃ na sevāmi, dhammaṃ isīhi sevitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
Paribbaja mahā loko <note>mahābrahme (ka.)</note>, pacantaññepi pāṇino;
```

```
Mā taṃ adhammo ācarito, asmā kumbhamivābhidā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
Dhiratthu <pb ed="M" n="1.0098" /> taṃ yasalābhaṃ, dhanalābhañca brāhmaṇa;
```

```
Yā vutti vinipātena, adhammacaraṇena vāti.
```

Chavakajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 310. Seyyajātakaṃ (4-1-10)

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
Sasamuddapariyāyaṃ<pb ed="T" n="1.0135" />, mahiṃ sāgarakuṇḍalaṃ;
```

```
Na icche saha nindāya, evaṃ seyya <note>sayha (sī. syā. pī.)</note> vijānahi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
Dhiratthu taṃ yasalābhaṃ, dhanalābhañca brāhmaṇa;
```

```
Yā vutti vinipātena, adhammacaraṇena vā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
Api ce pattamādāya, anagāro paribbaje;
```

```
Sāyeva jīvikā seyyo, yā cādhammena esanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
Api <pb ed="V" n="1.0085" /> ce pattamādāya, anagāro paribbaje;
```

```
Aññaṃ ahiṃsayaṃ loke, api rajjena taṃ varanti.
```

Seyyajātakaṃ <note>sayhajātakaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> dasamaṃ.

Kāliṅgavaggo <note>vivaravaggo (sī. pī.)</note> paṭhamo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Vivarañca adeyya samiddhavaraṃ, atha daddara pāpamahātiraho;
```

```
Atha koli palāsavarañca kara, carimaṃ sasamuddavarena dasāti.
```

#### 2. Pucimandavaggo

#### 311. Pucimandajātakaṃ (4-2-1)

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
Uṭṭhehi cora kiṃ sesi, ko attho supanena <note>supitena (sī.), supinena (pī. ka.)</note> te;
```

```
Mā <pb ed="T" n="1.0136" /> taṃ gahesuṃ <note>gaṇheyyuṃ (ka.)</note> rājāno, gāme kibbisakārakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
Yaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0099" /> nu <note>nūna (syā.)</note> coraṃ gahessanti, gāme kibbisakārakaṃ;
```

```
Kiṃ tattha pucimandassa, vane jātassa tiṭṭhato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
Na tvaṃ assattha jānāsi, mama corassa cantaraṃ;
```

```
Coraṃ gahetvā rājāno, gāme kibbisakārakaṃ;
```

```
Appenti <note>accenti (syā.)</note> nimbasūlasmiṃ, tasmiṃ me saṅkate mano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
Saṅkeyya saṅkitabbāni, rakkheyyānāgataṃ bhayaṃ;
```

```
Anāgatabhayā dhīro, ubho loke avekkhatīti.
```

Pucimandajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 312. Kassapamandiyajātakaṃ (4-2-2)

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
Api kassapa mandiyā, yuvā sapati hanti <note>sampaṭihanti (ka.)</note> vā;
```

```
Sabbaṃ taṃ khamate dhīro, paṇḍito taṃ titikkhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
Sacepi santo vivadanti, khippaṃ sandhīyare puna;
```

```
Bālā pattāva bhijjanti, na te samathamajjhagū.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
Ete <pb ed="V" n="1.0086" /> bhiyyo samāyanti, sandhi tesaṃ na jīrati;
```

```
Yo cādhipannaṃ jānāti, yo ca jānāti desanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
Eso hi uttaritaro, bhāravaho dhuraddharo;
```

```
Yo paresādhipannānaṃ<pb ed="T" n="1.0137" />, sayaṃ sandhātumarahatīti.
```

Kassapamandiyajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 313. Khantīvādījātakaṃ (4-2-3)

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
Yo te hatthe ca pāde ca, kaṇṇanāsañca chedayi;
```

```
Tassa kujjha mahāvīra, mā raṭṭhaṃ vinasā <note>vinassa (ka. sī. syā. ka.)</note> idaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
Yo me hatthe ca pāde ca, kaṇṇanāsañca chedayi;
```

```
Ciraṃ jīvatu so rājā, na hi kujjhanti mādisā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
Ahū atītamaddhānaṃ <note>ahu atītamaddhāne (syā. pī. ka.)</note>, samaṇo khantidīpano;
```

```
Taṃ khantiyāyeva ṭhitaṃ, kāsirājā achedayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
Tassa <pb ed="M" n="1.0100" /> kamma <note>kammassa (sī. pī.)</note> pharusassa, vipāko kaṭuko ahu;
```

```
Yaṃ kāsirājā vedesi, nirayamhi samappitoti.
```

Khantīvādījātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 314. Lohakumbhijātakaṃ (4-2-4)

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
Dujjīvitamajīvimha, ye sante <note>yesaṃ no (syā. ka.)</note> na dadamhase;
```

```
Vijjamānesu bhogesu, dīpaṃ nākamha attano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
Saṭṭhi <note>saṭṭhiṃ (syā.)</note> vassasahassāni, paripuṇṇāni sabbaso;
```

```
Niraye paccamānānaṃ, kadā anto bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
Natthi anto kuto anto, na anto paṭidissati;
```

```
Tadā <pb ed="T" n="1.0138" /> hi pakataṃ pāpaṃ, mama tuyhañca mārisā <note>mārisa (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
Sohaṃ nūna ito gantvā, yoniṃ laddhāna mānusiṃ;
```

```
Vadaññū sīlasampanno, kāhāmi kusalaṃ bahunti.
```

Lohakumbhijātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 315. Sabbamaṃsalābhajātakaṃ (4-2-5)

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
Pharusā <pb ed="V" n="1.0087" /> vata te vācā, maṃsaṃ <note>samma (pī. ka.)</note> yācanako asi <note>casi (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Kilomasadisī <note>kilomassa sadisā (pī.)</note> vācā, kilomaṃ samma dammi te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
Aṅgametaṃ manussānaṃ, bhātā loke pavuccati;
```

```
Aṅgassa sadisī vācā <note>aṅgassadisī te vācā (ka.)</note>, aṅgaṃ samma dadāmi te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
Tātāti putto vadamāno, kampeti <note>sammeti (ka.)</note> hadayaṃ pitu;
```

```
Hadayassa sadisī <note>hadayassadisī (ka.)</note> vācā, hadayaṃ samma dammi te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
Yassa gāme sakhā natthi, yathāraññaṃ tatheva taṃ;
```

```
Sabbassa sadisī vācā, sabbaṃ samma dadāmi teti.
```

Sabbamaṃsalābhajātakaṃ <note>maṃsajātakaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> pañcamaṃ.

#### 316. Sasapaṇḍitajātakaṃ (4-2-6)

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
Satta <pb ed="M" n="1.0101" /> me rohitā macchā, udakā thalamubbhatā;
```

```
Idaṃ brāhmaṇa me atthi, etaṃ bhutvā vane vasa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
Dussa me khettapālassa, rattibhattaṃ apābhataṃ;
```

```
Maṃsasūlā <pb ed="T" n="1.0139" /> ca dve godhā, ekañca dadhivārakaṃ;
```

```
Idaṃ brāhmaṇa me atthi, etaṃ bhutvā vane vasa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
Ambapakkaṃ dakaṃ <note>ambapakkodakaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> sītaṃ, sītacchāyā manoramā <note>sītacchāyaṃ manoramaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Idaṃ brāhmaṇa me atthi, etaṃ bhutvā vane vasa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
Na sasassa tilā atthi, na muggā napi taṇḍulā;
```

```
Iminā agginā pakkaṃ, mamaṃ <note>maṃsaṃ (ka.)</note> bhutvā vane vasāti.
```

Sasapaṇḍitajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 317. Matarodanajātakaṃ (4-2-7)

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
Mataṃ mataṃ eva <note>matamatameva (sī. syā. pī.)</note> rodatha, na hi taṃ rodatha yo marissati;
```

```
Sabbepi <note>sabbeva (sī. syā. pī.)</note> sarīradhārino, anupubbena jahanti jīvitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
Devamanussā catuppadā, pakkhigaṇā uragā ca bhogino;
```

```
Samhi <note>yamhi (syā.), asmiṃ (pī. ka.)</note> sarīre anissarā, ramamānāva jahanti jīvitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
Evaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0088" /> calitaṃ asaṇṭhitaṃ, sukhadukkhaṃ manujesvapekkhiya;
```

```
Kanditaruditaṃ niratthakaṃ, kiṃ vo sokagaṇābhikīrare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
Dhuttā ca soṇḍā <note>dhuttā soṇḍā (sī.), dhuttā soṇḍā ca (syā.)</note> akatā, bālā sūrā ayogino <note>bālā sūrā vīrā ayogino (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Dhīraṃ maññanti bāloti, ye dhammassa akovidāti.
```

Matarodanajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 318. Kaṇaverajātakaṃ (4-2-8)

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
Yaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0140" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0102" /> taṃ vasantasamaye, kaṇaveresu bhāṇusu;
```

```
Sāmaṃ bāhāya pīḷesi, sā taṃ ārogyamabravi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
Ambho na kira saddheyyaṃ, yaṃ vāto pabbataṃ vahe;
```

```
Pabbatañce vahe vāto, sabbampi pathaviṃ vahe;
```

```
Yattha sāmā kālakatā <note>kālaṅkatā (ka.)</note>, sā maṃ ārogyamabravi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
Na ceva sā kālakatā, na ca sā aññamicchati;
```

```
Ekabhattikinī <note>ekabhattā kira (sī. syā.), ekabhattakinī (pī.)</note> sāmā, tameva abhikaṅkhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
Asanthutaṃ maṃ cirasanthutena <note>asandhataṃ maṃ cirasandhatena (ka.)</note>, nimīni sāmā adhuvaṃ dhuvena;
```

```
Mayāpi sāmā nimineyya aññaṃ, ito ahaṃ dūrataraṃ gamissanti.
```

Kaṇaverajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 319. Tittirajātakaṃ (4-2-9)

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
Susukhaṃ vata jīvāmi, labhāmi ceva bhuñjituṃ;
```

```
Paripantheva tiṭṭhāmi, kā nu bhante gatī mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
Mano ce te nappaṇamati, pakkhi pāpassa kammuno;
```

```
Abyāvaṭassa bhadrassa, na pāpamupalimpati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
Ñātako no nisinnoti, bahu āgacchate jano;
```

```
Paṭicca <pb ed="T" n="1.0141" /> kammaṃ phusati, tasmiṃ me saṅkate mano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
Na paṭicca kammaṃ phusati, mano ce nappadussati;
```

```
Appossukkassa bhadrassa, na pāpamupalimpatīti.
```

Tittirajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 320. Succajajātakaṃ (4-2-10)

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
Succajaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0089" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0103" /> vata naccaji, vācāya adadaṃ giriṃ;
```

```
Kiṃ hitassa cajantassa, vācāya adada pabbataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
Yañhi kayirā tañhi vade, yaṃ na kayirā na taṃ vade;
```

```
Akarontaṃ bhāsamānaṃ, parijānanti paṇḍitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
Rājaputta namo tyatthu, sacce dhamme ṭhito casi;
```

```
Yassa te byasanaṃ patto, saccasmiṃ ramate mano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
Yā daliddī daliddassa, aḍḍhā aḍḍhassa kittima <note>kittimā (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Sā hissa paramā bhariyā, sahiraññassa itthiyoti.
```

Succajajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Pucimandavaggo dutiyo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Atha cora sakassapa khantīvaro, dujjīvitatā ca varā pharusā;
```

```
Atha <pb ed="T" n="1.0142" /> sasa matañca vasanta sukhaṃ, succajaṃvatanaccajinā ca dasāti.
```

#### 3. Kuṭidūsakavaggo

#### 321. Kuṭidūsakajātakaṃ (4-3-1)

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
Manussasseva te sīsaṃ, hatthapādā ca vānara;
```

```
Atha kena nu vaṇṇena, agāraṃ te na vijjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
Manussasseva me sīsaṃ, hatthapādā ca siṅgila <note>siṅgāla (ka.), piṅgala (ṭīkā)</note>;
```

```
Yāhu seṭṭhā manussesu, sā me paññā na vijjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
Anavaṭṭhitacittassa<pb ed="M" n="1.0104" />, lahucittassa dubbhino <note>dūbhino (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Niccaṃ addhuvasīlassa, sukhabhāvo <note>sucibhāvo (sī.), sukhabhāgo (?)</note> na vijjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
So <pb ed="V" n="1.0090" /> karassu ānubhāvaṃ, vītivattassu sīliyaṃ;
```

```
Sītavātaparittāṇaṃ, karassu kuṭavaṃ <note>kuṭikaṃ (sī. syā.)</note> kapīti.
```

Kuṭidūsaka <note>siṅgālasakuṇa (ka.)</note> jātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 322. Duddubhajātakaṃ (4-3-2)

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
Duddubhāyati <note>daddabhāyati (sī. pī.)</note> bhaddante, yasmiṃ dese vasāmahaṃ;
```

```
Ahampetaṃ na jānāmi, kimetaṃ duddubhāyati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
Beluvaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0143" /> patitaṃ sutvā, duddubhanti <note>daddabhanti (sī.)</note> saso javi;
```

```
Sasassa vacanaṃ sutvā, santattā migavāhinī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
Appatvā padaviññāṇaṃ, paraghosānusārino;
```

```
Panādaparamā bālā, te honti parapattiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
Ye ca sīlena sampannā, paññāyūpasame ratā;
```

```
Ārakā viratā dhīrā, na honti parapattiyāti.
```

Duddubhajātakaṃ <note>daddabhajātakaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> dutiyaṃ.

#### 323. Brahmadattajātakaṃ (4-3-3)

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
Dvayaṃ yācanako rāja, brahmadatta nigacchati;
```

```
Alābhaṃ dhanalābhaṃ vā, evaṃ dhammā hi yācanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
Yācanaṃ rodanaṃ āhu, pañcālānaṃ rathesabha;
```

```
Yo yācanaṃ paccakkhāti, tamāhu paṭirodanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
Mā maddasaṃsu rodantaṃ, pañcālā susamāgatā;
```

```
Tuvaṃ vā paṭirodantaṃ, tasmā icchāmahaṃ raho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
Dadāmi <pb ed="M" n="1.0105" /> te brāhmaṇa rohiṇīnaṃ, gavaṃ sahassaṃ saha puṅgavena;
```

```
Ariyo hi ariyassa kathaṃ na dajjā <note>dajje (sī.), dajjaṃ (?)</note>, sutvāna gāthā tava dhammayuttāti.
```

Brahmadattajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 324. Cammasāṭakajātakaṃ (4-3-4)

<p rend="hangnum">§93.</p>

```
Kalyāṇarūpo <pb ed="T" n="1.0144" /> vatayaṃ catuppado, subhaddako ceva supesalo ca;
```

```
Yo brāhmaṇaṃ jātimantūpapannaṃ, apacāyati meṇḍavaro yasassī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§94.</p>

```
Mā <pb ed="V" n="1.0091" /> brāhmaṇa ittaradassanena, vissāsamāpajji catuppadassa;
```

```
Daḷhappahāraṃ abhikaṅkhamāno <note>abhikattukāmo (syā.)</note>, avasakkatī dassati suppahāraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§95.</p>

```
Ūruṭṭhi <note>ūraṭṭhi (sī.)</note> bhaggaṃ pavaṭṭito <note>patito (sī. syā.)</note> khāribhāro, sabbañca bhaṇḍaṃ brāhmaṇassa <note>brāhmaṇassīdha (ka. sī. pī.), brāhmaṇasseva (ka. sī. syā. ka.)</note> bhinnaṃ;
```

```
Ubhopi bāhā paggayha <note>paggayyeva (syā.), paggahīya (?)</note> kandati <note>bāhā paggayya kandati (pī. ka.)</note>, abhidhāvatha haññate brahmacārī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§96.</p>

```
Evaṃ so nihato seti, yo apūjaṃ pasaṃsati <note>namassati (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Yathāhamajja pahato, hato meṇḍena dummatīti.
```

Cammasāṭakajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 325. Godharājajātakaṃ (4-3-5)

<p rend="hangnum">§97.</p>

```
Samaṇaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0145" /> taṃ maññamāno, upagacchimasaññataṃ;
```

```
So maṃ daṇḍena pāhāsi, yathā assamaṇo tathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§98.</p>

```
Kiṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0106" /> te jaṭāhi dummedha, kiṃ te ajinasāṭiyā;
```

```
Abbhantaraṃ te gahanaṃ, bāhiraṃ parimajjasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§99.</p>

```
Ehi godha nivattassu, bhuñja sālīnamodanaṃ;
```

```
Telaṃ loṇañca me atthi, pahūtaṃ mayha pipphali.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§100.</p>

```
Esa bhiyyo pavekkhāmi, vammikaṃ sataporisaṃ;
```

```
Telaṃ loṇañca kittesi <note>kintesi (syā. pī.)</note>, ahitaṃ mayha pipphalīti.
```

Godharājajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 326. Kakkārujātakaṃ (4-3-6)

<p rend="hangnum">§101.</p>

```
Kāyena yo nāvahare, vācāya na musā bhaṇe;
```

```
Yaso laddhā na majjeyya, sa ve kakkārumarahati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§102.</p>

```
Dhammena vittameseyya, na nikatyā dhanaṃ hare;
```

```
Bhoge laddhā na majjeyya, sa ve kakkārumarahati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§103.</p>

```
Yassa cittaṃ ahāliddaṃ, saddhā ca avirāginī;
```

```
Eko sāduṃ na bhuñjeyya, sa ve kakkārumarahati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§104.</p>

```
Sammukhā vā tirokkhā vā <note>parokkhā vā (pī.), parammukhā (ka.)</note>, yo sante na paribhāsati;
```

```
Yathāvādī <pb ed="T" n="1.0146" /> tathākārī, sa ve kakkārumarahatīti.
```

Kakkārujātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 327. Kākavatījātakaṃ (4-3-7)

<p rend="hangnum">§105.</p>

```
Vāti <pb ed="V" n="1.0092" /> cāyaṃ <note>vāyaṃ (ka.)</note> tato gandho, yattha me vasatī piyā;
```

```
Dūre ito hi kākavatī <note>kākātī (sī.), kākāti (syā. pī.)</note>, yattha me nirato mano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§106.</p>

```
Kathaṃ samuddamatarī, kathaṃ atari kepukaṃ <note>kebukaṃ (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Kathaṃ satta samuddāni, kathaṃ simbalimāruhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§107.</p>

```
Tayā samuddamatariṃ, tayā atari kepukaṃ <note>kebukaṃ (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Tayā satta samuddāni, tayā simbalimāruhiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§108.</p>

```
Dhiratthumaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0107" /> mahākāyaṃ, dhiratthumaṃ acetanaṃ;
```

```
Yattha jāyāyahaṃ jāraṃ, āvahāmi vahāmi cāti.
```

Kākavatījātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 328. Ananusociyajātakaṃ (4-3-8)

<p rend="hangnum">§109.</p>

```
Bahūnaṃ vijjatī bhotī, tehi me kiṃ bhavissati;
```

```
Tasmā etaṃ na socāmi, piyaṃ sammillahāsiniṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§110.</p>

```
Taṃ taṃ ce anusoceyya, yaṃ yaṃ tassa na vijjati;
```

```
Attānamanusoceyya, sadā maccuvasaṃ pataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§111.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="T" n="1.0147" /> heva ṭhitaṃ nāsīnaṃ, na sayānaṃ na paddhaguṃ <note>patthaguṃ (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Yāva byāti nimisati, tatrāpi rasatī <note>saratī (sī. syā. pī.)</note> vayo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§112.</p>

```
Tatthattani vatappaddhe <note>vata panthe (syā.), vata bandhe (ka.) vata + pa-addhe = vatappaddhe</note>, vinābhāve asaṃsaye;
```

```
Bhūtaṃ sesaṃ dayitabbaṃ, vītaṃ ananusociyanti <note>cavitaṃ nānusociyanti (syā.), matantaṃ nānusociyaṃ (ka.)</note>.
```

Ananusociyajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 329. Kāḷabāhujātakaṃ (4-3-9)

<p rend="hangnum">§113.</p>

```
Yaṃ annapānassa pure labhāma, taṃ dāni sākhamigameva gacchati;
```

```
Gacchāma dāni vanameva rādha, asakkatā casma dhanañjayāya <note>dhanañcayāya (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§114.</p>

```
Lābho alābho yaso ayaso ca, nindā pasaṃsā ca sukhañca dukkhaṃ;
```

```
Ete aniccā manujesu dhammā, mā soci kiṃ socasi poṭṭhapāda.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§115.</p>

```
Addhā <pb ed="M" n="1.0108" /> tuvaṃ paṇḍitakosi rādha, jānāsi atthāni anāgatāni;
```

```
Kathaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0148" /> nu sākhāmigaṃ dakkhisāma <note>dakkhiyāma (ka.), dakkhāma (syā.)</note>, niddhāvitaṃ <note>niddhāpitaṃ (sī. syā.), nibbāpitaṃ (pī.), nicchadaṃ (ka.)</note> rājakulatova jammaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§116.</p>

```
Cāleti <pb ed="V" n="1.0093" /> kaṇṇaṃ bhakuṭiṃ karoti, muhuṃ muhuṃ bhāyayate <note>bhāyate (syā.), bhāyāpate (ka.)</note> kumāre;
```

```
Sayameva taṃ kāhati kāḷabāhu, yenārakā ṭhassati annapānāti.
```

Kāḷabāhujātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 330. Sīlavīmaṃsajātakaṃ (4-3-10)

<p rend="hangnum">§117.</p>

```
Sīlaṃ kireva kalyāṇaṃ, sīlaṃ loke anuttaraṃ;
```

```
Passa ghoraviso nāgo, sīlavāti na haññati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§118.</p>

```
Yāvadevassahū kiñci, tāvadeva akhādisuṃ;
```

```
Saṅgamma kulalā loke, na hiṃsanti akiñcanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§119.</p>

```
Sukhaṃ nirāsā supati, āsā phalavatī sukhā;
```

```
Āsaṃ nirāsaṃ katvāna, sukhaṃ supati piṅgalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§120.</p>

```
Na samādhiparo atthi, asmiṃ loke paramhi ca;
```

```
Na paraṃ nāpi attānaṃ, vihiṃsati samāhitoti.
```

Sīlavīmaṃsajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Kuṭidūsakavaggo tatiyo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Samanussa <pb ed="T" n="1.0149" /> -saduddubha-yācanako, atha meṇḍavaruttama-godhavaro;
```

```
Atha kāyasakepuka bhotīvaro, atha rādhasusīlavarena dasāti.
```

#### 4. Kokilavaggo

#### 331. Kokilajātakaṃ (4-4-1)

<p rend="hangnum">§121.</p>

```
Yo <pb ed="M" n="1.0109" /> ve kāle asampatte, ativelaṃ pabhāsati;
```

```
Evaṃ so nihato seti, kokilāyiva atrajo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§122.</p>

```
Na hi satthaṃ sunisitaṃ, visaṃ halāhalāmiva <note>halāhalaṃ iva (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Evaṃ nikaṭṭhe <note>nikkaḍḍhe (syā.), nikaḍḍhe (ka.)</note> pāteti, vācā dubbhāsitā yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§123.</p>

```
Tasmā kāle akāle vā <note>akāle ca (sī. syā.)</note>, vācaṃ rakkheyya paṇḍito;
```

```
Nātivelaṃ pabhāseyya, api attasamamhi vā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§124.</p>

```
Yo <pb ed="V" n="1.0094" /> ca kāle mitaṃ bhāse, matipubbo vicakkhaṇo;
```

```
Sabbe amitte ādeti, supaṇṇo uragāmivāti.
```

Kokilajātakaṃ <note>kokālikajātakaṃ (sabbattha)</note> paṭhamaṃ.

#### 332. Rathalaṭṭhijātakaṃ (4-4-2)

<p rend="hangnum">§125.</p>

```
Api hantvā hato brūti, jetvā jitoti bhāsati;
```

```
Pubbavakkhāyino <pb ed="T" n="1.0150" /> <note>pubbamakkhāyino (sī. syā.)</note> rāja, aññadatthu <note>ekadatthu (sī. pī.)</note> na saddahe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§126.</p>

```
Tasmā paṇḍitajātiyo, suṇeyya itarassapi;
```

```
Ubhinnaṃ vacanaṃ sutvā, yathā dhammo tathā kare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§127.</p>

```
Alaso gihī kāmabhogī na sādhu, asaññato pabbajito na sādhu;
```

```
Rājā na sādhu anisammakārī, yo paṇḍito kodhano taṃ na sādhu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§128.</p>

```
Nisamma khattiyo kayirā, nānisamma disampati;
```

```
Nisammakārino rāja <note>rañño (sī. syā.)</note>, yaso kitti ca vaḍḍhatīti.
```

Rathalaṭṭhijātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 333. Pakkagodhajātakaṃ (4-4-3)

<p rend="hangnum">§129.</p>

```
Tadeva <pb ed="M" n="1.0110" /> me tvaṃ vidito, vanamajjhe rathesabha;
```

```
Yassa te khaggabaddhassa, sannaddhassa tirīṭino;
```

```
Assatthadumasākhāya, pakkā godhā palāyatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§130.</p>

```
Name namantassa bhaje bhajantaṃ, kiccānukubbassa kareyya kiccaṃ;
```

```
Nānatthakāmassa kareyya atthaṃ, asambhajantampi na sambhajeyya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§131.</p>

```
Caje <pb ed="T" n="1.0151" /> cajantaṃ vanathaṃ na kayirā, apetacittena na sambhajeyya;
```

```
Dijo dumaṃ khīṇaphalanti <note>phalaṃva (ka. sī. syā. ka.), dukanipāte puṭabhattajātakena saṃsandetabbaṃ</note> ñatvā, aññaṃ samekkheyya mahā hi loko.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§132.</p>

```
So te karissāmi yathānubhāvaṃ, kataññutaṃ khattiye <note>khattiyo (syā. ka.)</note> pekkhamāno;
```

```
Sabbañca te issariyaṃ dadāmi, yassicchasī tassa tuvaṃ dadāmīti.
```

Pakkagodhajātakaṃ <note>godhajātakaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> tatiyaṃ.

#### 334. Rājovādajātakaṃ (4-4-4)

<p rend="hangnum">§133.</p>

```
Gavaṃ ce taramānānaṃ, jimhaṃ gacchati puṅgavo;
```

```
Sabbā tā jimhaṃ gacchanti <note>sabbā gāvī jimhaṃ yanti (sī. syā.)</note>, nette jimhaṃ gate sati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§134.</p>

```
Evameva <pb ed="V" n="1.0095" /> manussesu, yo hoti seṭṭhasammato;
```

```
So ce adhammaṃ carati, pageva itarā pajā;
```

```
Sabbaṃ raṭṭhaṃ dukhaṃ seti, rājā ce hoti adhammiko.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§135.</p>

```
Gavaṃ ce taramānānaṃ, ujuṃ gacchati puṅgavo;
```

```
Sabbā gāvī ujuṃ yanti <note>sabbā tā ujuṃ gacchanti (pī. a. ni. 4.70)</note>, nette ujuṃ gate sati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§136.</p>

```
Evameva <pb ed="M" n="1.0111" /> manussesu, yo hoti seṭṭhasammato;
```

```
So sace dhammaṃ carati, pageva itarā pajā;
```

```
Sabbaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0152" /> raṭṭhaṃ sukhaṃ seti, rājā ce hoti dhammikoti.
```

Rājovādajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 335. Jambukajātakaṃ (4-4-5)

<p rend="hangnum">§137.</p>

```
Brahā pavaḍḍhakāyo so, dīghadāṭho ca jambuka;
```

```
Na tvaṃ tattha kule jāto, yattha gaṇhanti kuñjaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§138.</p>

```
Asīho sīhamānena, yo attānaṃ vikubbati;
```

```
Kotthūva <note>kuṭṭhūva (sī.), kutthuva (syā. pī)</note> gajamāsajja, seti bhūmyā anutthunaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§139.</p>

```
Yasassino uttamapuggalassa, sañjātakhandhassa mahabbalassa;
```

```
Asamekkhiya thāmabalūpapattiṃ, sa seti nāgena hatoyaṃ jambuko.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§140.</p>

```
Yo cīdha kammaṃ kurute pamāya, thāmabbalaṃ attani saṃviditvā;
```

```
Jappena mantena subhāsitena, parikkhavā so vipulaṃ jinātīti.
```

Jambukajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 336. Brahāchattajātakaṃ (4-4-6)

<p rend="hangnum">§141.</p>

```
Tiṇaṃ tiṇanti lapasi, ko nu te tiṇamāhari;
```

```
Kiṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0153" /> nu te tiṇakiccatthi, tiṇameva pabhāsasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§142.</p>

```
Idhāgamā brahmacārī, brahā chatto bahussuto;
```

```
So me <note>so ve (ka.)</note> sabbaṃ samādāya, tiṇaṃ nikkhippa gacchati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§143.</p>

```
Evetaṃ hoti kattabbaṃ, appena bahumicchatā;
```

```
Sabbaṃ sakassa ādānaṃ, anādānaṃ tiṇassa ca. ( ) <note>(tiṇassa cāṭīsu gato, tattha kā paridevanā) (sī. syā.) (cāṭīsu pakkhipitvāna, tattha kā paridevanā) (ka.)</note>
```

<p rend="hangnum">§144.</p>

```
Sīlavanto <pb ed="V" n="1.0096" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0112" /> na kubbanti, bālo sīlāni kubbati;
```

```
Aniccasīlaṃ dussīlyaṃ <note>dussīlaṃ (pī.)</note>, kiṃ paṇḍiccaṃ karissatīti.
```

Brahāchattajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 337. Pīṭhajātakaṃ (4-4-7)

<p rend="hangnum">§145.</p>

```
Na te pīṭhamadāyimhā <note>madāsimha (pī. ka.)</note>, na pānaṃ napi bhojanaṃ;
```

```
Brahmacāri khamassu me, etaṃ passāmi accayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§146.</p>

```
Nevābhisajjāmi na cāpi kuppe, na cāpi me appiyamāsi kiñci;
```

```
Athopi me āsi manovitakko, etādiso nūna kulassa dhammo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§147.</p>

```
Esasmākaṃ kule dhammo, pitupitāmaho sadā;
```

```
Āsanaṃ udakaṃ pajjaṃ, sabbetaṃ nipadāmase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§148.</p>

```
Esasmākaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0154" /> kule dhammo, pitupitāmaho sadā;
```

```
Sakkaccaṃ upatiṭṭhāma, uttamaṃ viya ñātakanti.
```

Pīṭhajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 338. Thusajātakaṃ (4-4-8)

<p rend="hangnum">§149.</p>

```
Viditaṃ thusaṃ undurānaṃ <note>undūrānaṃ (ka.)</note>, viditaṃ pana taṇḍulaṃ;
```

```
Thusaṃ thusaṃ <note>thusaṃ thūlaṃ (sī.)</note> vivajjetvā, taṇḍulaṃ pana khādare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§150.</p>

```
Yā mantanā araññasmiṃ, yā ca gāme nikaṇṇikā;
```

```
Yañcetaṃ iti cīti ca, etampi viditaṃ mayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§151.</p>

```
Dhammena kira jātassa, pitā puttassa makkaṭo;
```

```
Daharasseva santassa, dantehi phalamacchidā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§152.</p>

```
Yametaṃ parisappasi <note>parisabbesi (ka.)</note>, ajakāṇova sāsape;
```

```
Yopāyaṃ heṭṭhato seti <note>sesi (sī.)</note>, etampi viditaṃ mayāti.
```

Thusajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 339. Bāverujātakaṃ (4-4-9)

<p rend="hangnum">§153.</p>

```
Adassanena <pb ed="M" n="1.0113" /> morassa, sikhino mañjubhāṇino;
```

```
Kākaṃ tattha apūjesuṃ, maṃsena ca phalena ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§154.</p>

```
Yadā <pb ed="V" n="1.0097" /> ca sarasampanno, moro bāverumāgamā;
```

```
Atha <pb ed="T" n="1.0155" /> lābho ca sakkāro, vāyasassa ahāyatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§155.</p>

```
Yāva nuppajjatī buddho, dhammarājā pabhaṅkaro;
```

```
Tāva aññe apūjesuṃ, puthū samaṇabrāhmaṇe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§156.</p>

```
Yadā ca sarasampanno, buddho dhammaṃ adesayi;
```

```
Atha lābho ca sakkāro, titthiyānaṃ ahāyathāti.
```

Bāverujātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 340. Visayhajātakaṃ (4-4-10)

<p rend="hangnum">§157.</p>

```
Adāsi dānāni pure visayha, dadato ca te khayadhammo ahosi;
```

```
Ito paraṃ ce na dadeyya dānaṃ, tiṭṭheyyuṃ te saṃyamantassa bhogā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§158.</p>

```
Anariyamariyena sahassanetta, suduggatenāpi akiccamāhu;
```

```
Mā vo dhanaṃ taṃ ahu devarāja <note>ahuvā janinda (ka. sī. syā. pī.)</note>, yaṃ bhogahetu vijahemu saddhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§159.</p>

```
Yena eko ratho yāti, yāti tenāparo ratho;
```

```
Porāṇaṃ nihitaṃ vattaṃ, vattataññeva <note>vaddhaṃ, vaddhataññeva (ka. sī. pī.)</note> vāsava.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§160.</p>

```
Yadi <pb ed="T" n="1.0156" /> hessati dassāma, asante kiṃ dadāmase;
```

```
Evaṃbhūtāpi dassāma, mā dānaṃ pamadamhaseti.
```

Visayhajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Kokilavaggo <note>kokālikavaggo (ka.)</note> catuttho.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Ativelapabhāsati <pb ed="M" n="1.0114" /> jītavaro, vanamajjha rathesabha jimhagamo;
```

```
Atha jambu tiṇāsanapīṭhavaraṃ, atha taṇḍula mora visayha dasāti.
```

#### 5. Cūḷakuṇālavaggo

#### 341. Kaṇḍarījātakaṃ (4-5-1)

<p rend="hangnum">§161.</p>

```
Narānamārāmakarāsu nārisu, anekacittāsu aniggahāsu ca;
```

```
Sabbattha nāpītikarāpi <note>sabba’ttanā’pītikarāpi (sī. syā.)</note> ce siyā <note>siyuṃ (syā.)</note>, na vissase titthasamā hi nāriyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§162.</p>

```
Yaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0098" /> ve <note>yañca (syā. ka.)</note> disvā kaṇḍarīkinnarānaṃ <note>kinnarakinnarīnaṃ (syā.), kinnarīkinnarānaṃ (ka.)</note>, sabbitthiyo na ramanti agāre;
```

```
Taṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0157" /> tādisaṃ maccaṃ cajitvā bhariyā, aññaṃ disvā purisaṃ pīṭhasappiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§163.</p>

```
Bakassa ca bāvarikassa <note>pāvārikassa (sī.)</note> rañño, accantakāmānugatassa bhariyā;
```

```
Avācarī <note>accācari (syā.), anācari (ka.)</note> paṭṭhavasānugassa <note>baddhavasānugassa (sī. syā.), pattavasānugatassa (ka.)</note>, kaṃ vāpi itthī nāticare tadaññaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§164.</p>

```
Piṅgiyānī sabbalokissarassa, rañño piyā brahmadattassa bhariyā;
```

```
Avācarī paṭṭhavasānugassa, taṃ vāpi sā nājjhagā kāmakāminīti.
```

Kaṇḍarījātakaṃ <note>kinnarījātakaṃ (ka. sī. ka.), kuṇḍalikajātakaṃ (syā.)</note> paṭhamaṃ.

#### 342. Vānarajātakaṃ (4-5-2)

<p rend="hangnum">§165.</p>

```
Asakkhiṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0115" /> vata attānaṃ, uddhātuṃ udakā thalaṃ;
```

```
Na dānāhaṃ puna tuyhaṃ, vasaṃ gacchāmi vārija.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§166.</p>

```
Alametehi ambehi, jambūhi panasehi ca;
```

```
Yāni pāraṃ samuddassa, varaṃ mayhaṃ udumbaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§167.</p>

```
Yo ca uppatitaṃ atthaṃ, na khippamanubujjhati;
```

```
Amittavasamanveti<pb ed="T" n="1.0158" />, pacchā ca anutappati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§168.</p>

```
Yo ca uppatitaṃ atthaṃ, khippameva nibodhati;
```

```
Muccate sattusambādhā, na ca pacchānutappatīti.
```

Vānarajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 343. Kuntinījātakaṃ (4-5-3)

<p rend="hangnum">§169.</p>

```
Avasimha tavāgāre, niccaṃ sakkatapūjitā;
```

```
Tvameva dānimakari, handa rāja vajāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§170.</p>

```
Yo ve kate paṭikate, kibbise paṭikibbise;
```

```
Evaṃ taṃ sammatī veraṃ, vasa kuntini māgamā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§171.</p>

```
Na katassa ca kattā ca, metti <note>mettī (pī.), mittī (ka.)</note> sandhīyate puna;
```

```
Hadayaṃ nānujānāti, gacchaññeva rathesabha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§172.</p>

```
Katassa ceva kattā ca, metti sandhīyate puna;
```

```
Dhīrānaṃ no ca bālānaṃ, vasa kuntini māgamāti.
```

Kuntinījātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 344. Ambajātakaṃ (4-5-4)

<p rend="hangnum">§173.</p>

```
Yo <pb ed="V" n="1.0099" /> nīliyaṃ maṇḍayati, saṇḍāsena vihaññati;
```

```
Tassa sā vasamanvetu, yā te ambe avāhari.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§174.</p>

```
Vīsaṃ vā pañcavīsaṃ <note>paṇṇuvīsaṃ (ka. sī. pī.)</note> vā, ūnatiṃsaṃ va jātiyā;
```

```
Tādisā <pb ed="T" n="1.0159" /> pati mā laddhā <note>patiṃ mā laddhā (pī.), pati mā’lattha (?)</note>, yā te ambe avāhari.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§175.</p>

```
Dīghaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0116" /> gacchatu addhānaṃ, ekikā abhisārikā;
```

```
Saṅkete pati mā adda <note>mā addasa (sī. pī.)</note>, yā te ambe avāhari.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§176.</p>

```
Alaṅkatā suvasanā, mālinī candanussadā;
```

```
Ekikā sayane setu, yā te ambe avāharīti.
```

Ambajātakaṃ <note>ambacorajātakaṃ (ka. sī. pī.)</note> catutthaṃ.

#### 345. Gajakumbhajātakaṃ (4-5-5)

<p rend="hangnum">§177.</p>

```
Vanaṃ yadaggi dahati, pāvako kaṇhavattanī;
```

```
Kathaṃ karosi pacalaka, evaṃ dandhaparakkamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§178.</p>

```
Bahūni rukkhachiddāni, pathabyā vivarāni ca;
```

```
Tāni ce nābhisambhoma, hoti no kālapariyāyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§179.</p>

```
Yo dandhakāle tarati, taraṇīye ca dandhati;
```

```
Sukkhapaṇṇaṃva akkamma, atthaṃ bhañjati attano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§180.</p>

```
Yo dandhakāle dandheti, taraṇīye ca tārayi;
```

```
Sasīva rattiṃ vibhajaṃ, tassattho paripūratīti.
```

Gajakumbhajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 346. Kesavajātakaṃ (4-5-6)

<p rend="hangnum">§181.</p>

```
Manussindaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0160" /> jahitvāna, sabbakāmasamiddhinaṃ;
```

```
Kathaṃ nu bhagavā kesī, kappassa ramati assame <note>ramatassame (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§182.</p>

```
Sādūnī <note>sādhūni (ka. sī. syā. ka.)</note> ramaṇīyāni, santi vakkhā manoramā;
```

```
Subhāsitāni kappassa, nārada ramayanti maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§183.</p>

```
Sālīnaṃ odanaṃ bhuñje, suciṃ maṃsūpasecanaṃ;
```

```
Kathaṃ sāmākanīvāraṃ, aloṇaṃ chādayanti taṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§184.</p>

```
Sāduṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0100" /> vā <note>asāduṃ (pī.)</note> yadi vāsāduṃ, appaṃ vā yadi vā bahuṃ;
```

```
Vissattho yattha bhuñjeyya, vissāsaparamā rasāti.
```

Kesavajātakaṃ <note>kesījātakaṃ (ka.)</note> chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 347. Ayakūṭajātakaṃ (4-5-7)

<p rend="hangnum">§185.</p>

```
Sabbāyasaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0117" /> kūṭamatippamāṇaṃ, paggayha yo <note>so (pī.)</note> tiṭṭhasi antalikkhe;
```

```
Rakkhāya me <note>maṃ (sī.)</note> tvaṃ vihito nusajja, udāhu me cetayase <note>vāyamase (sī. syā.)</note> vadhāya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§186.</p>

```
Dūto ahaṃ rājidha rakkhasānaṃ, vadhāya tuyhaṃ pahitohamasmi;
```

```
Indo <pb ed="T" n="1.0161" /> ca taṃ rakkhati devarājā, tenuttamaṅgaṃ na te <note>na hi (ka. sī. pī.), te na (ka.)</note> phālayāmi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§187.</p>

```
Sace ca maṃ rakkhati devarājā, devānamindo maghavā sujampati;
```

```
Kāmaṃ pisācā vinadantu sabbe, na santase rakkhasiyā pajāya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§188.</p>

```
