Kāmaṃ kandantu <note>kantantu (ka.), kaṇḍantu (syā.)</note> kumbhaṇḍā, sabbe paṃsupisācakā;
```

```
Nālaṃ pisācā yuddhāya, mahatī sā vibhiṃsikāti <note>vibhesikāti (syā.), vihesikāti (pī.)</note>.
```

Ayakūṭajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 348. Araññajātakaṃ (4-5-8)

<p rend="hangnum">§189.</p>

```
Araññā gāmamāgamma, kiṃsīlaṃ kiṃvataṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Purisaṃ tāta seveyyaṃ, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§190.</p>

```
Yo taṃ vissāsaye tāta, vissāsañca khameyya te;
```

```
Sussūsī ca titikkhī ca, taṃ bhajehi ito <note>taṃ bhajeyyāsito (ka.)</note> gato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§191.</p>

```
Yassa kāyena vācāya, manasā natthi dukkaṭaṃ;
```

```
Urasīva patiṭṭhāya, taṃ bhajehi ito gato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§192.</p>

```
Haliddirāgaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0118" /> kapicittaṃ, purisaṃ rāgavirāginaṃ;
```

```
Tādisaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0162" /> tāta mā sevi, nimmanussampi ce siyāti.
```

Araññajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 349. Sandhibhedajātakaṃ (4-5-9)

<p rend="hangnum">§193.</p>

```
Neva itthīsu sāmaññaṃ, nāpi bhakkhesu sārathi;
```

```
Athassa sandhibhedassa, passa yāva sucintitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§194.</p>

```
Asi <pb ed="V" n="1.0101" /> tikkhova maṃsamhi, pesuññaṃ parivattati;
```

```
Yatthūsabhañca sīhañca, bhakkhayanti migādhamā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§195.</p>

```
Imaṃ so sayanaṃ seti, yamimaṃ <note>yayimaṃ (sī. pī.), yimaṃ (ka.)</note> passasi sārathi;
```

```
Yo vācaṃ sandhibhedassa, pisuṇassa nibodhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§196.</p>

```
Te janā sukhamedhanti, narā saggagatāriva;
```

```
Ye vācaṃ sandhibhedassa, nāvabodhanti sārathīti.
```

Sandhibhedajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 350. Devatāpañhajātakaṃ (4-5-10)

<p rend="hangnum">§197.</p>

```
Hanti hatthehi pādehi, mukhañca parisumbhati;
```

```
Sa ve rāja piyo hoti, kaṃ tena tvābhipassasi <note>mabhipassasi (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§198.</p>

```
Akkosati yathākāmaṃ, āgamañcassa icchati;
```

```
Sa <pb ed="T" n="1.0163" /> ve rāja piyo hoti, kaṃ tena tvābhipassasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§199.</p>

```
Abbhakkhāti abhūtena, alikenābhisāraye;
```

```
Sa ve rāja piyo hoti, kaṃ tena tvābhipassasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§200.</p>

```
Haraṃ annañca pānañca, vatthasenāsanāni ca;
```

```
Aññadatthuharā santā, te ve rāja piyā honti;
```

```
Kaṃ tena tvābhipassasīti.
```

Devatāpañhajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Cūḷakuṇālavaggo pañcamo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Narānaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0119" /> asakkhivasimhavaro, nīliyamaggivarañca puna;
```

```
Puna rasāyasakūṭavaro, tathārañña sārathi hanti dasāti.
```

Atha vagguddānaṃ –

```
Kāliṅgaṃ <note>vivaraṃ (bahūsu)</note> pucimandañca, kuṭidūsaka kokilā <note>kuṭidūsaṃ bahubhāṇakaṃ (bahūsu)</note>;
```

```
Cūḷakuṇālavaggo so, pañcamo suppakāsitoti.
```

<trailer rend="centre">Catukkanipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.</trailer>

### 5. Pañcakanipāto

#### 1. Maṇikuṇḍalavaggo

#### 351. Maṇikuṇḍalajātakaṃ (5-1-1)

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
Jīno <pb ed="T" n="1.0164" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0102" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0120" /> rathassaṃ maṇikuṇḍale ca, putte ca dāre ca tatheva jīno;
```

```
Sabbesu bhogesu asesakesu <note>asesitesu (sī. pī.), asesikesu (ka.)</note>, kasmā na santappasi sokakāle.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
Pubbeva maccaṃ vijahanti bhogā, macco vā te <note>ca ne (pī.), dhane (ka.)</note> pubbataraṃ jahāti;
```

```
Asassatā bhogino kāmakāmi, tasmā na socāmahaṃ sokakāle.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
Udeti āpūrati veti <note>pūreti khīyati (syā.)</note> cando, atthaṃ tapetvāna <note>andhaṃ tapetvāna (ka.), atthaṅgametvāna (syā.), ettha ‘‘tapetvāna atthaṃ paletī’’ti sambandho</note> paleti sūriyo;
```

```
Viditā <note>vijitā (syā.)</note> mayā sattuka lokadhammā, tasmā na socāmahaṃ sokakāle.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
Alaso gihī kāmabhogī na sādhu, asaññato <pb ed="T" n="1.0165" /> pabbajito na sādhu;
```

```
Rājā na sādhu anisammakārī, yo paṇḍito kodhano taṃ na sādhu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
Nisamma khattiyo kayirā, nānisamma disampati;
```

```
Nisammakārino rāja <note>rañño (sī. syā.)</note>, yaso kitti ca vaḍḍhatīti.
```

Maṇikuṇḍalajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 352. Sujātajātakaṃ (5-1-2)

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
Kiṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0121" /> nu santaramānova, lāyitvā haritaṃ tiṇaṃ;
```

```
Khāda khādāti lapasi, gatasattaṃ jaraggavaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
Na hi annena pānena, mato goṇo samuṭṭhahe;
```

```
Tvañca tucchaṃ vilapasi, yathā taṃ dummatī tathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
Tatheva tiṭṭhati sīsaṃ, hatthapādā ca vāladhi;
```

```
Sotā tatheva tiṭṭhanti <note>so tāta tatheva tiṭṭhati (ka.)</note>, maññe goṇo samuṭṭhahe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
Nevayyakassa sīsañca <note>sīsaṃ vā (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, hatthapādā ca dissare;
```

```
Rudaṃ mattikathūpasmiṃ, nanu tvaññeva dummati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
Ādittaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0103" /> vata maṃ santaṃ, ghatasittaṃva pāvakaṃ;
```

```
Vārinā viya osiñcaṃ <note>osiñci (ka.)</note>, sabbaṃ nibbāpaye daraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
Abbahī <note>abbūḷhaṃ (sī. syā.), abbhūḷhaṃ (ka.)</note> vata me sallaṃ, yamāsi hadayassitaṃ <note>sokaṃ hadayanissitaṃ (sī. syā.)</note>;
```

```
Yo <pb ed="T" n="1.0166" /> me sokaparetassa, pitu sokaṃ apānudi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
Sohaṃ abbūḷhasallosmi, vītasoko anāvilo;
```

```
Na socāmi na rodāmi, tava sutvāna māṇava.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
Evaṃ karonti sappaññā, ye honti anukampakā;
```

```
Vinivattenti sokamhā, sujāto pitaraṃ yathāti.
```

Sujātajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 353. Venasākhajātakaṃ (5-1-3)

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
Nayidaṃ niccaṃ bhavitabbaṃ brahmadatta, khemaṃ subhikkhaṃ sukhatā ca kāye;
```

```
Atthaccaye mā ahu sampamūḷho, bhinnaplavo sāgarasseva majjhe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
Yāni <pb ed="M" n="1.0122" /> karoti puriso, tāni attani passati;
```

```
Kalyāṇakārī kalyāṇaṃ, pāpakārī ca pāpakaṃ;
```

```
Yādisaṃ vapate bījaṃ, tādisaṃ harate phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
Idaṃ tadācariyavaco, pārāsariyo yadabravi;
```

```
Mā su <note>mā ssu (sī. syā. pī.)</note> tvaṃ akari pāpaṃ, yaṃ tvaṃ pacchā kataṃ tape.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
Ayameva so piṅgiya <note>so piṅgiyo (syā.), sopi bhiyyo (ka.)</note> venasākho, <note>dhonasākho (ka. sī. pī.)</note> yamhi <pb ed="T" n="1.0167" /> ghātayiṃ khattiyānaṃ sahassaṃ;
```

```
Alaṅkate candanasārānulitte, tameva dukkhaṃ paccāgataṃ mamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
Sāmā ca <note>sāmāpi (sī. syā.)</note> kho candanalittagattā <note>gattī (ka. sī. syā. pī.)</note>, laṭṭhīva sobhañjanakassa uggatā;
```

```
Adisvā <note>adisvāva (sī.)</note> kālaṃ karissāmi ubbariṃ, taṃ me ito dukkhataraṃ bhavissatīti.
```

Venasākhajātakaṃ <note>dhonasākhajātakaṃ (ka. sī. pī.)</note> tatiyaṃ.

#### 354. Uragajātakaṃ (5-1-4)

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
Uragova tacaṃ jiṇṇaṃ, hitvā gacchati saṃ tanuṃ;
```

```
Evaṃ sarīre nibbhoge, pete kālaṅkate sati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
Ḍayhamāno na jānāti, ñātīnaṃ paridevitaṃ;
```

```
Tasmā etaṃ na socāmi, gato so tassa yā gati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
Anavhito <pb ed="V" n="1.0104" /> tato āgā, ananuññāto <note>nānuññāto (ka.)</note> ito gato;
```

```
Yathāgato tathā gato, tattha kā paridevanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
Ḍayhamāno na jānāti, ñātīnaṃ paridevitaṃ;
```

```
Tasmā etaṃ na socāmi, gato so tassa yā gati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
Sace rode kisā <note>kisī (pī.)</note> assaṃ, tassā me kiṃ phalaṃ siyā;
```

```
Ñātimittasuhajjānaṃ<pb ed="T" n="1.0168" />, bhiyyo no aratī siyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
Ḍayhamāno <pb ed="M" n="1.0123" /> na jānāti, ñātīnaṃ paridevitaṃ;
```

```
Tasmā etaṃ na socāmi, gato so tassa yā gati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
Yathāpi dārako candaṃ, gacchantamanurodati;
```

```
Evaṃ sampadamevetaṃ, yo petamanusocati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
Ḍayhamāno na jānāti, ñātīnaṃ paridevitaṃ;
```

```
Tasmā etaṃ na socāmi, gato so tassa yā gati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
Yathāpi udakakumbho, bhinno appaṭisandhiyo;
```

```
Evaṃ sampadamevetaṃ, yo petamanusocati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
Ḍayhamāno na jānāti, ñātīnaṃ paridevitaṃ;
```

```
Tasmā etaṃ na socāmi, gato so tassa yā gatīti.
```

Uragajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 355. Ghaṭajātakaṃ (5-1-5)

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
Aññe socanti rodanti, aññe assumukhā janā;
```

```
Pasannamukhavaṇṇosi, kasmā ghaṭa <note>ghata (sī. pī.)</note> na socasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
Nābbhatītaharo soko, nānāgatasukhāvaho;
```

```
Tasmā dhaṅka <note>vaṃka (pī.)</note> na socāmi, natthi soke dutīyatā <note>soko dutīyakā (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
Socaṃ paṇḍu kiso hoti, bhattañcassa na ruccati;
```

```
Amittā sumanā honti, sallaviddhassa ruppato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
Gāme <pb ed="T" n="1.0169" /> vā yadi vāraññe, ninne vā yadi vā thale;
```

```
Ṭhitaṃ maṃ nāgamissati, evaṃ diṭṭhapado ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
Yassattā nālamekova, sabbakāmarasāharo;
```

```
Sabbāpi pathavī tassa, na sukhaṃ āvahissatīti.
```

Ghaṭajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 356. Koraṇḍiyajātakaṃ (5-1-6)

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
Eko <pb ed="V" n="1.0105" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0124" /> araññe girikandarāyaṃ, paggayha paggayha silaṃ pavecchasi <note>pavejjhasi (syā. sī. aṭṭha.)</note>;
```

```
Punappunaṃ santaramānarūpo, koraṇḍiya <note>kāraṇḍiya (sī. syā. pī.)</note> ko nu tava yidhattho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
Ahañhimaṃ sāgara sevitantaṃ, samaṃ karissāmi yathāpi pāṇi;
```

```
Vikiriya sānūni ca pabbatāni ca, tasmā silaṃ dariyā pakkhipāmi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
Nayimaṃ mahiṃ arahati pāṇikappaṃ, samaṃ manusso karaṇāya meko;
```

```
Maññāmimaññeva dariṃ jigīsaṃ <note>jigiṃsaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, koraṇḍiya <pb ed="T" n="1.0170" /> hāhasi <note>hāyasi (syā. ka.)</note> jīvalokaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
Sace ahaṃ <note>ayaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> bhūtadharaṃ na sakkā <note>sakko (syā. ka.)</note>, samaṃ manusso karaṇāya meko;
```

```
Evameva tvaṃ brahme ime manusse, nānādiṭṭhike nānayissasi te <note>ne (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
Saṅkhittarūpena bhavaṃ mamatthaṃ, akkhāsi koraṇḍiya evametaṃ;
```

```
Yathā na sakkā pathavī samāyaṃ, kattuṃ manussena tathā manussāti.
```

Koraṇḍiyajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 357. Laṭukikajātakaṃ (5-1-7)

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
Vandāmi taṃ kuñjara saṭṭhihāyanaṃ, āraññakaṃ yūthapatiṃ yasassiṃ;
```

```
Pakkhehi taṃ pañjalikaṃ karomi, mā me vadhī puttake dubbalāya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
Vandāmi <pb ed="M" n="1.0125" /> taṃ kuñjara ekacāriṃ, āraññakaṃ pabbatasānugocaraṃ;
```

```
Pakkhehi taṃ pañjalikaṃ karomi, mā <pb ed="T" n="1.0171" /> me vadhī puttake dubbalāya;
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
Vamissāmi te laṭukike puttakāni, kiṃ me tuvaṃ kāhasi dubbalāsi;
```

```
Sataṃ sahassānipi tādisīnaṃ, vāmena pādena papothayeyyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
Na heva sabbattha balena kiccaṃ, balañhi bālassa vadhāya hoti;
```

```
Karissāmi te nāgarājā anatthaṃ, yo me vadhī puttake dubbalāya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
Kākañca passa laṭukikaṃ, maṇḍūkaṃ nīlamakkhikaṃ;
```

```
Ete nāgaṃ aghātesuṃ, passa verassa verinaṃ;
```

```
Tasmā hi veraṃ na kayirātha, appiyenapi kenacīti.
```

Laṭukikajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 358. Cūḷadhammapālajātakaṃ (5-1-8)

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
Ahameva <pb ed="V" n="1.0106" /> dūsiyā bhūnahatā, rañño mahāpatāpassa;
```

```
Etaṃ muñcatu dhammapālaṃ, hatthe me deva chedehi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
Ahameva dūsiyā bhūnahatā, rañño mahāpatāpassa;
```

```
Etaṃ muñcatu dhammapālaṃ, pāde me deva chedehi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
Ahameva dūsiyā bhūnahatā, rañño mahāpatāpassa;
```

```
Etaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0172" /> muñcatu dhammapālaṃ, sīsaṃ me deva chedehi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
Na hi <note>naha (sī. syā. pī.) ettha ha-kāro khede</note> nūnimassa rañño, mittāmaccā ca vijjare suhadā;
```

```
Ye na vadanti rājānaṃ, mā ghātayi orasaṃ puttaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
Na hi <note>naha (sī. syā. pī.) ettha ha-kāro khede</note> nūnimassa rañño, ñātī mittā ca vijjare suhadā;
```

```
Ye na vadanti rājānaṃ, mā ghātayi atrajaṃ puttaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
Candanasārānulittā<pb ed="M" n="1.0126" />, bāhā chijjanti dhammapālassa;
```

```
Dāyādassa pathabyā, pāṇā me deva rujjhantīti.
```

Cūḷadhammapālajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 359. Suvaṇṇamigajātakaṃ (5-1-9)

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
Vikkama re haripāda <note>mahāmiga (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, vikkama re mahāmiga <note>harīpada (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Chinda vārattikaṃ pāsaṃ, nāhaṃ ekā vane rame.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
Vikkamāmi na pāremi, bhūmiṃ sumbhāmi vegasā;
```

```
Daḷho vārattiko pāso, pādaṃ me parikantati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
Attharassu palāsāni, asiṃ nibbāha luddaka;
```

```
Paṭhamaṃ maṃ vadhitvāna, hana pacchā mahāmigaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
Na me sutaṃ vā diṭṭhaṃ vā, bhāsantiṃ mānusiṃ migiṃ <note>na me sutā vā diṭṭhā vā, bhāsantī mānusiṃ migī (ṭīkā)</note>;
```

```
Tvañca bhadde sukhī hohi, eso cāpi mahāmigo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
Evaṃ luddaka nandassu, saha sabbehi ñātibhi;
```

```
Yathāhamajja <pb ed="T" n="1.0173" /> nandāmi, muttaṃ disvā mahāmiganti.
```

Suvaṇṇamigajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 360. Suyonandījātakaṃ (5-1-10)

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
Vāti <pb ed="V" n="1.0107" /> gandho timirānaṃ, kusamuddo ca <note>va (syā. pī.)</note> ghosavā;
```

```
Dūre ito suyonandī <note>ito hi susandī (sī. syā.), itopi sussondī (pī.)</note>, tambakāmā tudanti maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
Kathaṃ samuddamatari, kathaṃ addakkhi sedumaṃ <note>serumaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Kathaṃ tassā ca tuyhañca, ahu sagga <note>agga (sī. syā.)</note> samāgamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
Kurukacchā <note>bharukacchā (sī. syā. pī.)</note> payātānaṃ, vāṇijānaṃ dhanesinaṃ;
```

```
Makarehi abhidā <note>makarehibbhidā (sī.), makarehi’bhidā (syā.), makarehi bhinnā (pī.)</note> nāvā, phalakenāhamaplaviṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
Sā <pb ed="M" n="1.0127" /> maṃ saṇhena mudunā, niccaṃ candanagandhinī;
```

```
Aṅgena <note>aṅkena (pī. ka.)</note> uddharī bhaddā, mātā puttaṃva orasaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
Sā maṃ annena pānena, vatthena sayanena ca;
```

```
Attanāpi ca mandakkhī, evaṃ tamba vijānāhīti.
```

Suyonandījātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Maṇikuṇḍalavaggo paṭhamo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Atha jinavaro haritaṃ tiṇako, atha <pb ed="T" n="1.0174" /> bhinnaplavo uragova ghaṭo;
```

```
Dariyā puna kuñjara bhūnahatā, migamuttamasaggavarena dasāti.
```

#### 2. Vaṇṇārohavaggo

#### 361. Vaṇṇārohajātakaṃ (5-2-1)

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
Vaṇṇārohena jātiyā, balanikkamanena ca;
```

```
Subāhu na mayā seyyo, sudāṭha iti bhāsasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
Vaṇṇārohena jātiyā, balanikkamanena ca;
```

```
Sudāṭho na mayā seyyo, subāhu iti bhāsasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
Evaṃ ce maṃ viharantaṃ, subāhu samma dubbhasi;
```

```
Na dānāhaṃ tayā saddhiṃ, saṃvāsamabhirocaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
Yo <pb ed="V" n="1.0108" /> paresaṃ vacanāni, saddaheyya <note>saddahetha (sī. syā. pī.)</note> yathātathaṃ;
```

```
Khippaṃ bhijjetha mittasmiṃ, verañca pasave bahuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="M" n="1.0128" /> so mitto yo sadā appamatto, bhedāsaṅkī randhamevānupassī;
```

```
Yasmiñca setī urasīva putto, sa ve mitto yo abhejjo parehīti.
```

Vaṇṇārohajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 362. Sīlavīmaṃsajātakaṃ (5-2-2)

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
Sīlaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0175" /> seyyo sutaṃ seyyo, iti me saṃsayo ahu;
```

```
Sīlameva sutā seyyo, iti me natthi saṃsayo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
Moghā jāti ca vaṇṇo ca, sīlameva kiruttamaṃ;
```

```
Sīlena anupetassa, sutenattho na vijjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
Khattiyo ca adhammaṭṭho, vesso cādhammanissito;
```

```
Te pariccajjubho loke, upapajjanti duggatiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
Khattiyā brāhmaṇā vessā, suddā caṇḍālapukkusā;
```

```
Idha dhammaṃ caritvāna, bhavanti tidive samā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
Na vedā samparāyāya, na jāti nāpi <note>nopi (pī.)</note> bandhavā;
```

```
Sakañca sīlaṃ saṃsuddhaṃ, samparāyāya sukhāya cāti <note>sukhāvahanti (sī. syā.)</note>.
```

Sīlavīmaṃsajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 363. Hirijātakaṃ (5-2-3)

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
Hiriṃ tarantaṃ vijigucchamānaṃ, tavāhamasmī iti bhāsamānaṃ;
```

```
Seyyāni kammāni anādiyantaṃ, neso mamanti iti naṃ vijaññā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
Yañhi kayirā tañhi vade, yaṃ na kayirā na taṃ vade;
```

```
Akarontaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0176" /> bhāsamānaṃ, parijānanti paṇḍitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="M" n="1.0129" /> so mitto yo sadā appamatto, bhedāsaṅkī randhamevānupassī;
```

```
Yasmiñca setī urasīva putto, sa ve mitto yo abhejjo parehi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
Pāmojjakaraṇaṃ ṭhānaṃ, pasaṃsāvahanaṃ sukhaṃ;
```

```
Phalānisaṃso bhāveti, vahanto porisaṃ dhuraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
Pavivekarasaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0109" /> pitvā, rasaṃ upasamassa ca;
```

```
Niddaro hoti nippāpo, dhammappītirasaṃ pivanti.
```

Hirijātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 364. Khajjopanakajātakaṃ (5-2-4)

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
Ko nu santamhi pajjote, aggipariyesanaṃ caraṃ;
```

```
Addakkhi ratti <note>rattiṃ (syā.)</note> khajjotaṃ, jātavedaṃ amaññatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
Svassa gomayacuṇṇāni, abhimatthaṃ tiṇāni ca;
```

```
Viparītāya saññāya, nāsakkhi pajjaletave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
Evampi anupāyena, atthaṃ na labhate migo <note>mūgo (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Visāṇato gavaṃ dohaṃ, yattha khīraṃ na vindati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
Vividhehi upāyehi, atthaṃ papponti māṇavā;
```

```
Niggahena amittānaṃ, mittānaṃ paggahena ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
Senāmokkhapalābhena <pb ed="T" n="1.0177" /> <note>senī mokkhūpalābhena (syā.)</note>, vallabhānaṃ nayena ca;
```

```
Jagatiṃ jagatipālā, āvasanti vasundharanti.
```

Khajjopanakajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 365. Ahituṇḍikajātakaṃ (5-2-5)

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
Dhuttomhi samma sumukha, jūte akkhaparājito;
```

```
Harehi <note>sevehi (pī.)</note> ambapakkāni, vīriyaṃ te bhakkhayāmase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
Alikaṃ vata maṃ samma, abhūtena pasaṃsasi;
```

```
Ko te suto vā diṭṭho vā, sumukho nāma makkaṭo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
Ajjāpi <pb ed="M" n="1.0130" /> me taṃ manasi <note>te maṃ sarasi (ka.)</note>, yaṃ maṃ tvaṃ ahituṇḍika;
```

```
Dhaññāpaṇaṃ pavisitvā, matto <note>mutto (ka.)</note> chātaṃ hanāsi maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
Tāhaṃ saraṃ dukkhaseyyaṃ, api rajjampi kāraye;
```

```
Nevāhaṃ yācito dajjaṃ, tathā hi bhayatajjito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
Yañca jaññā kule jātaṃ, gabbhe tittaṃ amacchariṃ;
```

```
Tena sakhiñca mittañca, dhīro sandhātumarahatīti.
```

Ahituṇḍikajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 366. Gumbiyajātakaṃ (5-2-6)

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
Madhuvaṇṇaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0110" /> madhurasaṃ, madhugandhaṃ visaṃ ahu;
```

```
Gumbiyo <pb ed="T" n="1.0178" /> ghāsamesāno, araññe odahī visaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
Madhu iti maññamānā <note>madhūti maññamānāya (ka.)</note>, ye taṃ visamakhādisuṃ <note>visamasāyisuṃ (sī. syā.)</note>;
```

```
Tesaṃ taṃ kaṭukaṃ āsi, maraṇaṃ tenupāgamuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
Ye ca kho paṭisaṅkhāya, visaṃ taṃ parivajjayuṃ;
```

```
Te āturesu sukhitā, ḍayhamānesu nibbutā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
Evameva manussesu, visaṃ kāmā samohitā;
```

```
Āmisaṃ bandhanañcetaṃ, maccuveso <note>paccuvaso (sī. syā.)</note> guhāsayo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
Evameva ime kāme, āturā paricārike <note>paricārake (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Ye sadā parivajjenti, saṅgaṃ loke upaccagunti.
```

Gumbiyajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 367. Sāḷiyajātakaṃ (5-2-7)

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
Yvāyaṃ sāḷiya <note>sāliya (sī. syā. pī.), sāḷika (?)</note> chāpoti, kaṇhasappaṃ agāhayi;
```

```
Tena sappenayaṃ daṭṭho, hato pāpānusāsako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
Ahantāra <note>ahananta (pī.), aharanta (?)</note> mahantāraṃ, yo naro hantumicchati;
```

```
Evaṃ so nihato seti, yathāyaṃ puriso hato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
Ahantāra <pb ed="M" n="1.0131" /> <note>ahananta (sī. syā. pī.), aharanta (?)</note> maghātentaṃ, yo naro hantumicchati;
```

```
Evaṃ so nihato seti, yathāyaṃ puriso hato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§93.</p>

```
Yathā paṃsumuṭṭhiṃ puriso, paṭivātaṃ paṭikkhipe;
```

```
Tameva <pb ed="T" n="1.0179" /> so rajo hanti, tathāyaṃ puriso hato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§94.</p>

```
Yo appaduṭṭhassa narassa dussati, suddhassa posassa anaṅgaṇassa;
```

```
Tameva bālaṃ pacceti pāpaṃ, sukhumo rajo paṭivātaṃva khittoti.
```

Sāḷiyajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 368. Tacasārajātakaṃ (5-2-8)

<p rend="hangnum">§95.</p>

```
Amittahatthatthagatā <note>hatthattagatā (katthaci, sī. niyya)</note>, tacasārasamappitā;
```

```
Pasannamukhavaṇṇāttha, kasmā tumhe na socatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§96.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="V" n="1.0111" /> socanāya paridevanāya, atthova labbho <note>attho ca labbhā (sī. syā.), atthodha labbhā (a. ni. 5.48)</note> api appakopi;
```

```
Socantamenaṃ dukhitaṃ viditvā, paccatthikā attamanā bhavanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§97.</p>

```
Yato ca kho paṇḍito āpadāsu, na vedhatī atthavinicchayaññū;
```

```
Paccatthikāssa <note>paccatthikā te (ka.)</note> dukhitā bhavanti, disvā mukhaṃ avikāraṃ purāṇaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§98.</p>

```
Jappena mantena subhāsitena, anuppadānena paveṇiyā vā;
```

```
Yathā <pb ed="T" n="1.0180" /> yathā yattha labhetha atthaṃ, tathā tathā tattha parakkameyya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§99.</p>

```
Yato <pb ed="M" n="1.0132" /> ca jāneyya alabbhaneyyo, mayā va <note>mayā vā (syā. ka.)</note> aññena vā esa attho;
```

```
Asocamāno adhivāsayeyya, kammaṃ daḷhaṃ kinti karomi dānīti.
```

Tacasārajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 369. Mittavindakajātakaṃ (5-2-9)

<p rend="hangnum">§100.</p>

```
Kyāhaṃ devānamakaraṃ, kiṃ pāpaṃ pakataṃ mayā;
```

```
Yaṃ me sirasmiṃ ohacca <note>uhacca (ka.), uhacca (pī.)</note>, cakkaṃ bhamati matthake.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§101.</p>

```
Atikkamma ramaṇakaṃ, sadāmattañca dūbhakaṃ;
```

```
Brahmattarañca pāsādaṃ, kenatthena idhāgato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§102.</p>

```
Ito bahutarā bhogā, atra maññe bhavissare;
```

```
Iti etāya saññāya, passa maṃ byasanaṃ gataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§103.</p>

```
Catubbhi aṭṭhajjhagamā, aṭṭhāhipi ca <note>aṭṭhāhi cāpi (sī. syā.), aṭṭhābhi cāpi (ka.)</note> soḷasa;
```

```
Soḷasāhi ca bāttiṃsa, atricchaṃ cakkamāsado;
```

Icchāhatassa posassa, cakkaṃ bhamati matthake.

<p rend="hangnum">§104.</p>

```
Uparivisālā duppūrā, icchā visaṭagāminī <note>upari visālaṃ duppūraṃ, icchāvisadagāminī (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Ye <pb ed="T" n="1.0181" /> ca taṃ anugijjhanti, te honti cakkadhārinoti.
```

Mittavindakajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 370. Palāsajātakaṃ (5-2-10)

<p rend="hangnum">§105.</p>

```
Haṃso palāsamavaca, nigrodho samma jāyati;
```

```
Aṅkasmiṃ <note>aṅgasmiṃ (ka.)</note> te nisinnova, so te mammāni checchati <note>chijjati (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§106.</p>

```
Vaḍḍhatāmeva <note>vaddhitameva (ka.)</note> nigrodho, patiṭṭhassa bhavāmahaṃ;
```

```
Yathā pitā ca mātā ca <note>pitā vā mātā vā (pī.), mātā vā pitā vā (ka.)</note>, evaṃ me so bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§107.</p>

```
Yaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0112" /> tvaṃ aṅkasmiṃ vaḍḍhesi, khīrarukkhaṃ bhayānakaṃ;
```

```
Āmanta kho taṃ gacchāma, vuḍḍhi massa na ruccati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§108.</p>

```
Idāni <pb ed="M" n="1.0133" /> kho maṃ bhāyeti, mahānerunidassanaṃ;
```

```
Haṃsassa anabhiññāya, mahā me bhayamāgataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§109.</p>

```
Na tassa vuḍḍhi kusalappasatthā, yo vaḍḍhamāno ghasate patiṭṭhaṃ;
```

```
Tassūparodhaṃ parisaṅkamāno, patārayī mūlavadhāya dhīroti.
```

Palāsajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Vaṇṇārohavaggo dutiyo <note>imassuddānaṃ tatiyavaggapariyosāne bhavissati</note>.

#### 3. Aḍḍhavaggo

#### 371. Dīghītikosalajātakaṃ (5-3-1)

<p rend="hangnum">§110.</p>

```
Evaṃbhūtassa te rāja, āgatassa vase <note>vaso (pī. ka.)</note> mama;
```

```
Atthi nu koci pariyāyo, yo taṃ dukkhā pamocaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§111.</p>

```
Evaṃbhūtassa <pb ed="T" n="1.0182" /> me tāta, āgatassa vase tava;
```

```
Natthi no koci pariyāyo, yo maṃ dukkhā pamocaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§112.</p>

```
Nāññaṃ sucaritaṃ rāja, nāññaṃ rāja subhāsitaṃ;
```

```
Tāyate maraṇakāle, evamevitaraṃ dhanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§113.</p>

```
Akkocchi maṃ avadhi maṃ, ajini maṃ ahāsi me;
```

```
Ye ca taṃ upanayhanti, veraṃ tesaṃ na sammati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§114.</p>

```
Akkocchi maṃ avadhi maṃ, ajini maṃ ahāsi me;
```

```
Ye ca taṃ nupanayhanti, veraṃ tesūpasammati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§115.</p>

```
Na hi verena verāni, sammantīdha kudācanaṃ;
```

```
Averena ca sammanti, esa dhammo sanantanoti.
```

Dīghītikosalajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 372. Migapotakajātakaṃ (5-3-2)

<p rend="hangnum">§116.</p>

```
Agārā <pb ed="V" n="1.0113" /> paccupetassa, anagārassa te sato;
```

```
Samaṇassa na taṃ sādhu, yaṃ petamanusocasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§117.</p>

```
Saṃvāsena <pb ed="M" n="1.0134" /> have sakka, manussassa migassa vā;
```

```
Hadaye <pb ed="T" n="1.0183" /> jāyate pemaṃ, na taṃ sakkā asocituṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§118.</p>

```
Mataṃ marissaṃ rodanti, ye rudanti lapanti ca;
```

```
Tasmā tvaṃ isi mā rodi, roditaṃ moghamāhu santo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§119.</p>

```
Roditena have brahme, mato peto samuṭṭhahe;
```

```
Sabbe saṅgamma rodāma, aññamaññassa ñātake.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§120.</p>

```
Ādittaṃ vata maṃ santaṃ, ghatasittaṃva pāvakaṃ;
```

```
Vārinā viya osiñcaṃ, sabbaṃ nibbāpaye daraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§121.</p>

```
Abbahi vata me sallaṃ, yamāsi hadayassitaṃ;
```

```
Yo me sokaparetassa, puttasokaṃ apānudi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§122.</p>

```
Sohaṃ abbūḷhasallosmi, vītasoko anāvilo;
```

```
Na socāmi na rodāmi, tava sutvāna vāsavāti.
```

Migapotakajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 373. Mūsikajātakaṃ (5-3-3)

<p rend="hangnum">§123.</p>

```
Kuhiṃ gatā kattha gatā, iti lālappatī jano;
```

```
Ahameveko jānāmi, udapāne mūsikā hatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§124.</p>

```
Yañcetaṃ <note>yathetaṃ (pī.), yavetaṃ (ka.), yametaṃ (katthaci)</note> iti cīti ca, gadrabhova nivattasi;
```

```
Udapāne mūsikaṃ hantvā, yavaṃ bhakkhetumicchasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§125.</p>

```
Daharo cāsi dummedha, paṭhamuppattiko <note>paṭhamuppattito (sī. pī.)</note> susu;
```

```
Dīghañcetaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0184" /> <note>dīghametaṃ (pī.)</note> samāsajja <note>samāpajja (syā. ka.)</note>, na te dassāmi jīvitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§126.</p>

```
Nāntalikkhabhavanena, nāṅgaputtapinena <note>nāṅgaputtasirena (sī. syā. pī.)</note> vā;
```

```
Puttena hi patthayito, silokehi pamocito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§127.</p>

```
Sabbaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0114" /> sutamadhīyetha, hīnamukkaṭṭhamajjhimaṃ;
```

```
Sabbassa atthaṃ jāneyya, na ca sabbaṃ payojaye;
```

```
Hoti tādisako kālo, yattha atthāvahaṃ sutanti.
```

Mūsikajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 374. Cūḷadhanuggahajātakaṃ (5-3-4)

<p rend="hangnum">§128.</p>

```
Sabbaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0135" /> bhaṇḍaṃ samādāya, pāraṃ tiṇṇosi brāhmaṇa;
```

Paccāgaccha lahuṃ khippaṃ, mampi tārehi dānito <note>dānibho (syā.)</note>.

<p rend="hangnum">§129.</p>

```
Asanthutaṃ maṃ cirasanthutena, nimīni bhotī addhuvaṃ dhuvena;
```

```
Mayāpi bhotī nimineyya aññaṃ, ito ahaṃ dūrataraṃ gamissaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§130.</p>

```
Kāyaṃ eḷagalāgumbe <note>eḷagaṇagumbe (ka.)</note>, karoti ahuhāsiyaṃ;
```

```
Nayīdha naccagītaṃ vā <note>nayidha naccaṃ vā gītaṃ vā (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, tāḷaṃ vā susamāhitaṃ;
```

```
Anamhikāle <note>anamhakāle (pī.)</note> susoṇi <note>sussoṇi (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, kiṃ nu jagghasi sobhane <note>sobhaṇe (pī. ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§131.</p>

```
Siṅgāla bāla dummedha, appapaññosi jambuka;
```

```
Jīno <pb ed="T" n="1.0185" /> macchañca pesiñca, kapaṇo viya jhāyasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§132.</p>

```
Sudassaṃ vajjamaññesaṃ, attano pana duddasaṃ;
```

```
Jīnā patiñca jārañca, maññe tvaññeva <note>mampi tvaññeva (sī. syā.), tvampi maññeva (pī.)</note> jhāyasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§133.</p>

```
Evametaṃ migarāja, yathā bhāsasi jambuka;
```

```
Sā nūnāhaṃ ito gantvā, bhattu hessaṃ vasānugā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§134.</p>

```
Yo hare mattikaṃ thālaṃ, kaṃsathālampi so hare;
```

```
Katañceva <note>kataṃyeva (sī. syā. pī.)</note> tayā pāpaṃ, punapevaṃ karissasīti.
```

Cūḷadhanuggahajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 375. Kapotajātakaṃ (5-3-5)

<p rend="hangnum">§135.</p>

```
Idāni khomhi sukhito arogo, nikkaṇṭako nippatito kapoto;
```

```
Kāhāmi dānī hadayassa tuṭṭhiṃ, tathāhimaṃ maṃsasākaṃ baleti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§136.</p>

```
Kāyaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0136" /> balākā sikhino, corī laṅghipitāmahā;
```

```
Oraṃ balāke āgaccha, caṇḍo me vāyaso sakhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§137.</p>

```
Alañhi te jagghitāye, mamaṃ disvāna edisaṃ;
```

```
Vilūnaṃ sūdaputtena, piṭṭhamaṇḍena <note>piṭṭhamaddena (sī. syā. pī.)</note> makkhitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§138.</p>

```
Sunhāto <pb ed="V" n="1.0115" /> suvilittosi, annapānena tappito;
```

```
Kaṇṭhe <pb ed="T" n="1.0186" /> ca te veḷuriyo, agamā nu kajaṅgalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§139.</p>

```
Mā te mitto amitto vā, agamāsi kajaṅgalaṃ;
```

```
Piñchāni tattha lāyitvā, kaṇṭhe bandhanti vaṭṭanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§140.</p>

```
Punapāpajjasī samma, sīlañhi tava tādisaṃ;
```

```
Na hi mānusakā bhogā, subhuñjā honti pakkhināti.
```

Kapotajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

Aḍḍhavaggo tatiyo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Atha vaṇṇa sasīla hiri labhate, sumukhā visa sāḷiyamittavaro;
```

```
Atha cakka palāsa sarāja sato, yava bāla kapotaka pannarasāti.
```

Atha vagguddānaṃ –

```
Jīnañca vaṇṇaṃ asamaṃvaguppari, sudesitā jātakanti santi vīsati <note>jātaka pañcavīsati (?)</note>;
```

```
Mahesino brahmacarittamutta-mavoca gāthā atthavatī subyañjanāti.
```

<trailer rend="centre">Pañcakanipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.</trailer>

### 6. Chakkanipāto

#### 1. Avāriyavaggo

#### 376. Avāriyajātakaṃ (6-1-1)

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
Māsu <pb ed="T" n="1.0187" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0116" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0137" /> kujjha bhūmipati, māsu kujjha rathesabha;
```

```
Kuddhaṃ appaṭikujjhanto, rājā raṭṭhassa pūjito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
Gāme vā yadi vāraññe, ninne vā yadi vā thale;
```

```
Sabbattha anusāsāmi, māsu kujjha <note>māssu kujjhi (sī. pī.)</note> rathesabha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
Avāriyapitā nāma, ahu gaṅgāya nāviko;
```

```
Pubbe janaṃ tāretvāna, pacchā yācati vetanaṃ;
```

```
Tenassa bhaṇḍanaṃ hoti, na ca bhogehi vaḍḍhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
Atiṇṇaṃyeva yācassu, apāraṃ tāta nāvika;
```

```
Añño hi tiṇṇassa mano, añño hoti pāresino <note>taresino (sī. pī.), tiresino (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
Gāme vā yadi vāraññe, ninne vā yadi vā thale;
```

```
Sabbattha anusāsāmi, māsu kujjhittha nāvika.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
Yāyevānusāsaniyā, rājā gāmavaraṃ adā;
```

```
Tāyevānusāsaniyā, nāviko paharī mukhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
Bhattaṃ bhinnaṃ hatā bhariyā, gabbho ca patito chamā;
```

```
Migova jātarūpena, na tenatthaṃ abandhi sūti <note>avaḍḍhitunti (sī. syā.), avaḍḍhi sūti (?)</note>.
```

Avāriyajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 377. Setaketujātakaṃ (6-1-2)

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
Mā <pb ed="T" n="1.0188" /> tāta kujjhi na hi sādhu kodho, bahumpi te adiṭṭhamassutañca;
```

```
Mātā pitā disatā <note>disā tāta (syā.), disā tā (pī.)</note> setaketu, ācariyamāhu disataṃ pasatthā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
Agārino <pb ed="V" n="1.0117" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0138" /> annadapānavatthadā <note>annapānavatthadā (syā. ka.)</note>, avhāyikā tampi disaṃ vadanti;
```

```
Esā disā paramā setaketu, yaṃ patvā dukkhī sukhino bhavanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
Kharājinā jaṭilā paṅkadantā, dummakkharūpā <note>dumukkharūpā (sī. syā.), dummukkharūpā (pī. ka.)</note> yeme jappanti mante;
```

```
Kacci nu te mānusake payoge, idaṃ vidū parimuttā apāyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
Pāpāni kammāni katvāna rāja, bahussuto ce na <note>bahussuto neva (sī. syā.)</note> careyya dhammaṃ;
```

```
Sahassavedopi na taṃ paṭicca, dukkhā pamuñce caraṇaṃ apatvā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
Sahassavedopi na taṃ paṭicca, dukkhā pamuñce caraṇaṃ apatvā;
```

```
Maññāmi <pb ed="T" n="1.0189" /> vedā aphalā bhavanti, sasaṃyamaṃ caraṇameva <note>caraṇaññeva (sī. syā. pī.)</note> saccaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
Na heva vedā aphalā bhavanti, sasaṃyamaṃ caraṇameva saccaṃ;
```

```
Kittiñhi pappoti adhicca vede, santiṃ puṇeti <note>santaṃ pune’ti (sī. pī.)</note> caraṇena dantoti.
```

Setaketujātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 378. Darīmukhajātakaṃ (6-1-3)

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
Paṅko ca kāmā palipo ca kāmā, bhayañca metaṃ timūlaṃ pavuttaṃ;
```

```
Rajo ca dhūmo ca mayā pakāsitā, hitvā tuvaṃ pabbaja brahmadatta.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
Gadhito <pb ed="M" n="1.0139" /> <note>gathito (sī.)</note> ca ratto ca adhimucchito ca, kāmesvahaṃ brāhmaṇa bhiṃsarūpaṃ;
```

```
Taṃ nussahe jīvikattho pahātuṃ, kāhāmi puññāni anappakāni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
Yo atthakāmassa hitānukampino, ovajjamāno na karoti sāsanaṃ;
```

```
Idameva seyyo iti maññamāno, punappunaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0190" /> gabbhamupeti mando.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
So ghorarūpaṃ nirayaṃ upeti, subhāsubhaṃ muttakarīsapūraṃ;
```

```
Sattā sakāye na jahanti giddhā, ye honti kāmesu avītarāgā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
Mīḷhena littā ruhirena makkhitā, semhena littā upanikkhamanti;
```

```
Yaṃ yañhi kāyena phusanti tāvade, sabbaṃ asātaṃ dukhameva kevalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
Disvā vadāmi na hi aññato savaṃ, pubbenivāsaṃ bahukaṃ sarāmi;
```

```
Citrāhi gāthāhi subhāsitāhi, darīmukho nijjhāpayi sumedhanti.
```

Darīmukhajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 379. Nerujātakaṃ (6-1-4)

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
Kākolā kākasaṅghā ca, mayañca patataṃ varā <note>vara (ka.) mayantipadassa hi visesanaṃ</note>;
```

```
Sabbeva sadisā homa, imaṃ āgamma pabbataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
Idha <pb ed="V" n="1.0118" /> sīhā ca byagghā ca, siṅgālā ca migādhamā;
```

```
Sabbeva <pb ed="T" n="1.0191" /> sadisā honti, ayaṃ ko nāma pabbato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
Imaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0140" /> nerūti <note>nerunti (sī. syā.)</note> jānanti, manussā pabbatuttamaṃ;
```

```
Idha vaṇṇena sampannā, vasanti sabbapāṇino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
Amānanā yattha siyā, santānaṃ vā vimānanā;
```

```
Hīnasammānanā vāpi, na tattha vasatiṃ vase <note>vasatī vase (syā.), vasa divase (pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
Yatthālaso ca dakkho ca, sūro bhīru ca pūjiyā;
```

```
Na tattha santo vasanti, avisesakare nare <note>nage (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
Nāyaṃ neru vibhajati, hīnaukkaṭṭhamajjhime;
```

```
Avisesakaro neru, handa neruṃ jahāmaseti.
```

Nerujātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 380. Āsaṅkajātakaṃ (6-1-5)

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
Āsāvatī nāma latā, jātā cittalatāvane;
```

```
Tassā vassasahassena, ekaṃ nibbattate phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
Taṃ devā payirupāsanti, tāva dūraphalaṃ satiṃ;
```

```
Āsīseva <note>āsiṃseva (sī. syā. pī.)</note> tuvaṃ rāja, āsā phalavatī sukhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
Āsīsateva <note>āsiṃsetheva (sī. syā. pī.)</note> so pakkhī, āsīsateva <note>āsiṃsetheva (sī. syā. pī.)</note> so dijo;
```

```
Tassa cāsā <note>tassevāsā (syā.)</note> samijjhati, tāva dūragatā satī;
```

```
Āsīseva tuvaṃ rāja, āsā phalavatī sukhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
Sampesi kho maṃ vācāya, na ca sampesi <note>saṃsesi (ka.)</note> kammunā;
```

```
Mālā <pb ed="T" n="1.0192" /> sereyyakasseva, vaṇṇavantā agandhikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
Aphalaṃ madhuraṃ vācaṃ, yo mittesu pakubbati;
```

```
Adadaṃ avissajaṃ bhogaṃ, sandhi tenassa jīrati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
Yañhi kayirā tañhi vade, yaṃ na kayirā na taṃ vade;
```

```
Akarontaṃ bhāsamānaṃ, parijānanti paṇḍitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
Balañca vata me khīṇaṃ, pātheyyañca na vijjati;
```

```
Saṅke pāṇūparodhāya, handa dāni vajāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
Etadeva <pb ed="V" n="1.0119" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0141" /> hi me nāmaṃ, yaṃ nāmasmi rathesabha;
```

```
Āgamehi mahārāja, pitaraṃ āmantayāmahanti.
```

Āsaṅkajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 381. Migālopajātakaṃ (6-1-6)

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
Na me rucci migālopa, yassa te tādisī gatī;
```

```
Atuccaṃ tāta patasi, abhūmiṃ tāta sevasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
Catukkaṇṇaṃva kedāraṃ, yadā te pathavī siyā;
```

```
Tato tāta nivattassu, māssu etto paraṃ gami.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
Santi aññepi sakuṇā, pattayānā vihaṅgamā;
```

```
Akkhittā vātavegena, naṭṭhā te sassatīsamā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
Akatvā apanandassa <note>aparaṇṇassa (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, pitu vuddhassa sāsanaṃ;
```

```
Kālavāte <pb ed="T" n="1.0193" /> atikkamma, verambhānaṃ vasaṃ agā <note>gato (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
Tassa puttā ca dārā ca, ye caññe anujīvino;
```

```
Sabbe byasanamāpāduṃ, anovādakare dije.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
Evampi idha vuddhānaṃ, yo vākyaṃ nāvabujjhati;
```

```
Atisīmacaro <note>atisīmaṃ caro (sī. syā. ka.)</note> ditto, gijjhovātītasāsano;
```

```
Sabbe byasanaṃ papponti, akatvā buddhasāsananti.
```

Migālopajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 382. Sirikāḷakaṇṇijātakaṃ (6-1-7)

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
Kā nu kāḷena vaṇṇena, na cāpi <note>na cāsi (sī.)</note> piyadassanā;
```

```
Kā vā tvaṃ kassa vā dhītā, kathaṃ jānemu taṃ mayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
Mahārājassahaṃ dhītā, virūpakkhassa caṇḍiyā;
```

```
Ahaṃ kāḷī alakkhikā, kāḷakaṇṇīti maṃ vidū;
```

```
Okāsaṃ yācito dehi, vasemu tava santike.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
Kiṃsīle <pb ed="M" n="1.0142" /> kiṃsamācāre, purise nivisase tuvaṃ;
```

```
Puṭṭhā me kāḷi akkhāhi, kathaṃ <note>yathā (sī. pī.)</note> jānemu taṃ mayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
Makkhī paḷāsī sārambhī, issukī maccharī saṭho;
```

```
So mayhaṃ puriso kanto, laddhaṃ yassa vinassati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
Kodhano <pb ed="V" n="1.0120" /> upanāhī ca, pisuṇo ca vibhedako;
```

```
Kaṇḍakavāco <note>aṇḍakavāco (ka. sī. pī.)</note> pharuso, so me kantataro tato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
Ajja <pb ed="T" n="1.0194" /> suveti puriso, sadatthaṃ nāvabujjhati;
```

```
Ovajjamāno kuppati, seyyaṃ so atimaññati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
Davappaluddho <note>devappaluddho (ka.), davappaladdho (pī.)</note> puriso, sabbamittehi dhaṃsati;
```

```
So mayhaṃ puriso kanto, tasmiṃ homi anāmayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
Apehi etto tvaṃ kāḷi, netaṃ amhesu vijjati;
```

```
Aññaṃ janapadaṃ gaccha, nigame rājadhāniyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
Ahampi kho taṃ <note>cetaṃ (sī.)</note> jānāmi, netaṃ tumhesu vijjati;
```

```
Santi loke alakkhikā, saṅgharanti bahuṃ dhanaṃ;
```

```
Ahaṃ devo ca me bhātā, ubho naṃ vidhamāmase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
Kā nu dibbena vaṇṇena, pathabyā supatiṭṭhitā;
```

```
Kā vā tvaṃ kassa vā dhītā, kathaṃ jānemu taṃ mayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
Mahārājassahaṃ dhītā, dhataraṭṭhassa sirīmato <note>dhataraṭṭhasirīmato (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Ahaṃ sirī ca lakkhī ca, bhūripaññāti maṃ vidū;
```

```
Okāsaṃ yācito dehi, vasemu tava santike.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
Kiṃsīle kiṃsamācāre, purise nivisase tuvaṃ;
```

```
Puṭṭhā me lakkhi akkhāhi, kathaṃ <note>yathā (sī. pī.)</note> jānemu taṃ mayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
Yo <pb ed="M" n="1.0143" /> cāpi sīte athavāpi uṇhe, vātātape ḍaṃsasarīsape ca;
```

```
Khudhaṃ <note>khuddaṃ (syā. ka.), khudaṃ (pī.)</note> pipāsaṃ abhibhuyya sabbaṃ, rattintivaṃ yo satataṃ niyutto;
```

```
Kālāgatañca <pb ed="T" n="1.0195" /> na hāpeti atthaṃ, so me manāpo nivise ca tamhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
Akkodhano mittavā cāgavā ca, sīlūpapanno asaṭhojubhūto <note>asaṭho ujjubhūto (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Saṅgāhako sakhilo saṇhavāco, mahattapattopi nivātavutti;
```

```
Tasmiṃhaṃ <note>tasmāhaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> pose vipulā bhavāmi, ūmi samuddassa yathāpi vaṇṇaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
Yo cāpi mitte athavā amitte, seṭṭhe sarikkhe atha vāpi hīne;
```

```
Atthaṃ carantaṃ athavā anatthaṃ, āvī raho saṅgahameva vatte <note>vatto (syā. ka.)</note>.
```

```
Vācaṃ na vajjā pharusaṃ kadāci, matassa jīvassa ca tassa homi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
Etesaṃ yo aññataraṃ labhitvā, kantā sirī <note>kantasiriṃ (katthaci), kantaṃ siriṃ (syā.) aṭṭhakathāyaṃ dutiyatatiyapāṭhantarāni</note> majjati appapañño;
```

```
Taṃ dittarūpaṃ visamaṃ carantaṃ, karīsaṭhānaṃva <note>karīsajātaṃ va (sī. syā.)</note> vivajjayāmi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
Attanā <pb ed="V" n="1.0121" /> kurute lakkhiṃ, alakkhiṃ kurutattanā;
```

```
Na <pb ed="T" n="1.0196" /> hi lakkhiṃ alakkhiṃ vā, añño aññassa kārakoti.
```

Sirikāḷakaṇṇijātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 383. Kukkuṭajātakaṃ (6-1-8)

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
Sucittapattachadana<pb ed="M" n="1.0144" />, tambacūḷa vihaṅgama;
```

```
Oroha dumasākhāya, mudhā bhariyā bhavāmi te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
Catuppadī tvaṃ kalyāṇi, dvipadāhaṃ manorame;
```

```
Migī pakkhī asaññuttā, aññaṃ pariyesa sāmikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
Komārikā te hessāmi, mañjukā piyabhāṇinī;
```

```
Vinda maṃ ariyena vedena, sāvaya maṃ yadicchasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
Kuṇapādini lohitape, cori kukkuṭapothini;
```

```
Na tvaṃ ariyena vedena, mamaṃ bhattāramicchasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
Evampi caturā <note>cāturā (syā. ka.)</note> nārī, disvāna sadhanaṃ <note>pavaraṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> naraṃ;
```

```
Nenti saṇhāhi vācāhi, biḷārī viya kukkuṭaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
Yo ca uppatitaṃ atthaṃ, na khippamanubujjhati;
```

```
Amittavasamanveti, pacchā ca anutappati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
Yo ca uppatitaṃ atthaṃ, khippameva nibodhati;
```

```
Muccate <pb ed="T" n="1.0197" /> sattusambādhā, kukkuṭova biḷāriyāti.
```

Kukkuṭajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 384. Dhammadhajajātakaṃ (6-1-9)

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
Dhammaṃ caratha ñātayo, dhammaṃ caratha bhaddaṃ vo <note>bhadda vo (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Dhammacārī sukhaṃ seti, asmiṃ loke paramhi ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
Bhaddako vatayaṃ pakkhī, dijo paramadhammiko;
```

```
Ekapādena tiṭṭhanto, dhammamevānusāsati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
Nāssa sīlaṃ vijānātha, anaññāya pasaṃsatha;
```

```
Bhutvā aṇḍañca potañca <note>chāpe ca (sī. pī.)</note>, dhammo dhammoti bhāsati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
Aññaṃ bhaṇati vācāya, aññaṃ kāyena kubbati;
```

```
Vācāya no ca kāyena, na taṃ dhammaṃ adhiṭṭhito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
Vācāya <pb ed="V" n="1.0122" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0145" /> sakhilo manoviduggo, channo kūpasayova kaṇhasappo;
```

```
Dhammadhajo gāmanigamāsusādhu <note>gāmanigamāsu sādhusammato (sī.), gāmanigamasādhu (pī.)</note>, dujjāno purisena bālisena.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
Imaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0198" /> tuṇḍehi pakkhehi, pādā cimaṃ viheṭhatha <note>vipothatha (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Chavañhimaṃ vināsetha, nāyaṃ saṃvāsanārahoti.
```

Dhammadhajajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 385. Nandiyamigarājajātakaṃ (6-1-10)

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
Sace brāhmaṇa gacchesi, sākete <note>sāketaṃ (sī. syā.)</note> ajjunaṃ <note>añjhanaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> vanaṃ;
```

```
Vajjāsi nandiyaṃ nāma, puttaṃ asmākamorasaṃ;
```

```
Mātā pitā ca te vuddhā, te taṃ icchanti passituṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
Bhuttā mayā nivāpāni, rājino pānabhojanaṃ;
```

```
Taṃ rājapiṇḍaṃ avabhottuṃ <note>avabhottaṃ (ka.)</note>, nāhaṃ brāhmaṇa mussahe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
Odahissāmahaṃ passaṃ, khurappānissa <note>khurappāṇissa (sī.), khurapāṇissa (pī.), khurappapāṇissa (?)</note> rājino;
```

```
Tadāhaṃ sukhito mutto, api passeyya mātaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
Migarājā pure āsiṃ, kosalassa niketane <note>niketave (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Nandiyo nāma nāmena, abhirūpo catuppado.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
Taṃ maṃ vadhitumāgacchi, dāyasmiṃ ajjune vane;
```

```
Dhanuṃ ārajjaṃ <note>ārajjuṃ (niyya), adejjhaṃ (sī. pī.) advedhābhāvaṃ ekībhāvanti attho</note> katvāna, usuṃ sannayha <note>sandhāya (sī. pī.)</note> kosalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
Tassāhaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0146" /> odahiṃ passaṃ, khurappānissa rājino;
```

```
Tadāhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0199" /> sukhito mutto, mātaraṃ daṭṭhumāgatoti.
```

Nandiyamigarājajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Avāriyavaggo paṭhamo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Atha kujjharathesabha ketuvaro, sadarīmukha neru latā ca puna;
```

```
Apananda sirī ca sucittavaro, atha dhammika nandimigena dasāti.
```

#### 2. Kharaputtavaggo

#### 386. Kharaputtajātakaṃ (6-2-1)

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
Saccaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0123" /> kirevamāhaṃsu, vastaṃ <note>bhastaṃ (sī. pī.), kalakaṃ (syā.), garaṃ (ka.)</note> bāloti paṇḍitā;
```

```
Passa bālo rahokammaṃ, āvikubbaṃ na bujjhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
Tvaṃ khopi <note>tvaṃ nu kho (sī. syā.), tvañca kho (pī.)</note> samma bālosi, kharaputta vijānahi;
```

```
Rajjuyā hi <note>rajjuyāsi (pī.)</note> parikkhitto, vaṅkoṭṭho ohitomukho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
Aparampi samma te bālyaṃ <note>ayampi samma te bālo (ka.)</note>, yo mutto na palāyasi;
```

```
So ca bālataro samma, yaṃ tvaṃ vahasi senakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
Yaṃ nu samma ahaṃ bālo, ajarāja vijānahi;
```

```
Atha <pb ed="T" n="1.0200" /> kena senako bālo, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
Uttamatthaṃ labhitvāna, bhariyāya yo padassati <note>bhayiyā yo padassati (pī.), bhayiyā na bhavissati (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Tena jahissatattānaṃ, sā cevassa na hessati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="M" n="1.0147" /> ve piyammeti <note>na piyameti (ka.), na piyamedanti (katthaci)</note> janinda tādiso, attaṃ niraṃkatvā piyāni sevati <note>sevaye (?)</note>;
```

```
Attāva seyyo paramā ca seyyo, labbhā piyā ocitatthena pacchāti.
```

Kharaputtajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 387. Sūcijātakaṃ (6-2-2)

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
Akakkasaṃ apharusaṃ, kharadhotaṃ supāsiyaṃ;
```

```
Sukhumaṃ tikhiṇaggañca, ko sūciṃ ketumicchati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
Sumajjañca supāsañca, anupubbaṃ <note>anupubba (sī. syā.)</note> suvaṭṭitaṃ;
```

```
Ghanaghātimaṃ paṭithaddhaṃ, ko sūciṃ ketumicchati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
Ito dāni patāyanti, sūciyo baḷisāni ca;
```

```
Koyaṃ kammāragāmasmiṃ, sūciṃ vikketumicchati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
Ito satthāni gacchanti, kammantā vividhā puthū;
```

```
Koyaṃ kammāragāmasmiṃ, sūciṃ vikketumicchati <note>marahati (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
Sūciṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0201" /> kammāragāmasmiṃ, vikketabbā pajānatā;
```

```
Ācariyāva jānanti <note>ācariyā sañjānanti (ka.), ācariyā pajānanti (syā.), ācariyāva sañjānanti (pī.)</note>, kammaṃ sukatadukkaṭaṃ <note>dukkataṃ (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
Imaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0124" /> ce <note>imañca (sī. syā. pī.)</note> te pitā bhadde, sūciṃ jaññā mayā kataṃ;
```

```
Tayā ca maṃ nimanteyya, yañcatthaññaṃ ghare dhananti.
```

Sūcijātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 388. Tuṇḍilajātakaṃ (6-2-3)

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
Navachannake <note>navachandake (sī. pī.), navacchaddake (syā.)</note> dāni <note>doṇi (ka.), dānaṃ, dāne (katthaci)</note> diyyati, puṇṇāyaṃ doṇi suvāminī ṭhitā;
```

```
Bahuke jane pāsapāṇike, no ca kho me paṭibhāti bhuñjituṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
Tasasi <pb ed="M" n="1.0148" /> bhamasi leṇamicchasi, attāṇosi kuhiṃ gamissasi;
```

```
Appossukko bhuñja tuṇḍila, maṃsatthāya hi positāmhase <note>posiyāmase (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
Ogaha rahadaṃ akaddamaṃ, sabbaṃ sedamalaṃ pavāhaya;
```

```
Gaṇhāhi navaṃ vilepanaṃ, yassa <pb ed="T" n="1.0202" /> gandho na kadāci chijjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
Katamo rahado akaddamo, kiṃsu sedamalanti vuccati;
```

```
Katamañca navaṃ vilepanaṃ, yassa gandho na kadāci chijjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
Dhammo rahado akaddamo, pāpaṃ sedamalanti vuccati;
```

```
Sīlañca navaṃ vilepanaṃ, tassa gandho na kadāci chijjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§93.</p>

```
Nandanti sarīraghātino, na ca nandanti sarīradhārino;
```

```
Puṇṇāya ca puṇṇamāsiyā, ramamānāva jahanti jīvitanti.
```

Tuṇḍilajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 389. Suvaṇṇakakkaṭajātakaṃ (6-2-4)

<p rend="hangnum">§94.</p>

```
Siṅgīmigo āyatacakkhunetto, aṭṭhittaco vārisayo alomo;
```

```
Tenābhibhūto kapaṇaṃ rudāmi, hare sakhā kissa nu maṃ jahāsi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§95.</p>

```
So <pb ed="T" n="1.0203" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0149" /> passasanto mahatā phaṇena, bhujaṅgamo kakkaṭamajjhapatto;
```

```
Sakhā sakhāraṃ paritāyamāno, bhujaṅgamaṃ kakkaṭako gahesi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§96.</p>

```
Na vāyasaṃ no pana kaṇhasappaṃ, ghāsatthiko kakkaṭako adeyya;
```

```
Pucchāmi taṃ āyatacakkhunetta, atha kissa hetumha ubho gahītā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§97.</p>

```
Ayaṃ puriso mama atthakāmo, yo maṃ gahetvāna dakāya neti;
```

```
Tasmiṃ mate dukkhamanappakaṃ me, ahañca eso ca ubho na homa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§98.</p>

```
Mamañca disvāna pavaddhakāyaṃ, sabbo jano hiṃsitumeva micche;
```

```
Sāduñca thūlañca muduñca maṃsaṃ, kākāpi maṃ disvāna <note>disva (sī. pī.)</note> viheṭhayeyyuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§99.</p>

```
Sacetassa <pb ed="V" n="1.0125" /> hetumha ubho gahītā, uṭṭhātu poso visamāvamāmi <note>visamācamāmi (sī. pī. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Mamañca kākañca pamuñca khippaṃ, pure <pb ed="T" n="1.0204" /> visaṃ gāḷhamupeti maccaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§100.</p>

```
Sappaṃ pamokkhāmi na tāva kākaṃ, paṭibandhako <note>paṭibaddhako (sī. pī.)</note> hohiti <note>hoti hi (syā.)</note> tāva kāko;
```

```
Purisañca disvāna sukhiṃ arogaṃ, kākaṃ pamokkhāmi yatheva sappaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§101.</p>

```
Kāko <pb ed="M" n="1.0150" /> tadā devadatto ahosi, māro pana kaṇhasappo ahosi;
```

```
Ānandabhaddo kakkaṭako ahosi, ahaṃ tadā brāhmaṇo homi satthāti <note>tatthāti (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

Suvaṇṇakakkaṭajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 390. Mayhakajātakaṃ (6-2-5)

<p rend="hangnum">§102.</p>

```
Sakuṇo mayhako nāma, girisānudarīcaro;
```

```
Pakkaṃ pipphalimāruyha, mayhaṃ mayhanti kandati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§103.</p>

```
Tassevaṃ vilapantassa, dijasaṅghā samāgatā;
```

```
Bhutvāna pipphaliṃ yanti, vilapatveva so dijo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§104.</p>

```
Evameva idhekacco, saṅgharitvā bahuṃ dhanaṃ;
```

```
Nevattano na ñātīnaṃ, yathodhiṃ paṭipajjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§105.</p>

```
Na so acchādanaṃ bhattaṃ, na mālaṃ na vilepanaṃ;
```

```
Anubhoti <pb ed="T" n="1.0205" /> <note>nānubhoti (syā. ka.)</note> sakiṃ kiñci, na saṅgaṇhāti ñātake.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§106.</p>

```
Tassevaṃ vilapantassa, mayhaṃ mayhanti rakkhato;
```

```
Rājāno atha vā corā, dāyadā ye va <note>ye ca (syā. ka.)</note> appiyā;
```

```
Dhanamādāya gacchanti, vilapatveva so naro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§107.</p>

```
Dhīro <note>dhīro ca (sī.)</note> bhoge adhigamma, saṅgaṇhāti ca ñātake;
```

```
Tena so kittiṃ pappoti, pecca sagge pamodatīti <note>sagge ca modatīti (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

Mayhakajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 391. Vijjādharajātakaṃ (6-2-6)

<p rend="hangnum">§108.</p>

```
Dubbaṇṇarūpaṃ tuvamariyavaṇṇī, purakkhatvā <note>purakkhitvā (syā. ka.)</note> pañjaliko namassasi;
```

```
Seyyo nu te so udavā <note>udāhu (syā. ka.)</note> sarikkho, nāmaṃ parassattano cāpi brūhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§109.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="M" n="1.0151" /> nāmagottaṃ gaṇhanti rāja, sammaggatānujjugatāna <note>samaggatānujjugatāna (syā.), samuggatānujjugatāna (ka.)</note> devā;
```

```
Ahañca te nāmadheyyaṃ vadāmi, sakkohamasmī tidasānamindo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§110.</p>

```
Yo <pb ed="V" n="1.0126" /> disvā bhikkhuṃ caraṇūpapannaṃ, purakkhatvā pañjaliko namassati;
```

```
Pucchāmi taṃ devarājetamatthaṃ, ito <pb ed="T" n="1.0206" /> cuto kiṃ labhate sukhaṃ so.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§111.</p>

```
Yo disvā bhikkhuṃ caraṇūpapannaṃ, purakkhatvā pañjaliko namassati;
```

```
Diṭṭheva dhamme labhate pasaṃsaṃ, saggañca so yāti sarīrabhedā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§112.</p>

```
Lakkhī vata me udapādi ajja, yaṃ vāsavaṃ bhūtapatiddasāma;
```

```
Bhikkhuñca disvāna tuvañca sakka, kāhāmi puññāni anappakāni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§113.</p>

```
Addhā have sevitabbā sapaññā, bahussutā ye bahuṭhānacintino;
```

```
Bhikkhuñca disvāna mamañca rāja, karohi puññāni anappakāni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§114.</p>

```
Akkodhano niccapasannacitto, sabbātithīyācayogo bhavitvā;
```

```
Nihacca mānaṃ abhivādayissaṃ, sutvāna devinda subhāsitānīti.
```

Vijjādhara <note>dhajaviheṭhaka (sī. pī.), pabbajitaviheṭhaka (syā.)</note> jātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 392. Siṅghapupphajātakaṃ (6-2-7)

<p rend="hangnum">§115.</p>

```
Yametaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0207" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0152" /> <note>yamekaṃ (pī.)</note> vārijaṃ pupphaṃ, adinnaṃ upasiṅghasi;
```

```
Ekaṅgametaṃ theyyānaṃ, gandhathenosi mārisa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§116.</p>

```
Na harāmi na bhañjāmi, ārā siṅghāmi vārijaṃ;
```

```
Atha kena nu vaṇṇena, gandhathenoti vuccati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§117.</p>

```
Yoyaṃ bhisāni khaṇati, puṇḍarīkāni bhañjati;
```

```
Evaṃ ākiṇṇakammanto, kasmā eso na vuccati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§118.</p>

```
Ākiṇṇaluddo puriso, dhāticelaṃva makkhito;
```

```
Tasmiṃ me vacanaṃ natthi, tañcārahāmi vattave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§119.</p>

```
Anaṅgaṇassa posassa, niccaṃ sucigavesino;
```

```
Vālaggamattaṃ pāpassa, abbhāmattaṃva khāyati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§120.</p>

```
Addhā maṃ yakkha jānāsi, atho maṃ anukampasi;
```

```
Punapi yakkha vajjāsi, yadā passasi edisaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§121.</p>

```
Neva taṃ upajīvāmi, napi te bhatakāmhase <note>bhatakamhase (sī. pī.), bhatikamhase (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Tvameva bhikkhu jāneyya, yena gaccheyya suggatinti.
```

Siṅghapuppha <note>bhisapuppha (sī. pī.), upasiṅghapuppha (syā.)</note> jātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 393. Vighāsādajātakaṃ (6-2-8)

<p rend="hangnum">§122.</p>

```
Susukhaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0127" /> vata jīvanti, ye janā vighāsādino;
```

```
Diṭṭheva <pb ed="T" n="1.0208" /> dhamme pāsaṃsā, samparāye ca suggatī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§123.</p>

```
Sukassa <note>suvassa (sī. syā. pī.)</note> bhāsamānassa, na nisāmetha paṇḍitā;
```

```
Idaṃ suṇātha sodariyā, amhevāyaṃ pasaṃsati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§124.</p>

```
Nāhaṃ tumhe pasaṃsāmi, kuṇapādā suṇātha me;
```

```
Ucchiṭṭhabhojino <note>bhojanā (ka.)</note> tumhe, na tumhe vighāsādino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§125.</p>

```
Sattavassā <pb ed="M" n="1.0153" /> pabbajitā, mejjhāraññe <note>majjheraññe (ka.)</note> sikhaṇḍino;
```

```
Vighāseneva yāpentā, mayaṃ ce bhoto gārayhā;
```

```
Ke nu bhoto pasaṃsiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§126.</p>

```
Tumhe sīhānaṃ byagghānaṃ, vāḷānañcāvasiṭṭhakaṃ;
```

```
Ucchiṭṭheneva yāpentā, maññivho vighāsādino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§127.</p>

```
Ye brāhmaṇassa samaṇassa, aññassa vā <note>aññassa ca (sī. syā.), aññasseva (pī.)</note> vanibbino <note>vaṇibbino (sī. syā.)</note>;
```

```
Datvāva <note>datvāna (pī. ka.)</note> sesaṃ bhuñjanti, te janā vighāsādinoti.
```

Vighāsādajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 394. Vaṭṭakajātakaṃ (6-2-9)

<p rend="hangnum">§128.</p>

```
Paṇītaṃ bhuñjase bhattaṃ, sappitelañca mātula;
```

```
Atha kena nu vaṇṇena, kiso tvamasi vāyasa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§129.</p>

```
Amittamajjhe vasato, tesu āmisamesato;
```

```
Niccaṃ ubbiggahadayassa, kuto kākassa daḷhiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§130.</p>

```
Niccaṃ ubbegino <note>ubbiggino (syā. ka.), ubbedhino (sī.)</note> kākā, dhaṅkā pāpena kammunā;
```

```
Laddho <pb ed="T" n="1.0209" /> piṇḍo na pīṇeti, kiso tenasmi vaṭṭaka.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§131.</p>

```
Lūkhāni tiṇabījāni, appasnehāni bhuñjasi;
```

```
Atha kena nu vaṇṇena, thūlo tvamasi vaṭṭaka.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§132.</p>

```
Appicchā appacintāya, adūragamanena ca;
```

```
Laddhāladdhena yāpento, thūlo tenasmi vāyasa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§133.</p>

```
Appicchassa <pb ed="V" n="1.0128" /> hi posassa, appacintasukhassa <note>appacintisukhassa (sī. syā. pī.)</note> ca;
```

```
Susaṅgahitamānassa <note>susaṅgahitapamāṇassa (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, vuttī susamudānayāti.
```

Vaṭṭakajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 395. Pārāvatajātakaṃ (6-2-10)

<p rend="hangnum">§134.</p>

```
Cirassaṃ vata passāmi, sahāyaṃ maṇidhārinaṃ;
```

```
Sukatā <note>sukatāya (sī. pī.)</note> massukuttiyā, sobhate vata me sakhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§135.</p>

```
Parūḷhakacchanakhalomo<pb ed="M" n="1.0154" />, ahaṃ kammesu byāvaṭo;
```

```
Cirassaṃ nhāpitaṃ laddhā, lomaṃ taṃ ajjaṃ hārayiṃ <note>apahārayiṃ (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§136.</p>

```
Yaṃ nu lomaṃ ahāresi, dullabhaṃ laddha kappakaṃ;
```

```
Atha kiñcarahi te samma, kaṇṭhe kiṇikiṇāyati <note>idaṃ kaṇṭhe kiṇāyati (ka.), kaṇṭhe kiṃnikilāyati (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§137.</p>

```
Manussasukhumālānaṃ, maṇi kaṇṭhesu lambati;
```

```
Tesāhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0210" /> anusikkhāmi, mā tvaṃ maññi davā kataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§138.</p>

```
Sacepimaṃ pihayasi, massukuttiṃ sukāritaṃ;
```

```
Kārayissāmi te samma, maṇiñcāpi dadāmi te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§139.</p>

```
Tvaññeva maṇinā channo, sukatāya ca massuyā;
```

```
Āmanta kho taṃ gacchāmi, piyaṃ me tava dassananti.
```

Pārāvatajātakaṃ <note>kākajātakaṃ (sī. pī.), maṇijātakaṃ (syā.)</note> dasamaṃ.

Kharaputtavaggo <note>senakavaggo (sī. pī.), khuraputtavaggo (syā.), sūcivaggo (ka.)</note> dutiyo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Atha passa sasūci ca tuṇḍilako, miga mayhakapañcamapakkhivaro;
```

```
Atha pañjali vārija mejjha puna, atha vaṭṭa kapotavarena dasāti.
```

Atha vagguddānaṃ –

```
Atha vaggaṃ pakittissaṃ, chanipātaṃ varuttame;
```

```
Avāriyā ca kharo ca <note>senaka (sī.), sūci ca (syā. ka.)</note>, dve ca vuttā subyañjanāti.
```

<trailer rend="centre">Chakkanipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.</trailer>

### 7. Sattakanipāto

#### 1. Kukkuvaggo

#### 396. Kukkujātakaṃ (7-1-1)

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
Diyaḍḍhakukkū <pb ed="T" n="1.0211" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0129" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0155" /> udayena kaṇṇikā, vidatthiyo aṭṭha parikkhipanti naṃ;
```

```
Sā siṃsapā <note>sasiṃsapā (sī. pī.), sā sīsapā (syā.), yā siṃsapā (ka. sī. niyya)</note> sāramayā apheggukā, kuhiṃ ṭhitā upparito <note>uparito (sī. syā. pī.)</note> na dhaṃsati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
Yā tiṃsati sāramayā anujjukā, parikiriya <note>pakiriyā (ka.)</note> gopāṇasiyo samaṃ ṭhitā <note>samaṭṭhitā (sī. syā.)</note>;
```

```
Tāhi susaṅgahitā balasā pīḷitā <note>tā saṅgahitā balasā ca pīḷitā (sī.), tāhi susaṅgahitā balasā ca pīḷitā (syā.), tāhi saṅgahītā balasā ca pīḷitā (pī.)</note>, samaṃ ṭhitā upparito na dhaṃsati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
Evampi mittehi daḷhehi paṇḍito, abhejjarūpehi sucīhi mantibhi;
```

```
Susaṅgahīto siriyā na dhaṃsati, gopāṇasī bhāravahāva kaṇṇikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
Kharattacaṃ bellaṃ yathāpi satthavā, anāmasantopi karoti tittakaṃ;
```

```
Samāharaṃ sāduṃ karoti patthiva, asāduṃ kayirā tanubandhamuddharaṃ <note>tanuvaṭṭamuddharaṃ (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
Evampi <pb ed="T" n="1.0212" /> gāmanigamesu paṇḍito, asāhasaṃ rājadhanāni saṅgharaṃ;
```

```
Dhammānuvattī paṭipajjamāno, sa phāti kayirā aviheṭhayaṃ paraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
Odātamūlaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0156" /> sucivārisambhavaṃ, jātaṃ yathā pokkharaṇīsu ambujaṃ;
```

```
Padumaṃ yathā agginikāsiphālimaṃ, na kaddamo na rajo na vāri limpati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
Evampi vohārasuciṃ asāhasaṃ, visuddhakammantamapetapāpakaṃ;
```

```
Na limpati kammakilesa tādiso, jātaṃ yathā pokkharaṇīsu ambujanti.
```

Kukkujātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 397. Manojajātakaṃ (7-1-2)

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
Yathā cāpo ninnamati, jiyā cāpi nikūjati;
```

```
Haññate nūna manojo, migarājā sakhā mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
Handa dāni vanantāni, pakkamāmi yathāsukhaṃ;
```

```
Netādisā sakhā honti, labbhā me jīvato sakhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="V" n="1.0130" /> pāpajanasaṃsevī, accantaṃ sukhamedhati;
```

```
Manojaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0213" /> passa semānaṃ, giriyassānusāsanī <note>ariyassānusāsanī (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
Na pāpasampavaṅkena, mātā puttena nandati;
```

```
Manojaṃ passa semānaṃ, acchannaṃ <note>sacchannaṃ (ka.)</note> samhi lohite.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
Evamāpajjate poso, pāpiyo ca nigacchati;
```

```
Yo ve hitānaṃ vacanaṃ, na karoti atthadassinaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
Evañca so hoti tato ca pāpiyo, yo uttamo adhamajanūpasevī;
```

```
Passuttamaṃ adhamajanūpasevitaṃ <note>seviṃ (syā.)</note>, migādhipaṃ saravaraveganiddhutaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
Nihīyati <pb ed="M" n="1.0157" /> puriso nihīnasevī, na ca hāyetha kadāci tulyasevī;
```

```
Seṭṭhamupagamaṃ <note>mupanamaṃ (sī. pī. a. ni. 3.26)</note> udeti khippaṃ, tasmāttanā uttaritaraṃ <note>tasmā attano uttariṃ (sī. pī.), tasmā attano uttaraṃ (syā.)</note> bhajethāti.
```

Manojajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 398. Sutanujātakaṃ (7-1-3)

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
Rājā te bhattaṃ pāhesi, suciṃ maṃsūpasecanaṃ;
```

```
Maghadevasmiṃ <note>makhādevasmiṃ (sī. pī.), māghadevasmiṃ (ka.)</note> adhivatthe, ehi nikkhamma bhuñjassu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
Ehi māṇava orena, bhikkhamādāya sūpitaṃ;
```

```
Tvañca <pb ed="T" n="1.0214" /> māṇava bhikkhā ca <note>bhakkhosi (syā.), bhakkhāva (ka.)</note>, ubho bhakkhā bhavissatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
Appakena tuvaṃ yakkha, thullamatthaṃ jahissasi;
```

```
Bhikkhaṃ te nāharissanti, janā maraṇasaññino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
Laddhāya yakkhā <note>laddhāyaṃ yakkha (sī. syā. pī.)</note> tava niccabhikkhaṃ, suciṃ paṇītaṃ rasasā upetaṃ;
```

```
Bhikkhañca te āhariyo naro idha, sudullabho hehiti bhakkhite <note>khādite (sī. syā. pī.)</note> mayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
Mameva <note>mamesa (sī. pī.)</note> sutano attho, yathā bhāsasi māṇava;
```

```
Mayā tvaṃ samanuññāto, sotthiṃ passāhi mātaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
Khaggaṃ chattañca pātiñca, gacchamādāya <note>gacchevādāya (sī. syā. pī.)</note> māṇava;
```

```
Sotthiṃ passatu te mātā, tvañca passāhi mātaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
Evaṃ yakkha sukhī hohi, saha sabbehi ñātibhi;
```

```
Dhanañca me adhigataṃ, rañño ca vacanaṃ katanti.
```

Sutanujātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 399. Mātuposakagijjhajātakaṃ (7-1-4)

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
Te <pb ed="V" n="1.0131" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0158" /> kathaṃ nu karissanti, vuddhā giridarīsayā;
```

```
Ahaṃ baddhosmi pāsena, nilīyassa vasaṃ gato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
Kiṃ gijjha paridevasi, kā nu te paridevanā;
```

```
Na <pb ed="T" n="1.0215" /> me suto vā diṭṭho vā, bhāsanto mānusiṃ dijo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
Bharāmi mātāpitaro, vuddhe giridarīsaye;
```

```
Te kathaṃ nu karissanti, ahaṃ vasaṃ gato tava.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
Yaṃ nu gijjho yojanasataṃ, kuṇapāni avekkhati;
```

```
Kasmā jālañca pāsañca, āsajjāpi na bujjhasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
Yadā parābhavo hoti, poso jīvitasaṅkhaye;
```

```
Atha jālañca pāsañca, āsajjāpi na bujjhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
Bharassu mātāpitaro, vuddhe giridarīsaye;
```

```
Mayā tvaṃ samanuññāto, sotthiṃ passāhi ñātake.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
Evaṃ luddaka nandassu, saha sabbehi ñātibhi;
```

```
Bharissaṃ mātāpitaro, vuddhe giridarīsayeti.
```

Mātuposakagijjhajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 400. Dabbhapupphajātakaṃ (7-1-5)

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
Anutīracārī bhaddante, sahāyamanudhāva maṃ;
```

```
Mahā me gahito <note>rohito (ka.)</note> maccho, so maṃ harati vegasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
Gambhīracārī bhaddante, daḷhaṃ gaṇhāhi thāmasā;
```

```
Ahaṃ taṃ uddharissāmi, supaṇṇo uragāmiva <note>uragammiva (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
Vivādo no samuppanno, dabbhapuppha suṇohi me;
```

```
Samehi <pb ed="T" n="1.0216" /> medhagaṃ <note>medhakaṃ (pī.)</note> samma, vivādo vūpasammataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
Dhammaṭṭhohaṃ pure āsiṃ, bahū aḍḍā me tīritā <note>bahuaṭṭaṃ me tīritaṃ (sī.), bahuaṭṭaṃva tīritaṃ (syā.), bahu atthaṃ me tīritaṃ (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Samemi medhagaṃ samma, vivādo vūpasammataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
Anutīracāri <pb ed="M" n="1.0159" /> naṅguṭṭhaṃ, sīsaṃ gambhīracārino;
```

```
Accāyaṃ <note>athāyaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> majjhimo khaṇḍo, dhammaṭṭhassa bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
Cirampi <pb ed="V" n="1.0132" /> bhakkho abhavissa, sace na vivademase;
```

```
Asīsakaṃ anaṅguṭṭhaṃ, siṅgālo harati rohitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
Yathāpi rājā nandeyya, rajjaṃ laddhāna khattiyo;
```

```
Evāhamajja nandāmi, disvā puṇṇamukhaṃ patiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
Kathaṃ nu thalajo santo, udake macchaṃ parāmasi;
```

```
Puṭṭho me samma akkhāhi, kathaṃ adhigataṃ tayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
Vivādena kisā honti, vivādena dhanakkhayā;
```

```
Jīnā uddā vivādena, bhuñja māyāvi rohitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
Evameva manussesu, vivādo yattha jāyati;
```

```
Dhammaṭṭhaṃ paṭidhāvanti, so hi nesaṃ vināyako;
```

```
Dhanāpi tattha jīyanti, rājakoso pavaḍḍhatīti <note>ca vaḍḍhati (pī.)</note>.
```

Dabbhapupphajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 401. Paṇṇakajātakaṃ (7-1-6)

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
Paṇṇakaṃ <note>dasaṇṇakaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> tikhiṇadhāraṃ, asiṃ sampannapāyinaṃ;
```

```
Parisāyaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0217" /> puriso gilati, kiṃ dukkarataraṃ tato;
```

```
Yadaññaṃ dukkaraṃ ṭhānaṃ, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
Gileyya puriso lobhā, asiṃ sampannapāyinaṃ;
```

```
Yo ca vajjā dadāmīti, taṃ dukkarataraṃ tato;
```

```
Sabbaññaṃ sukaraṃ ṭhānaṃ, evaṃ jānāhi maddava <note>māgadha (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
Byākāsi āyuro pañhaṃ, atthaṃ <note>attha (pī. sī. niyya)</note> dhammassa kovido;
```

```
Pukkusaṃ dāni pucchāmi, kiṃ dukkarataraṃ tato;
```

```
Yadaññaṃ dukkaraṃ ṭhānaṃ, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="M" n="1.0160" /> vācamupajīvanti, aphalaṃ giramudīritaṃ;
```

```
Yo ca datvā avākayirā, taṃ dukkarataraṃ tato;
```

```
Sabbaññaṃ sukaraṃ ṭhānaṃ, evaṃ jānāhi maddava.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
Byākāsi pukkuso pañhaṃ, atthaṃ dhammassa kovido;
```

```
Senakaṃ dāni pucchāmi, kiṃ dukkarataraṃ tato;
```

```
Yadaññaṃ dukkaraṃ ṭhānaṃ, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
Dadeyya <pb ed="V" n="1.0133" /> puriso dānaṃ, appaṃ vā yadi vā bahuṃ;
```

```
Yo ca datvā nānutappe <note>tape (sī. pī.)</note>, taṃ dukkarataraṃ tato;
```

```
Sabbaññaṃ sukaraṃ ṭhānaṃ, evaṃ jānāhi maddava.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
Byākāsi āyuro pañhaṃ, atho pukkusaporiso;
```

```
Sabbe <pb ed="T" n="1.0218" /> pañhe atibhoti, yathā bhāsati senakoti.
```

Paṇṇaka <note>dasaṇṇaka (sī. syā. pī.)</note> jātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 402. Sattubhastajātakaṃ (7-1-7)

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
Vibbhantacitto kupitindriyosi, nettehi te vārigaṇā savanti;
```

```
Kiṃ te naṭṭhaṃ kiṃ pana patthayāno, idhāgamā brahme tadiṅgha <note>brāhmaṇa iṅgha (sī. syā.)</note> brūhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
Miyyetha bhariyā vajato mamajja, agacchato maraṇamāha yakkho;
```

```
Etena dukkhena pavedhitosmi, akkhāhi me senaka etamatthaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
Bahūni ṭhānāni vicintayitvā, yamettha vakkhāmi tadeva saccaṃ;
```

```
Maññāmi te brāhmaṇa sattubhastaṃ, ajānato kaṇhasappo paviṭṭho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
Ādāya <pb ed="M" n="1.0161" /> daṇḍaṃ parisumbha bhastaṃ, passeḷamūgaṃ uragaṃ dujivhaṃ <note>dijivhaṃ (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Chindajja kaṅkhaṃ vicikicchitāni, bhujaṅgamaṃ passa pamuñca bhastaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
Saṃviggarūpo <pb ed="T" n="1.0219" /> parisāya majjhe, so brāhmaṇo sattubhastaṃ pamuñci;
```

```
Atha nikkhami urago uggatejo, āsīviso sappo phaṇaṃ karitvā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
Suladdhalābhā janakassa rañño, yo passatī senakaṃ sādhupaññaṃ;
```

```
Vivaṭṭachaddo <note>vivattacchaddo (sī.), vivaṭṭacchado (syā.), vivaṭṭacchaddā (pī.)</note> nusi sabbadassī, ñāṇaṃ nu te brāhmaṇa bhiṃsarūpaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
Imāni me sattasatāni atthi, gaṇhāhi sabbāni dadāmi tuyhaṃ;
```

```
Tayā hi me jīvitamajja laddhaṃ, athopi bhariyāya makāsi sotthiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
Na paṇḍitā vetanamādiyanti, citrāhi gāthāhi subhāsitāhi;
```

```
Itopi te brahme dadantu vittaṃ, ādāya tvaṃ gaccha sakaṃ niketanti.
```

Sattubhastajātakaṃ <note>senakajātakaṃ (syā.)</note> sattamaṃ.

#### 403. Aṭṭhisenakajātakaṃ (7-1-8)

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
Yeme <pb ed="T" n="1.0220" /> ahaṃ na jānāmi, aṭṭhisena vanibbake;
```

```
Te maṃ saṅgamma yācanti, kasmā maṃ tvaṃ na yācasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
Yācako <pb ed="V" n="1.0134" /> appiyo hoti, yācaṃ adadamappiyo;
```

```
Tasmāhaṃ taṃ na yācāmi, mā me videssanā <note>viddesanā (sī. pī.)</note> ahu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
Yo <pb ed="M" n="1.0162" /> ve yācanajīvāno, kāle yācaṃ na yācati;
```

```
Parañca puññā <note>puññaṃ (syā. ka.)</note> dhaṃseti, attanāpi na jīvati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
Yo ca <note>yo ve (ka.)</note> yācanajīvāno, kāle yācañhi yācati <note>yācaṃpi yācati (syā.), yācāni yācati (pī.), yācati yācanaṃ (sī. niyya), yācanaṃ yācati (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Parañca puññaṃ labbheti, attanāpi ca jīvati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
Na ve dessanti <note>na ve dussanti (syā.), na ve dissanti (pī.), na videssanti (ka. aṭṭha.)</note> sappaññā, disvā yācakamāgate;
```

```
Brahmacāri piyo mesi, vada tvaṃ <note>vara taṃ (sī.), vara tvaṃ (pī.)</note> bhaññamicchasi <note>yaññamicchasi (?)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
Na ve yācanti sappaññā, dhīro ca veditumarahati;
```

```
Uddissa ariyā tiṭṭhanti, esā ariyāna yācanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
Dadāmi te brāhmaṇa rohiṇīnaṃ, gavaṃ sahassaṃ saha puṅgavena;
```

```
Ariyo hi ariyassa kathaṃ na dajjā, sutvāna gāthā tava dhammayuttāti.
```

Aṭṭhisenakajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 404. Kapijātakaṃ (7-1-9)

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
Yattha <pb ed="T" n="1.0221" /> verī nivasati, na vase tattha paṇḍito;
```

```
Ekarattaṃ dirattaṃ vā, dukkhaṃ vasati verisu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
Diso ve lahucittassa, posassānuvidhīyato;
```

```
Ekassa kapino hetu, yūthassa anayo kato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
Bālova <note>ca (sī. syā. pī.)</note> paṇḍitamānī, yūthassa parihārako;
```

```
Sacittassa vasaṃ gantvā, sayethāyaṃ <note>passethāyaṃ (ka.)</note> yathā kapi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
Na sādhu balavā bālo, yūthassa parihārako;
```

```
Ahito bhavati ñātīnaṃ, sakuṇānaṃva cetako <note>ceṭako (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
Dhīrova <pb ed="M" n="1.0163" /> balavā sādhu, yūthassa parihārako;
```

```
Hito bhavati ñātīnaṃ, tidasānaṃva vāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
Yo ca sīlañca paññañca, sutañcattani passati;
```

```
Ubhinnamatthaṃ carati, attano ca parassa ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
Tasmā tuleyya mattānaṃ, sīlapaññāsutāmiva <note>sīlaṃ paññaṃ sutaṃpiva (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Gaṇaṃ vā parihare dhīro, eko vāpi paribbajeti.
```

Kapijātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 405. Bakajātakaṃ (7-1-10)

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
Dvāsattati <pb ed="V" n="1.0135" /> gotama <note>bho gotama (ka.)</note> puññakammā, vasavattino <pb ed="T" n="1.0222" /> jātijaraṃ atītā;
```

```
Ayamantimā vedagū brahmapatti <note>brahmupapatti (syā. ka.)</note>, asmābhijappanti janā <note>pajā (ka.)</note> anekā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
Appañhi etaṃ <note>appañca hetaṃ (syā.), appaṃsi etaṃ (ka.)</note> na hi dīghamāyu, yaṃ tvaṃ baka maññasi dīghamāyuṃ;
```

```
Sataṃ sahassāni <note>sahassānaṃ (sī. pī. saṃ. ni. 1.175), sahassāna (syā. kaṃ.)</note> nirabbudānaṃ, āyuṃ pajānāmi tavāha brahme.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
Anantadassī bhagavāhamasmi, jātijjaraṃ sokamupātivatto;
```

```
Kiṃ me purāṇaṃ vatasīlavattaṃ <note>sīlavantaṃ (pī. ka.)</note>, ācikkha me taṃ yamahaṃ vijaññaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
Yaṃ tvaṃ apāyesi bahū manusse, pipāsite ghammani samparete;
```

```
Taṃ te purāṇaṃ vatasīlavattaṃ, suttappabuddhova anussarāmi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
Yaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0164" /> eṇikūlasmi janaṃ gahītaṃ, amocayī gayhaka niyyamānaṃ;
```

```
Taṃ te purāṇaṃ vatasīlavattaṃ, suttappabuddhova anussarāmi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
Gaṅgāya sotasmiṃ gahītanāvaṃ, luddena <pb ed="T" n="1.0223" /> nāgena manussakappā;
```

```
Amocayi tvaṃ balasā pasayha, taṃ te purāṇaṃ vatasīlavattaṃ;
```

```
Suttappabuddhova anussarāmi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
Kappo ca te baddhacaro <note>patthacaro (syā.), paṭṭhacaro (ka.)</note> ahosi, sambuddhimantaṃ <note>sambuddhivantaṃ (syā. pī.), sambuddhavantaṃ (ka.)</note> vatinaṃ <note>vatitaṃ (syā.), vatidaṃ (ka.)</note> amaññaṃ;
```

```
Taṃ te purāṇaṃ vatasīlavattaṃ, suttappabuddhova anussarāmi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
Addhā pajānāsi mametamāyuṃ, aññampi jānāsi tathā hi buddho;
```

```
Tathā hi tāyaṃ <note>tyāyaṃ (saṃ. ni. 1.175)</note> jalitānubhāvo, obhāsayaṃ tiṭṭhati brahmalokanti.
```

Bakajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Kukkuvaggo paṭhamo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Varakaṇṇika cāpavaro sutano, atha gijjha sarohitamacchavaro;
```

```
Puna paṇṇaka <note>dasaṇṇaka (sī. syā. pī.)</note> senaka yācanako, atha veri sabrahmabakena dasāti.
```

#### 2. Gandhāravaggo

#### 406. Gandhārajātakaṃ (7-2-1)

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
Hitvā <pb ed="T" n="1.0224" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0136" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0165" /> gāmasahassāni, paripuṇṇāni soḷasa;
```

```
Koṭṭhāgārāni phītāni, sannidhiṃ dāni kubbasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
Hitvā gandhāravisayaṃ, pahūtadhanadhāriyaṃ <note>dhāniyaṃ (sī. pī.), dhaññanti attho</note>;
```

```
Pasāsanato <note>pasāsanito (sī. syā.), pasāsanāto (pī.)</note> nikkhanto, idha dāni pasāsasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
Dhammaṃ bhaṇāmi vedeha, adhammo me na ruccati;
```

```
Dhammaṃ me bhaṇamānassa, na pāpamupalimpati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
Yena kenaci vaṇṇena, paro labhati ruppanaṃ;
```

```
Mahatthiyampi ce vācaṃ, na taṃ bhāseyya paṇḍito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
Kāmaṃ ruppatu vā mā vā, bhusaṃva vikirīyatu;
```

```
Dhammaṃ me bhaṇamānassa, na pāpamupalimpati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
No ce assa sakā buddhi, vinayo vā susikkhito;
```

```
Vane andhamahiṃsova <note>andhamahisova (sī. pī.)</note> careyya bahuko jano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
Yasmā ca panidhekacce, āceramhi <note>ācāramhi (sī. pī.)</note> susikkhitā;
```

```
Tasmā vinītavinayā, caranti susamāhitāti.
```

Gandhārajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 407. Mahākapijātakaṃ (7-2-2)

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
Attānaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0225" /> saṅkamaṃ katvā, yo sotthiṃ samatārayi;
```

```
Kiṃ tvaṃ tesaṃ kime <note>kimo (sī. pī.), kiṃ me (syā.)</note> tuyhaṃ, honti ete <note>hete (syā.), so te (ka.)</note> mahākapi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
Rājāhaṃ issaro tesaṃ, yūthassa parihārako;
```

```
Tesaṃ sokaparetānaṃ, bhītānaṃ te arindama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
Ullaṅghayitvā <note>sa laṅghayitvā (pī.), sulaṅghayitvā (ka.)</note> attānaṃ, vissaṭṭhadhanuno sataṃ;
```

```
Tato aparapādesu, daḷhaṃ bandhaṃ latāguṇaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
Chinnabbhamiva <pb ed="M" n="1.0166" /> vātena, nuṇṇo <note>nunno (sī.)</note> rukkhaṃ upāgamiṃ;
```

```
Sohaṃ appabhavaṃ tattha, sākhaṃ hatthehi aggahiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
Taṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0137" /> maṃ viyāyataṃ santaṃ, sākhāya ca latāya ca;
```

```
Samanukkamantā pādehi, sotthiṃ sākhāmigā gatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
Taṃ maṃ na tapate bandho, mato <note>vadho (sī. syā. pī.)</note> me na tapessati;
```

```
Sukhamāharitaṃ tesaṃ, yesaṃ rajjamakārayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
Esā te upamā rāja, taṃ suṇohi arindama <note>atthasandassanī katā (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Raññā raṭṭhassa yoggassa, balassa nigamassa ca;
```

```
Sabbesaṃ sukhameṭṭhabbaṃ, khattiyena pajānatāti.
```

Mahākapijātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 408. Kumbhakārajātakaṃ (7-2-3)

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
Ambāhamaddaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0226" /> vanamantarasmiṃ, nīlobhāsaṃ phalitaṃ <note>phalinaṃ (pī.)</note> saṃvirūḷhaṃ;
```

```
Tamaddasaṃ phalahetu vibhaggaṃ, taṃ disvā bhikkhācariyaṃ carāmi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
Selaṃ sumaṭṭhaṃ naravīraniṭṭhitaṃ <note>naravidduniṭṭhitaṃ (ka.)</note>, nārī yugaṃ dhārayi appasaddaṃ;
```

```
Dutiyañca āgamma ahosi saddo, taṃ disvā bhikkhācariyaṃ carāmi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
Dijā dijaṃ kuṇapamāharantaṃ, ekaṃ samānaṃ bahukā samecca;
```

```
Āhārahetū paripātayiṃsu, taṃ disvā bhikkhācariyaṃ carāmi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§93.</p>

```
Usabhāhamaddaṃ yūthassa majjhe, calakkakuṃ vaṇṇabalūpapannaṃ;
```

```
Tamaddasaṃ kāmahetu vitunnaṃ, taṃ disvā bhikkhācariyaṃ carāmi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§94.</p>

```
Karaṇḍako <pb ed="M" n="1.0167" /> <note>karaṇḍunāma (sī. pī.)</note> kaliṅgānaṃ, gandhārānañca naggaji;
```

```
Nimirājā videhānaṃ, pañcālānañca dummukho;
```

```
Ete raṭṭhāni hitvāna, pabbajiṃsu akiñcanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§95.</p>

```
Sabbepime <pb ed="T" n="1.0227" /> devasamā samāgatā, aggī yathā pajjalito tathevime;
```

```
Ahampi eko carissāmi bhaggavi, hitvāna kāmāni yathodhikāni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§96.</p>

```
Ayameva kālo na hi añño atthi, anusāsitā me na bhaveyya pacchā;
```

```
Ahampi ekā carissāmi bhaggava, sakuṇīva muttā purisassa hatthā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§97.</p>

```
Āmaṃ pakkañca jānanti, atho loṇaṃ aloṇakaṃ;
```

```
Tamahaṃ disvāna pabbajiṃ, careva tvaṃ carāmahanti.
```

Kumbhakārajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 409. Daḷhadhammajātakaṃ (7-2-4)

<p rend="hangnum">§98.</p>

```
Ahaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0138" /> ce daḷhadhammassa <note>daḷhadhammāya (pī.)</note>, vahanti nābhirādhayiṃ;
```

```
Dharantī urasi sallaṃ, yuddhe vikkantacārinī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§99.</p>

```
Nūna rājā na jānāti <note>na ha nūna rājā jānāti (sī. pī.)</note>, mama vikkamaporisaṃ;
```

```
Saṅgāme sukatantāni, dūtavippahitāni ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§100.</p>

```
Sā nūnāhaṃ marissāmi, abandhu aparāyinī <note>aparāyiṇī (sī.), aparāyaṇī (?)</note>;
```

```
Tadā <pb ed="T" n="1.0228" /> hi <note>tathā hi (pī.)</note> kumbhakārassa, dinnā chakaṇahārikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§101.</p>

```
Yāvatāsīsatī poso, tāvadeva pavīṇati;
```

```
Atthāpāye jahanti naṃ, oṭṭhibyādhiṃva khattiyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§102.</p>

```
Yo pubbe katakalyāṇo, katattho nāvabujjhati;
```

```
Atthā tassa palujjanti, ye honti abhipatthitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§103.</p>

```
Yo <pb ed="M" n="1.0168" /> pubbe katakalyāṇo, katattho manubujjhati;
```

```
Atthā tassa pavaḍḍhanti, ye honti abhipatthitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§104.</p>

```
Taṃ vo vadāmi bhaddante <note>bhaddaṃ vo (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, yāvantettha samāgatā;
```

```
Sabbe kataññuno hotha, ciraṃ saggamhi ṭhassathāti.
```

Daḷhadhammajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 410. Somadattajātakaṃ (7-2-5)

<p rend="hangnum">§105.</p>

```
Yo maṃ pure paccuḍḍeti <note>paccudeti (sī. syā. pī.), paccuṭṭheti (ka.)</note>, araññe dūramāyato;
```

```
So na dissati mātaṅgo, somadatto kuhiṃ gato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§106.</p>

```
Ayaṃ vā so mato seti, allasiṅgaṃva vacchito <note>allapiṅkava chijjito (sī. pī.), allapītaṃva vicchito (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Bhumyā nipatito seti, amarā vata kuñjaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§107.</p>

```
Anagāriyupetassa, vippamuttassa te sato;
```

```
Samaṇassa na taṃ sādhu, yaṃ petamanusocasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§108.</p>

```
Saṃvāsena have sakka, manussassa migassa vā;
```

```
