Hadaye <pb ed="T" n="1.0229" /> jāyate pemaṃ, taṃ na sakkā asocituṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§109.</p>

```
Mataṃ marissaṃ rodanti, ye rudanti lapanti ca;
```

```
Tasmā tvaṃ isi mā rodi, roditaṃ moghamāhu santo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§110.</p>

```
Kanditena <pb ed="V" n="1.0139" /> have brahme, mato peto samuṭṭhahe;
```

```
Sabbe saṅgamma rodāma, aññamaññassa ñātake.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§111.</p>

```
Ādittaṃ vata maṃ santaṃ, ghatasittaṃva pāvakaṃ;
```

```
Vārinā viya osiñcaṃ, sabbaṃ nibbāpaye daraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§112.</p>

```
Abbahī vata me sallaṃ, yamāsi hadayassitaṃ;
```

```
Yo me sokaparetassa, puttasokaṃ apānudi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§113.</p>

```
Sohaṃ abbūḷhasallosmi, vītasoko anāvilo;
```

```
Na socāmi na rodāmi, tava sutvāna vāsavāti.
```

Somadattajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 411. Susīmajātakaṃ (7-2-6)

<p rend="hangnum">§114.</p>

```
Kāḷāni <pb ed="M" n="1.0169" /> kesāni pure ahesuṃ, jātāni sīsamhi yathāpadese;
```

```
Tānajja setāni susīma <note>susima (ka.)</note> disvā, dhammaṃ cara brahmacariyassa kālo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§115.</p>

```
Mameva deva palitaṃ na tuyhaṃ, mameva sīsaṃ mama uttamaṅgaṃ;
```

```
‘‘Atthaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0230" /> karissa’’nti musā abhāṇiṃ <note>abhāsiṃ (ka.)</note>, ekāparādhaṃ khama rājaseṭṭha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§116.</p>

```
Daharo tuvaṃ dassaniyosi rāja, paṭhamuggato hosi <note>hohi (sī.), hoti (ka.)</note> yathā kaḷīro;
```

```
Rajjañca kārehi mamañca passa, mā kālikaṃ anudhāvī janinda.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§117.</p>

```
Passāmi vohaṃ dahariṃ kumāriṃ, sāmaṭṭhapassaṃ sutanuṃ sumajjhaṃ;
```

```
Kāḷappavāḷāva pavellamānā, palobhayantīva <note>sā lobhayantīva (pī.)</note> naresu gacchati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§118.</p>

```
Tamena passāmiparena nāriṃ, āsītikaṃ nāvutikaṃ va jaccā;
```

```
Daṇḍaṃ gahetvāna pavedhamānaṃ, gopānasībhoggasamaṃ carantiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§119.</p>

```
Sohaṃ tamevānuvicintayanto, eko sayāmi <note>passāmi (ka.)</note> sayanassa majjhe;
```

```
‘‘Ahampi evaṃ’’ iti pekkhamāno, na gahe rame <note>na gehe rame (sī.), gehe na rame (syā. ka.)</note> brahmacariyassa kālo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§120.</p>

```
Rajjuvālambanī <pb ed="M" n="1.0170" /> cesā, yā gehe vasato rati;
```

```
Evampi <pb ed="T" n="1.0231" /> chetvāna vajanti dhīrā, anapekkhino kāmasukhaṃ pahāyāti.
```

Susīmajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 412. Koṭasimbalijātakaṃ (7-2-7)

<p rend="hangnum">§121.</p>

```
Ahaṃ dasasataṃbyāmaṃ, uragamādāya āgato;
```

```
Tañca mañca mahākāyaṃ, dhārayaṃ nappavedhasi <note>na pavedhayi (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§122.</p>

```
Athimaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0140" /> khuddakaṃ pakkhiṃ, appamaṃsataraṃ mayā;
```

```
Dhārayaṃ byathasi <note>byādhase (sī.), byadhase (pī.), byādhasi (ka.)</note> bhītā <note>bhīto (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, kamatthaṃ koṭasimbali <note>koṭisimbali (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§123.</p>

```
Maṃsabhakkho tuvaṃ rāja, phalabhakkho ayaṃ dijo;
```

```
Ayaṃ nigrodhabījāni, pilakkhudumbarāni ca;
```

```
Assatthāni ca bhakkhitvā, khandhe me ohadissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§124.</p>

```
Te rukkhā saṃvirūhanti, mama passe nivātajā;
```

```
Te maṃ pariyonandhissanti, arukkhaṃ maṃ karissare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§125.</p>

```
Santi aññepi rukkhā se, mūlino khandhino dumā;
```

```
Iminā sakuṇajātena, bījamāharitā hatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§126.</p>

```
Ajjhārūhābhivaḍḍhanti <note>ajjhārūḷhābhivaḍḍhanti (sī. pī.)</note>, brahantampi vanappatiṃ;
```

```
Tasmā rāja pavedhāmi, sampassaṃnāgataṃ bhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§127.</p>

```
Saṅkeyya saṅkitabbāni, rakkheyyānāgataṃ bhayaṃ;
```

```
Anāgatabhayā <pb ed="T" n="1.0232" /> dhīro, ubho loke avekkhatīti.
```

Koṭasimbalijātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 413. Dhūmakārijātakaṃ (7-2-8)

<p rend="hangnum">§128.</p>

```
Rājā apucchi vidhuraṃ, dhammakāmo yudhiṭṭhilo;
```

```
Api brāhmaṇa jānāsi, ko eko bahu socati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§129.</p>

```
Brāhmaṇo <pb ed="M" n="1.0171" /> ajayūthena, pahūtedho <note>bahūtejo (pī. ka.), bahutendo (syā.)</note> vane vasaṃ;
```

```
Dhūmaṃ akāsi vāseṭṭho, rattindivamatandito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§130.</p>

```
Tassa taṃ dhūmagandhena, sarabhā makasaḍḍitā <note>makasadditā (sī. syā.), makasaṭṭitā (pī. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Vassāvāsaṃ upāgacchuṃ, dhūmakārissa santike.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§131.</p>

```
Sarabhesu manaṃ katvā, ajā so nāvabujjhatha;
```

```
Āgacchantī vajantī vā <note>āgacchanti vajanti vā (syā. pī.), āgacchantiṃ vajantiṃ vā (ka.)</note>, tassa tā vinasuṃ <note>vinassuṃ (sī.)</note> ajā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§132.</p>

```
Sarabhā sarade kāle, pahīnamakase vane;
```

```
Pāvisuṃ giriduggāni, nadīnaṃ pabhavāni ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§133.</p>

```
Sarabhe ca gate disvā, ajā ca vibhavaṃ gatā <note>aje ca vibhavaṃ gate (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Kiso ca vivaṇṇo cāsi, paṇḍurogī ca brāhmaṇo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§134.</p>

```
Evaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0141" /> yo saṃ niraṃkatvā, āgantuṃ kurute piyaṃ;
```

```
So eko bahu socati, dhūmakārīva brāhmaṇoti.
```

Dhūmakārijātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 414. Jāgarajātakaṃ (7-2-9)

<p rend="hangnum">§135.</p>

```
Kodha <pb ed="T" n="1.0233" /> jāgarataṃ sutto, kodha suttesu jāgaro;
```

```
Ko mametaṃ vijānāti, ko taṃ paṭibhaṇāti me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§136.</p>

```
Ahaṃ jāgarataṃ sutto, ahaṃ suttesu jāgaro;
```

```
Ahametaṃ vijānāmi, ahaṃ paṭibhaṇāmi te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§137.</p>

```
Kathaṃ jāgarataṃ sutto, kathaṃ suttesu jāgaro;
```

```
Kathaṃ etaṃ vijānāsi, kathaṃ paṭibhaṇāsi me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§138.</p>

```
Ye dhammaṃ nappajānanti, saṃyamoti damoti ca;
```

```
Tesu suppamānesu, ahaṃ jaggāmi devate.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§139.</p>

```
Yesaṃ rāgo ca doso ca, avijjā ca virājitā;
```

```
Tesu jāgaramānesu, ahaṃ suttosmi devate.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§140.</p>

```
Evaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0172" /> jāgarataṃ sutto, evaṃ suttesu jāgaro;
```

```
Evametaṃ vijānāmi, evaṃ paṭibhaṇāmi te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§141.</p>

```
Sādhu jāgarataṃ sutto, sādhu suttesu jāgaro;
```

```
Sādhumetaṃ vijānāsi, sādhu paṭibhaṇāsi meti.
```

Jāgarajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 415. Kummāsapiṇḍijātakaṃ (7-2-10)

<p rend="hangnum">§142.</p>

```
Na kiratthi anomadassisu, pāricariyā buddhesu appikā <note>appakā (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Sukkhāya <pb ed="T" n="1.0234" /> aloṇikāya ca, passaphalaṃ kummāsapiṇḍiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§143.</p>

```
Hatthigavassā cime bahū <note>hatthigavāssā ca me bahū (sī.), hatthī gavāssā cime bahū (syā.), hatthī gavāssā ca me bahū (pī.)</note>, dhanadhaññaṃ pathavī ca kevalā;
```

```
Nāriyo cimā accharūpamā, passaphalaṃ kummāsapiṇḍiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§144.</p>

```
Abhikkhaṇaṃ rājakuñjara, gāthā bhāsasi kosalādhipa;
```

```
Pucchāmi taṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhana, bāḷhaṃ pītimano pabhāsasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§145.</p>

```
Imasmiññeva nagare, kule aññatare ahuṃ;
```

```
Parakammakaro āsiṃ, bhatako sīlasaṃvuto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§146.</p>

```
Kammāya <pb ed="V" n="1.0142" /> nikkhamantohaṃ, caturo samaṇeddasaṃ;
```

```
Ācārasīlasampanne, sītibhūte anāsave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§147.</p>

```
Tesu cittaṃ pasādetvā, nisīdetvā <note>nisādetvā (?)</note> paṇṇasanthate;
```

```
Adaṃ buddhāna kummāsaṃ, pasanno sehi pāṇibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§148.</p>

```
Tassa <pb ed="M" n="1.0173" /> kammassa kusalassa, idaṃ me edisaṃ phalaṃ;
```

```
Anubhomi idaṃ rajjaṃ, phītaṃ dharaṇimuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§149.</p>

```
Dadaṃ bhuñja mā ca pamādo <note>dada bhuñja ca mā ca pamādo (sī. pī.)</note>, cakkaṃ vattaya kosalādhipa;
```

```
Mā <pb ed="T" n="1.0235" /> rāja adhammiko ahu, dhammaṃ pālaya kosalādhipa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§150.</p>

```
Sohaṃ tadeva punappunaṃ, vaṭumaṃ ācarissāmi sobhane;
```

```
Ariyācaritaṃ sukosale, arahanto me manāpāva passituṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§151.</p>

```
Devī viya accharūpamā, majjhe nārigaṇassa sobhasi;
```

```
Kiṃ kammamakāsi bhaddakaṃ, kenāsi vaṇṇavatī sukosale.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§152.</p>

```
Ambaṭṭhakulassa khattiya, dāsyāhaṃ parapesiyā ahuṃ;
```

```
Saññatā ca <note>saññatā (sī. pī.)</note> dhammajīvinī, sīlavatī ca apāpadassanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§153.</p>

```
Uddhaṭabhattaṃ ahaṃ tadā, caramānassa adāsi bhikkhuno;
```

```
Vittā sumanā sayaṃ ahaṃ, tassa kammassa phalaṃ mamedisanti.
```

Kummāsapiṇḍijātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

#### 416. Parantapajātakaṃ (7-2-11)

<p rend="hangnum">§154.</p>

```
Āgamissati <pb ed="T" n="1.0236" /> me pāpaṃ, āgamissati me bhayaṃ;
```

```
Tadā hi calitā sākhā, manussena migena vā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§155.</p>

```
Bhīruyā nūna me kāmo, avidūre vasantiyā;
```

```
Karissati kisaṃ paṇḍuṃ, sāva sākhā parantapaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§156.</p>

```
Socayissati <pb ed="M" n="1.0174" /> maṃ kantā, gāme vasamaninditā;
```

```
Karissati kisaṃ paṇḍuṃ, sāva sākhā parantapaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§157.</p>

```
Tayā maṃ asitāpaṅgi <note>hasitāpaṅgi (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, sitāni <note>mihitāni (sī. syā. pī.)</note> bhaṇitāni ca;
```

```
Kisaṃ paṇḍuṃ karissanti, sāva sākhā parantapaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§158.</p>

```
Agamā nūna so saddo, asaṃsi nūna so tava;
```

```
Akkhātaṃ nūna taṃ tena, yo taṃ sākhamakampayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§159.</p>

```
Idaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0143" /> kho taṃ samāgamma, mama bālassa cintitaṃ;
```

```
Tadā hi calitā sākhā, manussena migena vā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§160.</p>

```
Tatheva tvaṃ avedesi, avañci <note>avajjhi (ka.)</note> pitaraṃ mama;
```

```
Hantvā sākhāhi chādento, āgamissati me <note>te (syā. ka.)</note> bhayanti.
```

Parantapajātakaṃ ekādasamaṃ.

Gandhāravaggo dutiyo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Varagāma <pb ed="T" n="1.0237" /> mahākapi bhaggava ca, daḷhadhamma sakuñjara kesavaro;
```

```
Urago vidhuro puna jāgarataṃ, atha kosalādhipa parantapa cāti.
```

Atha vagguddānaṃ –

```
Atha sattanipātamhi, vaggaṃ me bhaṇato suṇa;
```

```
Kukku ca puna gandhāro, dveva guttā mahesināti.
```

<trailer rend="centre">Sattakanipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.</trailer>

### 8. Aṭṭhakanipāto

#### 417. Kaccānijātakaṃ (1)

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
Odātavatthā <pb ed="T" n="1.0238" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0144" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0175" /> suci allakesā, kaccāni kiṃ kumbhimadhissayitvā <note>kumbhimapassayitvā (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Piṭṭhā tilā dhovasi taṇḍulāni, tilodano hehiti kissa hetu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
Na kho ayaṃ brāhmaṇa bhojanatthā <note>bhojanatthaṃ (syā.)</note>, tilodano hehiti sādhupakko;
```

```
Dhammo mato tassa pahuttamajja <note>pahūnamajja (syā.), pahūtamajja (sī.), bahūtamajjā (pī.)</note>, ahaṃ karissāmi susānamajjhe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
Anuvicca kaccāni karohi kiccaṃ, dhammo mato ko nu taveva <note>taveta (sī. syā. pī.)</note> saṃsi;
```

```
Sahassanetto atulānubhāvo, na miyyatī dhammavaro kadāci.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
Daḷhappamāṇaṃ mama ettha brahme, dhammo mato natthi mamettha kaṅkhā;
```

```
Ye yeva dāni pāpā bhavanti, te <pb ed="T" n="1.0239" /> teva dāni sukhitā bhavanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
Suṇisā hi mayhaṃ vañjhā ahosi, sā maṃ vadhitvāna vijāyi puttaṃ;
```

```
Sā dāni sabbassa kulassa issarā, ahaṃ panamhi <note>vasāmi (syā.)</note> apaviddhā ekikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
Jīvāmi <pb ed="M" n="1.0176" /> vohaṃ na matohamasmi <note>nāhaṃ matosmi (sī. pī.)</note>, taveva atthāya idhāgatosmi;
```

```
Yā taṃ vadhitvāna vijāyi puttaṃ, sahāva puttena karomi bhasmaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
Evañca <note>etañca (sī. pī.)</note> te ruccati devarāja, mameva atthāya idhāgatosi;
```

```
Ahañca putto suṇisā ca nattā, sammodamānā gharamāvasema.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
Evañca te ruccati kātiyāni, hatāpi santā na jahāsi dhammaṃ;
```

```
Tuvañca <note>tvañca (pī. ka.)</note> putto suṇisā ca nattā, sammodamānā gharamāvasetha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
Sā kātiyānī suṇisāya saddhiṃ, sammodamānā gharamāvasittha;
```

```
Putto <pb ed="T" n="1.0240" /> ca nattā ca upaṭṭhahiṃsu, devānamindena adhiggahītāti.
```

Kaccānijātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 418. Aṭṭhasaddajātakaṃ (2)

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
Idaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0145" /> pure ninnamāhu, bahumacchaṃ mahodakaṃ;
```

```
Āvāso bakarājassa, pettikaṃ bhavanaṃ mama;
```

```
Tyajja bhekena <note>bhiṅgena (ka.)</note> yāpema, okaṃ na vajahāmase <note>okantaṃ na jahāmase (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
Ko dutiyaṃ asīlissa, bandharassakkhi bhecchati <note>bhejjati (sī. syā. pī.), bhindati (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Ko me putte kulāvakaṃ, mañca sotthiṃ karissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
Sabbā parikkhayā pheggu, yāva tassā gatī ahu;
```

```
Khīṇabhakkho mahārāja, sāre na ramatī ghuṇo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
Sā <pb ed="M" n="1.0177" /> nūnāhaṃ ito gantvā, rañño muttā nivesanā;
```

```
Attānaṃ ramayissāmi, dumasākhaniketinī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
So nūnāhaṃ ito gantvā, rañño mutto nivesanā;
```

```
Aggodakāni pissāmi, yūthassa purato vajaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
Taṃ maṃ kāmehi sammattaṃ, rattaṃ kāmesu mucchitaṃ;
```

```
Ānayī bharato <note>vanato (ka.)</note> luddo, bāhiko bhaddamatthu te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
Andhakāratimisāyaṃ, tuṅge uparipabbate;
```

```
Sā <pb ed="T" n="1.0241" /> maṃ saṇhena mudunā, mā pādaṃ khali <note>khaṇi (sī. syā. pī.)</note> yasmani.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
Asaṃsayaṃ jātikhayantadassī, na gabbhaseyyaṃ punarāvajissaṃ;
```

```
Ayamantimā pacchimā gabbhaseyyā <note>ayaṃ hi me antimā gabbhaseyyā (sī. pī.)</note>, khīṇo me saṃsāro punabbhavāyāti.
```

Aṭṭhasaddajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 419. Sulasājātakaṃ (3)

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
Idaṃ suvaṇṇakāyūraṃ, muttā veḷuriyā bahū;
```

```
Sabbaṃ harassu bhaddante, mañca dāsīti sāvaya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
Oropayassu kalyāṇi, mā bāḷhaṃ <note>bahuṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> paridevasi;
```

```
Na cāhaṃ abhijānāmi, ahantvā dhanamābhataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
Yato sarāmi attānaṃ, yato pattāsmi viññutaṃ;
```

```
Na cāhaṃ abhijānāmi, aññaṃ piyataraṃ tayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
Ehi taṃ upagūhissaṃ <note>upaguyhissaṃ (ka.)</note>, karissañca padakkhiṇaṃ;
```

```
Na hi dāni puna atthi, mama tuyhañca saṅgamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="V" n="1.0146" /> hi sabbesu ṭhānesu, puriso hoti paṇḍito;
```

```
Itthīpi paṇḍitā hoti, tattha tattha vicakkhaṇā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="M" n="1.0178" /> hi sabbesu ṭhānesu, puriso hoti paṇḍito;
```

```
Itthīpi <pb ed="T" n="1.0242" /> paṇḍitā hoti, lahuṃ atthaṃ vicintikā <note>lahumatthavicintikā (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
Lahuñca vata khippañca, nikaṭṭhe samacetayi;
```

```
Migaṃ puṇṇāyateneva <note>puṇṇāyataneva (syā.)</note>, sulasā sattukaṃ vadhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
Yodha uppatitaṃ atthaṃ, na khippamanubujjhati;
```

```
So haññati mandamati, corova girigabbhare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
Yo ca uppatitaṃ atthaṃ, khippameva nibodhati;
```

```
Muccate sattusambādhā, sulasā sattukāmivāti.
```

Sulasājātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 420. Sumaṅgalajātakaṃ (4)

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
Bhusamhi <note>bhusampi (ka.), bhusaṃ hi (sī. niyya)</note> kuddhoti avekkhiyāna, na tāva daṇḍaṃ paṇayeyya issaro;
```

```
Aṭṭhānaso appatirūpamattano, parassa dukkhāni bhusaṃ udīraye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
Yato ca jāneyya pasādamattano, atthaṃ niyuñjeyya parassa dukkaṭaṃ;
```

```
Tadāyamatthoti sayaṃ avekkhiya, athassa daṇḍaṃ sadisaṃ nivesaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
Na cāpi jhāpeti paraṃ na attanaṃ, amucchito yo nayate nayānayaṃ;
```

```
Yo <pb ed="T" n="1.0243" /> daṇḍadhāro bhavatīdha issaro, sa vaṇṇagutto siriyā na dhaṃsati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
Ye khattiyā se anisammakārino, paṇenti daṇḍaṃ sahasā pamucchitā;
```

```
Avaṇṇasaṃyutā <note>yuttāva (ka.)</note> jahanti jīvitaṃ, ito vimuttāpi ca yanti duggatiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
Dhamme <pb ed="M" n="1.0179" /> ca ye ariyappavedite ratā, anuttarā te vacasā manasā kammunā ca;
```

```
Te santisoraccasamādhisaṇṭhitā, vajanti lokaṃ dubhayaṃ tathāvidhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
Rājāhamasmi narapamadānamissaro, sacepi kujjhāmi ṭhapemi attanaṃ;
```

```
Nisedhayanto janataṃ tathāvidhaṃ, paṇemi daṇḍaṃ anukampa yoniso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
Sirī ca lakkhī ca taveva khattiya, janādhipa mā vijahi kudācanaṃ;
```

```
Akkodhano niccapasannacitto, anīgho tuvaṃ vassasatāni pālaya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
Guṇehi etehi upeta khattiya, ṭhitamariyavattī <note>vatti (sī.), vutti (ka.)</note> suvaco akodhano;
```

```
Sukhī <pb ed="T" n="1.0244" /> anuppīḷa pasāsamediniṃ <note>anuppīḷaṃ sahasamedaniṃ (ka.)</note>, ito vimuttopi ca yāhi suggatiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
Evaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0147" /> sunītena <note>suvinītena (pī.)</note> subhāsitena, dhammena ñāyena upāyaso nayaṃ;
```

```
Nibbāpaye saṅkhubhitaṃ mahājanaṃ, mahāva megho salilena medininti <note>medaninti (syā. ka.)</note>.
```

Sumaṅgalajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 421. Gaṅgamālajātakaṃ (5)

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
Aṅgārajātā pathavī, kukkuḷānugatā mahī;
```

```
Atha gāyasi vattāni <note>vatthāni (ka.)</note>, na taṃ tapati ātapo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
Uddhaṃ tapati ādicco, adho tapati vālukā;
```

```
Atha gāyasi vattāni <note>vatthāni (ka.)</note>, na taṃ tapati ātapo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="M" n="1.0180" /> maṃ tapati ātapo, ātapā <note>ātappā (sī. syā. pī.)</note> tapayanti maṃ;
```

```
Atthā hi vividhā rāja, te tapanti na ātapo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
Addasaṃ kāma te mūlaṃ, saṅkappā kāma jāyasi;
```

```
Na taṃ saṅkappayissāmi, evaṃ kāma na hehisi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
Appāpi kāmā na alaṃ, bahūhipi na tappati;
```

```
Ahahā bālalapanā, parivajjetha <note>paṭivijjhetha (pī. sī. aṭṭha.)</note> jaggato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
Appassa <pb ed="T" n="1.0245" /> kammassa phalaṃ mamedaṃ, udayo ajjhāgamā mahattapattaṃ;
```

```
Suladdhalābho vata māṇavassa, yo pabbajī kāmarāgaṃ pahāya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
Tapasā pajahanti pāpakammaṃ, tapasā nhāpitakumbhakārabhāvaṃ;
```

```
Tapasā abhibhuyya gaṅgamāla, nāmenālapasajja brahmadattaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
Sandiṭṭhikameva ‘‘amma’’ passatha, khantīsoraccassa ayaṃ <note>yo (syā. pī. ka.)</note> vipāko;
```

```
Yo <note>so (syā. ka.)</note> sabbajanassa vanditohu, taṃ vandāma sarājikā samaccā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
Mā kiñci avacuttha gaṅgamālaṃ, muninaṃ monapathesu sikkhamānaṃ;
```

```
Eso hi atari aṇṇavaṃ, yaṃ taritvā caranti vītasokāti.
```

Gaṅgamālajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 422. Cetiyajātakaṃ (6)

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
Dhammo <pb ed="T" n="1.0246" /> have hato hanti, nāhato hanti kiñcanaṃ <note>kañcinaṃ (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Tasmā hi dhammaṃ na hane, mā tvaṃ <note>taṃ (syā. pī.)</note> dhammo hato hani.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
Alikaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0148" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0181" /> bhāsamānassa, apakkamanti devatā;
```

```
Pūtikañca mukhaṃ vāti, sakaṭṭhānā ca dhaṃsati;
```

```
Yo jānaṃ pucchito pañhaṃ, aññathā naṃ viyākare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
Sace hi saccaṃ bhaṇasi, hohi rāja yathā pure;
```

```
Musā ce bhāsase rāja, bhūmiyaṃ tiṭṭha cetiya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
Akāle vassatī tassa, kāle tassa na vassati;
```

```
Yo jānaṃ pucchito pañhaṃ, aññathā naṃ viyākare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
Sace hi saccaṃ bhaṇasi, hohi rāja yathā pure;
```

```
Musā ce bhāsase rāja, bhūmiṃ pavisa cetiya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
Jivhā tassa dvidhā hoti, uragasseva disampati;
```

```
Yo jānaṃ pucchito pañhaṃ, aññathā naṃ viyākare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
Sace hi saccaṃ bhaṇasi, hohi rāja yathā pure;
```

```
Musā ce bhāsase rāja, bhiyyo pavisa cetiya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
Jivhā tassa na bhavati, macchasseva disampati;
```

```
Yo jānaṃ pucchito pañhaṃ, aññathā naṃ viyākare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
Sace hi saccaṃ bhaṇasi, hohi rāja yathā pure;
```

```
Musā ce bhāsase rāja, bhiyyo pavisa cetiya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
Thiyova <pb ed="T" n="1.0247" /> tassa jāyanti <note>thiyo tassa pajāyanti (ka.)</note>, na pumā jāyare kule;
```

```
Yo jānaṃ pucchito pañhaṃ, aññathā naṃ viyākare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
Sace hi saccaṃ bhaṇasi, hohi rāja yathā pure;
```

```
Musā ce bhāsase rāja, bhiyyo pavisa cetiya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
Puttā tassa na bhavanti, pakkamanti disodisaṃ;
```

```
Yo jānaṃ pucchito pañhaṃ, aññathā naṃ viyākare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
Sace hi saccaṃ bhaṇasi, hohi rāja yathā pure;
```

```
Musā ce bhāsase rāja, bhiyyo pavisa cetiya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
Sa <pb ed="M" n="1.0182" /> rājā isinā satto, antalikkhacaro pure;
```

```
Pāvekkhi pathaviṃ cecco, hīnatto patva pariyāyaṃ <note>attapariyāyaṃ (sī. syā.), pattapariyāyaṃ (ka. sī. niyya)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
Tasmā <pb ed="V" n="1.0149" /> hi chandāgamanaṃ, nappasaṃsanti paṇḍitā;
```

```
Aduṭṭhacitto bhāseyya, giraṃ saccūpasaṃhitanti.
```

Cetiyajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 423. Indriyajātakaṃ (7)

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
Yo indriyānaṃ kāmena, vasaṃ nārada gacchati;
```

```
So pariccajjubho loke, jīvantova visussati <note>jīvantopivisussati (syā.), jīvanto vāpi sussati (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
Sukhassānantaraṃ dukkhaṃ, dukkhassānantaraṃ sukhaṃ;
```

```
Sosi <note>sopi (syā. pī. ka.)</note> patto sukhā <note>sukha (syā.), sukhaṃ (ka.)</note> dukkhaṃ, pāṭikaṅkha varaṃ sukhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
Kicchakāle <pb ed="T" n="1.0248" /> kicchasaho, yo kicchaṃ nātivattati;
```

```
Sa kicchantaṃ sukhaṃ dhīro, yogaṃ samadhigacchati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
Na heva kāmāna kāmā, nānatthā nātthakāraṇā;
```

```
Na katañca niraṅkatvā, dhammā cavitumarahasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
Dakkhaṃ gahapatī <note>gahapataṃ (sī. syā. pī.), gahavataṃ (?)</note> sādhu, saṃvibhajjañca bhojanaṃ;
```

```
Ahāso atthalābhesu, atthabyāpatti abyatho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
Ettāvatetaṃ paṇḍiccaṃ, api so <note>asito (sī. syā. pī.)</note> davilo <note>devalo (sī. pī.)</note> bravi;
```

```
Na yito kiñci pāpiyo, yo indriyānaṃ vasaṃ vaje.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
Amittānaṃva hatthatthaṃ, sivi pappoti māmiva;
```

```
Kammaṃ vijjañca dakkheyyaṃ, vivāhaṃ sīlamaddavaṃ;
```

```
Ete ca yase hāpetvā, nibbatto sehi kammehi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
Sohaṃ sahassajīnova abandhu aparāyaṇo;
```

```
Ariyadhammā apakkanto, yathā peto tathevahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
Sukhakāme <pb ed="M" n="1.0183" /> dukkhāpetvā, āpannosmi padaṃ imaṃ;
```

```
So sukhaṃ nādhigacchāmi, ṭhito <note>cito (pī. sī. aṭṭha.)</note> bhāṇumatāmivāti.
```

Indriyajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 424. Ādittajātakaṃ (8)

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
Ādittasmiṃ agārasmiṃ, yaṃ nīharati bhājanaṃ;
```

```
Taṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0249" /> tassa hoti atthāya, no ca yaṃ tattha ḍayhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
Evāmādīpito <pb ed="V" n="1.0150" /> loko, jarāya maraṇena ca;
```

```
Nīharetheva dānena, dinnaṃ hoti sunīhataṃ <note>sunībhataṃ (sī. syā. pī.), sunibbhataṃ (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
Yo dhammaladdhassa dadāti dānaṃ, uṭṭhānavīriyādhigatassa jantu;
```

```
Atikkamma so vetaraṇiṃ <note>vettaraṇiṃ (ka.)</note> yamassa, dibbāni ṭhānāni upeti macco.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
Dānañca yuddhañca samānamāhu, appāpi santā bahuke jinanti;
```

```
Appampi ce saddahāno dadāti, teneva so hoti sukhī parattha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
Viceyya dānaṃ sugatappasatthaṃ, ye dakkhiṇeyyā idha jīvaloke;
```

```
Etesu dinnāni mahapphalāni, bījāni vuttāni yathā sukhette.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
Yo pāṇabhūtāni aheṭhayaṃ caraṃ, parūpavādā na karoti pāpaṃ;
```

```
Bhīruṃ pasaṃsanti na tattha sūraṃ, bhayā hi santo na karonti pāpaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
Hīnena brahmacariyena, khattiye upapajjati;
```

```
Majjhimena <pb ed="T" n="1.0250" /> ca devattaṃ, uttamena visujjhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
Addhā <pb ed="M" n="1.0184" /> hi dānaṃ bahudhā pasatthaṃ, dānā ca kho dhammapadaṃva seyyo;
```

```
Pubbeva hi pubbatareva santo <note>pubbe ca hi pubbatare ca santo (saṃ. ni. 1.33)</note>, nibbānamevajjhagamuṃ sapaññāti.
```

Ādittajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 425. Aṭṭhānajātakaṃ (9)

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
Gaṅgā kumudinī santā, saṅkhavaṇṇā ca kokilā;
```

```
Jambu tālaphalaṃ dajjā, atha nūna tadā siyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
Yadā kacchapalomānaṃ, pāvāro tividho siyā;
```

```
Hemantikaṃ pāvuraṇaṃ <note>pāpuraṇaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, atha nūna tadā siyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
Yadā makasapādānaṃ <note>dāṭhānaṃ (sī. pī.)</note>, aṭṭālo sukato siyā;
```

```
Daḷho ca avikampī ca <note>appakampī ca (sī. pī.)</note>, atha nūna tadā siyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
Yadā sasavisāṇānaṃ, nisseṇī sukatā siyā;
```

```
Saggassārohaṇatthāya, atha nūna tadā siyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
Yadā nisseṇimāruyha, candaṃ khādeyyu mūsikā;
```

```
Rāhuñca paripāteyyuṃ <note>paribāheyyuṃ (syā.)</note>, atha nūna tadā siyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
Yadā surāghaṭaṃ pitvā, makkhikā gaṇacāriṇī;
```

```
Aṅgāre <pb ed="T" n="1.0251" /> vāsaṃ kappeyyuṃ, atha nūna tadā siyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
Yadā <pb ed="V" n="1.0151" /> bimboṭṭhasampanno, gadrabho sumukho siyā;
```

```
Kusalo naccagītassa, atha nūna tadā siyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
Yadā kākā ulūkā ca, mantayeyyuṃ rahogatā;
```

```
Aññamaññaṃ pihayeyyuṃ, atha nūna tadā siyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
Yadā muḷāla <note>pulasa (sī. pī.), pulāsa (syā.)</note> pattānaṃ, chattaṃ thirataraṃ siyā;
```

```
Vassassa paṭighātāya, atha nūna tadā siyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
Yadā <pb ed="M" n="1.0185" /> kulako <note>kuluṅko (sī. pī.), kuluko (syā.)</note> sakuṇo, pabbataṃ gandhamādanaṃ;
```

```
Tuṇḍenādāya gaccheyya, atha nūna tadā siyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
Yadā sāmuddikaṃ nāvaṃ, sa-yantaṃ sa-vaṭākaraṃ <note>sapaṭākāraṃ (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Ceṭo ādāya gaccheyya, atha nūna tadā siyāti.
```

Aṭṭhānajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 426. Dīpijātakaṃ (10)

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
Khamanīyaṃ yāpanīyaṃ, kacci mātula te sukhaṃ;
```

```
Sukhaṃ te ammā avaca, sukhakāmāva <note>sukhakāmā hi (sī. syā. pī.)</note> te mayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
Naṅguṭṭhaṃ me avakkamma <note>apakkamma (ka.)</note>, heṭhayitvāna <note>pothayitvāna (ka.)</note> eḷike <note>eḷaki (syā.), eḷiki (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Sājja mātulavādena, muñcitabbā nu maññasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
Puratthāmukho nisinnosi, ahaṃ te mukhamāgatā;
```

```
Pacchato tuyhaṃ naṅguṭṭhaṃ, kathaṃ khvāhaṃ avakkamiṃ <note>apakkamiṃ (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
Yāvatā <pb ed="T" n="1.0252" /> caturo dīpā, sasamuddā sapabbatā;
```

```
Tāvatā mayhaṃ naṅguṭṭhaṃ, kathaṃ kho tvaṃ vivajjayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
Pubbeva metamakkhiṃsu <note>metaṃ akkhaṃsu (sī. pī.)</note>, mātā pitā ca bhātaro;
```

```
Dīghaṃ duṭṭhassa naṅguṭṭhaṃ, sāmhi vehāyasāgatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§93.</p>

```
Tañca disvāna āyantiṃ, antalikkhasmi eḷike;
```

```
Migasaṅgho palāyittha, bhakkho me nāsito tayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§94.</p>

```
Iccevaṃ vilapantiyā, eḷakiyā ruhagghaso;
```

```
Galakaṃ anvāvamaddi, natthi duṭṭhe subhāsitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§95.</p>

```
Neva <pb ed="V" n="1.0152" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0186" /> duṭṭhe nayo atthi, na dhammo na subhāsitaṃ;
```

```
Nikkamaṃ duṭṭhe yuñjetha, so ca sabbhiṃ na rañjatīti.
```

Dīpijātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

<trailer rend="centre">Aṭṭhakanipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.</trailer>

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Parisuddhā manāvilā vatthadharā, bakarājassa kāyuraṃ daṇḍavaro;
```

```
Atha aṅgāra cetiya devilinā, atha āditta gaṅgā daseḷakināti.
```

### 9. Navakanipāto

#### 427. Gijjhajātakaṃ (1)

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
Parisaṅkupatho <pb ed="T" n="1.0253" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0153" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0187" /> nāma, gijjhapantho sanantano;
```

```
Tatrāsi mātāpitaro, gijjho posesi jiṇṇake;
```

```
Tesaṃ ajagaramedaṃ, accahāsi bahuttaso <note>pahuttato (ka. sī.), pahūtaso (syā. pī.), bahudhaso (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
Pitā ca puttaṃ avaca, jānaṃ uccaṃ papātinaṃ;
```

```
Supattaṃ thāmasampannaṃ <note>pakkhasampannaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, tejassiṃ dūragāminaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
Pariplavantaṃ pathaviṃ, yadā tāta vijānahi;
```

```
Sāgarena parikkhittaṃ, cakkaṃva parimaṇḍalaṃ;
```

```
Tato tāta nivattassu, māssu etto paraṃ gami.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
Udapattosi <note>uddhaṃ pattosi (ka. sī.)</note> vegena, balī pakkhī dijuttamo;
```

```
Olokayanto vakkaṅgo, pabbatāni vanāni ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
Addassa pathaviṃ gijjho, yathāsāsi <note>yathāssāsi (syā. aṭṭha. pāṭhantaraṃ)</note> pitussutaṃ;
```

```
Sāgarena parikkhittaṃ, cakkaṃva parimaṇḍalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
Tañca so samatikkamma, paramevaccavattatha <note>parameva pavattatha (sī. syā.)</note>;
```

```
Tañca vātasikhā tikkhā, accahāsi baliṃ dijaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
Nāsakkhātigato poso, punadeva nivattituṃ;
```

```
Dijo byasanamāpādi, verambhānaṃ <note>verambānaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> vasaṃ gato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
Tassa <pb ed="T" n="1.0254" /> puttā ca dārā ca, ye caññe anujīvino;
```

```
Sabbe byasanamāpāduṃ, anovādakare dije.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
Evampi idha vuḍḍhānaṃ, yo vākyaṃ nāvabujjhati;
```

```
Atisīmacaro ditto, gijjhovātītasāsano;
```

```
Sa ve byasanaṃ pappoti, akatvā vuḍḍhasāsananti.
```

Gijjhajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 428. Kosambiyajātakaṃ (2)

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
Puthusaddo <pb ed="V" n="1.0154" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0188" /> samajano, na bālo koci maññatha;
```

```
Saṅghasmiṃ bhijjamānasmiṃ, nāññaṃ bhiyyo amaññaruṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
Parimuṭṭhā paṇḍitābhāsā, vācāgocarabhāṇino;
```

```
Yāvicchanti mukhāyāmaṃ, yena nītā na taṃ vidū.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
Akkocchi maṃ avadhi maṃ, ajini maṃ ahāsi me;
```

```
Ye ca taṃ upanayhanti, veraṃ tesaṃ na sammati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
Akkocchi maṃ avadhi maṃ, ajini maṃ ahāsi me;
```

```
Ye ca taṃ nupanayhanti, veraṃ tesūpasammati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
Na hi verena verāni, sammantīdha kudācanaṃ;
```

```
Averena ca sammanti, esa dhammo sanantano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
Pare ca na vijānanti, mayamettha yamāmase;
```

```
Ye ca tattha vijānanti, tato sammanti medhagā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
Aṭṭhicchinnā <pb ed="T" n="1.0255" /> pāṇaharā, gavassa <note>gavāssa (sī. syā. pī.)</note> dhanahārino;
```

```
Raṭṭhaṃ vilumpamānānaṃ, tesampi hoti saṅgati;
```

```
Kasmā tumhāka no siyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
Sace labhetha nipakaṃ sahāyaṃ, saddhiṃcaraṃ sādhuvihāridhīraṃ;
```

```
Abhibhuyya sabbāni parissayāni, careyya tenattamano satīmā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
No ce labhetha nipakaṃ sahāyaṃ, saddhiṃcaraṃ sādhuvihāridhīraṃ;
```

```
Rājāva raṭṭhaṃ vijitaṃ pahāya, eko care mātaṅgaraññeva nāgo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
Ekassa <pb ed="M" n="1.0189" /> caritaṃ seyyo, natthi bāle sahāyatā;
```

```
Eko care na pāpāni kayirā, appossukko mātaṅgaraññeva nāgoti.
```

Kosambiyajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 429. Mahāsuvajātakaṃ (3)

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
Dumo yadā hoti phalūpapanno, bhuñjanti naṃ vihaṅgamā <note>vihagā (sī. pī.)</note> sampatantā;
```

```
Khīṇanti ñatvāna dumaṃ phalaccaye <note>ñatvā dumapphalaccayena (ka.)</note>, disodisaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0256" /> yanti tato vihaṅgamā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
Cara cārikaṃ lohitatuṇḍa māmari, kiṃ tvaṃ suva sukkhadumamhi jhāyasi;
```

```
Tadiṅgha maṃ brūhi vasantasannibha, kasmā suva sukkhadumaṃ na riñcasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
Ye <pb ed="V" n="1.0155" /> ve sakhīnaṃ sakhāro bhavanti, pāṇaccaye <note>pāṇaṃ caje (ka.), pāṇaccaye maraṇakāle ca sukhadukkhesu ca na jahantīti sambandho</note> dukkhasukhesu haṃsa;
```

```
Khīṇaṃ akhīṇanti na taṃ jahanti, santo sataṃ dhammamanussarantā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
Sohaṃ sataṃ aññatarosmi haṃsa, ñātī ca me hoti sakhā ca rukkho;
```

```
Taṃ nussahe jīvikattho pahātuṃ, khīṇanti ñatvāna na hesa dhammo <note>na sosa (ka.), na esa (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
Sādhu sakkhi kataṃ hoti, metti saṃsati santhavo <note>mittaṃ saṅgati sandhavo (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Sacetaṃ dhammaṃ rocesi, pāsaṃsosi vijānataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
So te suva varaṃ dammi, pattayāna vihaṅgama;
```

```
Varaṃ varassu vakkaṅga, yaṃ kiñci manasicchasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
Varañca <pb ed="M" n="1.0190" /> me haṃsa bhavaṃ dadeyya, ayañca rukkho punarāyuṃ labhetha;
```

```
So <pb ed="T" n="1.0257" /> sākhavā phalimā saṃvirūḷho, madhutthiko tiṭṭhatu sobhamāno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
Taṃ passa samma phalimaṃ uḷāraṃ, sahāva te hotu udumbarena;
```

```
So sākhavā phalimā saṃvirūḷho, madhutthiko tiṭṭhatu sobhamāno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
Evaṃ sakka sukhī hohi, saha sabbehi ñātibhi;
```

```
Yathāhamajja sukhito, disvāna saphalaṃ dumaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
Suvassa ca varaṃ datvā, katvāna saphalaṃ dumaṃ;
```

```
Pakkāmi saha bhariyāya, devānaṃ nandanaṃ vananti.
```

Mahāsuvajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 430. Cūḷasuvajātakaṃ (4)

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
Santi rukkhā haripattā <note>haritapattā (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, dumā nekaphalā bahū;
```

```
Kasmā nu sukkhe <note>sukkha (ka.)</note> koḷāpe, suvassa nirato mano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
Phalassa upabhuñjimhā, nekavassagaṇe bahū;
```

```
Aphalampi viditvāna, sāva metti yathā pure.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
Sukhañca rukkhaṃ koḷāpaṃ, opattamaphalaṃ dumaṃ;
```

```
Ohāya sakuṇā yanti, kiṃ dosaṃ passase dija.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
Ye <pb ed="T" n="1.0258" /> phalatthā sambhajanti, aphaloti jahanti naṃ;
```

```
Attatthapaññā dummedhā, te honti pakkhapātino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
Sādhu sakkhi kataṃ hoti, metti saṃsati santhavo;
```

```
Sacetaṃ dhammaṃ rocesi, pāsaṃsosi vijānataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
So <pb ed="V" n="1.0156" /> te suva varaṃ dammi, pattayāna vihaṅgama;
```

```
Varaṃ varassu vakkaṅga, yaṃ kiñci manasicchasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
Api <pb ed="M" n="1.0191" /> nāma naṃ passeyyaṃ <note>api nāma naṃ puna passe (sī. syā.)</note>, sapattaṃ saphalaṃ dumaṃ;
```

```
Daliddova nidhi laddhā, nandeyyāhaṃ punappunaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
Tato amatamādāya, abhisiñci mahīruhaṃ;
```

```
Tassa sākhā virūhiṃsu <note>virūḷhassa (ka.)</note>, sītacchāyā manoramā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
Evaṃ sakka sukhī hohi, saha sabbehi ñātibhi;
```

```
Yathāhamajja sukhito, disvāna saphalaṃ dumaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
Suvassa ca varaṃ datvā, katvāna saphalaṃ dumaṃ;
```

```
Pakkāmi saha bhariyāya, devānaṃ nandanaṃ vananti.
```

Cūḷasuvajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 431. Haritacajātakaṃ (5)

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
Sutaṃ metaṃ mahābrahme, kāme bhuñjati hārito;
```

Kaccetaṃ vacanaṃ tucchaṃ, kacci suddho iriyyasi.

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
Evametaṃ mahārāja, yathā te vacanaṃ sutaṃ;
```

```
Kummaggaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0259" /> paṭipannosmi, mohaneyyesu mucchito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
Adu <note>ādu (sī. pī.)</note> paññā kimatthiyā, nipuṇā sādhucintinī <note>cintanī (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Yāya uppatitaṃ rāgaṃ, kiṃ mano na vinodaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
Cattārome mahārāja, loke atibalā bhusā;
```

```
Rāgo doso mado moho, yattha paññā na gādhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
Arahā sīlasampanno, suddho carati hārito;
```

```
Medhāvī paṇḍito ceva, iti no sammato bhavaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
Medhāvīnampi hiṃsanti, isiṃ dhammaguṇe rataṃ;
```

```
Vitakkā pāpakā rāja, subhā rāgūpasaṃhitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
Uppannāyaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0192" /> sarīrajo, rāgo vaṇṇavidūsano tava;
```

```
Taṃ pajaha bhaddamatthu te, bahunnāsi medhāvisammato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
Te andhakārake <note>karaṇe (sī. syā. pī.)</note> kāme, bahudukkhe mahāvise;
```

```
Tesaṃ mūlaṃ gavesissaṃ, checchaṃ rāgaṃ sabandhanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
Idaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0157" /> vatvāna hārito, isi saccaparakkamo;
```

```
Kāmarāgaṃ virājetvā, brahmalokūpago ahūti.
```

Haritacajātakaṃ <note>hāritajātakaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> pañcamaṃ.

#### 432. Padakusalamāṇavajātakaṃ (6)

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
Bahussutaṃ cittakathiṃ <note>cittakathaṃ (syā. ka.)</note>, gaṅgā vahati pāṭaliṃ <note>pāṭalaṃ (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Vuyhamānaka <pb ed="T" n="1.0260" /> bhaddante, ekaṃ me dehi gāthakaṃ <note>gītakaṃ (ka. aṭṭha.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
Yena siñcanti dukkhitaṃ, yena siñcanti āturaṃ;
```

```
Tassa majjhe marissāmi, jātaṃ saraṇato bhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
Yattha bījāni rūhanti, sattā yattha patiṭṭhitā;
```

```
Sā me sīsaṃ nipīḷeti, jātaṃ saraṇato bhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
Yena bhattāni paccanti, sītaṃ yena vihaññati;
```

```
So maṃ ḍahati <note>dayhati (ka.)</note> gattāni, jātaṃ saraṇato bhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
Yena bhuttena <note>bhattena (syā. ka.)</note> yāpenti, puthū brāhmaṇakhattiyā;
```

```
So maṃ bhutto byāpādeti, jātaṃ saraṇato bhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
Gimhānaṃ pacchime māse, vātamicchanti paṇḍitā;
```

```
So maṃ <note>so me (sī. pī.)</note> bhañjati gattāni, jātaṃ saraṇato bhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
Yaṃ nissitā jagatiruhaṃ, svāyaṃ aggiṃ pamuñcati;
```

```
Disā bhajatha vakkaṅgā, jātaṃ saraṇato bhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
Yamānayiṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0193" /> somanassaṃ, māliniṃ candanussadaṃ;
```

```
Sā maṃ gharā nicchubhati <note>nīharati (sī. syā.)</note>, jātaṃ saraṇato bhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
Yena jātena nandissaṃ, yassa ca bhavamicchisaṃ;
```

```
So maṃ gharā nicchubhati <note>nīharati (sī. syā.)</note>, jātaṃ saraṇato bhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
Suṇantu me jānapadā, negamā ca samāgatā;
```

```
Yatodakaṃ tadādittaṃ, yato khemaṃ tato bhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
Rājā <pb ed="T" n="1.0261" /> vilumpate raṭṭhaṃ, brāhmaṇo ca purohito;
```

```
Attaguttā viharatha, jātaṃ saraṇato bhayanti.
```

Padakusalamāṇavajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 433. Lomasakassapajātakaṃ (7)

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
Assa <pb ed="V" n="1.0158" /> indasamo rāja, accantaṃ ajarāmaro;
```

```
Sace tvaṃ yaññaṃ yājeyya, isiṃ lomasakassapaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
Sasamuddapariyāyaṃ, mahiṃ sāgarakuṇḍalaṃ;
```

```
Na icche saha nindāya, evaṃ seyya <note>sayha (sī. syā. pī.)</note> vijānahi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
Dhiratthu taṃ yasalābhaṃ, dhanalābhañca brāhmaṇa;
```

```
Yā vutti vinipātena, adhammacaraṇena vā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
Api ce pattamādāya, anagāro paribbaje;
```

```
Sāyeva jīvikā seyyo, yā cādhammena esanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
Api ce pattamādāya, anagāro paribbaje;
```

```
Aññaṃ ahiṃsayaṃ loke, api rajjena taṃ varaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
Balaṃ cando balaṃ suriyo, balaṃ samaṇabrāhmaṇā;
```

```
Balaṃ velā samuddassa, balātibalamitthiyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
Yathā uggatapaṃ santaṃ, isiṃ lomasakassapaṃ;
```

```
Pitu atthā candavatī, vājapeyyaṃ <note>vācapeyyaṃ (pī. ka.)</note> ayājayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
Taṃ lobhapakataṃ kammaṃ, kaṭukaṃ kāmahetukaṃ;
```

```
Tassa <pb ed="T" n="1.0262" /> mūlaṃ gavesissaṃ, checchaṃ rāgaṃ sabandhanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
Dhiratthu <pb ed="M" n="1.0194" /> kāme subahūpi loke, tapova seyyo kāmaguṇehi rāja;
```

```
Tapo karissāmi pahāya kāme, taveva raṭṭhaṃ candavatī ca hotūti.
```

Lomasakassapajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 434. Cakkavākajātakaṃ (8)

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
Kāsāyavatthe sakuṇe vadāmi, duve duve nandamane <note>nandimane (sī. pī.)</note> carante;
```

```
Kaṃ aṇḍajaṃ aṇḍajā mānusesu, jātiṃ pasaṃsanti tadiṅgha brūtha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
Amhe manussesu manussahiṃsa, anubbate <note>anupubbake (ka.)</note> cakkavāke vadanti;
```

```
Kalyāṇabhāvamhe <note>bhāva’mha (sī. pī.)</note> dijesu sammatā, abhirūpā <note>abhītarūpā (sī. syā. pī.)</note> vicarāma aṇṇave. ( ) <note>(na ghāsahetūpi karoma pāpaṃ) (ka.)</note>
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
Kiṃ aṇṇave kāni phalāni bhuñje, maṃsaṃ kuto khādatha cakkavākā;
```

```
Kiṃ bhojanaṃ bhuñjatha vo anomā <note>abhiṇhaṃ (ka.)</note>, balañca <pb ed="T" n="1.0263" /> vaṇṇo ca anapparūpā <note>anapparūpo (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="V" n="1.0159" /> aṇṇave santi phalāni dhaṅka, maṃsaṃ kuto khādituṃ cakkavāke;
```

```
Sevālabhakkhamha <note>bhakkhimha (ka.)</note> apāṇabhojanā <note>avākabhojanā (sī. pī.)</note>, na ghāsahetūpi karoma pāpaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
Na me idaṃ ruccati cakkavāka, asmiṃ bhave bhojanasannikāso;
```

```
Ahosi pubbe tato me aññathā, icceva me vimati ettha jātā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
Ahampi <pb ed="M" n="1.0195" /> maṃsāni phalāni bhuñje, annāni ca loṇiyateliyāni;
```

```
Rasaṃ manussesu labhāmi bhottuṃ, sūrova saṅgāmamukhaṃ vijetvā;
```

```
Na ca me tādiso vaṇṇo, cakkavāka yathā tava.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
Asuddhabhakkhosi khaṇānupātī, kicchena te labbhati annapānaṃ;
```

```
Na tussasī rukkhaphalehi dhaṅka, maṃsāni vā yāni susānamajjhe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
Yo sāhasena adhigamma bhoge, paribhuñjati <pb ed="T" n="1.0264" /> dhaṅka khaṇānupātī;
```

```
Tato upakkosati naṃ sabhāvo, upakkuṭṭho vaṇṇabalaṃ jahāti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
Appampi ce nibbutiṃ bhuñjatī yadi, asāhasena aparūpaghātī <note>asāhasenānupaghātino (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Balañca vaṇṇo ca tadassa hoti, na hi sabbo āhāramayena vaṇṇoti.
```

Cakkavākajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 435. Haliddirāgajātakaṃ (9)

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
Sutitikkhaṃ araññamhi, pantamhi sayanāsane;
```

```
Ye ca gāme titikkhanti, te uḷāratarā tayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
Araññā gāmamāgamma, kiṃsīlaṃ kiṃvataṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Purisaṃ tāta seveyyaṃ, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
Yo te <note>yo taṃ (syā. jā. 1.4.190 araññajātakepi)</note> vissāsaye tāta, vissāsañca khameyya te;
```

```
Sussūsī ca titikkhī ca, taṃ bhajehi ito gato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
Yassa <pb ed="M" n="1.0196" /> kāyena vācāya, manasā natthi dukkaṭaṃ;
```

```
Urasīva patiṭṭhāya, taṃ bhajehi ito gato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
Yo ca dhammena carati, carantopi na maññati;
```

```
Visuddhakāriṃ sappaññaṃ, taṃ bhajehi ito gato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
Haliddirāgaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0265" /> kapicittaṃ, purisaṃ rāgavirāginaṃ;
```

```
Tādisaṃ tāta mā sevi, nimmanussampi ce siyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
Āsīvisaṃva kupitaṃ, mīḷhalittaṃ mahāpathaṃ;
```

```
Ārakā parivajjehi, yānīva visamaṃ pathaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
Anatthā <pb ed="V" n="1.0160" /> tāta vaḍḍhanti, bālaṃ accupasevato;
```

```
Māssu bālena saṃgacchi, amitteneva sabbadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
Taṃ tāhaṃ tāta yācāmi, karassu vacanaṃ mama;
```

```
Māssu bālena saṃgacchi <note>saṃgañchi (sī. pī.)</note>, dukkho bālehi saṅgamoti.
```

Haliddirāgajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 436. Samuggajātakaṃ (10)

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
Kuto nu āgacchatha bho tayo janā, svāgatā etha <note>svāgataṃ ettha (sī. pī.)</note> nisīdathāsane;
```

```
Kaccittha bhonto kusalaṃ anāmayaṃ, cirassamabbhāgamanaṃ hi vo idha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
Ahameva eko idha majja patto, na cāpi me dutiyo koci vijjati;
```

```
Kimeva sandhāya te bhāsitaṃ ise, ‘‘kuto nu āgacchatha bho tayo janā’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
Tuvañca eko bhariyā ca te piyā, samuggapakkhittanikiṇṇamantare<pb ed="T" n="1.0266" />;
```

```
Sā rakkhitā kucchigatāva <note>kucchigatā ca (ka.)</note> te sadā, vāyussa <note>harissa (ka.)</note> puttena sahā tahiṃ ratā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
Saṃviggarūpo <pb ed="M" n="1.0197" /> isinā viyākato <note>pabyākato (ka.), byākato (syā. pī.)</note>, so dānavo tattha samuggamuggili;
```

```
Addakkhi bhariyaṃ suci māladhāriniṃ, vāyussa puttena sahā tahiṃ rataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
Sudiṭṭharūpamuggatapānuvattinā <note>sudiṭṭharūpuggatapānuvattinā (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, hīnā narā ye pamadāvasaṃ gatā;
```

```
Yathā have pāṇarivettha rakkhitā, duṭṭhā mayī aññamabhippamodayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
Divā ca ratto ca mayā upaṭṭhitā, tapassinā jotirivā vane vasaṃ;
```

```
Sā dhammamukkamma adhammamācari, akiriyarūpo pamadāhi santhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§93.</p>

```
Sarīramajjhamhi ṭhitātimaññahaṃ, mayhaṃ ayanti asatiṃ asaññataṃ;
```

```
Sā dhammamukkamma adhammamācari, akiriyarūpo pamadāhi santhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§94.</p>

```
Surakkhitaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0267" /> meti kathaṃ nu vissase, anekacittāsu na hatthi <note>anekacittā puna hettha (ka.)</note> rakkhaṇā;
```

```
Etā hi pātālapapātasannibhā, etthappamatto byasanaṃ nigacchati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§95.</p>

```
Tasmā hi te sukhino vītasokā, ye mātugāmehi caranti nissaṭā;
```

```
Etaṃ sivaṃ uttamamābhipatthayaṃ, na mātugāmehi kareyya santhavanti.
```

Samuggajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

#### 437. Pūtimaṃsajātakaṃ (11)

<p rend="hangnum">§96.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="M" n="1.0198" /> kho me ruccati āḷi, pūtimaṃsassa pekkhanā;
```

```
Etādisā sakhārasmā, ārakā parivajjaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§97.</p>

```
Ummattikā <pb ed="V" n="1.0161" /> ayaṃ veṇī, vaṇṇeti patino sakhiṃ;
```

```
Pajjhāyi <note>pajjhāti (sī. pī.), pajjhāyati (sī. niyya)</note> paṭigacchantiṃ, āgataṃ meṇḍa <note>meḷa (sī. pī.)</note> mātaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§98.</p>

```
Tvaṃ khosi samma ummatto, dummedho avicakkhaṇo;
```

```
Yo tvaṃ <note>so tvaṃ (syā.)</note> matālayaṃ katvā, akālena vipekkhasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§99.</p>

```
Na akāle vipekkheyya, kāle pekkheyya paṇḍito;
```

```
Pūtimaṃsova pajjhāyi <note>pajjhāti (sī. pī.), pajjhāyati (sī. niyya)</note>, yo akāle vipekkhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§100.</p>

```
Piyaṃ kho āḷi me hotu, puṇṇapattaṃ dadāhi me;
```

```
Pati <pb ed="T" n="1.0268" /> sañjīvito mayhaṃ, eyyāsi piyapucchikā <note>pucchitā (syā. ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§101.</p>

```
Piyaṃ kho āḷi te hotu, puṇṇapattaṃ dadāmi te;
```

```
Mahatā parivārena <note>parihārena (syā.)</note>, essaṃ <note>esaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> kayirāhi <note>kayirāsi (pī.)</note> bhojanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§102.</p>

```
Kīdiso tuyhaṃ parivāro, yesaṃ kāhāmi bhojanaṃ;
```

```
Kiṃnāmakā ca te sabbe, taṃ <note>te (sī. syā. pī.)</note> me akkhāhi pucchitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§103.</p>

```
Māliyo caturakkho ca, piṅgiyo atha jambuko;
```

```
Ediso mayhaṃ parivāro, tesaṃ kayirāhi <note>kayirāsi (pī.)</note> bhojanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§104.</p>

```
Nikkhantāya agārasmā, bhaṇḍakampi vinassati;
```

```
Ārogyaṃ āḷino vajjaṃ <note>vacchaṃ (?)</note>, idheva vasa māgamāti.
```

Pūtimaṃsajātakaṃ ekādasamaṃ.

#### 438. Daddarajātakaṃ (12)

<p rend="hangnum">§105.</p>

```
Yo te puttake akhādi, dinnabhatto adūsake;
```

```
Tasmiṃ dāṭhaṃ nipātehi, mā te muccittha jīvato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§106.</p>

```
Ākiṇṇaluddo <pb ed="M" n="1.0199" /> puriso, dhāticelaṃva makkhito;
```

```
Padesaṃ taṃ na passāmi, yattha dāṭhaṃ nipātaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§107.</p>

```
Akataññussa posassa, niccaṃ vivaradassino;
```

```
Sabbaṃ ce pathaviṃ dajjā, neva naṃ abhirādhaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§108.</p>

```
Kinnu subāhu taramānarūpo, paccāgatosi saha māṇavena;
```

```
Kiṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0269" /> kiccamatthaṃ idhamatthi tuyhaṃ, akkhāhi me pucchito etamatthaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§109.</p>

```
Yo te sakhā daddaro sādhurūpo, tassa vadhaṃ parisaṅkāmi ajja;
```

```
Purisassa kammāyatanāni sutvā, nāhaṃ sukhiṃ daddaraṃ ajja maññe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§110.</p>

```
Kānissa <pb ed="V" n="1.0162" /> kammāyatanāni assu, purisassa vuttisamodhānatāya;
```

```
Kaṃ vā paṭiññaṃ purisassa sutvā, parisaṅkasi daddaraṃ māṇavena.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§111.</p>

```
Ciṇṇā kaliṅgā caritā vaṇijjā, vettācaro saṅkupathopi ciṇṇo;
```

```
Naṭehi ciṇṇaṃ saha vākurehi <note>vākarehi (pī. sī. niyya), vāgurehi (?)</note>, daṇḍena yuddhampi samajjamajjhe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§112.</p>

```
Baddhā kulīkā <note>kuliṅkā (sī. pī.)</note> mitamāḷhakena, akkhā jitā <note>akkhācitā (sī. aṭṭha.)</note> saṃyamo abbhatīto;
```

```
Abbāhitaṃ <note>appahitaṃ (sī. syā.), abbūhitaṃ (pī. sī. niyya)</note> pubbakaṃ <note>pupphakaṃ (sī. syā.)</note> aḍḍharattaṃ, hatthā daḍḍhā piṇḍapaṭiggahena.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§113.</p>

```
Tānissa <pb ed="M" n="1.0200" /> kammāyatanāni assu, purisassa <pb ed="T" n="1.0270" /> vuttisamodhānatāya;
```

```
Yathā ayaṃ dissati lomapiṇḍo, gāvo hatā kiṃ pana daddarassāti.
```

Daddarajātakaṃ dvādasamaṃ.

<trailer rend="centre">Navakanipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.</trailer>

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Varagijjha samajjana haṃsavaro, nidhisavhaya hārita pāṭaliko;
```

```
Ajarāmara dhaṅka titikkha kuto, atha dvādasa pekkhana daddaribhīti.
```

### 10. Dasakanipāto

#### 439. Catudvārajātakaṃ (1)

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
Catudvāramidaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0271" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0163" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0201" /> nagaraṃ, āyasaṃ daḷhapākāraṃ;
```

```
Oruddhapaṭiruddhosmi, kiṃ pāpaṃ pakataṃ mayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
Sabbe apihitā dvārā, oruddhosmi yathā dijo;
```

```
Kimādhikaraṇaṃ yakkha, cakkābhinihato ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
Laddhā satasahassāni, atirekāni vīsati;
```

```
Anukampakānaṃ ñātīnaṃ, vacanaṃ samma nākari.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
Laṅghiṃ samuddaṃ pakkhandi, sāgaraṃ appasiddhikaṃ;
```

```
Catubbhi aṭṭhajjhagamā, aṭṭhāhipi ca soḷasa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
Soḷasāhi ca bāttiṃsa, atricchaṃ cakkamāsado;
```

Icchāhatassa posassa, cakkaṃ bhamati matthake.

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
Uparivisālā duppūrā, icchā visaṭagāminī <note>visaṭagāminiṃ (pī. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Ye ca taṃ anugijjhanti, te honti cakkadhārino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
Bahubhaṇḍaṃ <note>bahuṃ bhaṇḍaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> avahāya, maggaṃ appaṭivekkhiya;
```

```
Yesañcetaṃ asaṅkhātaṃ, te honti cakkadhārino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
Kammaṃ samekkhe vipulañca bhogaṃ, icchaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0272" /> na seveyya anatthasaṃhitaṃ;
```

```
Kareyya vākyaṃ anukampakānaṃ, taṃ tādisaṃ nātivatteyya cakkaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
Kīvaciraṃ nu me yakkha, cakkaṃ sirasi ṭhassati;
```

```
Kati vassasahassāni, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
Atisaro paccasaro <note>accasaro (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, mittavinda suṇohi me;
```

```
Cakkaṃ te sirasi <note>sirasmi (syā.)</note> māviddhaṃ, na taṃ jīvaṃ pamokkhasīti.
```

Catudvārajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 440. Kaṇhajātakaṃ (2)

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
Kaṇho <pb ed="V" n="1.0164" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0202" /> vatāyaṃ puriso, kaṇhaṃ bhuñjati bhojanaṃ;
```

```
Kaṇhe bhūmipadesasmiṃ, na mayhaṃ manaso piyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
Na kaṇho tacasā hoti, antosāro hi brāhmaṇo;
```

```
Yasmiṃ pāpāni kammāni, sa ve kaṇho sujampati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
Etasmiṃ te sulapite, patirūpe subhāsite;
```

```
Varaṃ brāhmaṇa te dammi, yaṃ kiñci manasicchasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
Varañce me ado sakka, sabbabhūtānamissara;
```

```
Sunikkodhaṃ suniddosaṃ, nillobhaṃ vuttimattano;
```

```
Nisnehamabhikaṅkhāmi, ete me caturo vare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
Kiṃ nu kodhe vā <note>kodheva (sī. pī.)</note> dose vā, lobhe snehe ca brāhmaṇa;
```

```
Ādīnavaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0273" /> tvaṃ passasi <note>sampassasi (sī. pī.)</note>, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
Appo hutvā bahu hoti, vaḍḍhate so akhantijo;
```

```
Āsaṅgī bahupāyāso, tasmā kodhaṃ na rocaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
Duṭṭhassa pharusā <note>paṭhamā (pī. sī. niyya)</note> vācā, parāmāso anantarā;
```

```
Tato pāṇi tato daṇḍo, satthassa paramā gati <note>parāmasati (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Doso kodhasamuṭṭhāno, tasmā dosaṃ na rocaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
Ālopasāhasākārā <note>sahasākārā (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, nikatī vañcanāni ca;
```

```
Dissanti lobhadhammesu, tasmā lobhaṃ na rocaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
Snehasaṅgathitā <note>saṅgadhitā (ka.), saṅgantitā (syā.)</note> ganthā, senti manomayā puthū;
```

```
Te bhusaṃ upatāpenti, tasmā snehaṃ na rocaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
Etasmiṃ te sulapite, patirūpe subhāsite;
```

```
Varaṃ brāhmaṇa te dammi, yaṃ kiñci manasicchasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
Varañce me ado sakka, sabbabhūtānamissara;
```

```
Araññe me viharato, niccaṃ ekavihārino;
```

```
Ābādhā mā <note>na (syā. pī.)</note> uppajjeyyuṃ, antarāyakarā bhusā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
Etasmiṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0203" /> te sulapite, patirūpe subhāsite;
```

```
Varaṃ brāhmaṇa te dammi, yaṃ kiñci manasicchasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
Varañce <pb ed="V" n="1.0165" /> me ado sakka, sabbabhūtānamissara;
```

```
Na mano vā sarīraṃ vā, maṃ-kate sakka kassaci;
```

```
Kadāci <pb ed="T" n="1.0274" /> upahaññetha, etaṃ sakka varaṃ vareti.
```

Kaṇhajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 441. Catuposathiyajātakaṃ (3)

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
Yo kopaneyye na karoti kopaṃ, na kujjhati sappuriso kadāci;
```

```
Kuddhopi so nāvikaroti kopaṃ, taṃ ve naraṃ samaṇamāhu <note>samaṇaṃ āhu (sī.)</note> loke.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
Ūnūdaro yo sahate jighacchaṃ, danto tapassī mitapānabhojano;
```

```
Āhārahetu na karoti pāpaṃ, taṃ ve naraṃ samaṇamāhu loke.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
Khiḍḍaṃ ratiṃ vippajahitvāna sabbaṃ, na cālikaṃ bhāsasi kiñci loke;
```

```
Vibhūsaṭṭhānā virato methunasmā, taṃ ve naraṃ samaṇamāhu loke.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
Pariggahaṃ lobhadhammañca sabbaṃ, yo ve pariññāya pariccajeti;
```

```
Dantaṃ ṭhitattaṃ amamaṃ nirāsaṃ, taṃ ve naraṃ samaṇamāhu loke.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
Pucchāma <pb ed="T" n="1.0275" /> kattāramanomapaññaṃ <note>manomapañña (syā. ka.)</note>, kathāsu no viggaho atthi jāto;
```

```
Chindajja kaṅkhaṃ vicikicchitāni, tadajja <note>tayājja (sī.)</note> kaṅkhaṃ vitaremu sabbe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
Ye <pb ed="M" n="1.0204" /> paṇḍitā atthadasā bhavanti, bhāsanti te yoniso tattha kāle;
```

```
Kathaṃ nu kathānaṃ abhāsitānaṃ, atthaṃ nayeyyuṃ kusalā janindā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
Kathaṃ have bhāsati nāgarājā, garuḷo pana venateyyo kimāha;
```

```
Gandhabbarājā pana kiṃ vadesi, kathaṃ pana kurūnaṃ rājaseṭṭho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
Khantiṃ have bhāsati nāgarājā, appāhāraṃ garuḷo venateyyo;
```

```
Gandhabbarājā rativippahānaṃ, akiñcanaṃ kurūnaṃ rājaseṭṭho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
Sabbāni etāni subhāsitāni, na hettha dubbhāsitamatthi kiñci;
```

```
Yasmiñca etāni patiṭṭhitāni, arāva <pb ed="T" n="1.0276" /> nābhyā susamohitāni;
```

```
Catubbhi dhammehi samaṅgibhūtaṃ, taṃ ve naraṃ samaṇamāhu loke.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
Tuvañhi <note>tuvaṃ nu (sī. pī.)</note> seṭṭho tvamanuttarosi, tvaṃ dhammagū dhammavidū sumedho;
```

```
Paññāya pañhaṃ samadhiggahetvā, acchecchi dhīro vicikicchitāni;
```

```
Acchecchi kaṅkhaṃ vicikicchitāni, cundo yathā nāgadantaṃ kharena.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
Nīluppalābhaṃ vimalaṃ anagghaṃ, vatthaṃ idaṃ dhūmasamānavaṇṇaṃ;
```

```
Pañhassa <pb ed="T" n="1.0277" /> veyyākaraṇena tuṭṭho, dadāmi te dhammapūjāya dhīra.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
Suvaṇṇamālaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0166" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0205" /> satapattaphullitaṃ, sakesaraṃ ratnasahassamaṇḍitaṃ;
```

```
Pañhassa veyyākaraṇena tuṭṭho, dadāmi te dhammapūjāya dhīra.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
Maṇiṃ anagghaṃ ruciraṃ pabhassaraṃ, kaṇṭhāvasattaṃ <note>vasitaṃ (ka.)</note> maṇibhūsitaṃ me;
```

```
Pañhassa veyyākaraṇena tuṭṭho, dadāmi te dhammapūjāya dhīra.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
Gavaṃ sahassaṃ usabhañca nāgaṃ, ājaññayutte ca rathe dasa ime;
```

```
Pañhassa veyyākaraṇena tuṭṭho, dadāmi te gāmavarāni soḷasa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
Sāriputto tadā nāgo, supaṇṇo pana kolito;
```

```
Gandhabbarājā anuruddho, rājā ānanda paṇḍito;
```

```
Vidhuro bodhisatto ca, evaṃ dhāretha jātakanti.
```

Catuposathiyajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 442. Saṅkhajātakaṃ (4)

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
Bahussuto sutadhammosi saṅkha, diṭṭhā tayā samaṇabrāhmaṇā ca;
```

```
Athakkhaṇe dassayase vilāpaṃ, añño nu ko te paṭimantako mayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
Subbhū <note>subbhā (syā.), sumbhā, subhmā (ka.)</note> subhā suppaṭimukkakambu, paggayha sovaṇṇamayāya pātiyā;
```

```
‘‘Bhuñjassu bhattaṃ’’ iti maṃ vadeti, saddhāvittā <note>saddhācittā (sī. pī. ka.)</note>, tamahaṃ noti brūmi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
Etādisaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0278" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0206" /> brāhmaṇa disvāna <note>disva (sī. pī.)</note> yakkhaṃ, puccheyya poso sukhamāsisāno <note>sukhamāsasāno (syā.), sukhamāsisamāno (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Uṭṭhehi naṃ pañjalikābhipuccha, devī nusi tvaṃ uda mānusī nu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
Yaṃ tvaṃ sukhenābhisamekkhase maṃ, bhuñjassu bhattaṃ iti maṃ vadesi;
```

```
Pucchāmi taṃ nāri mahānubhāve, devī nusi tvaṃ uda mānusī nu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
Devī ahaṃ saṅkha mahānubhāvā, idhāgatā sāgaravārimajjhe;
```

```
Anukampikā no ca paduṭṭhacittā, taveva atthāya idhāgatāsmi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
Idhannapānaṃ sayanāsanañca, yānāni nānāvividhāni saṅkha;
```

```
Sabbassa tyāhaṃ paṭipādayāmi, yaṃ kiñci tuyhaṃ manasābhipatthitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
Yaṃ kiñci yiṭṭhañca hutañca <note>yiṭṭhaṃva hutaṃva (sī. pī.)</note> mayhaṃ, sabbassa no issarā tvaṃ sugatte;
```

```
Susoṇi subbhamu <note>subbhu (sī.), subbhā (syā.)</note> suvilaggamajjhe <note>suvilākamajjhe (syā. pī. sī. aṭṭha.), suvilātamajjhe (ka.)</note>, kissa me kammassa ayaṃ vipāko.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
Ghamme <pb ed="T" n="1.0279" /> pathe brāhmaṇa ekabhikkhuṃ, ugghaṭṭapādaṃ tasitaṃ kilantaṃ;
```

```
Paṭipādayī saṅkha upāhanāni <note>upāhanāhi (sī. pī.)</note>, sā dakkhiṇā kāmaduhā tavajja.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
Sā <pb ed="M" n="1.0207" /> hotu nāvā phalakūpapannā, anavassutā erakavātayuttā;
```

```
Aññassa yānassa na hettha <note>na hatthi (pī.)</note> bhūmi, ajjeva maṃ moḷiniṃ pāpayassu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
Sā <pb ed="V" n="1.0167" /> tattha vittā sumanā patītā, nāvaṃ sucittaṃ abhinimminitvā;
```

```
Ādāya saṅkhaṃ purisena saddhiṃ, upānayī nagaraṃ sādhurammanti.
```

Saṅkhajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 443. Cūḷabodhijātakaṃ (5)

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
Yo te imaṃ visālakkhiṃ, piyaṃ samhitabhāsiniṃ <note>sammillabhāsiniṃ (sī. pī.), sammillahāsiniṃ (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Ādāya balā gaccheyya, kiṃ nu kayirāsi brāhmaṇa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
Uppajje <note>uppajja (sī. pī.)</note> me na mucceyya, na me mucceyya jīvato;
```

```
Rajaṃva <pb ed="T" n="1.0280" /> vipulā vuṭṭhi, khippameva nivāraye <note>nivārayiṃ (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
Yaṃ nu pubbe vikatthittho <note>vikatthito (ka. sī. syā. ka.)</note>, balamhiva apassito;
```

```
Svajja tuṇhikato <note>tuṇhikato (sī.), tuṇhikkhako (pī.)</note> dāni, saṅghāṭiṃ sibbamacchasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
Uppajji me na muccittha, na me muccittha jīvato;
```

```
Rajaṃva vipulā vuṭṭhi, khippameva nivārayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
Kiṃ te uppajji no mucci, kiṃ te na mucci jīvato;
```

```
Rajaṃva vipulā vuṭṭhi, katamaṃ tvaṃ nivārayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
Yamhi jāte na passati, ajāte sādhu passati;
```

```
So me uppajji no mucci, kodho dummedhagocaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
Yena jātena nandanti, amittā dukkhamesino;
```

```
So me uppajji no mucci, kodho dummedhagocaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
Yasmiñca <pb ed="M" n="1.0208" /> jāyamānamhi, sadatthaṃ nāvabujjhati;
```

```
So me uppajji no mucci, kodho dummedhagocaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
Yenābhibhūto kusalaṃ jahāti, parakkare vipulañcāpi atthaṃ;
```

```
Sa bhīmaseno balavā pamaddī, kodho mahārāja na me amuccatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
Kaṭṭhasmiṃ matthamānasmiṃ <note>manthamānasmiṃ (pī.), maddamānasmiṃ (ka.)</note>, pāvako nāma jāyati;
```

```
Tameva kaṭṭhaṃ ḍahati, yasmā so jāyate gini.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
Evaṃ mandassa posassa, bālassa avijānato;
```

```
Sārambhā <pb ed="T" n="1.0281" /> <note>sārabbhā (ka.)</note> jāyate kodho, sopi teneva ḍayhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
Aggīva tiṇakaṭṭhasmiṃ, kodho yassa pavaḍḍhati;
```

```
Nihīyati tassa yaso, kāḷapakkheva candimā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
Anedho <pb ed="V" n="1.0168" /> <note>anindho (sī. ka.), anindo (syā.)</note> dhūmaketūva, kodho yassūpasammati;
```

```
Āpūrati tassa yaso, sukkapakkheva candimāti.
```

Cūḷabodhijātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 444. Kaṇhadīpāyanajātakaṃ (6)

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
Sattāhamevāhaṃ pasannacitto, puññatthiko ācariṃ <note>acariṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> brahmacariyaṃ;
```

```
Athāparaṃ yaṃ caritaṃ mamedaṃ <note>mama yidaṃ (syā.), mamāyidaṃ (pī.)</note>, vassāni paññāsa samādhikāni;
```

```
Akāmako vāpi <note>vāhi (pī. ka.)</note> ahaṃ carāmi, etena <pb ed="T" n="1.0282" /> saccena suvatthi hotu;
```

```
Hataṃ visaṃ jīvatu yaññadatto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
Yasmā <pb ed="M" n="1.0209" /> dānaṃ nābhinandiṃ kadāci, disvānahaṃ atithiṃ vāsakāle;
```

```
Na cāpi me appiyataṃ aveduṃ, bahussutā samaṇabrāhmaṇā ca.
```

```
Akāmako vāpi ahaṃ dadāmi, etena saccena suvatthi hotu;
```

```
Hataṃ visaṃ jīvatu yaññadatto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
Āsīviso tāta pahūtatejo, yo taṃ adaṃsī <note>aḍaṃsī (syā.)</note> sacarā <note>bilarā (sī.), piḷārā (syā.), patarā (pī.)</note> udicca;
```

```
Tasmiñca me appiyatāya ajja, pitari ca te natthi koci viseso;
```

```
Etena saccena suvatthi hotu, hataṃ visaṃ jīvatu yaññadatto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
Santā dantāyeva <note>dantā santā ye ca (syā. ka.)</note> paribbajanti, aññatra kaṇhā natthākāmarūpā <note>anakāmarūpā (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Dīpāyana kissa jigucchamāno, akāmako carasi brahmacariyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
Saddhāya nikkhamma punaṃ nivatto, so eḷamūgova bālo <note>eḷamūgo capalo (syā. ka.)</note> vatāyaṃ;
```

```
Etassa vādassa jigucchamāno, akāmako carāmi brahmacariyaṃ;
```

```
Viññuppasatthañca satañca ṭhānaṃ <note>viññūpasatthaṃ vasitaṃ ca ṭhānaṃ (ka.)</note>, evampahaṃ puññakaro bhavāmi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
Samaṇe <pb ed="M" n="1.0210" /> tuvaṃ brāhmaṇe addhike ca, santappayāsi <pb ed="T" n="1.0283" /> annapānena bhikkhaṃ;
```

```
Opānabhūtaṃva gharaṃ tava yidaṃ, annena pānena upetarūpaṃ;
```

```
Atha kissa vādassa jigucchamāno, akāmako dānamimaṃ dadāsi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
Pitaro ca me āsuṃ pitāmahā ca, saddhā ahuṃ dānapatī vadaññū;
```

```
Taṃ kullavattaṃ anuvattamāno, māhaṃ kule antimagandhano <note>gandhino (syā. pī. ka.), gandhinī (sī.)</note> ahuṃ;
```

```
Etassa vādassa jigucchamāno, akāmako dānamimaṃ dadāmi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
Dahariṃ kumāriṃ asamatthapaññaṃ, yaṃ tānayiṃ ñātikulā sugatte;
```

```
Na cāpi me appiyataṃ avedi, aññatra kāmā paricārayantā <note>paricārayantī (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Atha kena vaṇṇena mayā te bhoti, saṃvāsadhammo ahu evarūpo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
Ārā <pb ed="V" n="1.0169" /> dūre nayidha kadāci atthi, paramparā nāma kule imasmiṃ;
```

```
Taṃ kullavattaṃ anuvattamānā, māhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0284" /> kule antimagandhinī ahuṃ;
```

```
Etassa vādassa jigucchamānā, akāmikā paddhacarāmhi <note>paṭṭhacarāmhi (syā. ka.)</note> tuyhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
Maṇḍabya <pb ed="M" n="1.0211" /> bhāsiṃ yamabhāsaneyyaṃ <note>bhāsissaṃ abhāsaneyyaṃ (sī. syā. pī.), bhāsissa’mabhāsaneyyaṃ (?)</note>, taṃ khamyataṃ puttakahetu majja;
```

```
Puttapemā na idha paratthi kiñci, so no ayaṃ jīvati yaññadattoti.
```

Kaṇhadīpāyanajātakaṃ <note>maṇḍabyajātakaṃ (syā. ka.)</note> chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 445. Nigrodhajātakaṃ (7)

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
Na vāhametaṃ <note>na cāhametaṃ (sī.)</note> jānāmi, ko vāyaṃ kassa vāti vā <note>cāti vā (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Yathā sākho cari <note>vadī (sī. syā. pī.)</note> evaṃ, nigrodha kinti maññasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
Tato galavinītena, purisā nīhariṃsu maṃ;
```

```
Datvā mukhapahārāni, sākhassa vacanaṃkarā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
Etādisaṃ dummatinā, akataññuna dubbhinā;
```

```
Kataṃ anariyaṃ sākhena, sakhinā te janādhipa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
Na vāhametaṃ jānāmi, napi me koci saṃsati;
```

```
Yaṃ me tvaṃ samma akkhāsi, sākhena kāraṇaṃ <note>kaḍḍhanaṃ (sī. syā.)</note> kataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
Sakhīnaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0285" /> sājīvakaro, mama sākhassa cūbhayaṃ;
```

```
Tvaṃ nosissariyaṃ dātā, manussesu mahantataṃ;
```

```
Tayāmā labbhitā iddhī, ettha me natthi saṃsayo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
Yathāpi bījamaggimhi, ḍayhati na virūhati;
```

```
Evaṃ kataṃ asappurise, nassati na virūhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
Kataññumhi ca posamhi, sīlavante ariyavuttine;
```

```
Sukhette viya bījāni, kataṃ tamhi na nassati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
Imaṃ jammaṃ nekatikaṃ, asappurisacintakaṃ;
```

```
Hanantu sākhaṃ sattīhi, nāssa icchāmi jīvitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
Khamatassa <pb ed="M" n="1.0212" /> mahārāja, pāṇā na paṭiānayā <note>duppaṭiānayā (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Khama deva asappurisassa, nāssa icchāmahaṃ vadhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
Nigrodhameva seveyya, na sākhamupasaṃvase;
```

```
Nigrodhasmiṃ mataṃ seyyo, yañce sākhasmi jīvitanti.
```

Nigrodhajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 446. Takkalajātakaṃ (8)

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="V" n="1.0170" /> takkalā santi na āluvāni <note>ālupāni (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, na biḷāliyo na kaḷambāni tāta;
```

```
Eko araññamhi susānamajjhe, kimatthiko tāta khaṇāsi kāsuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
Pitāmaho <pb ed="T" n="1.0286" /> tāta sudubbalo te, anekabyādhīhi dukhena phuṭṭho;
```

```
Tamajjahaṃ nikhaṇissāmi sobbhe, na hissa taṃ jīvitaṃ rocayāmi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
Saṅkappametaṃ paṭiladdha pāpakaṃ, accāhitaṃ kamma karosi luddaṃ;
```

```
Mayāpi tāta paṭilacchase tuvaṃ, etādisaṃ kamma jarūpanīto;
```

```
Taṃ kullavattaṃ anuvattamāno, ahampi taṃ nikhaṇissāmi sobbhe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
Pharusāhi vācāhi pakubbamāno, āsajja maṃ tvaṃ vadase kumāra;
```

```
Putto mamaṃ orasako samāno, ahitānukampī mama tvaṃsi putta.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="M" n="1.0213" /> tāhaṃ <note>tyāhaṃ (syā.)</note> tāta ahitānukampī, hitānukampī te ahampi <note>ahañhi (syā.)</note> tāta;
```

```
Pāpañca taṃ kamma pakubbamānaṃ, arahāmi no vārayituṃ tato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
Yo mātaraṃ vā pitaraṃ saviṭṭha <note>mātaraṃ pitaraṃ vā vasiṭṭha (sī. pī.)</note>, adūsake hiṃsati pāpadhammo;
```

```
Kāyassa <pb ed="T" n="1.0287" /> bhedā abhisamparāyaṃ, asaṃsayaṃ so nirayaṃ upeti <note>pareti (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
Yo mātaraṃ vā pitaraṃ saviṭṭha, annena pānena upaṭṭhahāti;
```

```
Kāyassa bhedā abhisamparāyaṃ, asaṃsayaṃ so sugatiṃ upeti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
Na me tvaṃ putta ahitānukampī, hitānukampī me <note>mama (?)</note> tvaṃsi putta;
```

```
Ahañca taṃ mātarā vuccamāno, etādisaṃ kamma karomi luddaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
Yā te sā bhariyā anariyarūpā, mātā mamesā sakiyā janetti;
```

```
Niddhāpaye <note>niddhāmase (pī.)</note> tañca sakā agārā, aññampi te sā dukhamāvaheyya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
Yā te sā bhariyā anariyarūpā, mātā mamesā sakiyā janetti;
```

```
Dantā kareṇūva vasūpanītā, sā pāpadhammā punarāvajātūti.
```

Takkalajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 447. Mahādhammapālajātakaṃ (9)

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
Kiṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0288" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0214" /> te vataṃ kiṃ pana brahmacariyaṃ, kissa suciṇṇassa ayaṃ vipāko;
```

```
Akkhāhi me brāhmaṇa etamatthaṃ, kasmā nu tumhaṃ daharā na miyyare <note>mīyare (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§93.</p>

```
Dhammaṃ carāma na musā bhaṇāma, pāpāni kammāni parivajjayāma <note>vivajjayāma (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Anariyaṃ parivajjemu sabbaṃ, tasmā hi amhaṃ daharā na miyyare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§94.</p>

```
Suṇoma <pb ed="V" n="1.0171" /> dhammaṃ asataṃ satañca, na cāpi dhammaṃ asataṃ rocayāma;
```

```
Hitvā asante na jahāma sante, tasmā hi amhaṃ daharā na miyyare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§95.</p>

```
Pubbeva dānā sumanā bhavāma, dadampi ve attamanā bhavāma;
```

```
Datvāpi ve nānutappāma pacchā, tasmā hi amhaṃ daharā na miyyare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§96.</p>

```
Samaṇe mayaṃ brāhmaṇe addhike ca, vanibbake yācanake dalidde;
```

```
Annena pānena abhitappayāma, tasmā <pb ed="T" n="1.0289" /> hi amhaṃ daharā na miyyare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§97.</p>

```
Mayañca bhariyaṃ nātikkamāma, amhe ca bhariyā nātikkamanti;
```

```
Aññatra tāhi brahmacariyaṃ carāma, tasmā hi amhaṃ daharā na miyyare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§98.</p>

```
Pāṇātipātā <pb ed="M" n="1.0215" /> viramāma sabbe, loke adinnaṃ parivajjayāma;
```

```
Amajjapā nopi musā bhaṇāma, tasmā hi amhaṃ daharā na miyyare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§99.</p>

```
Etāsu ve jāyare suttamāsu, medhāvino honti pahūtapaññā;
```

```
Bahussutā vedaguno <note>vedaguṇā (syā. ka.)</note> ca honti, tasmā hi amhaṃ daharā na miyyare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§100.</p>

```
Mātā pitā ca <note>mātā ca pitā (ka.), mātāpitarā (syā.)</note> bhaginī bhātaro ca, puttā ca dārā ca mayañca sabbe;
```

```
Dhammaṃ carāma paralokahetu, tasmā hi amhaṃ daharā na miyyare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§101.</p>

```
Dāsā ca dāsyo <note>dāsso (sī. pī.), dāsī (syā.)</note> anujīvino ca, paricārakā kammakarā ca sabbe;
```

```
Dhammaṃ caranti paralokahetu, tasmā <pb ed="T" n="1.0290" /> hi amhaṃ daharā na miyyare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§102.</p>

```
Dhammo have rakkhati dhammacāriṃ, dhammo suciṇṇo sukhamāvahāti;
```

```
Esānisaṃso dhamme suciṇṇe, na duggatiṃ gacchati dhammacārī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§103.</p>

```
Dhammo have rakkhati dhammacāriṃ, chattaṃ mahantaṃ viya vassakāle;
```

```
Dhammena gutto mama dhammapālo, aññassa aṭṭhīni sukhī kumāroti.
```

Mahādhammapālajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 448. Kukkuṭajātakaṃ (10)

<p rend="hangnum">§104.</p>

```
Nāsmase <pb ed="M" n="1.0216" /> katapāpamhi, nāsmase alikavādine;
```

```
Nāsmase attatthapaññamhi, atisantepi nāsmase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§105.</p>

```
Bhavanti heke purisā, gopipāsikajātikā <note>gopipāsakajātikā (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Ghasanti maññe mittāni, vācāya na ca kammunā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§106.</p>

```
Sukkhañjalipaggahitā, vācāya paliguṇṭhitā;
```

```
Manussapheggū nāsīde, yasmiṃ natthi kataññutā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§107.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="V" n="1.0172" /> hi aññaññacittānaṃ, itthīnaṃ purisāna vā;
```

```
Nānāvikatvā <note>nānāva katvā (sī. pī.)</note> saṃsaggaṃ, tādisampi ca nāsmase <note>tādisampi na vissase (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§108.</p>

```
Anariyakammamokkantaṃ<pb ed="T" n="1.0291" />, athetaṃ <note>atthetaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> sabbaghātinaṃ;
```

```
Nisitaṃva paṭicchannaṃ, tādisampi ca nāsmase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§109.</p>

```
Mittarūpenidhekacce, sākhalyena acetasā;
```

```
Vividhehi upāyanti, tādisampi ca nāsmase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§110.</p>

```
Āmisaṃ vā dhanaṃ vāpi, yattha passati tādiso;
```

```
Dubbhiṃ karoti dummedho, tañca hantvāna <note>jhātvāna (sī. pī.), hitvāna (syā.)</note> gacchati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§111.</p>

```
Mittarūpena bahavo, channā sevanti sattavo;
```

```
Jahe kāpurise hete, kukkuṭo viya senakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§112.</p>

```
Yo ca <note>yodha (jā. 1.8.25 sulasājātake)</note> uppatitaṃ atthaṃ, na khippamanubujjhati;
```

```
Amittavasamanveti, pacchā ca anutappati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§113.</p>

```
Yo ca uppatitaṃ atthaṃ, khippameva nibodhati;
```

```
Muccate sattusambādhā, kukkuṭo viya senakā;
```

<p rend="hangnum">§114.</p>

```
Taṃ tādisaṃ kūṭamivoḍḍitaṃ vane, adhammikaṃ niccavidhaṃsakārinaṃ;
```

```
Ārā vivajjeyya naro vicakkhaṇo, senaṃ yathā kukkuṭo vaṃsakānaneti.
```

Kukkuṭajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

#### 449. Maṭṭhakuṇḍalījātakaṃ (11)

<p rend="hangnum">§115.</p>

```
Alaṅkato <pb ed="T" n="1.0292" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0217" /> maṭṭhakuṇḍalī <note>maṭṭakuṇḍalī (sī. pī.)</note>, māladhārī <note>mālabhārī (sī. pī.)</note> haricandanussado;
```

```
Bāhā paggayha kandasi, vanamajjhe kiṃ dukkhito tuvaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§116.</p>

```
Sovaṇṇamayo pabhassaro, uppanno rathapañjaro mama;
```

```
Tassa cakkayugaṃ na vindāmi, tena dukkhena jahāmi jīvitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§117.</p>

```
Sovaṇṇamayaṃ maṇīmayaṃ, lohamayaṃ atha rūpiyāmayaṃ;
```

```
<note>ācikkha me bhaddamāṇava (vi. va. 1209)</note> Pāvada rathaṃ karissāmi <note>kārayāmi (sī. pī.)</note> te <note>ācikkha me bhaddamāṇava (vi. va. 1209)</note>, cakkayugaṃ paṭipādayāmi taṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§118.</p>

```
So <note>atha (syā.)</note> māṇavo tassa pāvadi, candimasūriyā <note>candimasūriyā (syā.)</note> ubhayettha bhātaro <note>dissare (vi. va. 1210)</note>;
```

```
Sovaṇṇamayo ratho mama, tena cakkayugena sobhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§119.</p>

```
Bālo kho tvaṃsi māṇava, yo tvaṃ patthayase apatthiyaṃ;
```

```
Maññāmi tuvaṃ marissasi, na <pb ed="T" n="1.0293" /> hi tvaṃ lacchasi candasūriye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§120.</p>

```
Gamanāgamanampi <pb ed="V" n="1.0173" /> dissati, vaṇṇadhātu ubhayettha vīthiyo;
```

```
Peto pana neva dissati, ko nu kho <note>ko nidha (vi. va. 1212)</note> kandataṃ bālyataro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§121.</p>

```
Saccaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0218" /> kho vadesi māṇava, ahameva kandataṃ bālyataro;
```

```
Candaṃ viya dārako rudaṃ, petaṃ kālakatābhipatthaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§122.</p>

```
Ādittaṃ vata maṃ santaṃ, ghatasittaṃva pāvakaṃ;
```

```
Vārinā viya osiñcaṃ, sabbaṃ nibbāpaye daraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§123.</p>

```
Abbahī <note>abbuhi (syā.), abbhuḷhaṃ (ka.)</note> vata me sallaṃ, yamāsi hadayassitaṃ <note>sokaṃ hadayanissitaṃ (vi. va. 1215)</note>;
```

```
Yo me sokaparetassa, puttasokaṃ apānudi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§124.</p>

```
Sohaṃ abbūḷhasallosmi, vītasoko anāvilo;
```

```
Na socāmi na rodāmi, tava sutvāna māṇavāti.
```

Maṭṭhakuṇḍalījātakaṃ ekādasamaṃ.

#### 450. Bilārakosiyajātakaṃ (12)

<p rend="hangnum">§125.</p>

```
Apacantāpi dicchanti, santo laddhāna bhojanaṃ;
```

```
Kimeva tvaṃ pacamāno, yaṃ na dajjā na taṃ samaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§126.</p>

```
Maccherā <pb ed="T" n="1.0294" /> ca pamādā ca, evaṃ dānaṃ na diyyati;
```

```
Puññaṃ ākaṅkhamānena, deyyaṃ hoti vijānatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§127.</p>

```
Yasseva bhīto na dadāti maccharī, tadevādadato bhayaṃ;
```

```
Jighacchā ca pipāsā ca, yassa bhāyati maccharī;
```

```
Tameva bālaṃ phusati, asmiṃ loke paramhi ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§128.</p>

```
Tasmā vineyya maccheraṃ, dajjā dānaṃ malābhibhū;
```

```
Puññāni paralokasmiṃ, patiṭṭhā honti pāṇinaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§129.</p>

```
Duddadaṃ dadamānānaṃ, dukkaraṃ kamma kubbataṃ;
```

```
Asanto nānukubbanti, sataṃ dhammo durannayo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§130.</p>

```
Tasmā satañca asataṃ <note>asatañca (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, nānā hoti ito gati;
```

```
Asanto nirayaṃ yanti, santo saggaparāyanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§131.</p>

```
Appasmeke <pb ed="M" n="1.0219" /> <note>appampeke (syā.)</note> pavecchanti, bahuneke na dicchare;
```

```
Appasmā dakkhiṇā dinnā, sahassena samaṃ mitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§132.</p>

```
Dhammaṃ care yopi samuñchakaṃ care, dārañca posaṃ dadamappakasmiṃ <note>dadaṃ appakasmipi (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Sataṃ sahassānaṃ sahassayāginaṃ, kalampi <pb ed="T" n="1.0295" /> nāgghanti tathāvidhassa te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§133.</p>

```
Kenesa <pb ed="V" n="1.0174" /> yañño vipulo mahagghato <note>mahaggato (saṃ. ni. 1.32)</note>, samena dinnassa na agghameti;
```

```
Kathaṃ sataṃ sahassānaṃ <note>kathaṃ sahassānaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> sahassayāginaṃ, kalampi nāgghanti tathāvidhassa te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§134.</p>

```
Dadanti heke visame niviṭṭhā, chetvā <note>jhatvā (sī. pī.), ghatvā (syā.)</note> vadhitvā atha socayitvā;
```

```
Sā dakkhiṇā assumukhā sadaṇḍā, samena dinnassa na agghameti;
```

```
Evaṃ sataṃ sahassānaṃ <note>evaṃ sahassānaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> sahassayāginaṃ, kalampi nāgghanti tathāvidhassa teti.
```

Bilārakosiyajātakaṃ dvādasamaṃ.

#### 451. Cakkavākajātakaṃ (13)

<p rend="hangnum">§135.</p>

```
Vaṇṇavā abhirūposi, ghano sañjātarohito;
```

```
Cakkavāka surūposi, vippasannamukhindriyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§136.</p>

```
Pāṭhīnaṃ pāvusaṃ macchaṃ, balajaṃ <note>vālajaṃ (sī. pī.), balajjaṃ (syā.)</note> muñjarohitaṃ;
```

```
Gaṅgāya tīre nisinno <note>gaṅgātīre nisinnosi (syā. ka.)</note>, evaṃ bhuñjasi bhojanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§137.</p>

```
Na vāhametaṃ <note>sabbatthapi samānaṃ</note> bhuñjāmi, jaṅgalānodakāni vā;
```

```
Aññatra sevālapaṇakā, etaṃ <note>aññaṃ (syā.)</note> me samma bhojanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§138.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="M" n="1.0220" /> vāhametaṃ saddahāmi, cakkavākassa bhojanaṃ;
```

```
Ahampi samma bhuñjāmi, gāme loṇiyateliyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§139.</p>

```
Manussesu kataṃ bhattaṃ, suciṃ maṃsūpasecanaṃ;
```

```
Na <pb ed="T" n="1.0296" /> ca me tādiso vaṇṇo, cakkavāka yathā tuvaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§140.</p>

```
Sampassaṃ attani veraṃ, hiṃsayaṃ <note>hiṃsāya (syā. pī. ka.)</note> mānusiṃ pajaṃ;
```

```
Utrasto ghasasī bhīto, tena vaṇṇo tavediso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§141.</p>

```
Sabbalokaviruddhosi, dhaṅka pāpena kammunā;
```

```
Laddho piṇḍo na pīṇeti, tena vaṇṇo tavediso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§142.</p>

```
Ahampi <note>ahañca (?)</note> samma bhuñjāmi, ahiṃsaṃ sabbapāṇinaṃ;
```

```
Appossukko nirāsaṅkī, asoko akutobhayo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§143.</p>

```
So karassu ānubhāvaṃ, vītivattassu sīliyaṃ;
```

```
Ahiṃsāya cara loke, piyo hohisi maṃmiva.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§144.</p>

```
Yo na hanti na ghāteti, na jināti na jāpaye;
```

```
Mettaṃso sabbabhūtesu, veraṃ tassa na kenacīti.
```

Cakkavākajātakaṃ terasamaṃ.

#### 452. Bhūripaññajātakaṃ (14)

<p rend="hangnum">§145.</p>

```
Saccaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0175" /> kira tvaṃ api <note>tvampi (sī.), tuvampi (syā.), tvaṃ asi (ka.)</note> bhūripañña, yā tādisī sīri dhitī matī ca;
```

```
Na tāyatebhāvavasūpanitaṃ, yo yavakaṃ bhuñjasi appasūpaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§146.</p>

```
Sukhaṃ dukkhena paripācayanto, kālā kālaṃ vicinaṃ chandachanno;
```

```
Atthassa <pb ed="T" n="1.0297" /> dvārāni avāpuranto, tenāhaṃ tussāmi yavodanena.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§147.</p>

```
Kālañca <pb ed="M" n="1.0221" /> ñatvā abhijīhanāya, mantehi atthaṃ paripācayitvā;
```

```
Vijambhissaṃ sīhavijambhitāni, tāyiddhiyā dakkhasi maṃ punāpi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§148.</p>

```
Sukhīpi heke <note>sukhī hi eke (sī.), sukhīti heke (?)</note> na karonti pāpaṃ, avaṇṇasaṃsaggabhayā puneke;
```

```
Pahū samāno vipulatthacintī, kiṃkāraṇā me na karosi dukkhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§149.</p>

```
Na paṇḍitā attasukhassa hetu, pāpāni kammāni samācaranti;
```

```
Dukkhena phuṭṭhā khalitāpi santā, chandā ca dosā na jahanti dhammaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§150.</p>

```
Yena kenaci vaṇṇena, mudunā dāruṇena vā;
```

```
Uddhare dīnamattānaṃ, pacchā dhammaṃ samācare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§151.</p>

```
Yassa rukkhassa chāyāya, nisīdeyya sayeyya vā;
```

```
Na tassa sākhaṃ bhañjeyya, mittadubbho hi pāpako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§152.</p>

```
Yassāpi <note>yassa hi (sī. ka.)</note> dhammaṃ puriso <note>manujo (sī.)</note> vijaññā, ye cassa kaṅkhaṃ vinayanti santo;
```

```
Taṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0298" /> hissa dīpañca parāyanañca, na tena mettiṃ jarayetha pañño.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§153.</p>

```
Alaso gihī kāmabhogī na sādhu, asaññato pabbajito na sādhu;
```

```
