Rājā na sādhu anisammakārī, yo paṇḍito kodhano taṃ na sādhu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§154.</p>

```
Nisamma khattiyo kayirā, nānisamma disampati;
```

```
Nisammakārino rāja, yaso kitti ca vaḍḍhatīti.
```

Bhūripaññajātakaṃ cuddasamaṃ.

#### 453. Mahāmaṅgalajātakaṃ (15)

<p rend="hangnum">§155.</p>

```
Kiṃsu <pb ed="M" n="1.0222" /> naro jappamadhiccakāle, kaṃ vā vijjaṃ katamaṃ vā sutānaṃ;
```

```
So macco asmiñca <note>asmiṃva (pī.)</note> paramhi loke, kathaṃ karo sotthānena gutto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§156.</p>

```
Yassa devā pitaro ca sabbe, sarīsapā <note>siriṃsapā (sī. syā. pī.)</note> sabbabhūtāni cāpi;
```

```
Mettāya niccaṃ apacitāni honti, bhūtesu ve sotthānaṃ tadāhu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§157.</p>

```
Yo <pb ed="V" n="1.0176" /> sabbalokassa nivātavutti, itthīpumānaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0299" /> sahadārakānaṃ;
```

```
Khantā duruttānamappaṭikūlavādī, adhivāsanaṃ sotthānaṃ tadāhu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§158.</p>

```
Yo nāvajānāti sahāyamitte <note>sahāyamatte (sī. pī.)</note>, sippena kulyāhi dhanena jaccā;
```

```
Rucipañño atthakāle matīmā <note>mutīmā (sī. pī.)</note>, sahāyesu ve sotthānaṃ tadāhu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§159.</p>

```
Mittāni ve yassa bhavanti santo, saṃvissatthā avisaṃvādakassa;
```

```
Na mittadubbhī saṃvibhāgī dhanena, mittesu ve sotthānaṃ tadāhu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§160.</p>

```
Yassa bhariyā tulyavayā samaggā, anubbatā dhammakāmā pajātā <note>sajātā (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Koliniyā sīlavatī patibbatā, dāresu ve sotthānaṃ tadāhu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§161.</p>

```
Yassa <pb ed="M" n="1.0223" /> rājā bhūtapati <note>bhūtapatī (sī. syā. pī.)</note> yasassī, jānāti soceyyaṃ parakkamañca;
```

```
Advejjhatā suhadayaṃ mamanti, rājūsu ve sotthānaṃ tadāhu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§162.</p>

```
Annañca <pb ed="T" n="1.0300" /> pānañca dadāti saddho, mālañca gandhañca vilepanañca;
```

```
Pasannacitto anumodamāno, saggesu ve sotthānaṃ tadāhu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§163.</p>

```
Yamariyadhammena punanti vuddhā, ārādhitā samacariyāya santo;
```

```
Bahussutā isayo sīlavanto, arahantamajjhe sotthānaṃ tadāhu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§164.</p>

```
Etāni kho sotthānāni loke, viññuppasatthāni sukhudrayāni <note>sukhindriyāni (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Tānīdha sevetha naro sapañño, na hi maṅgale kiñcanamatthi saccanti.
```

Mahāmaṅgalajātakaṃ pannarasamaṃ.

#### 454. Ghaṭapaṇḍitajātakaṃ (16)

<p rend="hangnum">§165.</p>

```
Uṭṭhehi kaṇha kiṃ sesi, ko attho supanena te;
```

```
Yopi tuyhaṃ <note>tāyaṃ (pī.)</note> sako bhātā, hadayaṃ cakkhu ca <note>cakkhuṃva (pī.)</note> dakkhiṇaṃ;
```

```
Tassa vātā balīyanti, ghaṭo jappati <note>sasaṃ jappati (?)</note> kesava.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§166.</p>

```
Tassa taṃ vacanaṃ sutvā, rohiṇeyyassa kesavo;
```

```
Taramānarūpo vuṭṭhāsi, bhātusokena aṭṭito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§167.</p>

```
Kiṃ nu <pb ed="T" n="1.0301" /> ummattarūpova, kevalaṃ dvārakaṃ imaṃ;
```

```
Saso sasoti lapasi, ko nu te sasamāhari.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§168.</p>

```
Sovaṇṇamayaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0224" /> maṇīmayaṃ, lohamayaṃ atha rūpiyāmayaṃ;
```

```
Saṅkhasilāpavāḷamayaṃ, kārayissāmi te sasaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§169.</p>

```
Santi aññepi sasakā, araññe vanagocarā;
```

```
Tepi te ānayissāmi, kīdisaṃ sasamicchasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§170.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="V" n="1.0177" /> cāhamete <note>na cāhametaṃ (sī.), na vāhamete (syā.), na vāhametaṃ (pī.)</note> icchāmi, ye sasā pathavissitā <note>paṭhaviṃsitā (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Candato sasamicchāmi, taṃ me ohara kesava.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§171.</p>

```
So nūna madhuraṃ ñāti, jīvitaṃ vijahissasi;
```

```
Apatthiyaṃ yo patthayasi, candato sasamicchasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§172.</p>

```
Evaṃ ce kaṇha jānāsi, yadaññamanusāsasi;
```

```
Kasmā pure mataṃ puttaṃ, ajjāpi manusocasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§173.</p>

```
Yaṃ na labbhā manussena, amanussena vā puna <note>pana (pe. va. 215)</note>;
```

```
Jāto me mā marī putto, kuto labbhā alabbhiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§174.</p>

```
Na mantā mūlabhesajjā, osadhehi dhanena vā;
```

```
Sakkā ānayituṃ kaṇha, yaṃ petamanusocasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§175.</p>

```
Yassa etādisā assu, amaccā purisapaṇḍitā;
```

```
Yathā nijjhāpaye ajja, ghaṭo purisapaṇḍito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§176.</p>

```
Ādittaṃ vata maṃ santaṃ, ghatasittaṃva pāvakaṃ;
```

```
Vārinā viya osiñcaṃ, sabbaṃ nibbāpaye daraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§177.</p>

```
Abbahī <pb ed="T" n="1.0302" /> vata me sallaṃ, yamāsi hadayassitaṃ;
```

```
Yo me sokaparetassa, puttasokaṃ apānudi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§178.</p>

```
Sohaṃ abbūḷhasallosmi, vītasoko anāvilo;
```

```
Na socāmi na rodāmi, tava sutvāna māṇava <note>bhātika (pe. va. 224)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§179.</p>

```
Evaṃ karonti sappaññā, ye honti anukampakā;
```

```
Nivattayanti sokamhā, ghaṭo jeṭṭhaṃva bhātaranti.
```

Ghaṭapaṇḍitajātakaṃ soḷasamaṃ.

<trailer rend="centre">Dasakanipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.</trailer>

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Daḷha <pb ed="M" n="1.0225" /> kaṇha dhanañjaya saṅkhavaro, raja sattaha kassa ca <note>sattāhasasākha (syā.)</note> takkalinā;
```

```
Dhammaṃ kukkuṭa kuṇḍali bhojanadā, cakkavāka subhūrisa sotthi ghaṭoti.
```

### 11. Ekādasakanipāto

#### 455. Mātuposakajātakaṃ (1)

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
Tassa <pb ed="T" n="1.0303" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0178" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0226" /> nāgassa vippavāsena, virūḷhā sallakī ca kuṭajā ca;
```

```
Kuruvindakaravīrā <note>karavarā (sī. syā.)</note> tisasāmā ca, nivāte pupphitā ca kaṇikārā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
Kocideva suvaṇṇakāyurā, nāgarājaṃ bharanti piṇḍena;
```

```
Yattha rājā rājakumāro vā, kavacamabhihessati achambhito <note>asambhīto (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
Gaṇhāhi nāga kabaḷaṃ, mā nāga kisako bhava;
```

```
Bahūni rājakiccāni, tāni <note>yāni (sī. pī.)</note> nāga karissasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
Sā nūnasā kapaṇikā, andhā apariṇāyikā;
```

```
Khāṇuṃ pādena ghaṭṭeti, giriṃ caṇḍoraṇaṃ pati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
Kā nu te sā mahānāga, andhā apariṇāyikā;
```

```
Khāṇuṃ pādena ghaṭṭeti, giriṃ caṇḍoraṇaṃ pati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
Mātā me sā mahārāja, andhā apariṇāyikā;
```

```
Khāṇuṃ pādena ghaṭṭeti, giriṃ caṇḍoraṇaṃ pati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
Muñcathetaṃ mahānāgaṃ, yoyaṃ bharati mātaraṃ;
```

```
Sametu <pb ed="T" n="1.0304" /> mātarā nāgo, saha sabbehi ñātibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
Mutto ca bandhanā nāgo, muttamādāya kuñjaro <note>kāsirājena pesito (sī. syā.), mutto dāmāto kuñjaro (pī. sī. niyya)</note>;
```

```
Muhuttaṃ assāsayitvā <note>vissamitvāna (sī.)</note>, agamā yena pabbato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
Tato so naḷiniṃ <note>nilinaṃ (syā.)</note> gantvā, sītaṃ kuñjarasevitaṃ;
```

```
Soṇḍāyūdakamāhatvā <note>māhitvā (syā. ka.)</note>, mātaraṃ abhisiñcatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
Koya <pb ed="M" n="1.0227" /> anariyo devo, akālenapi vassati <note>akālena pavassati (sī. syā.), akālena’tivassati (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Gato me atrajo putto, yo mayhaṃ paricārako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
Uṭṭhehi amma kiṃ sesi, āgato tyāhamatrajo;
```

```
Muttomhi kāsirājena, vedehena yasassinā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
Ciraṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0179" /> jīvatu so rājā, kāsīnaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhano;
```

```
Yo me puttaṃ pamocesi, sadā vuddhāpacāyikanti.
```

Mātuposakajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 456. Juṇhajātakaṃ (2)

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
Suṇohi mayhaṃ vacanaṃ janinda, atthena juṇhamhi idhānupatto;
```

```
Na brāhmaṇe addhike tiṭṭhamāne, gantabba <note>gantabya (ka.)</note> māhu dvipadinda <note>dipadāna (sī. pī.), dvipadāna (syā.)</note> seṭṭha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
Suṇomi <pb ed="T" n="1.0305" /> tiṭṭhāmi vadehi brahme, yenāsi <note>yenāpi (syā. ka.)</note> atthena idhānupatto;
```

```
Kaṃ vā tvamatthaṃ mayi patthayāno, idhāgamā brahme tadiṅgha brūhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
Dadāhi me gāmavarāni pañca, dāsīsataṃ satta gavaṃsatāni;
```

```
Parosahassañca suvaṇṇanikkhe, bhariyā ca me sādisī dve dadāhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
Tapo nu te brāhmaṇa bhiṃsarūpo, mantā nu te brāhmaṇa cittarūpā;
```

```
Yakkhā nu <note>yakkhā va (sī. pī.)</note> te assavā santi keci, atthaṃ vā me abhijānāsi kattaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="M" n="1.0228" /> me tapo atthi na cāpi mantā, yakkhāpi me assavā natthi keci;
```

```
Atthampi te nābhijānāmi kattaṃ, pubbe ca kho <note>pubbeva kho (syā. ka.)</note> saṅgatimattamāsi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
Paṭhamaṃ idaṃ dassanaṃ jānato me, na tābhijānāmi ito puratthā;
```

```
Akkhāhi me pucchito etamatthaṃ, kadā kuhiṃ vā ahu saṅgamo no.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
Gandhārarājassa <pb ed="T" n="1.0306" /> puramhi ramme, avasimhase takkasīlāyaṃ deva;
```

```
Tatthandhakāramhi timīsikāyaṃ <note>timissikāyaṃ (sī. aṭṭha.), timissakāyaṃ (syā.)</note>, aṃsena aṃsaṃ samaghaṭṭayimha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
Te tattha ṭhatvāna ubho janinda, sārāṇiyaṃ <note>sāraṇīyaṃ (ka.)</note> vītisārayimha <note>vītisārimha (sī. syā. pī.)</note> tattha;
```

```
Sāyeva no saṅgatimattamāsi, tato na pacchā na pure ahosi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
Yadā kadāci manujesu brahme, samāgamo sappurisena hoti;
```

```
Na paṇḍitā saṅgatisanthavāni, pubbe kataṃ vāpi vināsayanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
Bālāva <note>bālā ca (sī. syā. pī.)</note> kho saṅgatisanthavāni, pubbe kataṃ vāpi vināsayanti;
```

```
Bahumpi bālesu kataṃ vinassati, tathā hi bālā akataññurūpā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
Dhīrā ca kho saṅgatisanthavāni, pubbe kataṃ vāpi na nāsayanti;
```

```
Appampi dhīresu kataṃ na nassati, tathā hi dhīrā sukataññurūpā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
Dadāmi <pb ed="T" n="1.0307" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0229" /> te gāmavarāni pañca, dāsīsataṃ satta gavaṃsatāni;
```

```
Parosahassañca suvaṇṇanikkhe, bhariyā ca te sādisī dve dadāmi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
Evaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0180" /> sataṃ hoti samecca rāja, nakkhattarājāriva tārakānaṃ;
```

```
Āpūratī kāsipatī tathāhaṃ, tayāpi me saṅgamo ajja laddhoti.
```

Juṇhajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 457. Dhammadevaputtajātakaṃ (3)

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
Yasokaro puññakarohamasmi, sadātthuto samaṇabrāhmaṇānaṃ;
```

```
Maggāraho devamanussapūjito, dhammo ahaṃ dehi adhamma maggaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
Adhammayānaṃ daḷhamāruhitvā, asantasanto balavāhamasmi;
```

```
Sa kissa hetumhi tavajja dajjaṃ, maggaṃ ahaṃ dhamma adinnapubbaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
Dhammo have pāturahosi pubbe, pacchā <pb ed="T" n="1.0308" /> adhammo udapādi loke;
```

```
Jeṭṭho ca seṭṭho ca sanantano ca, uyyāhi jeṭṭhassa kaniṭṭha maggā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
Na yācanāya napi pātirūpā, na arahatā <note>na arahati (sī. pī.), arahati (ka.)</note> tehaṃ dadeyyaṃ maggaṃ;
```

```
Yuddhañca no hotu ubhinnamajja, yuddhamhi yo jessati tassa maggo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
Sabbā <pb ed="M" n="1.0230" /> disā anuvisaṭohamasmi, mahabbalo amitayaso atulyo;
```

```
Guṇehi sabbehi upetarūpo, dhammo adhamma tvaṃ kathaṃ vijessasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
Lohena ve haññati jātarūpaṃ, na jātarūpena hananti lohaṃ;
```

```
Sace adhammo hañchati <note>haññati (sī. syā.), haññiti (katthaci)</note> dhammamajja, ayo suvaṇṇaṃ viya dassaneyyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
Sace tuvaṃ yuddhabalo adhamma <note>yuddhabalo’si’dhamma (ka. sī.), yuddhabalo’sa’dhamma (pī.)</note>, na tuyha vuḍḍhā <note>vaddhā (sī. pī.)</note> ca garū ca atthi;
```

```
Maggañca te dammi piyāppiyena, vācāduruttānipi te khamāmi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
Idañca sutvā vacanaṃ adhammo, avaṃsiro <pb ed="T" n="1.0309" /> patito uddhapādo;
```

```
‘‘Yuddhatthiko ce na labhāmi yuddhaṃ’’, ettāvatā hoti hato adhammo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
Khantībalo yuddhabalaṃ vijetvā, hantvā adhammaṃ nihanitva <note>vihanitvā (ka.)</note> bhūmyā;
```

```
Pāyāsi vitto <note>citto (syā.)</note> abhiruyha sandanaṃ, maggeneva atibalo saccanikkamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
Mātā pitā samaṇabrāhmaṇā ca, asammānitā yassa sake agāre;
```

```
Idheva nikkhippa sarīradehaṃ, kāyassa bhedā nirayaṃ vajanti te <note>vajanti (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Yathā adhammo patito avaṃsiro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
Mātā <pb ed="M" n="1.0231" /> pitā samaṇabrāhmaṇā ca, susammānitā yassa sake agāre;
```

```
Idheva nikkhippa sarīradehaṃ, kāyassa bhedā sugatiṃ vajanti te;
```

```
Yathāpi dhammo abhiruyha sandananti.
```

Dhammadevaputtajātakaṃ <note>dhammajātakaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> tatiyaṃ.

#### 458. Udayajātakaṃ (4)

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
Ekā <pb ed="T" n="1.0310" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0181" /> nisinnā suci saññatūrū, pāsādamāruyha aninditaṅgī;
```

```
Yācāmi taṃ kinnaranettacakkhu, imekarattiṃ ubhayo vasema.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
Okiṇṇantaraparikhaṃ, daḷhamaṭṭālakoṭṭhakaṃ;
```

```
Rakkhitaṃ khaggahatthehi, duppavesamidaṃ puraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
Daharassa yuvino cāpi, āgamo ca na vijjati;
```

```
Atha kena nu vaṇṇena, saṅgamaṃ icchase mayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
Yakkhohamasmi kalyāṇi, āgatosmi tavantike <note>tavantikaṃ (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Tvaṃ maṃ nandaya <note>nandassu (syā. ka.)</note> bhaddante, puṇṇakaṃsaṃ dadāmi te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
Devaṃ va yakkhaṃ atha vā manussaṃ, na patthaye udayamaticca aññaṃ;
```

```
Gaccheva tvaṃ yakkha mahānubhāva, mā cassu gantvā punarāvajittha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
Yā sā rati uttamā kāmabhoginaṃ, yaṃ hetu sattā visamaṃ caranti;
```

```
Mā taṃ ratiṃ jīyi tuvaṃ sucimhi te, dadāmi te rūpiyaṃ kaṃsapūraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
Nāriṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0311" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0232" /> naro nijjhapayaṃ dhanena, ukkaṃsatī yattha karoti chandaṃ;
```

```
Vipaccanīko tava devadhammo, paccakkhato thokatarena esi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
Āyu ca vaṇṇo ca <note>āyuṃ ca vaṇṇaṃ ca (ka. sī. pī.)</note> manussaloke, nihīyati manujānaṃ suggatte;
```

```
Teneva vaṇṇena dhanampi tuyhaṃ, nihīyati jiṇṇatarāsi ajja.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
Evaṃ me pekkhamānassa, rājaputti yasassini;
```

```
Hāyateva tava <note>hāyate vata te (sī. syā. ka.), hāyateva tato (pī.)</note> vaṇṇo, ahorattānamaccaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
Imināva tvaṃ vayasā, rājaputti sumedhase;
```

```
Brahmacariyaṃ careyyāsi, bhiyyo vaṇṇavatī siyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
Devā na jīranti yathā manussā, gattesu tesaṃ valiyo na honti;
```

```
Pucchāmi taṃ yakkha mahānubhāva, kathaṃ nu devāna <note>kathaṃ na devānaṃ (pī.)</note> sarīradeho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
Devā na jīranti yathā manussā, gattesu tesaṃ valiyo na honti;
```

```
Suve suve bhiyyatarova <note>bhiyyataro ca (ka.)</note> tesaṃ, dibbo <pb ed="T" n="1.0312" /> ca vaṇṇo vipulā ca bhogā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
Kiṃsūdha bhītā janatā anekā, maggo ca nekāyatanaṃ pavutto;
```

```
Pucchāmi taṃ yakkha mahānubhāva, katthaṭṭhito paralokaṃ na bhāye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
Vācaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0182" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0233" /> manañca paṇidhāya sammā, kāyena pāpāni akubbamāno;
```

```
Bahunnapānaṃ gharamāvasanto, saddho mudū saṃvibhāgī vadaññū;
```

```
Saṅgāhako sakhilo saṇhavāco, etthaṭṭhito paralokaṃ na bhāye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
Anusāsasi maṃ yakkha, yathā mātā yathā pitā;
```

```
Uḷāravaṇṇaṃ pucchāmi, ko nu tvamasi subrahā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
Udayohamasmi kalyāṇi, saṅkarattā idhāgato <note>saṅgaratthā idhāgato (sī. pī.), saṅgaratthāyidhāgato (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Āmanta kho taṃ gacchāmi, muttosmi tava saṅkarā <note>saṅgarā (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
Sace kho tvaṃ udayosi, saṅkarattā idhāgato;
```

```
Anusāsa maṃ rājaputta, yathāssa puna saṅgamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
Atipatati <note>adhipatatī (sī. pī.)</note> vayo khaṇo tatheva, ṭhānaṃ natthi dhuvaṃ cavanti sattā;
```

```
Parijiyyati addhuvaṃ sarīraṃ, udaye <pb ed="T" n="1.0313" /> mā pamāda <note>mā pamādaṃ (sī.)</note> carassu dhammaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
Kasiṇā pathavī dhanassa pūrā, ekasseva siyā anaññadheyyā;
```

```
Tañcāpi jahati <note>jahāti (sī. syā. pī.), jahātī (?)</note> avītarāgo, udaye mā pamāda carassu dhammaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
Mātā ca pitā ca bhātaro ca, bhariyā yāpi dhanena hoti kītā <note>bhariyāpi dhanena honti atittā (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Te cāpi jahanti aññamaññaṃ, udaye mā pamāda carassu dhammaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
Kāyo <pb ed="M" n="1.0234" /> parabhojananti ñatvā <note>kāyo ca parabhojanaṃ viditvā (ka.)</note>, saṃsāre sugatiñca duggatiñca <note>sugatī ca duggatī ca (sī. syā. pī.), suggatiṃ duggatiñca (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Ittaravāsoti jāniyāna, udaye mā pamāda carassu dhammaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
Sādhu bhāsatiyaṃ <note>bhāsatayaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> yakkho, appaṃ maccāna jīvitaṃ;
```

```
Kasirañca parittañca, tañca dukkhena saṃyutaṃ;
```

```
Sāhaṃ ekā pabbajissāmi, hitvā kāsiṃ surundhananti.
```

Udayajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 459. Pānīyajātakaṃ (5)

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
Mitto <pb ed="T" n="1.0314" /> mittassa pānīyaṃ, adinnaṃ paribhuñjisaṃ;
```

```
Tena pacchā vijigucchiṃ, taṃ pāpaṃ pakataṃ mayā;
```

```
Mā puna akaraṃ pāpaṃ, tasmā pabbajito ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
Paradārañca disvāna, chando me udapajjatha <note>upapajjatha (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Tena pacchā vijigucchiṃ, taṃ pāpaṃ pakataṃ mayā;
```

```
Mā puna akaraṃ pāpaṃ, tasmā pabbajito ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
Pitaraṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0183" /> me mahārāja, corā agaṇhu <note>agaṇhuṃ (sī. pī.), agaṇhi (ka.)</note> kānane;
```

```
Tesāhaṃ pucchito jānaṃ, aññathā naṃ viyākariṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
Tena pacchā vijigucchiṃ, taṃ pāpaṃ pakataṃ mayā;
```

```
Mā puna akaraṃ pāpaṃ, tasmā pabbajito ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
Pāṇātipātamakaruṃ, somayāge upaṭṭhite;
```

```
Tesāhaṃ samanuññāsiṃ, tena pacchā vijigucchiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
Taṃ pāpaṃ pakataṃ mayā, mā puna akaraṃ pāpaṃ;
```

```
Tasmā pabbajito ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
Surāmerayamādhukā <note>madhukā (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, ye janā paṭhamāsu no;
```

```
Bahūnaṃ te anatthāya, majjapānamakappayuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
Tesāhaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0235" /> samanuññāsiṃ, tena pacchā vijigucchiṃ;
```

```
Taṃ pāpaṃ pakataṃ mayā, mā puna akaraṃ pāpaṃ;
```

```
Tasmā pabbajito ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
Dhiratthu <pb ed="T" n="1.0315" /> subahū kāme, duggandhe bahukaṇṭake;
```

```
Ye ahaṃ paṭisevanto, nālabhiṃ tādisaṃ sukhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
Mahassādā sukhā kāmā, natthi kāmā paraṃ <note>kāmaparaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> sukhaṃ;
```

```
Ye kāme paṭisevanti, saggaṃ te upapajjare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
Appassādā dukhā kāmā, natthi kāmā paraṃ dukhaṃ;
```

```
Ye kāme paṭisevanti, nirayaṃ te upapajjare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
Asī yathā sunisito, nettiṃsova supāyiko <note>supāsito (ka. sī. niyya), supāyito (ka. aṭṭha.)</note>;
```

```
Sattīva urasi khittā, kāmā dukkhatarā tato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
Aṅgārānaṃva jalitaṃ, kāsuṃ sādhikaporisaṃ;
```

```
Phālaṃva divasaṃtattaṃ, kāmā dukkhatarā tato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
Visaṃ yathā halāhalaṃ, telaṃ pakkuthitaṃ <note>ukkaṭṭhitaṃ (sī. pī.), pakkuṭṭhitaṃ (syā.)</note> yathā;
```

```
Tambaloha <note>tampalohaṃ (syā.)</note> vilīnaṃva, kāmā dukkhatarā tatoti.
```

Pānīyajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 460. Yudhañcayajātakaṃ (6)

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
Mittāmaccaparibyūḷhaṃ <note>paribbūḷhaṃ (sī. pī.)</note>, ahaṃ vande rathesabhaṃ;
```

```
Pabbajissāmahaṃ rāja <note>pabbajissaṃ mahārāja (sī. pī.)</note>, taṃ devo anumaññatu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
Sace <pb ed="V" n="1.0184" /> te ūnaṃ kāmehi, ahaṃ paripūrayāmi <note>ahaṃva pūrayāmi (ka.)</note> te;
```

```
Yo taṃ hiṃsati vāremi, mā pabbaja <note>pabbaji (pī.)</note> yudhañcaya <note>yudhañjaya (sī. syā.), yuvañjaya (pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="T" n="1.0316" /> matthi ūnaṃ kāmehi, hiṃsitā me na vijjati;
```

```
Dīpañca kātumicchāmi, yaṃ jarā nābhikīrati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
Putto <pb ed="M" n="1.0236" /> vā pitaraṃ yāce, pitā vā puttamorasaṃ;
```

```
Negamo taṃ yāce <note>negamo yācate (sī. syā. pī.)</note> tāta, mā pabbaja yudhañcaya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
Mā maṃ deva nivārehi, pabbajantaṃ rathesabha;
```

```
Māhaṃ kāmehi sammatto, jarāya vasamanvagū.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
Ahaṃ taṃ tāta yācāmi, ahaṃ putta nivāraye;
```

```
Ciraṃ taṃ daṭṭhumicchāmi, mā pabbaja yudhañcaya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
Ussāvova tiṇaggamhi, sūriyuggamanaṃ pati;
```

```
Evamāyu manussānaṃ, mā maṃ amma nivāraya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
Taramāno imaṃ yānaṃ, āropetu <note>taramānā imaṃ yānaṃ, āropentu (sī. pī.)</note> rathesabha;
```

```
Mā me mātā tarantassa, antarāyakarā ahu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
Abhidhāvatha bhaddante, suññaṃ hessati rammakaṃ;
```

```
Yudhañcayo anuññāto, sabbadattena rājinā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
Yohu seṭṭho sahassassa <note>manussānaṃ (syā.), sahassānaṃ (ka.)</note>, yuvā kañcanasannibho;
```

```
Soyaṃ kumāro pabbajito, kāsāyavasano balī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
Ubho kumārā pabbajitā, yudhañcayo yudhiṭṭhilo;
```

```
Pahāya mātāpitaro, saṅgaṃ chetvāna maccunoti.
```

Yudhañcayajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 461. Dasarathajātakaṃ (7)

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
Etha <pb ed="T" n="1.0317" /> lakkhaṇa sītā ca, ubho otarathodakaṃ;
```

```
Evāyaṃ bharato āha, ‘‘rājā dasaratho mato’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
Kena rāmappabhāvena, socitabbaṃ na socasi;
```

```
Pitaraṃ kālakataṃ <note>kālaṅkataṃ (ka.)</note> sutvā, na taṃ pasahate dukhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
Yaṃ na sakkā nipāletuṃ, posena lapataṃ bahuṃ;
```

```
Sa kissa viññū medhāvī, attānamupatāpaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
Daharā <pb ed="V" n="1.0185" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0237" /> ca hi vuddhā ca <note>ye vuddhā (sī. aṭṭha.), ye vuḍḍhā (syā.)</note>, ye bālā ye ca paṇḍitā;
```

```
Aḍḍhā ceva daliddā ca, sabbe maccuparāyaṇā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
Phalānamiva pakkānaṃ, niccaṃ patanato bhayaṃ;
```

```
Evaṃ jātāna maccānaṃ, nicca maraṇato bhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
Sāyameke na dissanti, pāto diṭṭhā bahujjanā;
```

```
Pāto eke na dissanti, sāyaṃ diṭṭhā bahujjanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
Paridevayamāno ce, kiñcidatthaṃ udabbahe;
```

```
Sammūḷho hiṃsamattānaṃ, kayirā taṃ vicakkhaṇo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
Kiso vivaṇṇo bhavati, hiṃsamattānamattano <note>mattanā (sī. aṭṭha. su. ni. 590)</note>;
```

```
Na tena petā pālenti, niratthā paridevanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
Yathā saraṇamādittaṃ, vārinā parinibbaye <note>vārināvanibbāpaye (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Evampi dhīro sutavā, medhāvī paṇḍito naro;
```

```
Khippamuppatitaṃ sokaṃ, vāto tūlaṃva dhaṃsaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§93.</p>

```
Macco ekova <pb ed="T" n="1.0318" /> <note>ekova macco (sī. syā. pī.)</note> acceti, ekova jāyate kule;
```

```
Saṃyogaparamātveva, sambhogā sabbapāṇinaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§94.</p>

```
Tasmā hi dhīrassa bahussutassa, sampassato lokamimaṃ parañca;
```

```
Aññāya dhammaṃ hadayaṃ manañca, sokā mahantāpi na tāpayanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§95.</p>

```
Sohaṃ dassañca bhokkhañca, bharissāmi ca <note>sohaṃ yasañca bhogañca, bhariyāpi ca (syā. ka.)</note> ñātake;
```

```
Sesañca pālayissāmi, kiccametaṃ <note>kiccamevaṃ (pī.)</note> vijānato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§96.</p>

```
Dasa vassasahassāni, saṭṭhi vassasatāni ca;
```

```
Kambugīvo mahābāhu, rāmo rajjamakārayīti.
```

Dasarathajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 462. Saṃvarajātakaṃ (8)

<p rend="hangnum">§97.</p>

```
Jānanto <pb ed="M" n="1.0238" /> no mahārāja, tava sīlaṃ janādhipo;
```

```
Ime kumāre pūjento, na taṃ kenaci maññatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§98.</p>

```
Tiṭṭhante no mahārāje, adu <note>ādu (sī. pī.), ādū (syā.)</note> deve divaṅgate;
```

```
Ñātī taṃ samanuññiṃsu, sampassaṃ atthamattano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§99.</p>

```
Kena saṃvaravattena, sañjāte abhitiṭṭhasi;
```

```
Kena taṃ nātivattanti, ñātisaṅghā samāgatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§100.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="V" n="1.0186" /> rājaputta usūyāmi <note>rājaputta nussuyyāmi (ka.)</note>, samaṇānaṃ mahesinaṃ;
```

```
Sakkaccaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0319" /> te namassāmi, pāde vandāmi tādinaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§101.</p>

```
Te maṃ dhammaguṇe yuttaṃ, sussūsamanusūyakaṃ;
```

```
Samaṇā manusāsanti <note>samanusāsanti (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, isī dhammaguṇe ratā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§102.</p>

```
Tesāhaṃ vacanaṃ sutvā, samaṇānaṃ mahesinaṃ;
```

```
Na kiñci atimaññāmi, dhamme me nirato mano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§103.</p>

```
Hatthārohā anīkaṭṭhā, rathikā pattikārakā;
```

```
Tesaṃ <note>tesu (pī.)</note> nappaṭibandhāmi, niviṭṭhaṃ <note>nibaddhaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> bhattavetanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§104.</p>

```
Mahāmattā ca me atthi, mantino paricārakā;
```

```
Bārāṇasiṃ voharanti, bahumaṃsasurodakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§105.</p>

```
Athopi vāṇijā phītā, nānāraṭṭhehi āgatā;
```

```
Tesu me vihitā rakkhā, evaṃ jānāhuposatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§106.</p>

```
Dhammena kira ñātīnaṃ, rajjaṃ kārehi saṃvara;
```

```
Medhāvī paṇḍito cāsi <note>cāpi (sī. pī.)</note>, athopi ñātinaṃ hito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§107.</p>

```
Taṃ taṃ ñātiparibyūḷhaṃ, nānāratanamocitaṃ;
```

```
Amittā nappasahanti, indaṃva asurādhipoti.
```

Saṃvarajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 463. Suppārakajātakaṃ (9)

<p rend="hangnum">§108.</p>

```
Ummujjanti <pb ed="M" n="1.0239" /> nimujjanti, manussā khuranāsikā;
```

```
Suppārakaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0320" /> taṃ pucchāma, samuddo katamo ayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§109.</p>

```
Kurukacchā <note>bharukacchā (sī. syā. pī. aṭṭha.)</note> payātānaṃ, vāṇijānaṃ dhanesinaṃ;
```

```
Nāvāya vippanaṭṭhāya, khuramālīti vuccati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§110.</p>

```
Yathā aggīva suriyova <note>aggi suriyo ca (syā.), aggīva sūriyo (ka.)</note>, samuddo paṭidissati;
```

```
Suppārakaṃ taṃ pucchāma, samuddo katamo ayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§111.</p>

```
Kurukacchā payātānaṃ, vāṇijānaṃ dhanesinaṃ;
```

```
Nāvāya vippanaṭṭhāya, aggimālīti vuccati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§112.</p>

```
Yathā dadhīva khīraṃva <note>dadhi ca khīraṃ ca (syā.), evamuparipi</note>, samuddo paṭidissati;
```

```
Suppārakaṃ taṃ pucchāma, samuddo katamo ayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§113.</p>

```
Kurukacchā <pb ed="V" n="1.0187" /> payātānaṃ, vāṇijānaṃ dhanesinaṃ;
```

```
Nāvāya vippanaṭṭhāya, dadhimālīti <note>khīramālīti (ka.)</note> vuccati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§114.</p>

```
Yathā kusova sassova, samuddo paṭidissati;
```

```
Suppārakaṃ taṃ pucchāma, samuddo katamo ayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§115.</p>

```
Kurukacchā payātānaṃ, vāṇijānaṃ dhanesinaṃ;
```

```
Nāvāya vippanaṭṭhāya, kusamālīti vuccati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§116.</p>

```
Yathā naḷova veḷūva, samuddo paṭidissati;
```

```
Suppārakaṃ taṃ pucchāma, samuddo katamo ayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§117.</p>

```
Kurukacchā payātānaṃ, vāṇijānaṃ dhanesinaṃ;
```

```
Nāvāya vippanaṭṭhāya, naḷamālīti vuccati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§118.</p>

```
Mahabbhayo bhiṃsanako, saddo suyyatimānuso <note>samuddo suyyata’mānuso (sī. pī. aṭṭha.)</note>;
```

```
Yathā <pb ed="T" n="1.0321" /> sobbho papātova, samuddo paṭidissati;
```

```
Suppārakaṃ taṃ pucchāma, samuddo katamo ayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§119.</p>

```
Kurukacchā <pb ed="M" n="1.0240" /> payātānaṃ, vāṇijānaṃ dhanesinaṃ;
```

```
Nāvāya vippanaṭṭhāya, baḷavāmukhīti <note>vaḷabhāmukhīti (sī. syā.), balavāmukhīti (syā. ka.)</note> vuccati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§120.</p>

```
Yato sarāmi attānaṃ, yato pattosmi viññutaṃ;
```

```
Nābhijānāmi sañcicca, ekapāṇampi hiṃsitaṃ;
```

```
Etena saccavajjena, sotthiṃ nāvā nivattatūti.
```

Suppārakajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

<trailer rend="centre">Ekādasakanipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.</trailer>

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Sirimātusuposakanāgavaro, puna juṇhaka dhammamudayavaro;
```

```
Atha pāni yudhañcayako ca, dasaratha saṃvara pāragatena navāti.
```

### 12. Dvādasakanipāto

#### 464. Cūḷakuṇālajātakaṃ (1)

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
Luddhānaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0322" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0188" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0241" /> <note>khuddānaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> lahucittānaṃ, akataññūna dubbhinaṃ;
```

```
Nādevasatto puriso, thīnaṃ saddhātumarahati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
Na tā pajānanti kataṃ na kiccaṃ, na mātaraṃ pitaraṃ bhātaraṃ vā;
```

```
Anariyā samatikkantadhammā, sasseva cittassa vasaṃ vajanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
Cirānuvuṭṭhampi <note>cirānuvutthampi (sī. pī.)</note> piyaṃ manāpaṃ, anukampakaṃ pāṇasamampi bhattuṃ <note>santaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Āvāsu kiccesu ca naṃ jahanti, tasmāhamitthīnaṃ na vissasāmi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
Thīnañhi cittaṃ yathā vānarassa, kannappakannaṃ yathā rukkhachāyā;
```

```
Calācalaṃ hadayamitthiyānaṃ, cakkassa nemi viya parivattati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
Yadā tā passanti samekkhamānā, ādeyyarūpaṃ purisassa vittaṃ;
```

```
Saṇhāhi vācāhi nayanti menaṃ, kambojakā <pb ed="T" n="1.0323" /> jalajeneva assaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
Yadā na passanti samekkhamānā, ādeyyarūpaṃ purisassa vittaṃ;
```

```
Samantato naṃ parivajjayanti, tiṇṇo nadīpāragatova kullaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
Silesūpamā <pb ed="M" n="1.0242" /> sikhiriva sabbabhakkhā, tikkhamāyā nadīriva sīghasotā;
```

```
Sevanti hetā piyamappiyañca, nāvā yathā orakūlaṃ parañca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
Na tā ekassa na dvinnaṃ, āpaṇova pasārito;
```

```
Yo tā mayhanti maññeyya, vātaṃ jālena bādhaye <note>bandhaye (syā. ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
Yathā nadī ca pantho ca, pānāgāraṃ sabhā papā;
```

```
Evaṃ lokitthiyo nāma, velā tāsaṃ na vijjati <note>imissā gāthāya pubbaddhāparaddhaṃ vipariyāyena dissati (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
Ghatāsanasamā etā, kaṇhasappasirūpamā;
```

```
Gāvo bahitiṇasseva, omasanti varaṃ varaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
Ghatāsanaṃ kuñjaraṃ kaṇhasappaṃ, muddhābhisittaṃ pamadā ca sabbā;
```

```
Ete naro niccayato <note>niccayatto (sī. pī.)</note> bhajetha, tesaṃ have dubbidu sabbabhāvo <note>saccabhāvo (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
Naccantavaṇṇā <pb ed="T" n="1.0324" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0189" /> na bahūnaṃ kantā, na dakkhiṇā pamadā sevitabbā;
```

```
Na parassa bhariyā na dhanassa hetu, etitthiyo pañca na sevitabbāti.
```

Cūḷakuṇālajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 465. Bhaddasālajātakaṃ (2)

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
Kā tvaṃ suddhehi vatthehi, aghe vehāyasaṃ <note>vehāsayaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> ṭhitā;
```

```
Kena tyāssūni vattanti, kuto taṃ bhayamāgataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
Taveva deva vijite, bhaddasāloti maṃ vidū;
```

```
Saṭṭhi <note>saṭṭhiṃ (sī. pī.)</note> vassasahassāni, tiṭṭhato pūjitassa me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
Kārayantā <pb ed="M" n="1.0243" /> nagarāni, agāre ca disampati;
```

```
Vividhe cāpi pāsāde, na maṃ te accamaññisuṃ;
```

```
Yatheva maṃ te pūjesuṃ, tatheva tvampi pūjaya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
Taṃ ivāhaṃ <note>tañca ahaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> na passāmi, thūlaṃ kāyena te dumaṃ;
```

```
Ārohapariṇāhena, abhirūposi jātiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
Pāsādaṃ kārayissāmi, ekatthambhaṃ manoramaṃ;
```

```
Tattha taṃ upanessāmi, ciraṃ te yakkha jīvitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
Evaṃ cittaṃ udapādi, sarīrena vinābhāvo;
```

```
Puthuso maṃ vikantitvā, khaṇḍaso avakantatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
Agge <pb ed="T" n="1.0325" /> ca chetvā majjhe ca, pacchā mūlamhi chindatha <note>mūlañca chindatha (sī.), mūlaṃ vichindatha (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Evaṃ me chijjamānassa, na dukkhaṃ maraṇaṃ siyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
Hatthapādaṃ <note>hatthapāde (ka.)</note> yathā chinde <note>chinne (ka.)</note>, kaṇṇanāsañca jīvato;
```

```
Tato pacchā siro chinde, taṃ dukkhaṃ maraṇaṃ siyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
Sukhaṃ nu khaṇḍaso chinnaṃ, bhaddasālavanappati;
```

```
Kiṃ hetu kiṃ upādāya, khaṇḍaso chinnamicchasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
Yañca hetumupādāya, hetuṃ dhammūpasaṃhitaṃ;
```

```
Khaṇḍaso chinnamicchāmi, mahārāja suṇohi me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
Ñātī me sukhasaṃvaddhā, mama passe nivātajā;
```

```
Tepihaṃ upahiṃseyyaṃ, paresaṃ asukhocitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
Ceteyyarūpaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0190" /> <note>cetabbarūpaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> cetesi, bhaddasālavanappati;
```

```
Hitakāmosi ñātīnaṃ, abhayaṃ samma dammi teti.
```

Bhaddasālajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 466. Samuddavāṇijajātakaṃ (3)

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
Kasanti <pb ed="M" n="1.0244" /> vapanti te janā, manujā kammaphalūpajīvino;
```

```
Nayimassa dīpakassa bhāgino, jambudīpā idameva no varaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
Tipañcarattūpagatamhi cande, vego <pb ed="T" n="1.0326" /> mahā hehiti sāgarassa;
```

```
Uplavissaṃ dīpamimaṃ uḷāraṃ, mā vo vadhī gacchatha leṇamaññaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
Na jātuyaṃ sāgaravārivego, uplavissaṃ dīpamimaṃ uḷāraṃ;
```

```
Taṃ me nimittehi bahūhi diṭṭhaṃ, mā bhetha kiṃ socatha modathavho <note>modatha vo (ka.) 6.38 moggallānasuttaṃ passitabbaṃ</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
Pahūtabhakkhaṃ bahuannapānaṃ, pattattha āvāsamimaṃ uḷāraṃ;
```

```
Na vo bhayaṃ paṭipassāmi kiñci, āputtaputtehi pamodathavho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
Yo devoyaṃ dakkhiṇāyaṃ <note>dakkhiṇassaṃ (sī.)</note> disāyaṃ, khemanti pakkosati tassa saccaṃ;
```

```
Na uttaro vedi bhayābhayassa, mā bhetha kiṃ socatha modathavho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
Yathā ime vippavadanti yakkhā, eko bhayaṃ saṃsati khemameko;
```

```
Tadiṅgha mayhaṃ vacanaṃ suṇātha, khippaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0327" /> lahuṃ mā vinassimha sabbe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
Sabbe <pb ed="M" n="1.0245" /> samāgamma karoma nāvaṃ, doṇiṃ daḷhaṃ sabbayantūpapannaṃ;
```

```
Sace ayaṃ dakkhiṇo saccamāha, moghaṃ paṭikkosati uttaroyaṃ;
```

```
Sā ceva no hehiti āpadatthā, imañca dīpaṃ na pariccajema.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
Sace ca kho uttaro saccamāha, moghaṃ paṭikkosati dakkhiṇoyaṃ;
```

```
Tameva nāvaṃ abhiruyha sabbe, evaṃ mayaṃ sotthi taremu pāraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
Na ve sugaṇhaṃ paṭhamena seṭṭhaṃ, kaniṭṭhamāpāthagataṃ gahetvā;
```

```
Yo cīdha tacchaṃ <note>majjhaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> paviceyya gaṇhati <note>gaṇhi (ka.)</note>, sa ve naro seṭṭhamupeti ṭhānaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
Yathāpi te sāgaravārimajjhe, sakammunā sotthi vahiṃsu vāṇijā;
```

```
Anāgatatthaṃ paṭivijjhiyāna, appampi nācceti sa bhūripañño.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
Bālā <pb ed="T" n="1.0328" /> ca mohena rasānugiddhā, anāgataṃ appaṭivijjhiyatthaṃ;
```

Paccuppanne sīdanti atthajāte, samuddamajjhe yathā te manussā.

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
Anāgataṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0191" /> paṭikayirātha kiccaṃ, ‘‘mā maṃ kiccaṃ kiccakāle byadhesi’’;
```

```
Taṃ tādisaṃ paṭikata <note>paṭikataṃ (ka.), paṭigata (sī. aṭṭha.), paṭikacca (?)</note> kiccakāriṃ, na taṃ kiccaṃ kiccakāle byadhetīti.
```

Samuddavāṇijajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 467. Kāmajātakaṃ (4)

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
Kāmaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0246" /> kāmayamānassa, tassa ce taṃ samijjhati;
```

```
Addhā pītimano hoti, laddhā macco yadicchati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
Kāmaṃ kāmayamānassa, tassa ce taṃ samijjhati;
```

```
Tato naṃ aparaṃ kāme, dhamme taṇhaṃva vindati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
Gavaṃva siṅgino siṅgaṃ, vaḍḍhamānassa vaḍḍhati;
```

```
Evaṃ mandassa posassa, bālassa avijānato;
```

```
Bhiyyo taṇhā pipāsā ca, vaḍḍhamānassa vaḍḍhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
Pathabyā sāliyavakaṃ, gavassaṃ <note>gavāsaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> dāsaporisaṃ;
```

```
Datvā ca <note>datvāpi (sī. syā.), datvā vā (pī.)</note> nālamekassa, iti vidvā <note>viddhā (syā.)</note> samaṃ care.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
Rājā <pb ed="T" n="1.0329" /> pasayha pathaviṃ vijitvā, sasāgarantaṃ mahimāvasanto;
```

```
Oraṃ samuddassa atittarūpo <note>atittirūpo (ka.)</note>, pāraṃ samuddassapi patthayetha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
Yāva anussaraṃ kāme, manasā titti nājjhagā;
```

```
Tato nivattā paṭikamma disvā, te ve sutittā ye <note>tittā (sī. syā. pī.)</note> paññāya tittā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
Paññāya tittinaṃ <note>tittīnaṃ (sī. syā.)</note> seṭṭhaṃ, na so kāmehi tappati;
```

```
Paññāya tittaṃ purisaṃ, taṇhā na kurute vasaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
Apacinetheva kāmānaṃ <note>kāmāni (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, appicchassa alolupo;
```

```
Samuddamatto puriso, na so kāmehi tappati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
Rathakārova cammassa, parikantaṃ upāhanaṃ;
```

```
Yaṃ yaṃ cajati <note>jahati (syā. ka.)</note> kāmānaṃ, taṃ taṃ sampajjate sukhaṃ;
```

```
Sabbaṃ ce sukhamiccheyya, sabbe kāme pariccaje.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
Aṭṭha <pb ed="M" n="1.0247" /> te bhāsitā gāthā, sabbā honti sahassiyo <note>sahassiyā (?) upari sutasomajātake tathā dissati</note>;
```

```
Paṭigaṇha mahābrahme, sādhetaṃ tava bhāsitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
Na me attho sahassehi, satehi nahutehi vā;
```

```
Pacchimaṃ bhāsato gāthaṃ, kāme me na rato mano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
Bhadrako <pb ed="V" n="1.0192" /> <note>saddo (sī.)</note> vatāyaṃ māṇavako, sabbalokavidū muni;
```

```
Yo <pb ed="T" n="1.0330" /> imaṃ taṇhaṃ <note>yo taṇhaṃ (sī. syā.)</note> dukkhajananiṃ, parijānāti paṇḍitoti.
```

Kāmajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 468. Janasandhajātakaṃ (5)

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
Dasa khalu imāni <note>khalumāni (syā.)</note> ṭhānāni, yāni pubbe akaritvā;
```

```
Sa pacchā manutappati, iccevāha <note>iccāha rājā (sī. syā. pī.)</note> janasandho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
Aladdhā vittaṃ tappati, pubbe asamudānitaṃ;
```

```
Na pubbe dhanamesissaṃ, iti pacchānutappati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
Sakyarūpaṃ pure santaṃ, mayā sippaṃ na sikkhitaṃ;
```

```
Kicchā vutti asippassa, iti pacchānutappati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
Kūṭavedī pure āsiṃ, pisuṇo piṭṭhimaṃsiko;
```

```
Caṇḍo ca pharuso cāpi <note>cāsiṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, iti pacchānutappati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
Pāṇātipātī pure āsiṃ, luddo cāpi <note>cāsiṃ (sī. pī.)</note> anāriyo;
```

```
Bhūtānaṃ nāpacāyissaṃ, iti pacchānutappati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
Bahūsu vata santīsu, anāpādāsu itthisu;
```

```
Paradāraṃ asevissaṃ, iti pacchānutappati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
Bahumhi vata santamhi, annapāne upaṭṭhite;
```

```
Na pubbe adadaṃ <note>adadiṃ (sī.)</note> dānaṃ, iti pacchānutappati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
Mātaraṃ pitarañcāpi, jiṇṇakaṃ gatayobbanaṃ <note>jiṇṇake gatayobbane (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Pahu <pb ed="T" n="1.0331" /> santo na posissaṃ, iti pacchānutappati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
Ācariyamanusatthāraṃ<pb ed="M" n="1.0248" />, sabbakāmarasāharaṃ;
```

```
Pitaraṃ atimaññissaṃ, iti pacchānutappati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
Samaṇe brāhmaṇe cāpi, sīlavante bahussute;
```

```
Na pubbe payirupāsissaṃ, iti pacchānutappati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
Sādhu hoti tapo ciṇṇo, santo ca payirupāsito;
```

```
Na ca pubbe tapo ciṇṇo, iti pacchānutappati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
Yo ca etāni ṭhānāni, yoniso paṭipajjati;
```

```
Karaṃ purisakiccāni, sa pacchā nānutappatīti.
```

Janasandhajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 469. Mahākaṇhajātakaṃ (6)

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
Kaṇho <pb ed="V" n="1.0193" /> kaṇho ca ghoro ca, sukkadāṭho pabhāsavā <note>patāpavā (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Baddho pañcahi rajjūhi, kiṃ ravi <note>dhīra (sī. pī.), vīra (syā.)</note> sunakho tava.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
Nāyaṃ migānamatthāya, usīnaka <note>usīnara (sī. pī.), usīnnara (syā.)</note> bhavissati;
```

```
Manussānaṃ anayo hutvā, tadā kaṇho pamokkhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
Pattahatthā samaṇakā, muṇḍā saṅghāṭipārutā;
```

```
Naṅgalehi kasissanti, tadā kaṇho pamokkhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
Tapassiniyo <note>tapanīyā (ka.) dutiyantapadāni hetāni</note> pabbajitā, muṇḍā saṅghāṭipārutā;
```

```
Yadā loke gamissanti, tadā kaṇho pamokkhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
Dīghottaroṭṭhā <pb ed="T" n="1.0332" /> jaṭilā, paṅkadantā rajassirā;
```

```
Iṇaṃ codāya <note>vodāya (sī. pī.), codaya (syā.)</note> gacchanti, tadā kaṇho pamokkhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
Adhicca vede <note>vedaṃ (ka.)</note> sāvittiṃ, yaññatantañca <note>tantrañca (sī. syā. pī.)</note> brāhmaṇā;
```

```
Bhatikāya yajissanti, tadā kaṇho pamokkhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
Mātaraṃ pitarañcāpi, jiṇṇakaṃ gatayobbanaṃ;
```

```
Pahū santo <note>santā (sī.)</note> na bharanti, tadā kaṇho pamokkhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
Mātaraṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0249" /> pitarañcāpi, jiṇṇakaṃ gatayobbanaṃ;
```

```
Bālā tumheti vakkhanti, tadā kaṇho pamokkhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
Ācariyabhariyaṃ sakhiṃ <note>ācariyabhariyaṃ sakhābhariyaṃ (sī. pī.)</note>, mātulāniṃ pitucchakiṃ <note>pitucchayaṃ (sī.), pitucchasaṃ (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Yadā loke gamissanti, tadā kaṇho pamokkhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
Asicammaṃ gahetvāna, khaggaṃ paggayha brāhmaṇā;
```

```
Panthaghātaṃ karissanti, tadā kaṇho pamokkhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
Sukkacchavī vedhaverā, thūlabāhū apātubhā;
```

```
Mittabhedaṃ karissanti, tadā kaṇho pamokkhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
Māyāvino nekatikā, asappurisacintakā;
```

```
Yadā loke bhavissanti, tadā kaṇho pamokkhatīti.
```

Mahākaṇhajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 470. Kosiyajātakaṃ (7)

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
Neva <pb ed="V" n="1.0194" /> kiṇāmi napi vikkiṇāmi, na <pb ed="T" n="1.0333" /> cāpi me sannicayo ca atthi <note>idhatthi (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Sukiccharūpaṃ vatidaṃ parittaṃ, patthodano nālamayaṃ duvinnaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
Appamhā appakaṃ dajjā, anumajjhato majjhakaṃ;
```

```
Bahumhā bahukaṃ dajjā, adānaṃ nupapajjati <note>na upapajjati (sī. pī.), nūpapajjati (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
Taṃ taṃ vadāmi kosiya, dehi dānāni bhuñja ca.
```

```
Ariyamaggaṃ samārūha <note>ariyaṃ maggaṃ samāruha (sī. pī.)</note>, nekāsī labhate sukhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
Moghañcassa hutaṃ hoti, moghañcāpi samīhitaṃ;
```

```
Atithismiṃ yo nisinnasmiṃ, eko bhuñjati bhojanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
Taṃ taṃ vadāmi kosiya, dehi dānāni bhuñja ca;
```

```
Ariyamaggaṃ samārūha, nekāsī labhate sukhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
Saccañcassa <pb ed="M" n="1.0250" /> hutaṃ hoti, saccañcāpi samīhitaṃ;
```

```
Atithismiṃ yo nisinnasmiṃ, neko bhuñjati bhojanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
Taṃ taṃ vadāmi kosiya, dehi dānāni bhuñja ca;
```

```
Ariyamaggaṃ samārūha, nekāsī labhate sukhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
Sarañca juhati poso, bahukāya gayāya ca;
```

```
Doṇe timbarutitthasmiṃ, sīghasote mahāvahe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
Atra cassa hutaṃ hoti, atra cassa samīhitaṃ;
```

```
Atithismiṃ yo nisinnasmiṃ, neko bhuñjati bhojanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
Taṃ taṃ vadāmi kosiya, dehi dānāni bhuñja ca;
```

```
Ariyamaggaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0334" /> samārūha, nekāsī labhate sukhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
Baḷisañhi so nigilati <note>niggilati (sī. pī.)</note>, dīghasuttaṃ sabandhanaṃ;
```

```
Atithismiṃ yo nisinnasmiṃ, eko bhuñjati bhojanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
Taṃ taṃ vadāmi kosiya, dehi dānāni bhuñja ca;
```

```
Ariyamaggaṃ samārūha, nekāsī labhate sukhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
Uḷāravaṇṇā vata brāhmaṇā ime, ayañca vo sunakho kissa hetu;
```

```
Uccāvacaṃ vaṇṇanibhaṃ vikubbati, akkhātha no brāhmaṇā ke nu tumhe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
Cando ca suriyo ca <note>sūriyo ca (ka.)</note> ubho idhāgatā, ayaṃ pana mātali devasārathi;
```

```
Sakkohamasmi tidasānamindo, eso ca kho pañcasikhoti vuccati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
Pāṇissarā <pb ed="V" n="1.0195" /> mudiṅgā ca <note>mutiṅgā ca (sī. syā. pī.</note>, murajālambarāni ca;
```

```
Suttamenaṃ pabodhenti, paṭibuddho ca nandati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
Ye kecime maccharino kadariyā, paribhāsakā samaṇabrāhmaṇānaṃ;
```

```
Idheva nikkhippa sarīradehaṃ, kāyassa bhedā nirayaṃ vajanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
Ye <pb ed="M" n="1.0251" /> kecime suggatimāsamānā <note>suggatimāsasānā (sī. pī.), suggatāsisamānā (ka.)</note>, dhamme <pb ed="T" n="1.0335" /> ṭhitā saṃyame saṃvibhāge;
```

```
Idheva nikkhippa sarīradehaṃ, kāyassa bhedā sugatiṃ vajanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
Tvaṃ nosi ñāti purimāsu jātisu, so maccharī rosako <note>kosiyo (syā. ka.)</note> pāpadhammo;
```

```
Taveva atthāya idhāgatamhā, mā pāpadhammo nirayaṃ gamittha <note>appattha (ka. sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
Addhā hi maṃ vo hitakāmā, yaṃ maṃ samanusāsatha;
```

```
Sohaṃ tathā karissāmi, sabbaṃ vuttaṃ hitesibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
Esāhamajjeva upāramāmi, na cāpihaṃ <note>na cāpahaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> kiñci kareyya pāpaṃ;
```

```
Na cāpi me kiñci adeyyamatthi, na cāpidatvā udakaṃ pivāmi <note>udakampahaṃ pibe (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§93.</p>

```
Evañca me dadato sabbakālaṃ <note>kāle (ka.)</note>, bhogā ime vāsava khīyissanti;
```

```
Tato ahaṃ pabbajissāmi sakka, hitvāna kāmāni yathodhikānīti.
```

Kosiyajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 471. Meṇḍakapañhajātakaṃ (8)

<p rend="hangnum">§94.</p>

```
Yesaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0336" /> na kadāci bhūtapubbaṃ, sakhyaṃ <note>sakkhiṃ (sī. pī.), sakhi (syā.)</note> sattapadampimasmi loke;
```

```
Jātā amittā duve sahāyā, paṭisandhāya caranti kissa hetu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§95.</p>

```
Yadi <pb ed="M" n="1.0252" /> me ajja pātarāsakāle, pañhaṃ na sakkuṇeyyātha vattumetaṃ;
```

```
Raṭṭhā pabbājayissāmi vo sabbe, na hi mattho duppaññajātikehi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§96.</p>

```
Mahājanasamāgamamhi ghore, janakolāhalasaṅgamamhi jāte;
```

```
Vikkhittamanā anekacittā, pañhaṃ na sakkuṇoma vattumetaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§97.</p>

```
Ekaggacittāva ekamekā, rahasi gatā atthaṃ nicintayitvā <note>atthāni cintayitvā (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Paviveke sammasitvāna dhīrā, atha vakkhanti janinda etamatthaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§98.</p>

```
Uggaputta-rājaputtiyānaṃ, urabbhassa maṃsaṃ piyaṃ manāpaṃ;
```

```
Na sunakhassa te adenti maṃsaṃ, atha meṇḍassa suṇena sakhyamassa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§99.</p>

```
Cammaṃ vihananti eḷakassa, assapiṭṭhattharassukhassa <note>assapiṭṭhattharaṇasukhassa (sī.)</note> hetu;
```

```
Na ca te sunakhassa attharanti, atha <pb ed="T" n="1.0337" /> meṇḍassa suṇena sakhyamassa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§100.</p>

```
Āvellitasiṅgiko <pb ed="V" n="1.0196" /> hi meṇḍo, na ca sunakhassa visāṇakāni atthi;
```

```
Tiṇabhakkho maṃsabhojano ca, atha meṇḍassa suṇena sakhyamassa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§101.</p>

```
Tiṇamāsi palāsamāsi meṇḍo, na ca sunakho tiṇamāsi no palāsaṃ;
```

```
Gaṇheyya suṇo sasaṃ biḷāraṃ, atha meṇḍassa suṇena sakhyamassa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§102.</p>

```
Aṭṭhaḍḍhapado <pb ed="M" n="1.0253" /> catuppadassa, meṇḍo aṭṭhanakho adissamāno;
```

```
Chādiyamāharatī ayaṃ imassa, maṃsaṃ āharatī ayaṃ amussa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§103.</p>

```
Pāsādavaragato videhaseṭṭho, vitihāraṃ aññamaññabhojanānaṃ;
```

```
Addakkhi <note>addasa (syā. ka.)</note> kira sakkhikaṃ janindo, bubhukkassa <pb ed="T" n="1.0338" /> puṇṇaṃ mukhassa <note>bhobhukkhassa ca puṇṇamukhassa (sī.)</note> cetaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§104.</p>

```
Lābhā vata me anapparūpā, yassa medisā paṇḍitā kulamhi;
```

```
Pañhassa gambhīragataṃ nipuṇamatthaṃ, paṭivijjhanti subhāsitena dhīrā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§105.</p>

```
Assatarirathañca ekamekaṃ, phītaṃ gāmavarañca ekamekaṃ;
```

```
Sabbesaṃ vo dammi paṇḍitānaṃ, paramappatītamano subhāsitenāti.
```

Meṇḍakapañhajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 472. Mahāpadumajātakaṃ (9)

<p rend="hangnum">§106.</p>

```
Nādaṭṭhā <note>nādiṭṭhā (ka. sī. syā. ka.)</note> parato dosaṃ, aṇuṃ thūlāni sabbaso;
```

```
Issaro paṇaye daṇḍaṃ, sāmaṃ appaṭivekkhiya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§107.</p>

```
Yo ca appaṭivekkhitvā, daṇḍaṃ kubbati khattiyo;
```

```
Sakaṇṭakaṃ so gilati, jaccandhova samakkhikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§108.</p>

```
Adaṇḍiyaṃ daṇḍayati <note>daṇḍiyati (syā. pī.)</note>, daṇḍiyañca adaṇḍiyaṃ <note>adaṇḍiya (niyya), na daṇḍaye (?)</note>;
```

```
Andhova visamaṃ maggaṃ, na jānāti samāsamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§109.</p>

```
Yo ca etāni ṭhānāni, aṇuṃ thūlāni sabbaso;
```

```
Sudiṭṭhamanusāseyya, sa ve voharitu <note>vohātu (pī.)</note> marahati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§110.</p>

```
Nekantamudunā <pb ed="T" n="1.0339" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0254" /> sakkā, ekantatikhiṇena vā;
```

```
Attaṃ mahante <note>mahatte (syā. ka.)</note> ṭhapetuṃ <note>ṭhāpetuṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, tasmā ubhayamācare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§111.</p>

```
Paribhūto mudu hoti, atitikkho ca veravā;
```

```
Etañca ubhayaṃ ñatvā, anumajjhaṃ samācare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§112.</p>

```
Bahumpi ratto bhāseyya, duṭṭhopi bahu bhāsati;
```

```
Na itthikāraṇā rāja, puttaṃ ghātetumarahasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§113.</p>

```
Sabbova <pb ed="V" n="1.0197" /> <note>sabbo ca (ka. sī. pī.)</note> loko ekato <note>ekanto (sī. pī.)</note>, itthī ca ayamekikā;
```

```
Tenāhaṃ paṭipajjissaṃ, gacchatha pakkhipatheva <note>pakkhipetha (syā. aṭṭha.)</note> taṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§114.</p>

```
Anekatāle narake, gambhīre ca suduttare <note>gambhīre suduruttare (pī. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Pātito giriduggasmiṃ, kena tvaṃ tattha nāmari.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§115.</p>

```
Nāgo jātaphaṇo tattha, thāmavā girisānujo;
```

```
Paccaggahi maṃ bhogehi, tenāhaṃ tattha nāmariṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§116.</p>

```
Ehi taṃ paṭinessāmi, rājaputta sakaṃ gharaṃ;
```

```
Rajjaṃ kārehi <note>kāresi (sī.)</note> bhaddante, kiṃ araññe karissasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§117.</p>

```
Yathā gilitvā baḷisaṃ, uddhareyya salohitaṃ;
```

```
Uddharitvā sukhī assa, evaṃ <note>sukhaṃ (pī. ka.)</note> passāmi attanaṃ <note>attani (pī. ka.), attanā (syā.), evaṃ ahampi puna sotthibhāvappattaṃ gilitabaḷisaṃ purisamiva attānaṃ passāmīti (aṭṭha. saṃvaṇṇanā)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§118.</p>

```
Kiṃ nu tvaṃ baḷisaṃ brūsi, kiṃ tvaṃ brūsi salohitaṃ;
```

```
Kiṃ nu tvaṃ ubbhataṃ brūsi, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§119.</p>

```
Kāmāhaṃ baḷisaṃ brūmi, hatthiassaṃ salohitaṃ;
```

```
Cattāhaṃ ubbhataṃ brūmi, evaṃ jānāhi khattiya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§120.</p>

```
Ciñcāmāṇavikā <pb ed="T" n="1.0340" /> mātā, devadatto ca me pitā;
```

```
Ānando paṇḍito nāgo, sāriputto ca devatā;
```

```
Rājaputto ahaṃ āsiṃ <note>ahaṃ tadā rājaputto (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, evaṃ dhāretha jātakanti.
```

Mahāpadumajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 473. Mittāmittajātakaṃ (10)

<p rend="hangnum">§121.</p>

```
Kāni <pb ed="M" n="1.0255" /> kammāni kubbānaṃ, kathaṃ viññū parakkame;
```

```
Amittaṃ jāneyya medhāvī, disvā sutvā ca paṇḍito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§122.</p>

```
Na naṃ umhayate disvā, na ca naṃ paṭinandati;
```

```
Cakkhūni cassa <note>cakkhūnissa (syā. ka.)</note> na dadāti, paṭilomañca vattati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§123.</p>

```
Amitte tassa bhajati, mitte tassa na sevati;
```

```
Vaṇṇakāme nivāreti, akkosante pasaṃsati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§124.</p>

```
Guyhañca tassa nakkhāti, tassa guyhaṃ na gūhati;
```

```
Kammaṃ tassa na vaṇṇeti, paññassa nappasaṃsati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§125.</p>

```
Abhave <pb ed="V" n="1.0198" /> nandati tassa, bhave tassa na nandati;
```

```
Accheraṃ <note>acchariyaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> bhojanaṃ laddhā, tassa nuppajjate sati;
```

```
Tato naṃ nānukampati, aho sopi <note>ahāsopi (ka. sī. syā. ka.)</note> labheyyito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§126.</p>

```
Iccete soḷasākārā, amittasmiṃ patiṭṭhitā;
```

```
Yehi amittaṃ jāneyya, disvā sutvā ca paṇḍito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§127.</p>

```
Kāni kammāni kubbānaṃ, kathaṃ viññū parakkame;
```

```
Mittaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0341" /> jāneyya medhāvī, disvā sutvā ca paṇḍito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§128.</p>

```
Pavutthaṃ tassa sarati, āgataṃ abhinandati;
```

```
Tato kelāyito hoti, vācāya paṭinandati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§129.</p>

```
Mitte tasseva bhajati, amitte tassa na sevati;
```

```
Akkosante nivāreti, vaṇṇakāme pasaṃsati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§130.</p>

```
Guyhañca tassa akkhāti, tassa guyhañca gūhati;
```

```
Kammañca tassa vaṇṇeti, paññaṃ tassa <note>paññamassa (syā. ka.)</note> pasaṃsati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§131.</p>

```
Bhave ca nandati tassa <note>bhave nandati tassa ca (ka.)</note>, abhave tassa na nandati;
```

```
Accheraṃ <note>acchariyaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> bhojanaṃ laddhā, tassa uppajjate sati;
```

```
Tato naṃ anukampati, aho sopi <note>pahāsopi (ka. sī. syā. ka.)</note> labheyyito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§132.</p>

```
Iccete <pb ed="M" n="1.0256" /> soḷasākārā, mittasmiṃ suppatiṭṭhitā;
```

```
Yehi mittañca jāneyya <note>mittaṃ sujāneyya (pī. ka.)</note>, disvā sutvā ca paṇḍitoti.
```

Mittāmittajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

<trailer rend="centre">Dvādasakanipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.</trailer>

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Lahucitta sasāla kasanti puna, atha kāma dasakhaluṭṭhānavaro;
```

```
Atha kaṇha sukosiya meṇḍavaro, padumo puna mittavarena dasāti.
```

### 13. Terasakanipāto

#### 474. Ambajātakaṃ (1)

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
Ahāsi <pb ed="T" n="1.0342" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0199" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0257" /> <note>āhāsi (?)</note> me ambaphalāni pubbe, aṇūni thūlāni ca brahmacāri;
```

```
Teheva mantehi na dāni tuyhaṃ, dumapphalā pātubhavanti brahme.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
Nakkhattayogaṃ paṭimānayāmi, khaṇaṃ muhuttañca mante na passaṃ <note>khaṇaṃ muhuttaṃ na maṃ tosayanti (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Nakkhattayogañca khaṇañca laddhā, addhāharissambaphalaṃ <note>athāharissambaphalaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> pahūtaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
Nakkhattayogaṃ na pure abhāṇi, khaṇaṃ muhuttaṃ na pure asaṃsi;
```

```
Sayaṃ harī <note>athāharī (sī. syā. pī.)</note> ambaphalaṃ pahūtaṃ, vaṇṇena gandhena rasenupetaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
Mantābhijappena pure hi <note>pura’ssa (sī. pī.), purepi (syā.)</note> tuyhaṃ, dumapphalā pātubhavanti brahme;
```

```
Svājja na pāresi jappampi mantaṃ <note>japampi mante (sī. pī.)</note>, ayaṃ so ko nāma tavajja dhammo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
Caṇḍālaputto <pb ed="T" n="1.0343" /> mama sampadāsi, dhammena mante pakatiñca saṃsi;
```

```
Mā cassu me pucchito nāmagottaṃ, guyhittho atthaṃ <note>mā taṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> vijaheyya manto <note>vijaheyyumantā (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
Sohaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0258" /> janindena janamhi puṭṭho, makkhābhibhūto alikaṃ abhāṇiṃ;
```

```
‘‘Mantā ime brāhmaṇassā’’ti micchā, pahīnamanto kapaṇo rudāmi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
Eraṇḍā pucimandā vā, atha vā pālibhaddakā;
```

```
Madhuṃ madhutthiko vinde, so hi tassa dumuttamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
Khattiyā brāhmaṇā vessā, suddā caṇḍālapukkusā;
```

```
Yamhā dhammaṃ vijāneyya, so hi tassa naruttamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
Imassa daṇḍañca vadhañca datvā, gale gahetvā khalayātha <note>balayātha (syā.), galayātha (ka.)</note> jammaṃ;
```

```
Yo uttamatthaṃ kasirena laddhaṃ, mānātimānena vināsayittha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
Yathā samaṃ maññamāno pateyya, sobbhaṃ guhaṃ narakaṃ pūtipādaṃ;
```

```
Rajjūti vā akkame kaṇhasappaṃ, andho <pb ed="T" n="1.0344" /> yathā jotimadhiṭṭhaheyya;
```

```
Evampi maṃ tvaṃ khalitaṃ sapañña <note>sapaññā (pī.)</note>, pahīnamantassa punappadāhi <note>puna sampadāhi (syā.), punappasīda (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
Dhammena mantaṃ <note>mante (sī. syā. pī.)</note> tava sampadāsiṃ, tuvampi dhammena <note>tvampi dhammeneva (ka.)</note> pariggahesi;
```

```
Pakatimpi te attamano asaṃsiṃ, dhamme ṭhitaṃ taṃ <note>patiṭṭhaṃ (ka.)</note> na jaheyya manto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
Yo <pb ed="V" n="1.0200" /> bāla mantaṃ <note>balamantaṃ (ka.)</note> kasirena laddhaṃ, yaṃ dullabhaṃ ajja manussaloke;
```

```
Kiñcāpi laddhā jīvituṃ appapañño <note>kicchā laddhaṃ jīvikaṃ appapañño (sī. syā.), kacchāpi laddhā jīvikaṃ appañña (pī.)</note>, vināsayī alikaṃ bhāsamāno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
Bālassa <pb ed="M" n="1.0259" /> mūḷhassa akataññuno ca, musā bhaṇantassa asaññatassa;
```

```
Mante mayaṃ tādisake na dema, kuto mantā gaccha na mayha ruccasīti.
```

Ambajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 475. Phandanajātakaṃ (2)

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
Kuṭhārihattho <pb ed="T" n="1.0345" /> <note>kudhārihattho (ka.)</note> puriso, vanamogayha tiṭṭhasi;
```

```
Puṭṭho me samma akkhāhi, kiṃ dāruṃ chetumicchasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
Isso <note>iso (sī.), īso (syā. pī.)</note> vanāni carasi, samāni visamāni ca;
```

```
Puṭṭho me samma akkhāhi, kiṃ dāruṃ nemiyā daḷhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
Neva sālo na khadiro, nāssakaṇṇo kuto dhavo;
```

```
Rukkho ca <note>rukkhova (sī. pī.)</note> phandano nāma, taṃ dāruṃ nemiyā daḷhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
Kīdisānissa pattāni, khandho vā pana kīdiso;
```

```
Puṭṭho me samma akkhāhi, yathā jānemu phandanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
Yassa sākhā palambanti, namanti na ca bhañjare;
```

```
So rukkho phandano nāma, yassa mūle ahaṃ ṭhito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
Arānaṃ cakkanābhīnaṃ, īsānemirathassa ca;
```

```
Sabbassa te kammaniyo, ayaṃ hessati phandano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
Iti phandanarukkhopi, tāvade ajjhabhāsatha;
```

```
Mayhampi vacanaṃ atthi, bhāradvāja suṇohi me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
Issassa <note>imassa (ka. sī. ka.)</note> upakkhandhamhā <note>upakhandhamhā (ka. sī. pī. ka.)</note>, ukkacca caturaṅgulaṃ;
```

```
Tena nemiṃ pasāresi <note>pariharesi (sī. pī.)</note>, evaṃ daḷhataraṃ siyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
Iti phandanarukkhopi, veraṃ appesi tāvade;
```

```
Jātānañca ajātānaṃ, issānaṃ dukkhamāvahi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
Iccevaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0260" /> <note>icceva (sī. pī.)</note> phandano issaṃ, isso ca pana phandanaṃ;
```

```
Aññamaññaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0346" /> vivādena, aññamaññamaghātayuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
Evameva manussānaṃ, vivādo yattha jāyati;
```

```
Mayūranaccaṃ naccanti, yathā te issaphandanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
Taṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0201" /> vo vadāmi bhaddaṃ vo <note>bhaddante (ka.)</note>, yāvantettha samāgatā;
```

```
Sammodatha mā vivadatha <note>māvivadittha (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, mā hotha issaphandanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
Sāmaggimeva <note>sāmagyameva (syā. ka.)</note> sikkhetha, buddhehetaṃ pasaṃsitaṃ;
```

```
Sāmaggirato dhammaṭṭho, yogakkhemā na dhaṃsatīti.
```

Phandanajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 476. Javanahaṃsajātakaṃ (3)

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
Idheva haṃsa nipata, piyaṃ me tava dassanaṃ;
```

```
Issarosi anuppatto, yamidhatthi pavedaya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
Savanena ekassa piyā bhavanti, disvā panekassa viyeti <note>vineti (syā.), viheti (pī.), vigeti (ka. aṭṭha.)</note> chando;
```

```
Disvā ca sutvā ca piyā bhavanti, kaccinnu me pīyasi <note>piyyasi (sī. pī.)</note> dassanena.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
Savanena piyo mesi, bhiyyo cāgamma dassanaṃ;
```

```
Evaṃ piyadassano me <note>evaṃ piyadassano samāno (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, vasa haṃsa mamantike <note>mama santike (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
Vaseyyāma tavāgāre, niccaṃ sakkatapūjitā;
```

```
Matto ca ekadā vajje <note>vajjā (sī. pī.)</note>, ‘‘haṃsarājaṃ pacantu me’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
Dhiratthu <pb ed="T" n="1.0347" /> taṃ majjapānaṃ, yaṃ me piyataraṃ tayā;
```

```
Na cāpi majjaṃ pissāmi <note>pivissāmi (syā.), pāyāmi (sī. pī.)</note>, yāva me vacchasī ghare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
Suvijānaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0261" /> siṅgālānaṃ, sakuṇānañca <note>sakuntānañca (sī. syā. pī.)</note> vassitaṃ;
```

```
Manussavassitaṃ rāja, dubbijānataraṃ tato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
Api ce maññatī poso, ñāti mitto sakhāti vā;
```

```
Yo pubbe sumano hutvā, pacchā sampajjate diso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
Yasmiṃ mano nivisati, avidūre sahāpi so;
```

```
Santikepi hi so dūre, yasmiṃ nāvisate <note>yasmā vivasate (sī. syā. pī.)</note> mano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
Antopi so hoti pasannacitto, pāraṃ samuddassa pasannacitto;
```

```
Antopi so hoti paduṭṭhacitto, pāraṃ samuddassa paduṭṭhacitto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
Saṃvasantā vivasanti, ye disā te rathesabha;
```

```
Ārā santo saṃvasanti, manasā raṭṭhavaḍḍhana.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
Aticiraṃ nivāsena, piyo bhavati appiyo;
```

```
Āmanta kho taṃ gacchāma <note>gacchāmi (syā.)</note>, purā te homa appiyā <note>homi appiyo (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
Evaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0202" /> ce yācamānānaṃ, añjaliṃ nāvabujjhasi;
```

```
Paricārakānaṃ sataṃ <note>santānaṃ (sī. syā.), sattānaṃ (pī.)</note>, vacanaṃ na karosi no;
```

```
Evaṃ taṃ abhiyācāma, puna kayirāsi pariyāyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
Evaṃ ce no viharataṃ, antarāyo na hessati;
```

```
Tuyhañcāpi <pb ed="T" n="1.0348" /> <note>vāpi (syā. pī. ka.)</note> mahārāja, mayhañca <note>vā (bahūsu)</note> raṭṭhavaḍḍhana;
```

```
Appeva nāma passemu <note>passema (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, ahoratānamaccayeti.
```

Javanahaṃsajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 477. Cūḷanāradajātakaṃ (4)

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
Na te kaṭṭhāni bhinnāni, na te udakamābhataṃ;
```

```
Aggīpi te na hāpito <note>hāsito (sī. syā.)</note>, kiṃ nu mandova jhāyasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="M" n="1.0262" /> ussahe vane vatthuṃ, kassapāmantayāmi taṃ;
```

```
Dukkho vāso araññasmiṃ, raṭṭhaṃ icchāmi gantave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
Yathā ahaṃ ito gantvā, yasmiṃ janapade vasaṃ;
```

```
Ācāraṃ brahme <note>brahmaṃ (ka.)</note> sikkheyyaṃ, taṃ dhammaṃ anusāsa maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
Sace araññaṃ hitvāna, vanamūlaphalāni ca;
```

```
Raṭṭhe rocayase vāsaṃ, taṃ dhammaṃ nisāmehi me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
Visaṃ mā paṭisevittho <note>paṭisevittha (syā. ka.)</note>, papātaṃ parivajjaya;
```

```
Paṅke ca mā visīdittho <note>paṅko ca mā visiyittho (ka.)</note>, yatto cāsīvise care.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
Kiṃ nu visaṃ papāto vā, paṅko vā brahmacārinaṃ;
```

```
Kaṃ tvaṃ āsīvisaṃ brūsi, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito;
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
Āsavo tāta lokasmiṃ, surā nāma pavuccati;
```

```
Manuñño <note>manuññā (sī. syā. pī.)</note> surabhī vaggu, sādu <note>madhu (sī. syā.)</note> khuddarasūpamo <note>rasūpamā (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Visaṃ tadāhu ariyā se, brahmacariyassa nārada.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
Itthiyo <pb ed="T" n="1.0349" /> tāta lokasmiṃ, pamattaṃ pamathenti tā;
```

```
Haranti yuvino cittaṃ, tūlaṃ bhaṭṭhaṃva māluto;
```

```
Papāto eso akkhāto, brahmacariyassa nārada.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
Lābho siloko sakkāro, pūjā parakulesu ca;
```

```
Paṅko eso ca <note>esova (sī. syā. pī.)</note> akkhāto, brahmacariyassa nārada.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
Sasatthā <pb ed="V" n="1.0203" /> <note>mahantā (syā. ka.)</note> tāta rājāno, āvasanti mahiṃ imaṃ;
```

```
Te tādise manussinde, mahante tāta nārada.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
Issarānaṃ adhipatīnaṃ, na tesaṃ pādato care;
```

```
Āsīvisoti <note>āsīviso so (sī. pī.)</note> akkhāto, brahmacariyassa nārada.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
Bhattattho bhattakāle ca <note>yaṃ (sī. pī.)</note>, yaṃ gehamupasaṅkame;
```

```
Yadettha kusalaṃ jaññā, tattha ghāsesanaṃ care.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
Pavisitvā <pb ed="M" n="1.0263" /> parakulaṃ, pānatthaṃ <note>pānattho (syā. pī.)</note> bhojanāya vā;
```

```
Mitaṃ khāde mitaṃ bhuñje, na ca rūpe manaṃ kare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
Goṭṭhaṃ majjaṃ kirāṭañca <note>kirāsañca (sī. syā.), kirāsaṃ vā (pī.)</note>, sabhā nikiraṇāni ca;
```

```
Ārakā parivajjehi, yānīva visamaṃ pathanti.
```

Cūḷanāradajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 478. Dūtajātakaṃ (5)

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
Dūte <pb ed="T" n="1.0350" /> te brahme <note>dūte brāhmaṇa (ka.)</note> pāhesiṃ, gaṅgātīrasmi jhāyato;
```

```
Tesaṃ puṭṭho na byākāsi, dukkhaṃ guyhamataṃ <note>guyhaṃ mataṃ (sī.), tuyhaṃ mataṃ (syā. ka.)</note> nu te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
Sace te dukkhamuppajje, kāsīnaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhana;
```

```
Mā kho naṃ tassa akkhāhi, yo taṃ dukkhā na mocaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
Yo tassa <note>yo ca tathā (pī.)</note> dukkhajātassa, ekaṅgamapi bhāgaso <note>ekantamapi bhāsato (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Vippamoceyya dhammena, kāmaṃ tassa pavedaya <note>pavedaye (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
Suvijānaṃ siṅgālānaṃ, sakuṇānañca vassitaṃ;
```

```
Manussavassitaṃ rāja, dubbijānataraṃ tato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
Api ce maññatī poso, ñāti mitto sakhāti vā;
```

```
Yo pubbe sumano hutvā, pacchā sampajjate diso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
Yo attano dukkhamanānupuṭṭho, pavedaye jantu akālarūpe;
```

```
Ānandino tassa bhavantimittā <note>bhavanta’mittā (sī. pī.)</note>, hitesino tassa dukhī bhavanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
Kālañca ñatvāna tathāvidhassa, medhāvīnaṃ ekamanaṃ viditvā;
```

```
Akkheyya tibbāni <note>tippāni (sī. syā. pī.)</note> parassa dhīro, saṇhaṃ giraṃ atthavatiṃ pamuñce.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
Sace <pb ed="T" n="1.0351" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0264" /> ca jaññā avisayhamattano, na te hi mayhaṃ <note>nāyaṃ nīti mayha (sī. pī.)</note> sukhāgamāya;
```

```
Ekova tibbāni saheyya dhīro, saccaṃ hirottappamapekkhamāno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
Ahaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0204" /> raṭṭhāni vicaranto, nigame rājadhāniyo;
```

```
Bhikkhamāno mahārāja, ācariyassa dhanatthiko.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
Gahapatī rājapurise, mahāsāle ca brāhmaṇe;
```

```
Alatthaṃ satta nikkhāni, suvaṇṇassa janādhipa;
```

```
Te me naṭṭhā mahārāja, tasmā socāmahaṃ bhusaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
Purisā te mahārāja, manasānuvicintitā;
```

```
Nālaṃ dukkhā pamocetuṃ, tasmā tesaṃ na byāhariṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
Tvañca kho me mahārāja, manasānuvicintito;
```

```
Alaṃ dukkhā pamocetuṃ, tasmā tuyhaṃ pavedayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
Tassādāsi pasannatto, kāsīnaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhano;
```

```
Jātarūpamaye nikkhe, suvaṇṇassa catuddasāti.
```

Dūtajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 479. Kāliṅgabodhijātakaṃ (6)

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
Rājā <pb ed="T" n="1.0352" /> kāliṅgo cakkavatti, dhammena pathavimanusāsaṃ <note>manusāsi (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Agamā <note>agamāsi (syā. ka.)</note> bodhisamīpaṃ, nāgena mahānubhāvena.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
Kāliṅgo bhāradvājo ca, rājānaṃ kāliṅgaṃ samaṇakolaññaṃ;
```

```
Cakkaṃ vattayato pariggahetvā <note>pariṇetvā (pī.)</note>, pañjalī idamavoca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
Paccoroha mahārāja, bhūmibhāgo yathā samaṇuggato <note>samanugīto (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Idha anadhivarā buddhā, abhisambuddhā virocanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
Padakkhiṇato <pb ed="M" n="1.0265" /> āvaṭṭā, tiṇalatā asmiṃ bhūmibhāgasmiṃ;
```

```
Pathaviyā nābhiyaṃ <note>puthuviyā ayaṃ (sī.), paṭhaviyā ayaṃ (syā.), puthaviyā’yaṃ (pī.)</note> maṇḍo, iti no sutaṃ mante mahārāja <note>sutaṃ mahārāja (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
Sāgarapariyantāya, mediniyā sabbabhūtadharaṇiyā;
```

```
Pathaviyā ayaṃ maṇḍo, orohitvā namo karohi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
Ye te bhavanti nāgā ca, abhijātā ca kuñjarā;
```

```
Ettāvatā padesaṃ te, nāgā neva mupayanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
Abhijāto nāgo <note>abhijāto te nāgo (sī. pī. aṭṭha.)</note> kāmaṃ, pesehi kuñjaraṃ dantiṃ;
```

```
Ettāvatā padeso <note>padeso ca (syā. ka.)</note>, sakkā <note>na sakkā (syā.)</note> nāgena mupagantuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
Taṃ sutvā rājā kāliṅgo, veyyañjanikavaco nisāmetvā;
```

```
Sampesesi nāgaṃ ñassāma, mayaṃ yathimassidaṃ <note>yathā idaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> vacanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
Sampesito <pb ed="V" n="1.0205" /> ca raññā, nāgo koñcova abhinaditvāna;
```

```
Paṭisakkitvā <pb ed="T" n="1.0353" /> <note>paṭiosakkitvā (ka.)</note> nisīdi, garuṃva bhāraṃ asahamāno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
Kāliṅgabhāradvājo, nāgaṃ khīṇāyukaṃ viditvāna;
```

```
Rājānaṃ kāliṅgaṃ, taramāno ajjhabhāsittha;
```

```
Aññaṃ saṅkama nāgaṃ, nāgo khīṇāyuko mahārāja.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
Taṃ sutvā kāliṅgo, taramāno saṅkamī nāgaṃ;
```

```
Saṅkanteva raññe, nāgo tattheva pati <note>patito (ka.)</note> bhumyā;
```

```
Veyyañjanikavaco, yathā tathā ahu nāgo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
Kāliṅgo rājā kāliṅgaṃ, brāhmaṇaṃ etadavoca;
```

```
Tvameva asi sambuddho, sabbaññū sabbadassāvī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
Taṃ anadhivāsento kāliṅgaṃ <note>kāliṅgo (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, brāhmaṇo idamavoca;
```

```
Veyyañjanikā hi mayaṃ, buddhā sabbaññuno mahārāja.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
Sabbaññū sabbavidū ca, buddhā na lakkhaṇena jānanti;
```

```
Āgamabalasā <note>āgamapurisā (pī.)</note> hi mayaṃ, buddhā sabbaṃ pajānanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
Mahayitvā <pb ed="M" n="1.0266" /> sambodhiṃ <note>mahāyitvāna sambodhiṃ (sī. pī.), pahaṃsitvāna sambodhiṃ (syā.), mamāyitvāna taṃ bodhiṃ (ka.)</note>, nānāturiyehi vajjamānehi;
```

```
Mālāvilepanaṃ abhiharitvā <note>mālāgandhavilepanaṃ āharitvā (sī. pī.); pākāraparikkhepaṃ kāresi; atha rājā pāyāsi (sī. syā. pī.)</note> atha rājā manupāyāsi <note>pākāraparikkhepaṃ kāresi; atha rājā pāyāsi (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
Saṭṭhi vāhasahassāni, pupphānaṃ sannipātayi;
```

```
Pūjesi <pb ed="T" n="1.0354" /> rājā kāliṅgo, bodhimaṇḍamanuttaranti <note>varuttameti (sī.)</note>.
```

Kāliṅgabodhijātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 480. Akittijātakaṃ (7)

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
Akittiṃ <note>akattiṃ (ka.)</note> disvā sammantaṃ, sakko bhūtapatī bravi;
```

```
Kiṃ patthayaṃ mahābrahme, eko sammasi ghammani.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
Dukkho punabbhavo sakka, sarīrassa ca bhedanaṃ;
```

```
Sammohamaraṇaṃ dukkhaṃ, tasmā sammāmi vāsava.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
Etasmiṃ te sulapite, patirūpe subhāsite;
```

```
Varaṃ kassapa te dammi, yaṃ kiñci manasicchasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
Varaṃ ce me ado sakka, sabbabhūtānamissara;
```

```
Yena putte ca dāre ca, dhanadhaññaṃ piyāni ca;
```

```
Laddhā narā na <note>laddhā naññāni (ka.)</note> tappanti, so lobho na mayī vase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
Etasmiṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0206" /> te sulapite, patirūpe subhāsite;
```

```
Varaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0355" /> kassapa te dammi, yaṃ kiñci manasicchasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
Varaṃ ce me ado sakka, sabbabhūtānamissara;
```

```
Khettaṃ vatthuṃ hiraññañca, gavassaṃ dāsaporisaṃ;
```

```
Yena jātena jīyanti, so doso na mayī vase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
Etasmiṃ te sulapite, patirūpe subhāsite;
```

```
Varaṃ kassapa te dammi, yaṃ kiñci manasicchasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
Varaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0267" /> ce me ado sakka, sabbabhūtānamissara;
```

```
Bālaṃ na passe na suṇe, na ca bālena saṃvase;
```

```
Bālenallāpa <note>bālenā’lāpa (?)</note> sallāpaṃ, na kare na ca rocaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
Kiṃ nu te akaraṃ bālo, vada kassapa kāraṇaṃ;
```

```
Kena kassapa bālassa, dassanaṃ nābhikaṅkhasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
Anayaṃ nayati dummedho, adhurāyaṃ niyuñjati;
```

```
Dunnayo seyyaso hoti, sammā vutto pakuppati;
```

```
Vinayaṃ so na jānāti, sādhu tassa adassanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§93.</p>

```
Etasmiṃ te sulapite, patirūpe subhāsite;
```

```
Varaṃ kassapa te dammi, yaṃ kiñci manasicchasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§94.</p>

```
Varaṃ ce me ado sakka, sabbabhūtānamissara;
```

```
Dhīraṃ passe suṇe dhīraṃ, dhīrena saha saṃvase;
```

```
Dhīrenallāpasallāpaṃ, taṃ kare tañca rocaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§95.</p>

```
Kiṃ nu te akaraṃ dhīro, vada kassapa kāraṇaṃ;
```

```
Kena kassapa dhīrassa, dassanaṃ abhikaṅkhasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§96.</p>

```
Nayaṃ nayati medhāvī, adhurāyaṃ na yuñjati;
```

```
Sunayo seyyaso hoti, sammā vutto na kuppati;
```

```
Vinayaṃ so pajānāti, sādhu tena samāgamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§97.</p>

```
Etasmiṃ te sulapite, patirūpe subhāsite;
```

```
Varaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0356" /> kassapa te dammi, yaṃ kiñci manasicchasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§98.</p>

```
Varaṃ ce me ado sakka, sabbabhūtānamissara;
```

```
Tato ratyā vivasāne <note>vivasane (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, sūriyuggamanaṃ <note>suriyassuggamanaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> pati;
```

```
Dibbā bhakkhā pātubhaveyyuṃ, sīlavanto ca yācakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§99.</p>

```
Dadato <pb ed="V" n="1.0207" /> me <note>dadato ca me (pī.)</note> na khīyetha, datvā nānutapeyyahaṃ;
```

```
Dadaṃ cittaṃ pasādeyyaṃ, etaṃ sakka varaṃ vare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§100.</p>

```
Etasmiṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0268" /> te sulapite, patirūpe subhāsite;
```

```
Varaṃ kassapa te dammi, yaṃ kiñci manasicchasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§101.</p>

```
Varaṃ ce me ado sakka, sabbabhūtānamissara;
```

```
Na maṃ puna upeyyāsi, etaṃ sakka varaṃ vare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§102.</p>

```
Bahūhi vatacariyāhi <note>vattacariyāhi (sī. syā. ka.)</note>, narā ca atha nāriyo;
```

```
Dassanaṃ abhikaṅkhanti, kiṃ nu me dassane bhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§103.</p>

```
Taṃ tādisaṃ devavaṇṇaṃ <note>devavaṇṇiṃ (pī.)</note>, sabbakāmasamiddhinaṃ;
```

```
Disvā tapo pamajjeyya <note>disvā tapo pamajjeyyaṃ (sī. syā. pī.), disvānahaṃ pamajjeyyaṃ (cariyāpiṭakaṭṭhakathā)</note>, etaṃ te dassane bhayanti.
```

Akittijātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 481. Takkāriyajātakaṃ (8)

<p rend="hangnum">§104.</p>

```
Ahameva dubbhāsitaṃ bhāsi bālo, bhekovaraññe ahimavhāyamāno <note>mavhayāno (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Takkāriye sobbhamimaṃ <note>sobbhamhi ahaṃ (ka.)</note> patāmi, na <pb ed="T" n="1.0357" /> kireva sādhu ativelabhāṇī <note>sādhūtyativelabhāṇī (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§105.</p>

```
Pappoti macco ativelabhāṇī, bandhaṃ vadhaṃ sokapariddavañca;
```

```
Attānameva garahāsi ettha, ācera yaṃ taṃ nikhaṇanti sobbhe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§106.</p>

```
Kimevahaṃ tuṇḍilamanupucchiṃ, kareyya saṃ <note>kareyyāsaṃ (syā.), kareyya sa (ka.), bhareyya saṃ (?)</note> bhātaraṃ kāḷikāyaṃ <note>kāḷikāya (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Naggovahaṃ <note>naggoca’haṃ (?)</note> vatthayugañca jīno, ayampi attho bahutādisova.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§107.</p>

```
Yo <pb ed="M" n="1.0269" /> yujjhamānānamayujjhamāno <note>yujjhamānena ayujjhamāno (ka.)</note>, meṇḍantaraṃ accupatī kuliṅgo;
```

```
So piṃsito meṇḍasirehi tattha, ayampi attho bahutādisova.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§108.</p>

```
Caturo janā potthakamaggahesuṃ, ekañca posaṃ anurakkhamānā;
```

```
Sabbeva te bhinnasirā sayiṃsu, ayampi attho bahutādisova.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§109.</p>

```
Ajā yathā veḷugumbasmiṃ baddhā <note>bandhaṃ (syā. ka.)</note>, avakkhipantī asimajjhagacchi;
```

```
Teneva <pb ed="T" n="1.0358" /> tassā galakāvakantaṃ <note>galayā vikantuṃ (ka.), galakaṃ vikantā (syā.)</note>, ayampi attho bahutādisova.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§110.</p>

```
Ime na devā na gandhabbaputtā, migā ime atthavasaṃ gatā me <note>atthavasābhatā ime (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Ekañca naṃ sāyamāse pacantu, ekaṃ punappātarāse <note>ekañca naṃ pātarāse (ka. sī. pī.)</note> pacantu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§111.</p>

```
Sataṃ sahassāni dubhāsitāni, kalampi nāgghanti subhāsitassa;
```

```
Dubbhāsitaṃ saṅkamāno kileso <note>kilissati (?)</note>, tasmā tuṇhī kimpurisā <note>kiṃpuriso (sī. syā.)</note> na bālyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§112.</p>

```
Yā <pb ed="V" n="1.0208" /> mesā byāhāsi <note>byākāsi (sī. syā. pī.)</note> pamuñcathetaṃ, giriñca naṃ <note>giriṃ varaṃ (ka.)</note> himavantaṃ nayantu;
```

```
Imañca kho dentu mahānasāya, pātova naṃ pātarāse pacantu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§113.</p>

```
Pajjunnanāthā <pb ed="M" n="1.0270" /> pasavo, pasunāthā ayaṃ pajā;
```

```
Tvaṃ nāthosi <note>tvaṃ-nātho’smi (sī. syā. pī.)</note> mahārāja, nāthohaṃ bhariyāya me <note>amha-nāthā mama bhariyā (ka. sī. syā.)</note>;
```

```
Dvinnamaññataraṃ ñatvā, mutto gaccheyya pabbataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§114.</p>

```
Na ve nindā suparivajjayetha <note>suparivajjayātha (syā.)</note>, nānā <pb ed="T" n="1.0359" /> janā sevitabbā janinda;
```

```
Yeneva eko labhate pasaṃsaṃ, teneva añño labhate ninditāraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§115.</p>

```
Sabbo loko paricitto aticitto <note>paracittena aticitto (sī. syā.), paracittena acitto (sī. aṭṭha.)</note>, sabbo loko cittavā samhi citte;
```

```
Paccekacittā puthu sabbasattā, kassīdha cittassa vase na vatte.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§116.</p>

```
Tuṇhī ahū kimpuriso sabhariyo <note>abhāṇī (ka.)</note>, yo dāni byāhāsi bhayassa bhīto;
```

```
So dāni mutto sukhito arogo, vācākirevattavatī narānanti.
```

Takkāriyajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 482. Rurumigarājajātakaṃ (9)

<p rend="hangnum">§117.</p>

```
Tassa <note>kassa (sī. pī.)</note> gāmavaraṃ dammi, nāriyo ca alaṅkatā;
```

```
Yo <note>ko (sī. syā. pī.)</note> metaṃ migamakkhāti <note>makkhāsi (syā. ka.)</note>, migānaṃ migamuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§118.</p>

```
Mayhaṃ gāmavaraṃ dehi, nāriyo ca alaṅkatā;
```

```
Ahaṃ te migamakkhissaṃ, migānaṃ migamuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§119.</p>

```
Etasmiṃ vanasaṇḍasmiṃ, ambā sālā ca pupphitā;
```

```
Indagopakasañchannā<pb ed="T" n="1.0360" />, ettheso tiṭṭhate migo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§120.</p>

```
Dhanuṃ advejjhaṃ <note>adejjhaṃ (sī. pī.), sarajjaṃ (ka.)</note> katvāna, usuṃ sannayhupāgami <note>sandhāyupāgami (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Migo ca disvā rājānaṃ, dūrato ajjhabhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§121.</p>

```
Āgamehi <pb ed="M" n="1.0271" /> mahārāja, mā maṃ vijjhi rathesabha;
```

```
Ko nu te idamakkhāsi, ettheso tiṭṭhate migo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§122.</p>

```
Esa pāpacaro poso, samma tiṭṭhati ārakā;
```

```
Soyaṃ <note>so hi (sī. syā. pī.)</note> me idamakkhāsi, ettheso tiṭṭhate migo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§123.</p>

```
Saccaṃ kireva māhaṃsu, narā ekacciyā idha;
```

```
Kaṭṭhaṃ niplavitaṃ seyyo, na tvevekacci yo naro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§124.</p>

```
Kiṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0209" /> nu ruru garahasi migānaṃ, kiṃ pakkhīnaṃ kiṃ pana mānusānaṃ;
```

```
Bhayañhi maṃ vindatinapparūpaṃ, sutvāna taṃ mānusiṃ bhāsamānaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§125.</p>

```
Yamuddhariṃ vāhane vuyhamānaṃ, mahodake salile sīghasote;
```

```
Tatonidānaṃ bhayamāgataṃ mama, dukkho have rāja asabbhi saṅgamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§126.</p>

```
Sohaṃ catuppattamimaṃ vihaṅgamaṃ, tanucchidaṃ hadaye ossajāmi;
```

```
Hanāmi <pb ed="T" n="1.0361" /> taṃ mittadubbhiṃ akiccakāriṃ <note>hanāmi mittaddu’makiccakāriṃ (sī. pī.)</note>, yo tādisaṃ kammakataṃ na jāne.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§127.</p>

```
Dhīrassa bālassa have janinda, santo vadhaṃ nappasaṃsanti jātu;
```

```
Kāmaṃ gharaṃ gacchatu pāpadhammo, yañcassa bhaṭṭhaṃ tadetassa dehi;
```

```
Ahañca te kāmakaro bhavāmi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§128.</p>

```
Addhā ruru aññataro sataṃ so <note>sataṃ’se (sī.)</note>, yo dubbhato <note>dubbhino (syā.), dūbhato (pī.)</note> mānusassa na dubbhi;
```

```
Kāmaṃ gharaṃ gacchatu pāpadhammo, yañcassa bhaṭṭhaṃ tadetassa dammi;
```

```
Ahañca te kāmacāraṃ dadāmi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§129.</p>

```
Suvijānaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0272" /> siṅgālānaṃ, sakuṇānañcavassitaṃ;
```

```
Manussavassitaṃ rāja, dubbijānataraṃ tato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§130.</p>

```
Api ce maññatī poso, ñāti mitto sakhāti vā;
```

```
Yo pubbe sumano hutvā, pacchā sampajjate diso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§131.</p>

```
Samāgatā jānapadā, negamā ca samāgatā;
```

```
Migā sassāni khādanti, taṃ devo paṭisedhatu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§132.</p>

```
Kāmaṃ janapado māsi, raṭṭhañcāpi vinassatu;
```

```
Na tvevāhaṃ ruruṃ dubbhe, datvā abhayadakkhiṇaṃ.
