```

<p rend="hangnum">§133.</p>

```
Mā <pb ed="T" n="1.0362" /> me janapado āsi <note>mā maṃ janapado ahu (syā.)</note>, raṭṭhañcāpi vinassatu;
```

```
Na tvevāhaṃ <note>na tveva (ka. sī. ka.)</note> migarājassa, varaṃ datvā musā bhaṇeti.
```

Rurumigarājajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 483. Sarabhamigajātakaṃ (10)

<p rend="hangnum">§134.</p>

```
Āsīsetheva <note>āsiṃsetheva (sī. syā. pī.)</note> puriso, na nibbindeyya paṇḍito;
```

```
Passāmi vohaṃ attānaṃ, yathā icchiṃ tathā ahu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§135.</p>

```
Āsīsetheva puriso, na nibbindeyya paṇḍito;
```

```
Passāmi vohaṃ attānaṃ, udakā thalamubbhataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§136.</p>

```
Vāyametheva <pb ed="V" n="1.0210" /> puriso, na nibbindeyya paṇḍito;
```

```
Passāmi vohaṃ attānaṃ, yathā icchiṃ tathā ahu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§137.</p>

```
Vāyametheva puriso, na nibbindeyya paṇḍito;
```

```
Passāmi vohaṃ attānaṃ, udakā thalamubbhataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§138.</p>

```
Dukkhūpanītopi naro sapañño, āsaṃ na chindeyya sukhāgamāya;
```

```
Bahū hi phassā ahitā hitā ca, avitakkitā maccamupabbajanti <note>maccumupabbajanti (ka. sī. pī.), maccumupapajjanti (syā. ka.) ettha ‘‘avitakkitāpi phasso maccaṃ janaṃ upagacchantī’’ti attho</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§139.</p>

```
Acintitampi <pb ed="M" n="1.0273" /> bhavati, cintitampi vinassati;
```

```
Na hi cintāmayā bhogā, itthiyā purisassa vā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§140.</p>

```
Sarabhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0363" /> giriduggasmiṃ, yaṃ tvaṃ anusarī pure;
```

```
Alīnacittassa tuvaṃ, vikkantamanujīvasi <note>tava, vikkantaṃ jīvitaṃ labhi (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§141.</p>

```
Yo taṃ viduggā narakā samuddhari, silāya yoggaṃ sarabho karitvā;
```

```
Dukkhūpanītaṃ maccumukhā pamocayi, alīnacittaṃ taṃ migaṃ <note>tameva (syā. ka.)</note> vadesi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§142.</p>

```
Kiṃ tvaṃ nu <note>tuvannu (sī. pī.)</note> tattheva tadā ahosi, udāhu te koci naṃ <note>taṃ (ka.)</note> etadakkhā;
```

```
Vivaṭṭacchaddo nusi sabbadassī, ñāṇaṃ nu te brāhmaṇa bhiṃsarūpaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§143.</p>

```
Na cevahaṃ tattha tadā ahosiṃ, na cāpi me koci naṃ <note>taṃ (ka.)</note> etadakkhā;
```

```
Gāthāpadānañca subhāsitānaṃ, atthaṃ tadānenti janinda dhīrā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§144.</p>

```
Ādāya pattiṃ <note>pattaṃ (syā.), paṭṭiṃ (ka.)</note> paraviriyaghātiṃ, cāpe saraṃ kiṃ vicikicchase tuvaṃ;
```

```
Nunno <note>nuṇṇo (ka. sī. syā.), tuṇṇo (ka.)</note> saro sarabhaṃ hantu khippaṃ, annañhi etaṃ varapañña rañño.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§145.</p>

```
Addhā pajānāmi ahampi etaṃ, annaṃ migo brāhmaṇa khattiyassa;
```

```
Pubbe <pb ed="T" n="1.0364" /> katañca <note>pubbe ca kataṃ (ka.)</note> apacāyamāno, tasmā migaṃ sarabhaṃ no hanāmi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§146.</p>

```
Neso migo mahārāja, asureso disampati;
```

```
Etaṃ hantvā manussinda, bhavassu amarādhipo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§147.</p>

```
Sace <pb ed="M" n="1.0274" /> ca rājā <note>rāja (sī. syā. pī.)</note> vicikicchase tuvaṃ, hantuṃ migaṃ sarabhaṃ sahāyakaṃ <note>sahāyakaṃ me (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Saputtadāro naravīraseṭṭha <note>naraviriyaseṭṭha (sī. pī.)</note>, gantvā <note>gantā (sī. pī. aṭṭha.)</note> tuvaṃ vetaraṇiṃ yamassa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§148.</p>

```
Kāmaṃ ahaṃ jānapadā ca sabbe, puttā ca dārā ca sahāyasaṅghā;
```

```
Gacchemu taṃ vetaraṇiṃ yamassa, na tveva hañño mama pāṇado yo <note>pāṇada’ssa (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§149.</p>

```
Ayaṃ migo kicchagatassa mayhaṃ, ekassa kattā vivanasmi ghore;
```

```
Taṃ tādisaṃ pubbakiccaṃ saranto, jānaṃ mahābrahme kathaṃ haneyyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§150.</p>

```
Mittābhirādhī <pb ed="V" n="1.0211" /> cirameva jīva, rajjaṃ imaṃ dhammaguṇe <note>rajjampimaṃ cassa gaṇe (ka.)</note> pasāsa;
```

```
Nārīgaṇehi paricāriyanto, modassu raṭṭhe tidiveva vāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§151.</p>

```
Akkodhano <pb ed="T" n="1.0365" /> niccapasannacitto, sabbātithī yācayogo bhavitvā <note>pāhunake karitvā (syā.), yācayogo viditvā (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Datvā ca bhutvā ca yathānubhāvaṃ, anindito saggamupehi ṭhānanti.
```

Sarabhamigajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

<trailer rend="centre">Terasakanipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.</trailer>

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Varaamba <pb ed="M" n="1.0275" /> kuṭhāri sahaṃsavaro, atharaññasmiṃ dūtakapañcamako;
```

```
Atha bodhi akitti sutakkarinā, atha rurumigenaparo sarabhoti.
```

### 14. Pakiṇṇakanipāto

#### 484. Sālikedārajātakaṃ (1)

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
Sampannaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0366" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0212" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0276" /> sālikedāraṃ, suvā bhuñjanti kosiya;
```

```
Paṭivedemi te brahme, na ne <note>te (sī. syā.), naṃ (sī. syā. pī. aṭṭha.), taṃ (ka. aṭṭha.)</note> vāretumussahe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
Eko ca tattha sakuṇo, yo nesaṃ <note>tesaṃ (sī. aṭṭha.)</note> sabbasundaro;
```

```
Bhutvā sāliṃ yathākāmaṃ, tuṇḍenādāya gacchati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
Oḍḍentu <note>ujjhuntu (syā. ka.) aṅguttaranikāye passitabbaṃ</note> vāḷapāsāni, yathā vajjhetha so dijo;
```

```
Jīvañca naṃ gahetvāna, ānayehi <note>ānayetha (sī. pī.)</note> mamantike.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
Ete bhutvā pivitvā ca <note>bhutvā ca pitvā ca (pī.)</note>, pakkamanti vihaṅgamā;
```

```
Eko baddhosmi pāsena, kiṃ pāpaṃ pakataṃ mayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
Udaraṃ nūna aññesaṃ, suva accodaraṃ tava;
```

```
Bhutvā sāliṃ yathākāmaṃ, tuṇḍenādāya gacchasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
Koṭṭhaṃ nu tattha pūresi, suva veraṃ nu te mayā;
```

```
Puṭṭho me samma akkhāhi, kuhiṃ sāliṃ nidāhasi <note>nidhīyasi (pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
Na me veraṃ tayā saddhiṃ, koṭṭho mayhaṃ na vijjati;
```

```
Iṇaṃ muñcāmiṇaṃ dammi, sampatto koṭasimbaliṃ;
```

```
Nidhimpi tattha nidahāmi, evaṃ jānāhi kosiya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
Kīdisaṃ te iṇadānaṃ, iṇamokkho ca kīdiso;
```

```
Nidhinidhānamakkhāhi<pb ed="T" n="1.0367" />, atha pāsā pamokkhasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
Ajātapakkhā taruṇā, puttakā mayha kosiya;
```

```
Te maṃ bhatā bharissanti, tasmā tesaṃ iṇaṃ dade.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
Mātā pitā ca me vuddhā, jiṇṇakā gatayobbanā;
```

```
Tesaṃ tuṇḍena hātūna, muñce pubbakataṃ <note>pubbe kataṃ (sī.)</note> iṇaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
Aññepi <pb ed="M" n="1.0277" /> tattha sakuṇā, khīṇapakkhā sudubbalā;
```

```
Tesaṃ puññatthiko dammi, taṃ nidhiṃ āhu paṇḍitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
Īdisaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0213" /> <note>edisaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> me iṇadānaṃ, iṇamokkho ca īdiso;
```

```
Nidhinidhānamakkhāmi <note>nidhiṃ nidhānaṃ akkhātaṃ (sī. pī.)</note>, evaṃ jānāhi kosiya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
Bhaddako vatayaṃ pakkhī, dijo paramadhammiko;
```

```
Ekaccesu manussesu, ayaṃ dhammo na vijjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
Bhuñja sāliṃ yathākāmaṃ, saha sabbehi ñātibhi;
```

```
Punāpi suva passemu, piyaṃ me tava dassanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
Bhuttañca pītañca tavassamamhi <note>tavassabyamhi (ka.)</note>, rattiñca <note>ratī ca (sī. pī.)</note> no kosiya te sakāse;
```

```
Nikkhittadaṇḍesu dadāhi dānaṃ, jiṇṇe ca mātāpitaro bharassu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
Lakkhī vata me udapādi ajja, yo addasāsiṃ pavaraṃ <note>yohaṃ adassaṃ paramaṃ (syā. ka.)</note> dijānaṃ;
```

```
Suvassa sutvāna subhāsitāni, kāhāmi <pb ed="T" n="1.0368" /> puññāni anappakāni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
So kosiyo attamano udaggo, annañca pānañcabhisaṅkharitvā <note>annañca pānaṃ abhisaṃharitvā (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Annena pānena pasannacitto, santappayi samaṇabrāhmaṇe cāti.
```

Sālikedārajātakaṃ <note>kedārajātakaṃ (ka.)</note> paṭhamaṃ.

#### 485. Candakinnarījātakaṃ (2)

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
Upanīyatidaṃ maññe, cande <note>lohitamadena majjāmi; vijahāmi jīvitaṃ pāṇā, (sī. pī. aṭṭha.)</note> lohitamaddane;
```

```
Ajja jahāmi jīvitaṃ, pāṇā <note>lohitamadena majjāmi; vijahāmi jīvitaṃ pāṇā, (sī. pī. aṭṭha.)</note> me cande nirujjhanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
Osīdi <pb ed="M" n="1.0278" /> <note>osadhi (sī. syā. pī.), osaṭṭhi (ka.), osati (abhinavaṭīkā), osīdati (?)</note> me dukkhaṃ <note>dukkhaṃ me (sī. pī.)</note> hadayaṃ, me ḍayhate nitammāmi;
```

```
Tava candiyā socantiyā, na naṃ aññehi sokehi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
Tiṇamiva vanamiva milāyāmi <note>milayāmi (sī.), miyyāmi (sī. pī. aṭṭha.)</note>, nadī aparipuṇṇāva <note>aparipuṇṇiyāva (sī. pī.)</note> sussāmi;
```

```
Tava candiyā socantiyā, na naṃ aññehi sokehi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
Vassamiva sare pāde <note>vassaṃva sare pāde (sī.), vassaṃva sare pabbatapāde (pī.)</note>, imāni assūni vattare mayhaṃ;
```

```
Tava candiyā socantiyā, na naṃ aññehi sokehi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
Pāpo khosi <note>pāposi kho (sī.), pāpo kho (syā. pī.)</note> rājaputta, yo me icchitaṃ <note>icchita (sī. syā. pī.)</note> patiṃ varākiyā;
```

```
Vijjhasi vanamūlasmiṃ, soyaṃ viddho chamā seti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
Imaṃ mayhaṃ hadayasokaṃ, paṭimuñcatu rājaputta tava mātā;
```

```
Yo mayhaṃ hadayasoko, kimpurisaṃ avekkhamānāya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
Imaṃ mayhaṃ hadayasokaṃ, paṭimuñcatu rājaputta tava jāyā;
```

```
Yo <pb ed="T" n="1.0369" /> mayhaṃ hadayasoko, kimpurisaṃ avekkhamānāya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
Mā <pb ed="V" n="1.0214" /> ca puttaṃ <note>putte (sī. pī.)</note> mā ca patiṃ, addakkhi rājaputta tava mātā;
```

```
Yo kimpurisaṃ avadhi, adūsakaṃ mayha kāmā hi <note>mayhaṃ kāmā (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
Mā ca puttaṃ mā ca patiṃ, addakkhi rājaputta tava jāyā;
```

```
Yo kimpurisaṃ avadhi, adūsakaṃ mayha kāmā hi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
Mā tvaṃ cande rodi, mā soci vanatimiramattakkhi;
```

```
Mama tvaṃ hehisi bhariyā, rājakule pūjitā nārībhi <note>nārī (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
Api nūnahaṃ marissaṃ, nāhaṃ <note>na ca panāhaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> rājaputta tava hessaṃ;
```

```
Yo kimpurisaṃ avadhi, adūsakaṃ mayha kāmā hi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
Api bhīruke api jīvitukāmike, kimpurisi gaccha himavantaṃ;
```

```
Tālīsatagarabhojanā, aññe <note>tālissatagarabhojane, araññe (sī. pī.)</note> taṃ migā ramissanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
Te <pb ed="M" n="1.0279" /> pabbatā tā ca kandarā, <note>tā ca giriguhāyo (sī. syā. pī.)</note> tā ca giriguhāyo tatheva tiṭṭhanti <note>tā ca giriguhāyo (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Tattheva <note>tattha (sī. syā. pī.)</note> taṃ apassantī, kimpurisa kathaṃ ahaṃ kassaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
Te paṇṇasanthatā ramaṇīyā, vāḷamigehi anuciṇṇā;
```

```
Tattheva taṃ apassantī, kimpurisa kathaṃ ahaṃ kassaṃ <note>kāsaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
Te <pb ed="T" n="1.0370" /> pupphasanthatā ramaṇīyā, vāḷamigehi anuciṇṇā;
```

```
Tattheva taṃ apassantī, kimpurisa kathaṃ ahaṃ kassaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
Acchā savanti girivana <note>girivara (sī. pī.)</note> nadiyo, kusumābhikiṇṇasotāyo;
```

```
Tattheva taṃ apassantī, kimpurisa kathaṃ ahaṃ kassaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
Nīlāni himavato pabbatassa, kūṭāni dassanīyāni <note>dassaneyyāni (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Tattheva taṃ apassantī, kimpurisa kathaṃ ahaṃ kassaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
Pītāni himavato pabbatassa, kūṭāni dassanīyāni;
```

```
Tattheva taṃ apassantī, kimpurisa kathaṃ ahaṃ kassaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
Tambāni himavato pabbatassa, kūṭāni dassanīyāni;
```

```
Tattheva taṃ apassantī, kimpurisa kathaṃ ahaṃ kassaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
Tuṅgāni himavato pabbatassa, kūṭāni dassanīyāni;
```

```
Tattheva taṃ apassantī, kimpurisa kathaṃ ahaṃ kassaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
Setāni himavato pabbatassa, kūṭāni dassanīyāni;
```

```
Tattheva taṃ apassantī, kimpurisa kathaṃ ahaṃ kassaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
Citrāni himavato pabbatassa, kūṭāni dassanīyāni;
```

```
Tattheva taṃ apassantī, kimpurisa kathaṃ ahaṃ kassaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
Yakkhagaṇasevite <pb ed="V" n="1.0215" /> gandhamādane, osadhebhi sañchanne;
```

```
Tattheva taṃ apassantī, kimpurisa kathaṃ ahaṃ kassaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
Kimpurisasevite gandhamādane, osadhebhi sañchanne;
```

```
Tattheva <pb ed="T" n="1.0371" /> taṃ apassantī, kimpurisa kathaṃ ahaṃ kassaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
Vande <pb ed="M" n="1.0280" /> te ayirabrahme <note>ayyire brahme (ka.)</note>, yo me icchitaṃ patiṃ varākiyā;
```

```
Amatena abhisiñci, samāgatāsmi piyatamena.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
Vicarāma dāni girivana <note>girivara (sī. pī.)</note> nadiyo, kusumābhikiṇṇasotāyo;
```

```
Nānādumavasanāyo <note>sevanāyo (pī.)</note>, piyaṃvadā aññamaññassāti.
```

Candakinnarījātakaṃ <note>candakinnarajātakaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> dutiyaṃ.

#### 486. Mahāukkusajātakaṃ (3)

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
Ukkā cilācā <note>milācā (sī. syā. pī.)</note> bandhanti dīpe <note>bandhanti luddā, dīpe (ka.)</note>, pajā mamaṃ khādituṃ patthayanti;
```

```
Mittaṃ sahāyañca vadehi senaka, ācikkha ñātibyasanaṃ dijānaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
Dijo dijānaṃ pavarosi pakkhima <note>pakkhi (sī. pī.), pakkhi ca (syā.)</note>, ukkusarāja saraṇaṃ taṃ upema <note>upemi (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Pajā mamaṃ khādituṃ patthayanti, luddā cilācā <note>milācā (sī. syā. pī.)</note> bhava me sukhāya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
Mittaṃ sahāyañca karonti paṇḍitā, kāle akāle sukhamesamānā <note>māsayānā (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Karomi te senaka etamatthaṃ, ariyo <pb ed="T" n="1.0372" /> hi ariyassa karoti kiccaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
Yaṃ hoti kiccaṃ anukampakena, ariyassa ariyena kataṃ tayīdaṃ <note>tava yidaṃ (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Attānurakkhī bhava mā adayhi <note>aḍayha (sī. pī.)</note>, lacchāma putte tayi jīvamāne.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
Taveva <pb ed="M" n="1.0281" /> <note>tameva (syā. ka.)</note> rakkhāvaraṇaṃ karonto, sarīrabhedāpi na santasāmi;
```

```
Karonti heke <note>hete (ka. sī. syā. pī.)</note> sakhīnaṃ sakhāro, pāṇaṃ cajantā <note>cajanti (sī. pī.)</note> satamesa <note>satānesa (pī.)</note> dhammo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
Sudukkaraṃ kammamakāsi <note>makā (sī. pī.)</note>, aṇḍajāyaṃ vihaṅgamo;
```

```
Atthāya kuraro putte, aḍḍharatte anāgate.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
Cutāpi heke <note>eke (sī. pī.)</note> khalitā sakammunā, mittānukampāya patiṭṭhahanti;
```

```
Puttā mamaṭṭā gatimāgatosmi, atthaṃ caretho <note>caretha (sī. syā. pī.)</note> mama vāricara <note>vārichanna (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
Dhanena dhaññena ca attanā ca, mittaṃ sahāyañca karonti paṇḍitā;
```

```
Karomi te senaka etamatthaṃ, ariyo hi ariyassa karoti kiccaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
Appossukko tāta tuvaṃ nisīda, putto <pb ed="T" n="1.0373" /> pitu carati atthacariyaṃ;
```

```
Ahaṃ carissāmi tavetamatthaṃ, senassa putte paritāyamāno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
Addhā <pb ed="V" n="1.0216" /> hi tāta satamesa dhammo, putto pitu yaṃ care <note>pitunaṃ care (ka.), pitu yañcaretha (sī. pī.)</note> atthacariyaṃ;
```

```
Appeva maṃ disvāna pavaḍḍhakāyaṃ, senassa puttā na viheṭhayeyyuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
Pasū manussā migavīraseṭṭha <note>migaviriyaseṭṭha (sī. pī.)</note>, bhayaṭṭitā <note>bhayadditā (sī. pī.)</note> seṭṭhamupabbajanti;
```

```
Puttā mamaṭṭā gatimāgatosmi, tvaṃ nosi rājā bhava me sukhāya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
Karomi <pb ed="M" n="1.0282" /> te senaka etamatthaṃ, āyāmi te taṃ disataṃ vadhāya;
```

```
Kathañhi viññū pahu sampajāno, na vāyame attajanassa guttiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
Mittañca kayirātha suhadayañca <note>suhaddayañca (sī.), sakhāgharañca (pī.)</note>, ayirañca kayirātha sukhāgamāya;
```

```
Nivatthakocova <note>kojova (sī. pī.)</note> sarebhihantvā, modāma puttehi samaṅgibhūtā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
Sakamittassa kammena, sahāyassāpalāyino;
```

```
Kūjantamupakūjanti<pb ed="T" n="1.0374" />, lomasā hadayaṅgamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
Mittaṃ sahāyaṃ adhigamma paṇḍito, so bhuñjatī putta pasuṃ dhanaṃ vā;
```

```
Ahañca puttā ca patī ca mayhaṃ, mittānukampāya samaṅgibhūtā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
Rājavatā sūravatā ca attho, sampannasakhissa bhavanti hete;
```

```
So mittavā yasavā uggatatto, asmiṃdhaloke <note>asmiñca loke (sī. syā. pī.)</note> modati kāmakāmī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
Karaṇīyāni mittāni, daliddenāpi senaka;
```

```
Passa mittānukampāya, samaggamhā sañātake <note>sañātakā (?)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
Sūrena balavantena, yo mitte <note>mette (sī.), mittaṃ (syā.)</note> kurute dijo;
```

```
Evaṃ so sukhito hoti, yathāhaṃ tvañca senakāti.
```

Mahāukkusajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 487. Uddālakajātakaṃ (4)

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
Kharājinā <pb ed="M" n="1.0283" /> jaṭilā paṅkadantā, dummakkharūpā <note>dummudharūpā (sī. pī. ka.)</note> ye mantaṃ jappanti <note>yeme japanti (sī. pī.), ye’me jappanti mante (jā. 1.6.10)</note>;
```

```
Kaccinnu te mānusake payoge, idaṃ vidū parimuttā apāyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
Pāpāni <pb ed="T" n="1.0375" /> kammāni karetha <note>kareyya (syā.), katvāna (jā. 1.6.11)</note> rāja, bahussuto ce na careyya dhammaṃ;
```

```
Sahassavedopi na taṃ paṭicca, dukkhā pamucce <note>pamuñce (syā.)</note> caraṇaṃ apatvā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
Sahassavedopi na taṃ paṭicca, dukkhā pamucce caraṇaṃ apatvā;
```

```
Maññāmi vedā aphalā bhavanti, sasaṃyamaṃ caraṇaññeva saccaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
Na heva vedā aphalā bhavanti, sasaṃyamaṃ caraṇaññeva saccaṃ;
```

```
Kittiñhi <note>kittiñca (syā.)</note> pappoti adhicca vede, santiṃ puṇāti <note>punoti (sī. aṭṭha.), puṇeti (syā. jā. 1.6.13), puneti (pī.)</note> caraṇena danto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
Bhaccā <pb ed="V" n="1.0217" /> mātā pitā bandhū, yena jāto sayeva so;
```

```
Uddālako ahaṃ bhoto <note>bhoti (ka.)</note>, sottiyākulavaṃsako <note>vaṃsato (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
Kathaṃ bho brāhmaṇo hoti, kathaṃ bhavati kevalī;
```

```
Kathañca parinibbānaṃ, dhammaṭṭho kinti vuccati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
Niraṃkatvā <pb ed="M" n="1.0284" /> aggimādāya brāhmaṇo, āpo siñcaṃ yajaṃ usseti yūpaṃ;
```

```
Evaṃkaro brāhmaṇo hoti khemī, dhamme ṭhitaṃ tena amāpayiṃsu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="T" n="1.0376" /> suddhi secanenatthi, nāpi kevalī brāhmaṇo;
```

```
Na khantī nāpi soraccaṃ, nāpi so parinibbuto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
Kathaṃ so <note>bho (syā. ka.)</note> brāhmaṇo hoti, kathaṃ bhavati kevalī;
```

```
Kathañca parinibbānaṃ, dhammaṭṭho kinti vuccati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
Akhettabandhū amamo nirāso, nillobhapāpo bhavalobhakhīṇo;
```

```
Evaṃkaro brāhmaṇo hoti khemī, dhamme ṭhitaṃ tena amāpayiṃsu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
Khattiyā brāhmaṇā vessā, suddā caṇḍālapukkusā;
```

```
Sabbeva soratā dantā, sabbeva parinibbutā;
```

```
Sabbesaṃ sītibhūtānaṃ, atthi seyyotha <note>seyyova (sī. pī.)</note> pāpiyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
Khattiyā brāhmaṇā vessā, suddā caṇḍālapukkusā;
```

```
Sabbeva soratā dantā, sabbeva parinibbutā;
```

```
Sabbesaṃ sītibhūtānaṃ, natthi seyyotha pāpiyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
Khattiyā brāhmaṇā vessā, suddā caṇḍālapukkusā;
```

```
Sabbeva soratā dantā, sabbeva parinibbutā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
Sabbesaṃ sītibhūtānaṃ, natthi seyyotha pāpiyo;
```

```
Panatthaṃ <note>pasatthaṃ (syā.), pasaṭṭhaṃ (ka.)</note> carasi brahmaññaṃ, sottiyākulavaṃsataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
Nānārattehi vatthehi, vimānaṃ bhavati chāditaṃ;
```

```
Na tesaṃ chāyā vatthānaṃ, so rāgo anupajjatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
Evameva <pb ed="T" n="1.0377" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0285" /> <note>evamevaṃ (pī.)</note> manussesu, yadā sujjhanti māṇavā;
```

```
Te sajātiṃ pamuñcanti <note>na tesaṃ jātiṃ pucchanti (sī. syā. pī.), na tesaṃ jāti sujjhati (ka.)</note>, dhammamaññāya subbatāti.
```

Uddālakajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 488. Bhisajātakaṃ (5)

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
Assaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0218" /> gavaṃ rajataṃ jātarūpaṃ, bhariyañca so idha labhataṃ manāpaṃ;
```

```
Puttehi dārehi samaṅgi hotu, bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yo ahāsi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
Mālañca so kāsikacandanañca, dhāretu puttassa bahū bhavantu;
```

```
Kāmesu tibbaṃ kurutaṃ apekkhaṃ, bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yo ahāsi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
Pahūtadhañño kasimā yasassī, putte gihī dhanimā sabbakāme;
```

```
Vayaṃ apassaṃ gharamāvasātu, bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yo ahāsi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
So khattiyo hotu pasayhakārī, rājābhirājā <note>rājādhirājā (syā. ka.)</note> balavā yasassī;
```

```
Sa <pb ed="T" n="1.0378" /> cāturantaṃ mahimāvasātu, bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yo ahāsi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
So brāhmaṇo hotu avītarāgo, muhuttanakkhattapathesu yutto;
```

```
Pūjetu naṃ raṭṭhapatī yasassī, bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yo ahāsi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
Ajjhāyakaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0286" /> sabbasamantavedaṃ <note>sabbasamattavedaṃ (sī.), sabbasamattavedanaṃ (pī.)</note>, tapassīnaṃ maññatu sabbaloko;
```

```
Pūjentu naṃ jānapadā samecca, bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yo ahāsi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
Catussadaṃ gāmavaraṃ samiddhaṃ, dinnañhi so bhuñjatu vāsavena;
```

```
Avītarāgo maraṇaṃ upetu, bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yo ahāsi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
So gāmaṇī hotu sahāyamajjhe, naccehi gītehi pamodamāno;
```

```
So rājato byasana mālattha <note>mā rājato vyasana’malattha (sī. syā. pī.)</note> kiñci, bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yo ahāsi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
Yaṃ ekarājā pathaviṃ vijetvā, itthīsahassāna <note>itthīsahassassa (sī. pī.)</note> ṭhapetu aggaṃ;
```

```
Sīmantinīnaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0379" /> pavarā bhavātu, bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yā ahāsi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
Isīnañhi sā sabbasamāgatānaṃ, bhuñjeyya sāduṃ avikampamānā;
```

```
Carātu lābhena vikatthamānā, bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yā ahāsi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
Āvāsiko hotu mahāvihāre, navakammiko hotu gajaṅgalāyaṃ <note>kajaṅgalāyaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Ālokasandhiṃ divasaṃ <note>divasā (sī. syā. pī.)</note> karotu, bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yo ahāsi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
So <pb ed="M" n="1.0287" /> bajjhatū pāsasatehi chabbhi <note>chamhi (sī. pī.), chassu (?)</note>, rammā vanā niyyatu rājadhāniṃ <note>rājaṭhāniṃ (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Tuttehi so haññatu pācanehi, bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yo ahāsi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
Alakkamālī tipukaṇṇaviddho, laṭṭhīhato sappamukhaṃ upetu;
```

```
Sakacchabandho <note>sakkaccabaddho (sī. pī.), saṃkaccabandho (niyya)</note> visikhaṃ carātu, bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yo ahāsi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
Yo ve anaṭṭhaṃva <note>anaṭṭhaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> naṭṭhanti cāha, kāmeva <pb ed="T" n="1.0380" /> so labhataṃ bhuñjatañca <note>labhatu bhuñjatu ca (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Agāramajjhe maraṇaṃ upetu, yo vā bhonto saṅkati kañcideva <note>kiñcideva (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
Yadesamānā <pb ed="V" n="1.0219" /> vicaranti loke, iṭṭhañca kantañca bahūnametaṃ;
```

```
Piyaṃ manuññaṃ cidha jīvaloke, kasmā isayo nappasaṃsanti kāme.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§93.</p>

```
Kāmesu ve haññare bajjhare ca, kāmesu dukkhañca bhayañca jātaṃ;
```

```
Kāmesu bhūtādhipatī pamattā, pāpāni kammāni karonti mohā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§94.</p>

```
Te pāpadhammā pasavetva pāpaṃ, kāyassa bhedā nirayaṃ vajanti;
```

```
Ādīnavaṃ kāmaguṇesu disvā, tasmā isayo nappasaṃsanti kāme.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§95.</p>

```
Vīmaṃsamāno isino bhisāni, tīre gahetvāna thale nidhesiṃ;
```

```
Suddhā apāpā isayo vasanti, etāni te brahmacārī bhisāni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§96.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="M" n="1.0288" /> te naṭā no pana kīḷaneyyā, na <pb ed="T" n="1.0381" /> bandhavā no pana te sahāyā;
```

```
Kismiṃ vupatthambha sahassanetta, isīhi tvaṃ kīḷasi devarāja.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§97.</p>

```
Ācariyo mesi pitā ca mayhaṃ, esā patiṭṭhā khalitassa brahme;
```

```
Ekāparādhaṃ khama bhūripañña, na paṇḍitā kodhabalā bhavanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§98.</p>

```
Suvāsitaṃ isinaṃ ekarattaṃ, yaṃ vāsavaṃ bhūtapatiddasāma;
```

```
Sabbeva bhonto sumanā bhavantu, yaṃ brāhmaṇo paccupādī bhisāni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§99.</p>

```
Ahañca sāriputto ca, moggallāno ca kassapo;
```

```
Anuruddho puṇṇo ānando, tadāsuṃ satta bhātaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§100.</p>

```
Bhaginī uppalavaṇṇā ca, dāsī khujjuttarā tadā;
```

```
Citto gahapati dāso, yakkho sātāgiro tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§101.</p>

```
Pālileyyo <note>pārileyyo (sī. pī.)</note> tadā nāgo, madhudo <note>madhuvā (sī. pī.)</note> seṭṭhavānaro;
```

```
Kāḷudāyī tadā sakko, evaṃ dhāretha jātakanti.
```

Bhisajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 489. Surucijātakaṃ (6)

<p rend="hangnum">§102.</p>

```
Mahesī <pb ed="T" n="1.0382" /> surucino <note>rucino (sī. syā. pī.)</note> bhariyā, ānītā paṭhamaṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Dasa vassasahassāni, yaṃ maṃ surucimānayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§103.</p>

```
Sāhaṃ brāhmaṇa rājānaṃ, vedehaṃ mithilaggahaṃ;
```

```
Nābhijānāmi kāyena, vācāya uda cetasā;
```

```
Suruciṃ atimaññittha <note>atimaññittho (sī. pī.), atimaññitā (?)</note>, āvi <note>āviṃ (sī. pī.)</note> vā yadi vā raho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§104.</p>

```
Etena <pb ed="M" n="1.0289" /> saccavajjena, putto uppajjataṃ ise;
```

```
Musā me bhaṇamānāya, muddhā phalatu sattadhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§105.</p>

```
Bhattu <pb ed="V" n="1.0220" /> mama sassu mātā, pitā cāpi ca sassuro;
```

```
Te maṃ brahme vinetāro, yāva aṭṭhaṃsu jīvitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§106.</p>

```
Sāhaṃ ahiṃsāratinī, kāmasā <note>kāmaso (sī.)</note> dhammacārinī <note>dhammacāriṇī (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Sakkaccaṃ te upaṭṭhāsiṃ, rattindivamatanditā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§107.</p>

```
Etena saccavajjena, putto uppajjataṃ ise;
```

```
Musā me bhaṇamānāya, muddhā phalatu sattadhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§108.</p>

```
Soḷasitthisahassāni, sahabhariyāni brāhmaṇa;
```

```
Tāsu issā vā kodho vā, nāhu mayhaṃ kudācanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§109.</p>

```
Hitena tāsaṃ nandāmi, na ca me kāci appiyā;
```

```
Attānaṃvānukampāmi, sadā sabbā sapattiyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§110.</p>

```
Etena saccavajjena, putto uppajjataṃ ise;
```

```
Musā me bhaṇamānāya, muddhā phalatu sattadhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§111.</p>

```
Dāse <pb ed="T" n="1.0383" /> kammakare pesse <note>pose (syā. ka.)</note>, ye caññe anujīvino;
```

```
Pesemi <note>posemi (sī. syā. pī.)</note> sahadhammena, sadā pamuditindriyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§112.</p>

```
Etena saccavajjena, putto uppajjataṃ ise;
```

```
Musā me bhaṇamānāya, muddhā phalatu sattadhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§113.</p>

```
Samaṇe brāhmaṇe cāpi, aññe cāpi vanibbake;
```

```
Tappemi annapānena, sadā payatapāṇinī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§114.</p>

```
Etena saccavajjena, putto uppajjataṃ ise;
```

```
Musā me bhaṇamānāya, muddhā phalatu sattadhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§115.</p>

```
Cātuddasiṃ pañcaddasiṃ <note>pannarasiṃ (sī. pī.)</note>, yā ca pakkhassa aṭṭhamī <note>aṭṭhamiṃ (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Pāṭihāriyapakkhañca, aṭṭhaṅgasusamāgataṃ <note>aṭṭhaṅgasusamāhitaṃ (sabbattha) vi. va. 129 pāḷiyā aṭṭhakathā passitabbā</note>;
```

```
Uposathaṃ upavasāmi <note>upavasiṃ (ka.)</note>, sadā sīlesu saṃvutā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§116.</p>

```
Etena <pb ed="M" n="1.0290" /> saccavajjena, putto uppajjataṃ ise;
```

```
Musā me bhaṇamānāya, muddhā phalatu sattadhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§117.</p>

```
Sabbeva te dhammaguṇā, rājaputti yasassini;
```

```
Saṃvijjanti tayi bhadde, ye tvaṃ kittesi attani.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§118.</p>

```
Khattiyo jātisampanno, abhijāto yasassimā;
```

```
Dhammarājā videhānaṃ, putto uppajjate tava <note>tavaṃ (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§119.</p>

```
Dummī <pb ed="V" n="1.0221" /> <note>rummī (sī. pī.)</note> rajojalladharo, aghe vehāyasaṃ ṭhito;
```

```
Manuññaṃ bhāsase vācaṃ, yaṃ mayhaṃ hadayaṅgamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§120.</p>

```
Devatānusi <pb ed="T" n="1.0384" /> saggamhā, isi vāsi <note>cāpi (ka.)</note> mahiddhiko;
```

```
Ko vāsi tvaṃ anuppatto, attānaṃ me pavedaya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§121.</p>

```
Yaṃ devasaṅghā vandanti, sudhammāyaṃ samāgatā;
```

```
Sohaṃ sakko sahassakkho, āgatosmi tavantike.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§122.</p>

```
Itthiyo <note>itthiyā (pī.)</note> jīvalokasmiṃ, yā hoti <note>honti (sī. syā.)</note> samacārinī <note>samacāriṇī (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Medhāvinī sīlavatī, sassudevā patibbatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§123.</p>

```
Tādisāya sumedhāya, sucikammāya nāriyā;
```

```
Devā dassanamāyanti, mānusiyā amānusā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§124.</p>

```
Tvañca bhadde suciṇṇena, pubbe sucaritena ca;
```

```
Idha rājakule jātā, sabbakāmasamiddhinī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§125.</p>

```
Ayañca te rājaputti, ubhayattha kaṭaggaho;
```

```
Devalokūpapattī ca, kittī ca idha jīvite.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§126.</p>

```
Ciraṃ sumedhe sukhinī, dhammamattani pālaya;
```

```
Esāhaṃ tidivaṃ yāmi, piyaṃ me tava dassananti.
```

Surucijātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 490. Pañcuposathikajātakaṃ (7)

<p rend="hangnum">§127.</p>

```
Appossukko <pb ed="M" n="1.0291" /> dāni tuvaṃ kapota, vihaṅgama na tava bhojanattho;
```

```
Khudaṃ <note>khuddaṃ (syā. ka.), khudhaṃ (sakkata-pākatānurūpaṃ)</note> pipāsaṃ adhivāsayanto, kasmā bhavaṃposathiko kapota <note>kapoto (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§128.</p>

```
Ahaṃ pure giddhigato kapotiyā, asmiṃ padesasmimubho ramāma;
```

```
Athaggahī sākuṇiko kapotiṃ, akāmako tāya vinā ahosiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§129.</p>

```
Nānābhavā vippayogena tassā, manomayaṃ vedana vedayāmi <note>vedanaṃ vediyāmi (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Tasmā ahaṃposathaṃ pālayāmi, rāgo mamaṃ mā punarāgamāsi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§130.</p>

```
Anujjugāmī uragā dujivha <note>uraga dvijivha (sī.)</note>, dāṭhāvudho ghoravisosi sappa;
```

```
Khudaṃ pipāsaṃ adhivāsayanto, kasmā <pb ed="T" n="1.0385" /> bhavaṃposathiko nu dīgha <note>dīgho (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§131.</p>

```
Usabho ahū balavā gāmikassa, calakkakū vaṇṇabalūpapanno;
```

```
So maṃ akkami taṃ kupito aḍaṃsi, dukkhābhituṇṇo maraṇaṃ upāgā <note>upāgami (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§132.</p>

```
Tato <pb ed="V" n="1.0222" /> janā nikkhamitvāna gāmā, kanditvā roditvā <note>kanditva roditva (sī.)</note> apakkamiṃsu;
```

```
Tasmā ahaṃposathaṃ pālayāmi, kodho <pb ed="T" n="1.0386" /> mamaṃ mā punarāgamāsi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§133.</p>

```
Matāna <pb ed="M" n="1.0292" /> maṃsāni bahū susāne, manuññarūpaṃ tava bhojane taṃ;
```

```
Khudaṃ pipāsaṃ adhivāsayanto, kasmā bhavaṃposathiko siṅgāla <note>sigālo (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§134.</p>

```
Pavisi <note>pavissaṃ (sī. pī.), pavissa (syā.)</note> kucchiṃ mahato gajassa, kuṇape rato hatthimaṃsesu giddho <note>hatthimaṃse pagiddho (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Uṇho ca vāto tikhiṇā ca rasmiyo, te sosayuṃ tassa karīsamaggaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§135.</p>

```
Kiso ca paṇḍū ca ahaṃ bhadante, na me ahū nikkhamanāya maggo;
```

```
Mahā ca megho sahasā pavassi, so temayī tassa karīsamaggaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§136.</p>

```
Tato ahaṃ nikkhamisaṃ bhadante, cando yathā rāhumukhā pamutto;
```

```
Tasmā ahaṃposathaṃ pālayāmi, lobho mamaṃ mā punarāgamāsi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§137.</p>

```
Vammīkathūpasmiṃ kipillikāni, nippothayanto tuvaṃ pure carāsi;
```

```
Khudaṃ pipāsaṃ adhivāsayanto, kasmā <pb ed="T" n="1.0387" /> bhavaṃposathiko nu accha <note>accho (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§138.</p>

```
Sakaṃ niketaṃ atihīḷayāno <note>atiheḷayāno (syā. ka.)</note>, atricchatā <note>atricchatāya (sī. syā. pī.)</note> mallagāmaṃ <note>malataṃ (sī. pī.), mallayataṃ (ka.)</note> agacchiṃ;
```

```
Tato janā nikkhamitvāna gāmā, kodaṇḍakena paripothayiṃsu maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§139.</p>

```
So <pb ed="M" n="1.0293" /> bhinnasīso ruhiramakkhitaṅgo, paccāgamāsiṃ sakaṃ <note>sa sakaṃ (syā. ka.),’tha sakaṃ (?)</note> niketaṃ;
```

```
Tasmā ahaṃposathaṃ pālayāmi, atricchatā mā punarāgamāsi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§140.</p>

```
Yaṃ no apucchittha tuvaṃ bhadante, sabbeva byākarimha yathā pajānaṃ;
```

```
Mayampi pucchāma tuvaṃ bhadante, kasmā bhavaṃposathiko nu brahme.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§141.</p>

```
Anūpalitto mama assamamhi, paccekabuddho muhuttaṃ nisīdi;
```

```
So maṃ avedī gatimāgatiñca, nāmañca gottaṃ caraṇañca sabbaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§142.</p>

```
Evampahaṃ vandi na <note>evampahaṃ naggahe (sī. pī.)</note> tassa pāde, na cāpi naṃ mānagatena pucchiṃ;
```

```
Tasmā ahaṃposathaṃ pālayāmi, māno <pb ed="T" n="1.0388" /> mamaṃ mā punarāgamāsīti.
```

Pañcuposathikajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 491. Mahāmorajātakaṃ (8)

<p rend="hangnum">§143.</p>

```
Sace hi tyāhaṃ dhanahetu gāhito, mā maṃ vadhī jīvagāhaṃ gahetvā;
```

```
Rañño ca <note>raññova (sī. pī.)</note> maṃ samma upantikaṃ <note>upanti (sī. syā. pī.)</note> nehi, maññe dhanaṃ lacchasinapparūpaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§144.</p>

```
Na me ayaṃ tuyha vadhāya ajja, samāhito cāpadhure <note>cāpavare (sī. pī.), cāpavaro (syā.)</note> khurappo;
```

```
Pāsañca tyāhaṃ adhipātayissaṃ, yathāsukhaṃ gacchatu morarājā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§145.</p>

```
Yaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0223" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0294" /> satta vassāni mamānubandhi, rattindivaṃ khuppipāsaṃ sahanto;
```

```
Atha kissa maṃ pāsavasūpanītaṃ, pamuttave <pb ed="T" n="1.0389" /> icchasi bandhanasmā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§146 .</p>

```
Pāṇātipātā virato nusajja, abhayaṃ nu te sabbabhūtesu dinnaṃ;
```

```
Yaṃ maṃ tuvaṃ pāsavasūpanītaṃ, pamuttave icchasi bandhanasmā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§147.</p>

```
Pāṇātipātā viratassa brūhi, abhayañca yo sabbabhūtesu deti;
```

```
Pucchāmi taṃ morarājetamatthaṃ, ito cuto kiṃ labhate sukhaṃ so.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§148.</p>

```
Pāṇātipātā viratassa brūmi, abhayañca yo sabbabhūtesu deti;
```

```
Diṭṭheva dhamme labhate pasaṃsaṃ, saggañca so yāti sarīrabhedā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§149.</p>

```
Na santi devā iti āhu <note>iccāhu (sī. pī.)</note> eke, idheva jīvo vibhavaṃ upeti;
```

```
Tathā phalaṃ sukatadukkaṭānaṃ, dattupaññattañca vadanti dānaṃ;
```

```
Tesaṃ vaco arahataṃ saddahāno, tasmā ahaṃ sakuṇe bādhayāmi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§150.</p>

```
Cando ca suriyo ca ubho sudassanā, gacchanti obhāsayamantalikkhe;
```

```
Imassa lokassa parassa vā te, kathaṃ nu te āhu manussaloke.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§151.</p>

```
Cando <pb ed="M" n="1.0295" /> ca suriyo ca ubho sudassanā, gacchanti <pb ed="T" n="1.0390" /> obhāsayamantalikkhe;
```

```
Parassa lokassa na te imassa, devāti te āhu manussaloke.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§152.</p>

```
Ettheva te nīhatā hīnavādā, ahetukā ye na vadanti kammaṃ;
```

```
Tathā phalaṃ sukatadukkaṭānaṃ, dattupaññattaṃ ye ca vadanti dānaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§153.</p>

```
Addhā hi saccaṃ vacanaṃ tavedaṃ <note>tavetaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, kathañhi dānaṃ aphalaṃ bhaveyya <note>vadeyya (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Tathā phalaṃ sukatadukkaṭānaṃ, dattupaññattañca kathaṃ bhaveyya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§154.</p>

```
Kathaṃkaro kintikaro kimācaraṃ, kiṃ sevamāno kena tapoguṇena;
```

```
Akkhāhi <note>akkhāhi taṃ dāni (ka.)</note> me morarājetamatthaṃ, yathā ahaṃ no nirayaṃ pateyyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§155.</p>

```
Ye keci atthi samaṇā pathabyā, kāsāyavatthā anagāriyā te;
```

```
Pātova piṇḍāya caranti kāle, vikālacariyā viratā hi santo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§156.</p>

```
Te tattha kālenupasaṅkamitvā, pucchāhi <pb ed="T" n="1.0391" /> yaṃ te manaso piyaṃ siyā;
```

```
Te te pavakkhanti yathāpajānaṃ, imassa lokassa parassa catthaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§157.</p>

```
Tacaṃva jiṇṇaṃ urago purāṇaṃ, paṇḍūpalāsaṃ harito dumova;
```

```
Esappahīno mama luddabhāvo, jahāmahaṃ luddakabhāvamajja.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§158.</p>

```
Ye <pb ed="M" n="1.0296" /> cāpi me sakuṇā atthi baddhā, satāninekāni nivesanasmiṃ;
```

```
Tesampahaṃ <note>tesaṃ ahaṃ (syā. ka.)</note> jīvitamajja dammi, mokkhañca te pattā <note>patto (sī.), accha (syā.)</note> sakaṃ niketaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§159.</p>

```
Luddo <pb ed="V" n="1.0224" /> carī pāsahattho araññe, bādhetu morādhipatiṃ yasassiṃ;
```

```
Bandhitvā <note>bandhitva (sī. pī.)</note> morādhipatiṃ yasassiṃ, dukkhā sa pamucci <note>dukkhā pamucci (sī.), dukkhā pamuñci (syā. pī.)</note> yathāhaṃ pamuttoti.
```

Mahāmorajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 492. Tacchasūkarajātakaṃ (9)

<p rend="hangnum">§160.</p>

```
Yadesamānā vicarimha, pabbatāni vanāni ca;
```

```
Anvesaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0392" /> vicariṃ <note>vipule (syā. ka.)</note> ñātī, teme adhigatā mayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§161.</p>

```
Bahuñcidaṃ mūlaphalaṃ, bhakkho cāyaṃ anappako;
```

```
Rammā cimā girīnajjo <note>girinadiyo (sī. pī.)</note>, phāsuvāso bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§162.</p>

```
Idhevāhaṃ vasissāmi, saha sabbehi ñātibhi;
```

```
Appossukko nirāsaṅkī, asoko akutobhayo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§163.</p>

```
Aññampi <note>aññaṃ hi (sī. pī.)</note> leṇaṃ pariyesa, sattu no idha vijjati;
```

```
So taccha sūkare hanti, idhāgantvā varaṃ varaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§164.</p>

```
Ko numhākaṃ <note>ko namhākaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> idha sattu, ko ñātī susamāgate;
```

```
Duppadhaṃse <note>appadhaṃse (sī. pī.)</note> padhaṃseti, taṃ me akkhātha pucchitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§165.</p>

```
Uddhaggarājī migarājā, balī dāṭhāvudho migo;
```

```
So taccha sūkare hanti, idhāgantvā varaṃ varaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§166.</p>

```
Na no dāṭhā na vijjanti <note>nu vijjanti (ka.)</note>, balaṃ kāye samohitaṃ;
```

```
Sabbe samaggā hutvāna, vasaṃ kāhāma ekakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§167.</p>

```
Hadayaṅgamaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0297" /> kaṇṇasukhaṃ, vācaṃ bhāsasi tacchaka;
```

```
Yopi yuddhe palāyeyya, tampi pacchā hanāmase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§168.</p>

```
Pāṇātipātā virato nu ajja, abhayaṃ nu te sabbabhūtesu dinnaṃ;
```

```
Dāṭhā nu te migavadhāya <note>miga viriyaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> na santi, yo saṅghapatto kapaṇova jhāyasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§169.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="T" n="1.0393" /> me dāṭhā na vijjanti, balaṃ kāye samohitaṃ;
```

```
Ñātī ca disvāna sāmaggī ekato, tasmā ca jhāyāmi vanamhi ekako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§170.</p>

```
Imassudaṃ yanti disodisaṃ pure, bhayaṭṭitā leṇagavesino puthu;
```

```
Te dāni saṅgamma vasanti ekato, yatthaṭṭhitā duppasahajja te mayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§171.</p>

```
Pariṇāyakasampannā, sahitā ekavādino;
```

```
Te maṃ samaggā hiṃseyyuṃ, tasmā nesaṃ na patthaye <note>apatthave (pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§172.</p>

```
Ekova <pb ed="V" n="1.0225" /> indo asure jināti, ekova seno hanti dije pasayha;
```

```
Ekova byaggho migasaṅghapatto, varaṃ varaṃ hanti balañhi tādisaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§173.</p>

```
Na heva indo na seno, napi byaggho migādhipo;
```

```
Samagge sahite ñātī, na byagghe <note>byagghe ca (sī. pī.), byaggho na (syā.)</note> kurute vase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§174.</p>

```
Kumbhīlakā sakuṇakā, saṅghino gaṇacārino;
```

```
Sammodamānā ekajjhaṃ, uppatanti ḍayanti ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§175.</p>

```
Tesañca ḍayamānānaṃ, ekettha apasakkati <note>apavattati (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Tañca seno nitāḷeti, veyyagghiyeva sā gati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§176.</p>

```
Ussāhito <pb ed="T" n="1.0394" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0298" /> jaṭilena, luddenāmisacakkhunā;
```

```
Dāṭhī dāṭhīsu pakkhandi, maññamāno yathā pure.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§177.</p>

```
Sādhu sambahulā ñātī, api rukkhā araññajā;
```

```
Sūkarehi samaggehi, byaggho ekāyane hato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§178.</p>

```
Brāhmaṇañceva byagghañca, ubho hantvāna sūkarā.
```

```
Ānandino pamuditā, mahānādaṃ panādisuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§179.</p>

```
Te su udumbaramūlasmiṃ, sūkarā susamāgatā;
```

```
Tacchakaṃ abhisiñciṃsu, ‘‘tvaṃ no rājāsi issaro’’ti.
```

Tacchasūkarajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 493. Mahāvāṇijajātakaṃ (10)

<p rend="hangnum">§180.</p>

```
Vāṇijā samitiṃ katvā, nānāraṭṭhato āgatā;
```

```
Dhanāharā pakkamiṃsu, ekaṃ katvāna gāmaṇiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§181.</p>

```
Te taṃ kantāramāgamma, appabhakkhaṃ anodakaṃ;
```

```
Mahānigrodhamaddakkhuṃ, sītacchāyaṃ manoramaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§182.</p>

```
Te ca tattha nisīditvā, tassa rukkhassa chāyayā <note>chādiyā (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Vāṇijā samacintesuṃ, bālā mohena pārutā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§183.</p>

```
Allāyate <note>addāyate (sī. pī.)</note> ayaṃ rukkho, api vārīva <note>vāri ca (sī. pī.)</note> sandati;
```

```
Iṅghassa purimaṃ sākhaṃ, mayaṃ chindāma vāṇijā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§184.</p>

```
Sā ca chinnāva pagghari, acchaṃ vāriṃ anāvilaṃ;
```

```
Te <pb ed="T" n="1.0395" /> tattha nhatvā pivitvā, yāvaticchiṃsu vāṇijā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§185.</p>

```
Dutiyaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0226" /> samacintesuṃ, bālā mohena pārutā;
```

```
Iṅghassa dakkhiṇaṃ sākhaṃ, mayaṃ chindāma vāṇijā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§186.</p>

```
Sā ca chinnāva pagghari, sālimaṃsodanaṃ bahuṃ;
```

```
Appodavaṇṇe kummāse, siṅgiṃ vidalasūpiyo <note>siṅgiṃ bidalasūpiyo (sī. pī.), siṅgīveraṃ lasūpiyo (ka.) siṅgīnti siṅgīverādikaṃ uttaribhaṅgaṃ; vidalasūpiyoti muggasūpādayo (aṭṭha.) vidalaṃ kalāyādimhi vattatīti sakkatābhidhāne</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§187.</p>

```
Te <pb ed="M" n="1.0299" /> tattha bhutvā khāditvā <note>bhutvā ca pivitvā ca (pī.)</note>, yāvaticchiṃsu vāṇijā;
```

```
Tatiyaṃ samacintesuṃ, bālā mohena pārutā;
```

```
Iṅghassa pacchimaṃ sākhaṃ, mayaṃ chindāma vāṇijā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§188.</p>

```
Sā ca chinnāva pagghari, nāriyo samalaṅkatā;
```

```
Vicitravatthābharaṇā, āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§189.</p>

```
Api su vāṇijā ekā, nāriyo paṇṇavīsati;
```

```
Samantā parivāriṃsu <note>parikariṃsu (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, tassa rukkhassa chāyayā <note>chādiyā (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§190.</p>

```
Te tāhi paricāretvā <note>parivāretvā (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, yāvaticchiṃsu vāṇijā;
```

```
Catutthaṃ samacintesuṃ, bālā mohena pārutā;
```

```
Iṅghassa uttaraṃ sākhaṃ, mayaṃ chindāma vāṇijā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§191.</p>

```
Sā ca chinnāva pagghari, muttā veḷuriyā bahū;
```

```
Rajataṃ jātarūpañca, kuttiyo paṭiyāni ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§192.</p>

```
Kāsikāni ca vatthāni, uddiyāni ca kambalā <note>uddiyāne ca kambale (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Te tattha bhāre bandhitvā, yāvaticchiṃsu vāṇijā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§193.</p>

```
Pañcamaṃ samacintesuṃ, bālā mohena pārutā;
```

```
Iṅghassa <pb ed="T" n="1.0396" /> mūle <note>mūlaṃ (sī. pī. ka.)</note> chindāma, api bhiyyo labhāmase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§194.</p>

```
Athuṭṭhahi satthavāho, yācamāno katañjalī;
```

```
Nigrodho kiṃ parajjhati <note>aparajjhatha (sī.), aparajjhati (syā. pī.)</note>, vāṇijā bhaddamatthu te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§195.</p>

```
Vāridā purimā sākhā, annapānañca dakkhiṇā;
```

```
Nāridā pacchimā sākhā, sabbakāme ca uttarā;
```

```
Nigrodho kiṃ parajjhati, vāṇijā bhaddamatthu te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§196.</p>

```
Yassa rukkhassa chāyāya, nisīdeyya sayeyya vā;
```

```
Na tassa sākhaṃ bhañjeyya, mittadubbho hi pāpako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§197.</p>

```
Te ca tassānādiyitvā <note>tassa anāditvā (sī. syā.)</note>, ekassa vacanaṃ bahū;
```

```
Nisitāhi kuṭhārīhi <note>kudhārīhi (ka.)</note>, mūlato naṃ upakkamuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§198.</p>

```
Tato <pb ed="V" n="1.0227" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0300" /> nāgā nikkhamiṃsu, sannaddhā paṇṇavīsati;
```

```
Dhanuggahānaṃ tisatā, chasahassā ca vammino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§199.</p>

```
Ete hanatha bandhatha, mā vo muñcittha <note>muccittha (pī.)</note> jīvitaṃ;
```

```
Ṭhapetvā satthavāhaṃva, sabbe bhasmaṃ <note>bhasmī (sī.)</note> karotha ne.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§200.</p>

```
Tasmā hi paṇḍito poso, sampassaṃ atthamattano;
```

```
Lobhassa na vasaṃ gacche, haneyyārisakaṃ <note>haneyya disataṃ (sī.), haneyya disakaṃ (syā.)</note> manaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§201.</p>

```
Eva <note>eta (sī. pī.)</note> mādīnavaṃ ñatvā, taṇhā dukkhassa sambhavaṃ;
```

```
Vītataṇho anādāno, sato bhikkhu paribbajeti.
```

Mahāvāṇijajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

#### 494. Sādhinajātakaṃ (11)

<p rend="hangnum">§202.</p>

```
Abbhuto <pb ed="T" n="1.0397" /> vata lokasmiṃ, uppajji lomahaṃsano;
```

```
Dibbo ratho pāturahu, vedehassa yasassino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§203.</p>

```
Devaputto mahiddhiko, mātali <note>mātalī (sī.)</note> devasārathi;
```

```
Nimantayittha rājānaṃ, vedehaṃ mithilaggahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§204.</p>

```
Ehimaṃ rathamāruyha, rājaseṭṭha disampati;
```

```
Devā dassanakāmā te, tāvatiṃsā saindakā;
```

```
Saramānā hi te devā, sudhammāyaṃ samacchare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§205.</p>

```
Tato ca rājā sādhino <note>sādhīno (sī. pī.)</note>, vedeho mithilaggaho <note>pamukho rathamāruhi (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Sahassayuttamāruyha <note>yuttaṃ abhiruyha (sī.)</note>, agā devāna santike;
```

```
Taṃ devā paṭinandiṃsu, disvā rājānamāgataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§206.</p>

```
Svāgataṃ te mahārāja, atho te adurāgataṃ;
```

```
Nisīda dāni rājīsi <note>rājisi (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, devarājassa santike.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§207.</p>

```
Sakkopi paṭinandittha, vedehaṃ mithilaggahaṃ;
```

```
Nimantayittha <note>nimantayī ca (sī. pī.)</note> kāmehi, āsanena ca vāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§208.</p>

```
Sādhu <pb ed="M" n="1.0301" /> khosi anuppatto, āvāsaṃ vasavattinaṃ;
```

```
Vasa <pb ed="T" n="1.0398" /> devesu rājīsi, sabbakāmasamiddhisu;
```

```
Tāvatiṃsesu devesu, bhuñja kāme amānuse.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§209.</p>

```
Ahaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0228" /> pure saggagato ramāmi, naccehi gītehi ca vāditehi;
```

```
So dāni ajja na ramāmi sagge, āyuṃ nu khīṇo <note>khīṇaṃ (syā.)</note> maraṇaṃ nu santike;
```

```
Udāhu mūḷhosmi janindaseṭṭha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§210.</p>

```
Na tāyu <note>na cāyu (sī. pī. ka.)</note> khīṇaṃ maraṇañca <note>maraṇaṃ te (sī. pī.)</note> dūre, na cāpi mūḷho naravīraseṭṭha;
```

```
Tuyhañca <note>tavañca (sī. pī.), tava ca (ka.)</note> puññāni parittakāni, yesaṃ vipākaṃ idha vedayittho <note>vedayato (pī. ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§211.</p>

```
Vasa devānubhāvena, rājaseṭṭha disampati;
```

```
Tāvatiṃsesu devesu, bhuñja kāme amānuse.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§212.</p>

```
Yathā yācitakaṃ yānaṃ, yathā yācitakaṃ dhanaṃ;
```

```
Evaṃ sampadamevetaṃ, yaṃ parato dānapaccayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§213.</p>

```
Na cāhametamicchāmi, yaṃ parato dānapaccayā;
```

```
Sayaṃkatāni puññāni, taṃ me āveṇikaṃ <note>āveṇiyaṃ (sī. syā. pī.), āvenikaṃ (ka.)</note> dhanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§214.</p>

```
Sohaṃ gantvā manussesu, kāhāmi kusalaṃ bahuṃ;
```

```
Dānena samacariyāya, saṃyamena damena ca;
```

```
Yaṃ katvā sukhito hoti, na ca pacchānutappati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§215.</p>

```
Imāni <pb ed="T" n="1.0399" /> tāni khettāni, imaṃ nikkhaṃ sukuṇḍalaṃ;
```

```
Imā tā haritānūpā, imā najjo savantiyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§216.</p>

```
Imā tā pokkharaṇī rammā, cakkavākapakūjitā <note>cakkavākūpakūjitā (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Mandālakehi sañchannā, padumuppalakehi ca;
```

```
Yassimāni mamāyiṃsu, kiṃ nu te disataṃ gatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§217.</p>

```
Tānīdha <pb ed="M" n="1.0302" /> khettāni so bhūmibhāgo, teyeva ārāmavanupacārā <note>te ārāmā te vana’me pacārā (sī. pī.), te yeva ārāmavanāni sañcarā (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Tameva mayhaṃ janataṃ apassato, suññaṃva me nārada khāyate disā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§218.</p>

```
Diṭṭhā mayā vimānāni, obhāsentā catuddisā;
```

```
Sammukhā devarājassa, tidasānañca sammukhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§219.</p>

```
Vutthaṃ me bhavanaṃ dibyaṃ <note>dibbaṃ (sī. pī.)</note>, bhuttā kāmā amānusā;
```

```
Tāvatiṃsesu devesu, sabbakāmasamiddhisu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§220.</p>

```
Sohaṃ etādisaṃ hitvā, puññāyamhi idhāgato;
```

```
Dhammameva carissāmi, nāhaṃ rajjena atthiko.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§221.</p>

```
Adaṇḍāvacaraṃ maggaṃ, sammāsambuddhadesitaṃ;
```

```
Taṃ maggaṃ paṭipajjissaṃ, yena gacchanti subbatāti.
```

Sādhinajātakaṃ <note>sādhinarājajātakaṃ (syā.)</note> ekādasamaṃ.

#### 495. Dasabrāhmaṇajātakaṃ (12)

<p rend="hangnum">§222.</p>

```
Rājā <pb ed="T" n="1.0400" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0229" /> avoca vidhuraṃ, dhammakāmo yudhiṭṭhilo;
```

```
Brāhmaṇe vidhura pariyesa, sīlavante bahussute.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§223.</p>

```
Virate methunā dhammā, ye me bhuñjeyyu <note>bhuñjeyyuṃ (sī.)</note> bhojanaṃ;
```

```
Dakkhiṇaṃ samma dassāma, yattha dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§224.</p>

```
Dullabhā brāhmaṇā deva, sīlavanto bahussutā;
```

```
Viratā methunā dhammā, ye te bhuñjeyyu bhojanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§225.</p>

```
Dasa khalu mahārāja, yā tā brāhmaṇajātiyo;
```

```
Tesaṃ vibhaṅgaṃ vicayaṃ <note>viciya (ka.)</note>, vitthārena suṇohi me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§226.</p>

```
Pasibbake gahetvāna, puṇṇe mūlassa saṃvute;
```

```
Osadhikāyo <note>osadhikāye (syā. ka.)</note> ganthenti, nhāpayanti <note>nahāyanti (sī. pī.)</note> japanti ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§227.</p>

```
Tikicchakasamā <pb ed="M" n="1.0303" /> rāja, tepi vuccanti brāhmaṇā;

```
Akkhātā te mahārāja, tādise nipatāmase.

```

(Iti rājā <note>rājā ca (syā. ka.)</note> korabyo)
```

```
Na te vuccanti brāhmaṇā;
```

```
Aññe vidhura pariyesa, sīlavante bahussute.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§229.</p>

```
Virate methunā dhammā, ye me bhuñjeyyu bhojanaṃ;
```

```
Dakkhiṇaṃ samma dassāma, yattha dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§230.</p>

```

```
Pesanānipi gacchanti, rathacariyāsu sikkhare.

Paccupessanti rājāno, gāmesu nigamesu ca;
```

```
Nādinne vuṭṭhahissāma, gāmamhi vā vanamhi vā <note>vāmamhi ca vanamhi ca (sī. pī.), gāmamhi nigamamhi vā (syā.)</note>.

<p rend="hangnum">§261.</p>

Apetā <pb ed="M" n="1.0306" /> te brahmaññā,

```
(Iti rājā korabyo)
```

```
Na te vuccanti brāhmaṇā;
```

```
Aññe vidhura pariyesa, sīlavante bahussute.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§262.</p>

```
Virate methunā dhammā, ye me bhuñjeyyu bhojanaṃ;
```

```
Dakkhiṇaṃ samma dassāma, yattha dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§263.</p>

```
Aññe dhanassa kāmā hi, heṭṭhāmañce pasakkitā <note>pasakkhitā (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Rājāno upari nhāyanti, somayāge upaṭṭhite.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§264.</p>

```
Malamajjakasamā rāja, tepi vuccanti brāhmaṇā;
```

```
Akkhātā te mahārāja, tādise nipatāmase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§265.</p>

```
Apetā <pb ed="T" n="1.0405" /> te brahmaññā,
```

```
(Iti rājā korabyo)
```

```
Na te vuccanti brāhmaṇā;
```

```
Aññe vidhura pariyesa, sīlavante bahussute.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§266.</p>

```
Virate methunā dhammā, ye me bhuñjeyyu bhojanaṃ;
```

```
Dakkhiṇaṃ samma dassāma, yattha dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§267.</p>

```
Atthi kho brāhmaṇā deva, sīlavanto bahussutā;
```

```
Viratā methunā dhammā, ye te bhuñjeyyu bhojanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§268.</p>

```
Ekañca <pb ed="V" n="1.0233" /> bhattaṃ bhuñjanti, na ca majjaṃ pivanti te;
```

```
Akkhātā te mahārāja, tādise nipatāmase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§269.</p>

```
Ete kho brāhmaṇā vidhura, sīlavanto bahussutā;
```

```
Ete vidhura pariyesa, khippañca ne <note>khippaṃva ne (ka.)</note> nimantayāti.
```

Dasabrāhmaṇajātakaṃ dvādasamaṃ.

#### 496. Bhikkhāparamparajātakaṃ (13)

<p rend="hangnum">§270.</p>

```
Sukhumālarūpaṃ disvā <note>disvāna (ka. sī. aṭṭha.)</note>, raṭṭhā vivanamāgataṃ;
```

```
Kūṭāgāravarūpetaṃ, mahāsayanamupāsitaṃ <note>mupocitaṃ (bahūsu)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§271.</p>

```
Tassa <pb ed="M" n="1.0307" /> te pemakenāhaṃ, adāsiṃ vaḍḍhamodanaṃ <note>baddhamodanaṃ (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Sālīnaṃ vicitaṃ bhattaṃ, suciṃ maṃsūpasecanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§272.</p>

```
Taṃ tvaṃ bhattaṃ paṭiggayha, brāhmaṇassa adāsayi <note>adāpayi (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Attānaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0406" /> <note>attanā (pī. aṭṭha. pāṭhantaraṃ)</note> anasitvāna, koyaṃ dhammo namatthu te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§273.</p>

```
Ācariyo brāhmaṇo mayhaṃ, kiccākiccesu byāvaṭo <note>vāvaṭo (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Garu ca āmantanīyo <note>āmantaṇīyo (sī. pī.)</note> ca, dātumarahāmi bhojanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§274.</p>

```
Brāhmaṇaṃ dāni pucchāmi, gotamaṃ rājapūjitaṃ;
```

```
Rājā te bhattaṃ pādāsi, suciṃ maṃsūpasecanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§275.</p>

```
Taṃ tvaṃ bhattaṃ paṭiggayha, isissa bhojanaṃ adā;
```

```
Akhettaññūsi dānassa, koyaṃ dhammo namatthu te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§276.</p>

```
Bharāmi putta <note>putte (sī. pī.)</note> dāre ca, gharesu gadhito <note>gathito (sī. pī.)</note> ahaṃ;
```

```
Bhuñje mānusake kāme, anusāsāmi rājino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§277.</p>

```
Āraññikassa <note>āraññakassa (sī. pī.)</note> isino, cirarattaṃ tapassino;
```

```
Vuḍḍhassa bhāvitattassa, dātumarahāmi bhojanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§278.</p>

```
Isiñca dāni pucchāmi, kisaṃ dhamanisanthataṃ;
```

```
Parūḷhakacchanakhalomaṃ, paṅkadantaṃ rajassiraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§279.</p>

```
Eko araññe viharasi <note>vihāsi (ka.)</note>, nāvakaṅkhasi jīvitaṃ;
```

```
Bhikkhu kena tayā seyyo, yassa tvaṃ bhojanaṃ adā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§280.</p>

```
Khaṇantālukalambāni <note>khaṇamālukalambāni (syā. ka.)</note>, bilālitakkalāni ca <note>biḷālitakkaḷāni ca (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Dhunaṃ sāmākanīvāraṃ, saṅghāriyaṃ pasāriyaṃ <note>saṃhāriyaṃ pahāriyaṃ (syā.), saṃsāriyaṃ pasāriyaṃ (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§281.</p>

```
Sākaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0234" /> bhisaṃ madhuṃ maṃsaṃ, badarāmalakāni ca;
```

```
Tāni āharitvā <note>āhatva (sī. syā.)</note> bhuñjāmi, atthi me so pariggaho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§282.</p>

```
Pacanto <pb ed="T" n="1.0407" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0308" /> apacantassa, amamassa sakiñcano <note>akiñcano (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Anādānassa sādāno, dātumarahāmi bhojanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§283.</p>

```
Bhikkhuñca dāni pucchāmi, tuṇhīmāsīna subbataṃ;
```

```
Isi te bhattaṃ pādāsi, suciṃ maṃsūpasecanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§284.</p>

```
Taṃ tvaṃ bhattaṃ paṭiggayha, tuṇhī bhuñjasi ekako;
```

```
Nāññaṃ kañci <note>kiñci (ka.)</note> nimantesi, koyaṃ dhammo namatthu te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§285.</p>

```
Na pacāmi na pācemi, na chindāmi na chedaye;
```

```
Taṃ maṃ akiñcanaṃ ñatvā, sabbapāpehi ārataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§286.</p>

```
Vāmena bhikkhamādāya, dakkhiṇena kamaṇḍaluṃ;
```

```
Isi me bhattaṃ pādāsi, suciṃ maṃsūpasecanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§287.</p>

```
Ete hi dātumarahanti, samamā sapariggahā;
```

```
Paccanīkamahaṃ maññe, yo dātāraṃ nimantaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§288.</p>

```
Atthāya vata me ajja, idhāgacchi rathesabho;
```

```
Sohaṃ ajja pajānāmi <note>ito pubbe na jānāmi (sī. pī.)</note>, yattha dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§289.</p>

```
Raṭṭhesu giddhā rājāno, kiccākiccesu brāhmaṇā;
```

```
Isī mūlaphale giddhā, vippamuttā ca bhikkhavoti.
```

Bhikkhāparamparajātakaṃ terasamaṃ.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Suva <pb ed="T" n="1.0408" /> kinnara mukka kharājinaso, bhisajāta mahesi kapotavaro;
```

```
Atha mora satacchaka vāṇijako, atha rāja sabrāhmaṇa bhikkhaparanti.
```

<trailer rend="centre">Pakiṇṇakanipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.</trailer>

### 15. Vīsatinipāto

#### 497. Mātaṅgajātakaṃ (1)

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
Kuto <pb ed="T" n="1.0409" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0235" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0309" /> nu āgacchasi dummavāsī <note>rummavāsī (sī. pī.)</note>, otallako paṃsupisācakova;
```

```
Saṅkāracoḷaṃ paṭimuñca <note>paṭimucca (sī. pī.)</note> kaṇṭhe, ko re tuvaṃ hosi <note>hohisi (sī. pī.)</note> adakkhiṇeyyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
Annaṃ tavedaṃ <note>tava idaṃ (ka. sī. pī.), tavayidaṃ (syā.)</note> pakataṃ yasassi, taṃ khajjare bhuñjare piyyare ca;
```

```
Jānāsi maṃ tvaṃ paradattūpajīviṃ, uttiṭṭhapiṇḍaṃ labhataṃ sapāko.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
Annaṃ mamedaṃ <note>mama idaṃ (ka. sī. pī.), mamayidaṃ (syā.)</note> pakataṃ brāhmaṇānaṃ, attatthāya saddahato mamedaṃ <note>mama idaṃ (ka. sī. pī.), mamayidaṃ (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Apehi etto kimidhaṭṭhitosi, na mādisā tuyhaṃ dadanti jamma.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
Thale ca ninne ca vapanti bījaṃ, anūpakhette phalamāsamānā <note>māsasānā (sī. pī.), māsiṃ samānā (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Etāya saddhāya dadāhi dānaṃ, appeva ārādhaye dakkhiṇeyye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
Khettāni mayhaṃ viditāni loke, yesāhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0410" /> bījāni patiṭṭhapemi;
```

```
Ye brāhmaṇā jātimantūpapannā, tānīdha khettāni supesalāni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
Jātimado ca atimānitā ca, lobho ca doso ca mado ca moho;
```

```
Ete aguṇā yesu ca santi <note>yesu vasanti (sī. pī.)</note> sabbe, tānīdha khettāni apesalāni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
Jātimado <pb ed="M" n="1.0310" /> ca atimānitā ca, lobho ca doso ca mado ca moho;
```

```
Ete aguṇā yesu na santi sabbe, tānīdha khettāni supesalāni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
Kvettha gatā <note>kvattha gatā (syā.), kattheva bhaṭṭhā (pī.)</note> upajotiyo ca, upajjhāyo ca athavā gaṇḍakucchi <note>aṇḍakucchi (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Imassa daṇḍañca vadhañca datvā, gale gahetvā khalayātha <note>galayātha (ka.)</note> jammaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
Giriṃ nakhena khaṇasi, ayo dantehi <note>dantena (sī. pī.)</note> khādasi;
```

```
Jātavedaṃ padahasi, yo isiṃ paribhāsasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
Idaṃ vatvāna mātaṅgo, isi saccaparakkamo;
```

```
Antalikkhasmiṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0411" /> pakkāmi <note>pakkami (ka.)</note>, brāhmaṇānaṃ udikkhataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
Āvellitaṃ <note>aveṭhitaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> piṭṭhito uttamaṅgaṃ, bāhuṃ <note>bāhaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> pasāreti akammaneyyaṃ <note>akampaneyyaṃ (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Setāni akkhīni yathā matassa, ko me imaṃ puttamakāsi evaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
Idhāgamā <pb ed="V" n="1.0236" /> samaṇo dummavāsī, otallako paṃsupisācakova;
```

```
Saṅkāracoḷaṃ paṭimuñca kaṇṭhe, so te imaṃ puttamakāsi evaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
Katamaṃ disaṃ agamā bhūripañño, akkhātha me māṇavā etamatthaṃ;
```

```
Gantvāna taṃ paṭikaremu accayaṃ, appeva naṃ putta labhemu jīvitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
Vehāyasaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0311" /> agamā bhūripañño, pathaddhuno pannaraseva cando;
```

```
Api cāpi so purimadisaṃ agacchi, saccappaṭiñño isi sādhurūpo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
Āvellitaṃ piṭṭhito uttamaṅgaṃ, bāhuṃ pasāreti akammaneyyaṃ;
```

```
Setāni akkhīni yathā matassa, ko <pb ed="T" n="1.0412" /> me imaṃ puttamakāsi evaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
Yakkhā have santi mahānubhāvā, anvāgatā isayo sādhurūpā;
```

```
Te duṭṭhacittaṃ kupitaṃ viditvā, yakkhā hi te puttamakaṃsu evaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
Yakkhā ca me puttamakaṃsu evaṃ, tvaññeva me mā kuddho <note>kuddha (ka.)</note> brahmacāri;
```

```
Tumheva <note>tuyheva (ka.)</note> pāde saraṇaṃ gatāsmi, anvāgatā puttasokena bhikkhu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
Tadeva hi etarahi ca mayhaṃ, manopadoso na mamatthi <note>mama natthi (pī.)</note> koci;
```

```
Putto ca te vedamadena matto, atthaṃ na jānāti adhicca vede.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
Addhā have bhikkhu muhuttakena, sammuyhateva purisassa saññā;
```

```
Ekāparādhaṃ <note>etāparādhaṃ (ka.)</note> khama bhūripañña, na paṇḍitā kodhabalā bhavanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
Idañca mayhaṃ uttiṭṭhapiṇḍaṃ, tava <note>natthi sī. pī. potthakesu</note> maṇḍabyo bhuñjatu appapañño;
```

```
Yakkhā ca te naṃ <note>te puttaṃ (syā.)</note> na viheṭhayeyyuṃ, putto <pb ed="T" n="1.0413" /> ca te hessati <note>hohiti (sī. pī.)</note> so arogo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
Maṇḍabya <pb ed="M" n="1.0312" /> bālosi parittapañño, yo puññakhettānamakovidosi;
```

```
Mahakkasāvesu dadāsi dānaṃ, kiliṭṭhakammesu asaññatesu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
Jaṭā ca kesā ajinā nivatthā, jarūdapānaṃva mukhaṃ parūḷhaṃ;
```

```
Pajaṃ imaṃ passatha dummarūpaṃ <note>rummarūpiṃ (sī. pī.)</note>, na jaṭājinaṃ tāyati appapaññaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
Yesaṃ rāgo ca doso ca, avijjā ca virājitā;
```

```
Khīṇāsavā arahanto, tesu dinnaṃ mahapphalanti.
```

Mātaṅgajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 498. Cittasambhūtajātakaṃ (2)

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
Sabbaṃ narānaṃ saphalaṃ suciṇṇaṃ, na kammunā kiñcana moghamatthi;
```

```
Passāmi sambhūtaṃ mahānubhāvaṃ, sakammunā <pb ed="T" n="1.0414" /> puññaphalūpapannaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
Sabbaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0237" /> narānaṃ saphalaṃ suciṇṇaṃ, na kammunā kiñcana moghamatthi;
```

```
Kaccinnu cittassapi evamevaṃ, iddho mano tassa yathāpi mayhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
Sabbaṃ narānaṃ saphalaṃ suciṇṇaṃ, na kammunā kiñcana moghamatthi;
```

```
Cittampi jānāhi <note>cittaṃ vijānāhi (sī. pī.)</note> tatheva deva, iddho mano tassa yathāpi tuyhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
Bhavaṃ nu citto sutamaññato te, udāhu te koci naṃ etadakkhā;
```

```
Gāthā sugītā na mamatthi kaṅkhā, dadāmi te gāmavaraṃ satañca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="M" n="1.0313" /> cāhaṃ citto sutamaññato me, isī ca me etamatthaṃ asaṃsi;
```

```
‘‘Gantvāna rañño paṭigāhi <note>paṭigāyi (syā. ka.), paṭigāya (?)</note> gāthaṃ, api te varaṃ attamano dadeyya’’ <note>api nu te varaṃ attamano dadeyya (syā.), api nu te attamano varaṃ dade (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
Yojentu ve rājarathe, sukate cittasibbane;
```

```
Kacchaṃ nāgānaṃ bandhatha, gīveyyaṃ paṭimuñcatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
Āhaññantu <pb ed="T" n="1.0415" /> <note>āhaññare (syā.)</note> bherimudiṅgasaṅkhe <note>saṅkhā (syā.)</note>, sīghāni yānāni ca yojayantu;
```

```
Ajjevahaṃ assamaṃ taṃ gamissaṃ, yattheva dakkhissamisiṃ nisinnaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
Suladdhalābho vata me ahosi, gāthā sugītā parisāya majjhe;
```

```
Svāhaṃ isiṃ sīlavatūpapannaṃ, disvā patīto sumanohamasmi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
Āsanaṃ udakaṃ pajjaṃ, paṭiggaṇhātu no bhavaṃ;
```

```
Agghe bhavantaṃ pucchāma, agghaṃ kurutu no bhavaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
Rammañca te āvasathaṃ karontu, nārīgaṇehi paricārayassu;
```

```
Karohi okāsamanuggahāya, ubhopi maṃ issariyaṃ karoma.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
Disvā phalaṃ duccaritassa rāja, atho suciṇṇassa mahāvipākaṃ;
```

```
Attānameva paṭisaṃyamissaṃ, na patthaye putta <note>puttaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> pasuṃ dhanaṃ vā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
Dasevimā vassadasā, maccānaṃ idha jīvitaṃ;
```

```
Apattaññeva <pb ed="T" n="1.0416" /> taṃ odhiṃ, naḷo chinnova sussati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
Tattha <pb ed="M" n="1.0314" /> kā nandi kā khiḍḍā, kā ratī kā dhanesanā;
```

```
Kiṃ me puttehi dārehi, rāja muttosmi bandhanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
Sohaṃ evaṃ pajānāmi <note>so ahaṃ suppajānāmi (sī. pī.)</note>, maccu me nappamajjati;
```

```
Antakenādhipannassa, kā ratī kā dhanesanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
Jāti narānaṃ adhamā janinda, caṇḍālayoni dvipadākaniṭṭhā <note>dipadākaniṭṭhā (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Sakehi kammehi supāpakehi, caṇḍālagabbhe <note>caṇḍāligabbhe (syā.)</note> avasimha pubbe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
Caṇḍālāhumha avantīsu, migā nerañjaraṃ pati;
```

```
Ukkusā nammadātīre <note>rammadātīre (syā. ka.)</note>, tyajja brāhmaṇakhattiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
Upanīyati <pb ed="V" n="1.0238" /> jīvitamappamāyu, jarūpanītassa <pb ed="T" n="1.0417" /> na santi tāṇā;
```

```
Karohi pañcāla mameta <note>mameva (syā. ka.)</note> vākyaṃ, mākāsi kammāni dukkhudrayāni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
Upanīyati jīvitamappamāyu, jarūpanītassa na santi tāṇā;
```

```
Karohi pañcāla mameta vākyaṃ, mākāsi kammāni dukkhapphalāni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
Upanīyati jīvitamappamāyu, jarūpanītassa na santi tāṇā;
```

```
Karohi pañcāla mameta vākyaṃ, mākāsi kammāni rajassirāni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
Upanīyati jīvitamappamāyu, vaṇṇaṃ jarā hanti narassa jiyyato;
```

```
Karohi pañcāla mameta vākyaṃ, mākāsi kammaṃ nirayūpapattiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
Addhā <pb ed="M" n="1.0315" /> hi saccaṃ vacanaṃ tavetaṃ, yathā isī bhāsasi evametaṃ;
```

```
Kāmā ca me santi anapparūpā, te duccajā mādisakena bhikkhu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
Nāgo yathā paṅkamajjhe byasanno, passaṃ thalaṃ nābhisambhoti gantuṃ;
```

```
Evampahaṃ <note>evamahaṃ (syā.)</note> kāmapaṅke byasanno, na bhikkhuno maggamanubbajāmi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
Yathāpi mātā ca pitā ca puttaṃ, anusāsare kinti sukhī bhaveyya;
```

```
Evampi maṃ tvaṃ anusāsa bhante, yathā ciraṃ <note>yamācaraṃ (sī. pī. ka. aṭṭha.)</note> pecca sukhī bhaveyyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
No <pb ed="T" n="1.0418" /> ce tuvaṃ ussahase janinda, kāme ime mānusake pahātuṃ;
```

```
Dhammiṃ <note>dhammaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> baliṃ paṭṭhapayassu rāja, adhammakāro tava <note>adhammakāro ca te (sī. syā. pī.)</note> māhu raṭṭhe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
Dūtā vidhāvantu disā catasso, nimantakā samaṇabrāhmaṇānaṃ;
```

```
Te annapānena upaṭṭhahassu, vatthena senāsanapaccayena ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
Annena pānena pasannacitto, santappaya samaṇabrāhmaṇe ca;
```

```
Datvā ca bhutvā ca yathānubhāvaṃ, anindito saggamupehi <note>mupeti (pī. ka.)</note> ṭhānaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
Sace ca taṃ rāja mado saheyya, nārīgaṇehi paricārayantaṃ;
```

```
Imameva gāthaṃ manasī karohi, bhāsesi <note>bhāsehi (syā. pī. ka.)</note> cenaṃ parisāya majjhe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
Abbhokāsasayo <pb ed="M" n="1.0316" /> jantu, vajantyā khīrapāyito;
```

```
Parikiṇṇo suvānehi <note>supinehi (sī. pī.)</note>, svājja rājāti vuccatīti.
```

Cittasambhūtajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 499. Sivijātakaṃ (3)

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
Dūre <pb ed="T" n="1.0419" /> apassaṃ therova, cakkhuṃ yācitumāgato;
```

```
Ekanettā bhavissāma, cakkhuṃ me dehi yācito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
Kenānusiṭṭho <pb ed="V" n="1.0239" /> idha māgatosi, vanibbaka <note>vaṇibbaka (sī.)</note> cakkhupathāni yācituṃ;
```

```
Suduccajaṃ yācasi uttamaṅgaṃ, yamāhu nettaṃ purisena duccajaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
Yamāhu devesu sujampatīti, maghavāti naṃ āhu manussaloke;
```

```
Tenānusiṭṭho idha māgatosmi, vanibbako cakkhupathāni yācituṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
Vanibbato <note>vanibbako (syā. pī.)</note> mayha vaniṃ <note>vanaṃ (ka.), vaṇiṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> anuttaraṃ, dadāhi te cakkhupathāni yācito;
```

```
Dadāhi me cakkhupathaṃ anuttaraṃ, yamāhu nettaṃ purisena duccajaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
Yena atthena āgacchi <note>āgañchi (sī. pī.)</note>, yamatthamabhipatthayaṃ;
```

```
Te te ijjhantu saṅkappā, labha cakkhūni brāhmaṇa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
Ekaṃ te yācamānassa, ubhayāni dadāmahaṃ;
```

```
Sa cakkhumā gaccha janassa pekkhato, yadicchase tvaṃ tadate samijjhatu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
Mā <pb ed="T" n="1.0420" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0317" /> no deva adā cakkhuṃ, mā no sabbe parākari <note>parakkari (syā. ka. aṭṭha.), parikkari (ka.) pari + ā + kari = parākari</note>;
```

```
Dhanaṃ dehi mahārāja, muttā veḷuriyā bahū.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
Yutte deva rathe dehi, ājānīye calaṅkate;
```

```
Nāge dehi mahārāja, hemakappanavāsase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
Yathā taṃ sivayo <note>sīviyo (syā.)</note> sabbe, sayoggā sarathā sadā;
```

```
Samantā parikireyyuṃ <note>parikareyyuṃ (syā. pī.)</note>, evaṃ dehi rathesabha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
Yo ve dassanti vatvāna, adāne kurute mano;
```

```
Bhūmyaṃ <note>bhūmyā (sī. pī.)</note> so patitaṃ pāsaṃ, gīvāyaṃ paṭimuñcati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
Yo ve dassanti vatvāna, adāne kurute mano;
```

```
Pāpā pāpataro hoti, sampatto yamasādhanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
Yañhi yāce tañhi dade, yaṃ na yāce na taṃ dade;
```

```
Svāhaṃ tameva dassāmi, yaṃ maṃ yācati brāhmaṇo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
Āyuṃ nu vaṇṇaṃ nu sukhaṃ balaṃ nu, kiṃ patthayāno nu janinda desi;
```

```
Kathañhi rājā sivinaṃ anuttaro, cakkhūni dajjā paralokahetu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
Na vāhametaṃ yasasā dadāmi, na puttamicche na dhanaṃ na raṭṭhaṃ;
```

```
Satañca dhammo carito purāṇo, icceva dāne ramate mano mama <note>mamaṃ (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
Sakhā <pb ed="T" n="1.0421" /> ca mitto ca mamāsi sīvika <note>sīvaka (sī. pī.)</note>, susikkhito sādhu karohi me vaco;
```

```
Uddharitvā <note>uddhatva (sī.), laddha tvaṃ (pī.)</note> cakkhūni mamaṃ jigīsato, hatthesu ṭhapehi <note>āvesi (sī.)</note> vanibbakassa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
Codito <pb ed="V" n="1.0240" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0318" /> sivirājena, siviko vacanaṅkaro;
```

```
Rañño cakkhūnuddharitvā <note>cakkhūni uddhatvā (sī. pī.)</note>, brāhmaṇassūpanāmayi;
```

```
Sacakkhu brāhmaṇo āsi, andho rājā upāvisi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
Tato so katipāhassa, uparūḷhesu cakkhusu;
```

```
Sūtaṃ āmantayī rājā, sivīnaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
Yojehi sārathi yānaṃ, yuttañca paṭivedaya;
```

```
Uyyānabhūmiṃ gacchāma, pokkharañño vanāni ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
So ca pokkharaṇītīre <note>pokkharaṇiyā tīre (sī. pī.)</note>, pallaṅkena upāvisi;
```

```
Tassa sakko pāturahu, devarājā sujampati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
Sakkohamasmi devindo, āgatosmi tavantike;
```

```
Varaṃ varassu rājīsi, yaṃ kiñci manasicchasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
Pahūtaṃ me dhanaṃ sakka, balaṃ koso canappako;
```

```
Andhassa me sato dāni, maraṇaññeva ruccati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
Yāni <pb ed="T" n="1.0422" /> saccāni dvipadinda, tāni bhāsassu khattiya;
```

```
Saccaṃ te bhaṇamānassa, puna cakkhu bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
Ye maṃ yācitumāyanti, nānāgottā vanibbakā;
```

```
Yopi maṃ yācate tattha, sopi me manaso piyo;
```

```
Etena saccavajjena, cakkhu me upapajjatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
Yaṃ maṃ so yācituṃ āgā, dehi cakkhunti brāhmaṇo;
```

```
Tassa cakkhūni pādāsiṃ, brāhmaṇassa vanibbato <note>vaṇibbino (sī.), vanibbino (pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
Bhiyyo maṃ āvisī pīti, somanassañcanappakaṃ;
```

```
Etena saccavajjena, dutiyaṃ me upapajjatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
Dhammena bhāsitā gāthā, sivīnaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhana;
```

```
Etāni tava nettāni, dibbāni paṭidissare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
Tirokuṭṭaṃ tiroselaṃ, samatiggayha pabbataṃ;
```

```
Samantā yojanasataṃ, dassanaṃ anubhontu te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
Ko <pb ed="M" n="1.0319" /> nīdha vittaṃ na dadeyya yācito, api visiṭṭhaṃ supiyampi attano;
```

```
Tadiṅgha sabbe sivayo samāgatā, dibbāni nettāni mamajja passatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
Tirokuṭṭaṃ tiroselaṃ, samatiggayha pabbataṃ;
```

```
Samantā yojanasataṃ, dassanaṃ anubhonti me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="V" n="1.0241" /> cāgamattā paramatthi kiñci, maccānaṃ idha jīvite;
```

```
Datvāna <pb ed="T" n="1.0423" /> mānusaṃ <note>datvā mānusakaṃ (sī.)</note> cakkhuṃ, laddhaṃ me <note>me iti padaṃ natthi sī. potthake</note> cakkhuṃ amānusaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
Etampi disvā sivayo, detha dānāni bhuñjatha;
```

```
Datvā ca bhutvā ca yathānubhāvaṃ, aninditā saggamupetha ṭhānanti.
```

Sivijātakaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 500. Sirīmantajātakaṃ (4)

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
Paññāyupetaṃ siriyā vihīnaṃ, yasassinaṃ vāpi apetapaññaṃ;
```

```
Pucchāmi taṃ senaka etamatthaṃ, kamettha seyyo kusalā vadanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
Dhīrā ca bālā ca have janinda, sippūpapannā ca asippino ca;
```

```
Sujātimantopi ajātimassa, yasassino pesakarā <note>pessakarā (sī. pī.)</note> bhavanti;
```

```
Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi, pañño nihīno sirīmāva <note>sirimāva (sī. syā. pī.)</note> seyyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
Tuvampi pucchāmi anomapañña, mahosadha kevaladhammadassi;
```

```
Bālaṃ yasassiṃ paṇḍitaṃ appabhogaṃ, kamettha <pb ed="T" n="1.0424" /> seyyo kusalā vadanti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
Pāpāni <pb ed="M" n="1.0320" /> kammāni karoti bālo <note>karonti bālā (syā. ka.)</note>, idhameva <note>idameva (syā. ka. aṭṭha.), imameva (ka.)</note> seyyo iti maññamāno <note>maññamānā (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Idhalokadassī paralokamadassī, ubhayattha bālo kalimaggahesi;
```

```
Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi, paññova seyyo na yasassi bālo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
Na sippametaṃ vidadhāti bhogaṃ, na bandhuvā <note>na bandhavā (sī. syā. ka.)</note> na sarīravaṇṇo yo <note>na sarīrāvakāso (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Passeḷamūgaṃ sukhamedhamānaṃ, sirī hi naṃ bhajate goravindaṃ <note>gorimandaṃ (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi, pañño nihīno sirīmāva seyyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
Laddhā sukhaṃ majjati appapañño, dukkhena phuṭṭhopi pamohameti;
```

```
Āgantunā dukkhasukhena phuṭṭho, pavedhati vāricarova ghamme;
```

```
Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi, paññova seyyo na yasassi bālo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
Dumaṃ yathā sāduphalaṃ araññe, samantato <pb ed="T" n="1.0425" /> samabhisaranti <note>samabhicaranti (sī. pī.)</note> pakkhī;
```

```
Evampi aḍḍhaṃ sadhanaṃ sabhogaṃ, bahujjano bhajati atthahetu;
```

```
Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi, pañño nihīno sirīmāva seyyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
Na sādhu balavā bālo, sāhasā vindate dhanaṃ;
```

```
Kandantametaṃ dummedhaṃ, kaḍḍhanti nirayaṃ bhusaṃ;
```

```
Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi, paññova seyyo na yasassi bālo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
Yā <pb ed="V" n="1.0242" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0321" /> kāci najjo gaṅgamabhissavanti, sabbāva tā nāmagottaṃ jahanti;
```

```
Gaṅgā samuddaṃ paṭipajjamānā, na khāyate iddhiṃ paññopi loke <note>iddhiparo hi loke (ka. sī. syā.), iddhiparo hi loko (sī. pī. aṭṭha.)</note>;
```

```
Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi, pañño nihīno sirīmāva seyyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
Yametamakkhā udadhiṃ mahantaṃ, savanti najjo sabbakālamasaṅkhyaṃ;
```

```
So sāgaro niccamuḷāravego, velaṃ na acceti mahāsamuddo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§93.</p>

```
Evampi <pb ed="T" n="1.0426" /> bālassa pajappitāni, paññaṃ na acceti sirī kadāci;
```

```
Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi, paññova seyyo na yasassi bālo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§94.</p>

```
Asaññato cepi paresamatthaṃ, bhaṇāti sandhānagato <note>saṇṭhānagato (syā. pī.), santhānagato (sī.)</note> yasassī;
```

```
Tasseva taṃ rūhati ñātimajjhe, sirī hi naṃ <note>sirihīnaṃ (sī. ka.), sirīhīnaṃ (syā. pī.)</note> kārayate na paññā <note>na pañño (sī.), na paññaṃ (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi, pañño nihīno sirīmāva seyyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§95.</p>

```
Parassa vā attano vāpi hetu, bālo musā bhāsati appapañño;
```

```
So nindito hoti sabhāya majjhe, pacchāpi <note>peccampi (sī. pī.), peccāpi (?)</note> so duggatigāmī hoti;
```

```
Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi, paññova seyyo na yasassi bālo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§96.</p>

```
Atthampi <pb ed="M" n="1.0322" /> ce bhāsati bhūripañño, anāḷhiyo <note>anālayo (pī.)</note> appadhano daliddo;
```

```
Na tassa taṃ rūhati ñātimajjhe, sirī <pb ed="T" n="1.0427" /> ca paññāṇavato na hoti;
```

```
Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi, pañño nihīno sirīmāva seyyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§97.</p>

```
Parassa vā attano vāpi hetu, na bhāsati alikaṃ bhūripañño;
```

```
So pūjito hoti sabhāya majjhe, pacchāpi so suggatigāmī hoti;
```

```
Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi, paññova seyyo na yasassi bālo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§98.</p>

```
Hatthī gavassā maṇikuṇḍalā ca, thiyo ca iddhesu kulesu jātā;
```

```
Sabbāva tā upabhogā bhavanti, iddhassa posassa aniddhimanto;
```

```
Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi, pañño nihīno sirīmāva seyyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§99.</p>

```
Asaṃvihitakammantaṃ, bālaṃ dummedhamantinaṃ;
```

```
Sirī jahati dummedhaṃ, jiṇṇaṃva urago tacaṃ;
```

```
Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi, paññova seyyo na yasassi bālo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§100.</p>

```
Pañca paṇḍitā mayaṃ bhaddante, sabbe <pb ed="T" n="1.0428" /> pañjalikā upaṭṭhitā;
```

```
Tvaṃ no abhibhuyya issarosi, sakkova bhūtapati devarājā;
```

```
Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi, pañño nihīno sirīmāva seyyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§101.</p>

```
Dāsova <pb ed="V" n="1.0243" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0323" /> paññassa yasassi bālo, atthesu jātesu tathāvidhesu;
```

```
Yaṃ paṇḍito nipuṇaṃ saṃvidheti, sammohamāpajjati tattha bālo;
```

```
Etampi disvāna ahaṃ vadāmi, paññova seyyo na yasassi bālo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§102.</p>

```
Addhā hi paññāva sataṃ pasatthā, kantā sirī bhogaratā manussā;
```

```
Ñāṇañca buddhānamatulyarūpaṃ, paññaṃ na acceti sirī kadāci.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§103.</p>

```
Yaṃ taṃ apucchimha akittayī no, mahosadha kevaladhammadassī;
```

```
Gavaṃ sahassaṃ usabhañca nāgaṃ, ājaññayutte ca rathe dasa ime;
```

```
Pañhassa veyyākaraṇena tuṭṭho, dadāmi <pb ed="T" n="1.0429" /> te gāmavarāni soḷasāti.
```

Sirīmantajātakaṃ <note>sirimandajātakaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> catutthaṃ.

#### 501. Rohaṇamigajātakaṃ (5)

<p rend="hangnum">§104.</p>

```
Ete yūthā patiyanti, bhītā maraṇassa <note>maraṇā (syā. pī.), maraṇa (ka.)</note> cittaka;
```

```
Gaccha tuvampi mākaṅkhi, jīvissanti tayā saha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§105.</p>

```
Nāhaṃ rohaṇa <note>rohanta (sī. pī.), rohana (syā.)</note> gacchāmi, hadayaṃ me avakassati;
```

```
Na taṃ ahaṃ jahissāmi, idha hissāmi jīvitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§106.</p>

```
Te hi nūna marissanti, andhā apariṇāyakā;
```

```
Gaccha tuvampi mākaṅkhi, jīvissanti tayā saha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§107.</p>

```
Nāhaṃ rohaṇa gacchāmi, hadayaṃ me avakassati;
```

```
Na taṃ baddhaṃ <note>bandhaṃ (ka.)</note> jahissāmi, idha hissāmi jīvitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§108.</p>

```
Gaccha <pb ed="M" n="1.0324" /> bhīru palāyassu, kūṭe baddhosmi āyase;
```

```
Gaccha tuvampi mākaṅkhi, jīvissanti tayā saha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§109.</p>

```
Nāhaṃ rohaṇa gacchāmi, hadayaṃ me avakassati;
```

```
Na taṃ ahaṃ jahissāmi, idha hissāmi jīvitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§110.</p>

```
Te hi nūna marissanti, andhā apariṇāyakā;
```

```
Gaccha tuvampi mākaṅkhi, jīvissanti tayā saha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§111.</p>

```
Nāhaṃ rohaṇa gacchāmi, hadayaṃ me avakassati;
```

```
Na <pb ed="T" n="1.0430" /> taṃ baddhaṃ jahissāmi, idha hissāmi jīvitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§112.</p>

```
Ayaṃ so luddako eti, luddarūpo <note>ruddarūpo (sī. pī.)</note> sahāvudho;
```

```
Yo no vadhissati ajja, usunā sattiyā api <note>mapi (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§113.</p>

```
Sā <pb ed="V" n="1.0244" /> muhuttaṃ palāyitvā, bhayaṭṭā <note>bhayaṭṭhā (pī.)</note> bhayatajjitā;
```

```
Sudukkaraṃ akarā bhīru, maraṇāyūpanivattatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§114.</p>

```
Kinnu teme migā honti, muttā baddhaṃ upāsare;
```

```
Na taṃ cajitumicchanti, jīvitassapi kāraṇā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§115.</p>

```
Bhātaro honti me ludda, sodariyā ekamātukā;
```

```
Na maṃ cajitumicchanti, jīvitassapi kāraṇā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§116.</p>

```
Te hi nūna marissanti, andhā apariṇāyakā;
```

```
Pañcannaṃ jīvitaṃ dehi, bhātaraṃ muñca luddaka.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§117.</p>

```
So vo ahaṃ pamokkhāmi, mātāpettibharaṃ migaṃ;
```

```
Nandantu mātāpitaro, muttaṃ disvā mahāmigaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§118.</p>

```
Evaṃ luddaka nandassu, saha sabbehi ñātibhi;
```

```
Yathāhamajja nandāmi, muttaṃ disvā mahāmigaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§119.</p>

```
Kathaṃ tvaṃ pamokkho <note>kathaṃ pamokkho (sī. pī.), kathaṃ te parokkho (?)</note> āsi, upanītasmi jīvite;
```

```
Kathaṃ putta amocesi, kūṭapāsamha luddako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§120.</p>

```
Bhaṇaṃ kaṇṇasukhaṃ vācaṃ, hadayaṅgaṃ hadayassitaṃ;
```

```
Subhāsitāhi vācāhi, cittako maṃ amocayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§121.</p>

```
Bhaṇaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0325" /> kaṇṇasukhaṃ vācaṃ, hadayaṅgaṃ hadayassitaṃ;
```

```
Subhāsitāhi <pb ed="T" n="1.0431" /> vācāhi, sutanā maṃ amocayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§122.</p>

```
Sutvā kaṇṇasukhaṃ vācaṃ, hadayaṅgaṃ hadayassitaṃ;
```

```
Subhāsitāni sutvāna, luddako maṃ amocayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§123.</p>

```
Evaṃ ānandito hotu, saha dārehi luddako;
```

```
Yathā mayajja nandāma, disvā rohaṇamāgataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§124.</p>

```
Nanu tvaṃ avaca <note>avacā (sī. pī.)</note> ludda, ‘‘migacammāni āhariṃ’’;
```

```
Atha kena nu vaṇṇena, migacammāni nāhari.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§125.</p>

```
