Āgamā ceva hatthatthaṃ, kūṭapāsañca so migo;
```

```
Abajjhi taṃ <note>abajjhi tañca (pī.)</note> migarājaṃ, tañca muttā upāsare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§126.</p>

```
Tassa me ahu saṃvego, abbhuto lomahaṃsano;
```

```
Imañcāhaṃ migaṃ haññe, ajja hissāmi jīvitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§127.</p>

```
Kīdisā te migā ludda, kīdisā dhammikā migā;
```

```
Kathaṃvaṇṇā kathaṃsīlā, bāḷhaṃ kho ne pasaṃsasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§128.</p>

```
Odātasiṅgā <pb ed="V" n="1.0245" /> sucivāḷā, jātarūpatacūpamā;
```

```
Pādā lohitakā tesaṃ, añjitakkhā manoramā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§129.</p>

```
Edisā te migā deva, edisā dhammikā migā;
```

```
Mātāpettibharā deva, na te so abhihārituṃ <note>abhihārayuṃ (ka. sī.), abhihārayiṃ (syā.), abhihārayaṃ (pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§130.</p>

```
Dammi nikkhasataṃ ludda, thūlañca maṇikuṇḍalaṃ;
```

```
Catussadañca <note>caturassañca (syā. ka.)</note> pallaṅkaṃ, umāpupphasarinnibhaṃ <note>ummāpupphasirinnibhaṃ (sī. syā. pī. ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§131.</p>

```
Dve <pb ed="T" n="1.0432" /> ca sādisiyo bhariyā, usabhañca gavaṃ sataṃ;
```

```
Dhammena rajjaṃ kāressaṃ, bahukāro mesi luddaka.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§132.</p>

```
Kasivāṇijjā <note>kasī vaṇijjā (sī. syā. pī.)</note> iṇadānaṃ, uñchācariyā ca luddaka;
```

```
Etena dāraṃ posehi, mā pāpaṃ akarī punāti <note>akarā punanti (ka. sī. pī.)</note>.
```

Rohaṇamigajātakaṃ <note>rohantamigajātakaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> pañcamaṃ.

#### 502. Cūḷahaṃsajātakaṃ (6)

<p rend="hangnum">§133.</p>

```
Ete <pb ed="M" n="1.0326" /> haṃsā pakkamanti, vakkaṅgā bhayameritā;
```

```
Harittaca hemavaṇṇa, kāmaṃ sumukha pakkama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§134.</p>

```
Ohāya maṃ ñātigaṇā, ekaṃ pāsavasaṃ gataṃ;
```

```
Anapekkhamānā <note>nāpekkhamānā (ka.)</note> gacchanti, kiṃ eso avahiyyasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§135.</p>

```
Pateva patataṃ seṭṭha, natthi baddhe sahāyatā <note>sahāyakā (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Mā anīghāya hāpesi, kāmaṃ sumukha pakkama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§136.</p>

```
Nāhaṃ ‘‘dukkhapareto’’ti <note>dukkhaparetopi (ka.)</note>, dhataraṭṭha tuvaṃ <note>tavaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> jahe;
```

```
Jīvitaṃ maraṇaṃ vā me, tayā saddhiṃ bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§137.</p>

```
Etadariyassa kalyāṇaṃ, yaṃ tvaṃ sumukha bhāsasi;
```

```
Tañca vīmaṃsamānohaṃ, ‘‘patatetaṃ’’ avassajiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§138.</p>

```
Apadena padaṃ yāti, antalikkhacaro <note>antalikkhe caro (sī. pī.)</note> dijo;
```

```
Ārā pāsaṃ na bujjhi tvaṃ, haṃsānaṃ pavaruttama <note>pavaruttamo (ka. sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§139.</p>

```
Yadā parābhavo hoti, poso jīvitasaṅkhaye;
```

```
Atha <pb ed="T" n="1.0433" /> jālañca pāsañca, āsajjāpi na bujjhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§140.</p>

```
Ete haṃsā pakkamanti, vakkaṅgā bhayameritā;
```

```
Harittaca hemavaṇṇa, tvaññeva <note>tvañca taṃ (sī.), tvañca (pī.)</note> avahiyyasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§141.</p>

```
Ete <pb ed="V" n="1.0246" /> bhutvā ca pitvā ca, pakkamanti vihaṅgamā;
```

```
Anapekkhamānā vakkaṅgā, tvaññeveko upāsasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§142.</p>

```
Kinnu tyāyaṃ <note>tāyaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> dijo hoti, mutto baddhaṃ upāsasi;
```

```
Ohāya sakuṇā yanti, kiṃ eko avahiyyasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§143.</p>

```
Rājā me so dijo mitto, sakhā pāṇasamo ca me;
```

```
Neva naṃ vijahissāmi, yāva kālassa pariyāyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§144.</p>

```
Yo ca tvaṃ sakhino hetu, pāṇaṃ cajitumicchasi;
```

```
So te sahāyaṃ muñcāmi, hotu rājā tavānugo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§145.</p>

```
Evaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0327" /> luddaka nandassu, saha sabbehi ñātibhi;
```

```
Yathāhamajja nandāmi, disvā muttaṃ dijādhipaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§146.</p>

```
Kaccinnu bhoto kusalaṃ, kacci bhoto anāmayaṃ;
```

```
Kacci raṭṭhamidaṃ phītaṃ, dhammena manusāsasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§147.</p>

```
Kusalañceva me haṃsa, atho haṃsa anāmayaṃ;
```

```
Atho raṭṭhamidaṃ phītaṃ, dhammena manusāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§148.</p>

```
Kacci bhoto amaccesu, doso koci na vijjati;
```

```
Kacci ārā amittā te, chāyā dakkhiṇatoriva.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§149.</p>

```
Athopi me amaccesu, doso koci na vijjati;
```

```
Atho <pb ed="T" n="1.0434" /> ārā amittā me, chāyā dakkhiṇatoriva.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§150.</p>

```
Kacci te sādisī bhariyā, assavā piyabhāṇinī;
```

```
Puttarūpayasūpetā, tava chandavasānugā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§151.</p>

```
Atho me sādisī bhariyā, assavā piyabhāṇinī;
```

```
Puttarūpayasūpetā, mama chandavasānugā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§152.</p>

```
Kacci te bahavo puttā, sujātā raṭṭhavaḍḍhana;
```

```
Paññājavena sampannā, sammodanti tato tato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§153.</p>

```
Satameko ca me puttā, dhataraṭṭha mayā sutā;
```

```
Tesaṃ tvaṃ kiccamakkhāhi, nāvarujjhanti <note>nāvarajjhanti (ka. sī. pī.)</note> te vaco.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§154.</p>

```
Upapannopi ce hoti, jātiyā vinayena vā;
```

```
Atha pacchā kurute yogaṃ, kicche <note>kicce (sī. syā. pī.)</note> āpāsu <note>āvāsu (syā.), āpadāsu (ka.)</note> sīdati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§155.</p>

```
Tassa saṃhīrapaññassa, vivaro jāyate mahā;
```

```
Rattimandhova <note>nattamandhova (sī. pī.)</note> rūpāni, thūlāni manupassati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§156.</p>

```
Asāre <pb ed="V" n="1.0247" /> sārayogaññū, matiṃ na tveva vindati;
```

```
Sarabhova giriduggasmiṃ, antarāyeva sīdati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§157.</p>

```
Hīnajaccopi ce hoti, uṭṭhātā dhitimā naro;
```

```
Ācārasīlasampanno, nise aggīva bhāsati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§158.</p>

```
Etaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0328" /> me upamaṃ katvā, putte vijjāsu vācaya <note>ṭhāpasa (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Saṃvirūḷhetha medhāvī, khette bījaṃva <note>khettabījaṃva (sī. pī.)</note> vuṭṭhiyāti.
```

Cūḷahaṃsajātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 503. Sattigumbajātakaṃ (7)

<p rend="hangnum">§159.</p>

```
Migaluddo <pb ed="T" n="1.0435" /> mahārājā, pañcālānaṃ rathesabho;
```

```
Nikkhanto saha senāya, ogaṇo vanamāgamā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§160.</p>

```
Tatthaddasā araññasmiṃ, takkarānaṃ kuṭiṃ kataṃ;
```

```
Tassā <note>tasmā (syā. pī. ka.)</note> kuṭiyā nikkhamma, suvo luddāni bhāsati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§161.</p>

```
Sampannavāhano poso, yuvā sammaṭṭhakuṇḍalo <note>kuṇḍalī (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Sobhati lohituṇhīso, divā sūriyova bhāsati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§162.</p>

```
Majjhanhike <note>majjhantike (sabbattha)</note> sampatike, sutto rājā sasārathi;
```

```
Handassābharaṇaṃ sabbaṃ, gaṇhāma sāhasā <note>sahasā (sī. syā. pī.)</note> mayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§163.</p>

```
Nisīthepi raho dāni, sutto rājā sasārathi;
```

```
Ādāya vatthaṃ maṇikuṇḍalañca, hantvāna sākhāhi avattharāma.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§164.</p>

```
Kinnu ummattarūpova, sattigumba pabhāsasi;
```

```
Durāsadā hi rājāno, aggi pajjalito yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§165.</p>

```
Atha tvaṃ patikolamba, matto thullāni gajjasi;
```

```
Mātari mayhaṃ naggāya, kinnu tvaṃ vijigucchase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§166.</p>

```
Uṭṭhehi samma taramāno, rathaṃ yojehi sārathi;
```

```
Sakuṇo me na ruccati, aññaṃ gacchāma assamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§167.</p>

```
Yutto ratho mahārāja, yutto ca balavāhano;
```

```
Adhitiṭṭha mahārāja, aññaṃ gacchāma assamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§168.</p>

```
Ko <pb ed="T" n="1.0436" /> numeva gatā <note>kva nu’me’pagatā (?)</note> sabbe, ye asmiṃ paricārakā;
```

```
Esa gacchati pañcālo, mutto tesaṃ adassanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§169.</p>

```
Kodaṇḍakāni <pb ed="V" n="1.0248" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0329" /> gaṇhatha, sattiyo tomarāni ca;
```

```
Esa gacchati pañcālo, mā vo muñcittha jīvataṃ <note>jīvitaṃ (bahūsu)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§170.</p>

```
Athāparo paṭinandittha, suvo lohitatuṇḍako;
```

```
Svāgataṃ te mahārāja, atho te adurāgataṃ;
```

```
Issarosi anuppatto, yaṃ idhatthi pavedaya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§171.</p>

```
Tindukāni piyālāni, madhuke kāsumāriyo;
```

```
Phalāni khuddakappāni, bhuñja rāja varaṃ varaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§172.</p>

```
Idampi pānīyaṃ sītaṃ, ābhataṃ girigabbharā;
```

```
Tato piva mahārāja, sace tvaṃ abhikaṅkhasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§173.</p>

```
Araññaṃ uñchāya gatā, ye asmiṃ paricārakā;
```

```
Sayaṃ uṭṭhāya gaṇhavho, hatthā me natthi dātave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§174.</p>

```
Bhaddako vatayaṃ pakkhī, dijo paramadhammiko;
```

```
Atheso itaro pakkhī, suvo luddāni bhāsati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§175.</p>

```
‘‘Etaṃ hanatha bandhatha, mā vo muñcittha jīvataṃ’’;
```

```
Iccevaṃ vilapantassa, sotthiṃ <note>sotthī (syā.)</note> pattosmi assamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§176.</p>

```
Bhātarosma mahārāja, sodariyā ekamātukā;
```

```
Ekarukkhasmiṃ saṃvaḍḍhā, nānākhettagatā ubho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§177.</p>

```
Sattigumbo ca corānaṃ, ahañca isīnaṃ idha;
```

```
Asataṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0437" /> so, sataṃ ahaṃ, tena dhammena no vinā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§178.</p>

```
Tattha vadho ca bandho ca, nikatī vañcanāni ca;
```

```
Ālopā sāhasākārā, tāni so tattha sikkhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§179.</p>

```
Idha saccañca dhammo ca, ahiṃsā saṃyamo damo;
```

```
Āsanūdakadāyīnaṃ, aṅke vaddhosmi bhāradha <note>bhārata (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§180.</p>

```
Yaṃ yañhi rāja bhajati, santaṃ vā yadi vā asaṃ;
```

```
Sīlavantaṃ visīlaṃ vā, vasaṃ tasseva gacchati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§181.</p>

```
Yādisaṃ kurute mittaṃ, yādisaṃ cūpasevati;
```

```
Sopi tādisako hoti, sahavāso hi <note>sahavāsopi (syā. ka.)</note> tādiso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§182.</p>

```
Sevamāno <pb ed="M" n="1.0330" /> sevamānaṃ, samphuṭṭho samphusaṃ paraṃ;
```

```
Saro diddho kalāpaṃva, alittamupalimpati;
```

```
Upalepabhayā <note>upalimpabhayā (syā. ka.)</note> dhīro, neva pāpasakhā siyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§183.</p>

```
Pūtimacchaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0249" /> kusaggena, yo naro upanayhati;
```

```
Kusāpi pūti <note>pūtī (sī. pī.)</note> vāyanti, evaṃ bālūpasevanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§184.</p>

```
Tagarañca palāsena, yo naro upanayhati;
```

```
Pattāpi surabhi <note>surabhī (sī. syā. pī.)</note> vāyanti, evaṃ dhīrūpasevanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§185.</p>

```
Tasmā pattapuṭasseva <note>phalapuṭasseva (sī. pī.), palapuṭasseva (ka. aṭṭha.), palāsapuṭasseva (syā. ka.)</note>, ñatvā sampākamattano;
```

```
Asante nopaseveyya, sante seveyya paṇḍito;
```

```
Asanto nirayaṃ nenti, santo pāpenti suggatinti.
```

Sattigumbajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 504. Bhallātiyajātakaṃ (8)

<p rend="hangnum">§186.</p>

```
Bhallātiyo <pb ed="T" n="1.0438" /> <note>bhallāṭiyo (sī. pī.)</note> nāma ahosi rājā, raṭṭhaṃ pahāya migavaṃ acāri so;
```

```
Agamā girivaraṃ gandhamādanaṃ, supupphitaṃ <note>sampupphitaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> kimpurisānuciṇṇaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§187.</p>

```
Sāḷūrasaṅghañca nisedhayitvā, dhanuṃ <note>dhanu (sī. syā. pī.)</note> kalāpañca so nikkhipitvā;
```

```
Upāgami vacanaṃ vattukāmo, yatthaṭṭhitā kimpurisā ahesuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§188.</p>

```
Himaccaye hemavatāya tīre, kimidhaṭṭhitā mantayavho abhiṇhaṃ;
```

```
Pucchāmi vo mānusadehavaṇṇe, kathaṃ nu <note>kathaṃ vo (sī. syā. pī.)</note> jānanti manussaloke.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§189.</p>

```
Mallaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0331" /> giriṃ paṇḍarakaṃ tikūṭaṃ, sītodakā <note>sītodiyā (sī. pī.), sītodikā (?)</note> anuvicarāma najjo;
```

```
Migā manussāva nibhāsavaṇṇā, jānanti no kimpurisāti ludda.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§190.</p>

```
Sukiccharūpaṃ paridevayavho <note>paridevathavho (?) moggallānabyākaraṇe 6.38 suttaṃ</note>, āliṅgito cāsi piyo piyāya;
```

```
Pucchāmi vo mānusadehavaṇṇe, kimidha vane rodatha appatītā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§191.</p>

```
Sukiccharūpaṃ paridevayavho, āliṅgito cāsi piyo piyāya;
```

```
Pucchāmi vo mānusadehavaṇṇe, kimidha vane vilapatha appatītā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§192.</p>

```
Sukiccharūpaṃ paridevayavho, āliṅgito cāsi piyo piyāya;
```

```
Pucchāmi vo mānusadehavaṇṇe, kimidha <pb ed="T" n="1.0439" /> vane socatha appatītā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§193.</p>

```
Mayekarattaṃ <note>rattiṃ (pī.)</note> vippavasimha ludda, akāmakā aññamaññaṃ sarantā;
```

```
Tamekarattaṃ anutappamānā, socāma ‘‘sā ratti punaṃ na hessati’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§194.</p>

```
Yamekarattaṃ anutappathetaṃ, dhanaṃ va naṭṭhaṃ pitaraṃ va petaṃ;
```

```
Pucchāmi vo mānusadehavaṇṇe, kathaṃ vinā vāsamakappayittha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§195.</p>

```
Yamimaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0250" /> <note>yayimaṃ (ka. sī.)</note> nadiṃ passasi sīghasotaṃ, nānādumacchādanaṃ selakūlaṃ <note>dumacchadanaṃ selakūṭaṃ (sī. pī.), dumasañchannaṃ selakūlaṃ (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Taṃ me piyo uttari vassakāle, mamañca <pb ed="T" n="1.0440" /> maññaṃ anubandhatīti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§196.</p>

```
Ahañca <pb ed="M" n="1.0332" /> aṅkolakamocināmi, atimuttakaṃ sattaliyothikañca;
```

```
‘‘Piyo ca me hehiti mālabhārī, ahañca naṃ mālinī ajjhupessaṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§197.</p>

```
Ahañcidaṃ kuravakamocināmi, uddālakā pāṭalisindhuvārakā <note>sindhuvāritā (syā. pī. ka.)</note>;
```

```
‘‘Piyo ca me hehiti mālabhārī, ahañca naṃ mālinī ajjhupessaṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§198.</p>

```
Ahañca sālassa supupphitassa, oceyya pupphāni karomi mālaṃ;
```

```
‘‘Piyo ca me hehiti mālabhārī, ahañca naṃ mālinī ajjhupessaṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§199.</p>

```
Ahañca sālassa supupphitassa, oceyya pupphāni karomi bhāraṃ;
```

```
Idañca no hehiti santharatthaṃ, yatthajjimaṃ <note>yatthajjamaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> viharissāma <note>viharissāmu (pī.)</note> rattiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§200.</p>

```
Ahañca kho agaḷuṃ <note>aggalu (syā. ka.), akaluṃ (pī.)</note> candanañca, silāya piṃsāmi pamattarūpā;
```

```
‘‘Piyo ca me hehiti rositaṅgo, ahañca <pb ed="T" n="1.0441" /> naṃ rositā ajjhupessaṃ’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§201.</p>

```
Athāgamā salilaṃ sīghasotaṃ, nudaṃ sāle salaḷe kaṇṇikāre;
```

```
Āpūratha <note>apūratha (sī. pī.), āpūrathe (syā.)</note> tena muhuttakena, sāyaṃ nadī āsi mayā suduttarā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§202.</p>

```
Ubhosu tīresu mayaṃ tadā ṭhitā, sampassantā ubhayo aññamaññaṃ;
```

```
Sakimpi rodāma sakiṃ hasāma, kicchena no āgamā <note>agamā (sī. syā. pī.)</note> saṃvarī sā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§203.</p>

```
Pātova <pb ed="M" n="1.0333" /> <note>pāto ca (sī. syā. pī.)</note> kho uggate sūriyamhi, catukkaṃ nadiṃ uttariyāna ludda;
```

```
Āliṅgiyā aññamaññaṃ mayaṃ ubho, sakimpi rodāma sakiṃ hasāma.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§204.</p>

```
Tīhūnakaṃ sattasatāni ludda, yamidha mayaṃ vippavasimha pubbe;
```

```
Vassekimaṃ <note>vāsekimaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> jīvitaṃ bhūmipāla, ko nīdha kantāya vinā vaseyya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§205.</p>

```
Āyuñca vo kīvatako nu samma, sacepi jānātha vadetha āyuṃ;
```

```
Anussavā vuḍḍhato āgamā vā, akkhātha <pb ed="T" n="1.0442" /> me taṃ avikampamānā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§206.</p>

```
Āyuñca no vassasahassaṃ ludda, na cantarā pāpako atthi rogo;
```

```
Appañca <note>appaṃva (syā. ka.)</note> dukkhaṃ sukhameva bhiyyo, avītarāgā vijahāma jīvitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§207.</p>

```
Idañca sutvāna amānusānaṃ, bhallātiyo ittara jīvitanti;
```

```
Nivattatha na migavaṃ acari, adāsi dānāni abhuñji bhoge.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§208.</p>

```
Idañca sutvāna amānusānaṃ, sammodatha mā kalahaṃ akattha;
```

```
Mā vo tapī attakammāparādho, yathāpi te kimpurisekarattaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§209.</p>

```
Idañca <pb ed="V" n="1.0251" /> sutvāna amānusānaṃ, sammodatha mā vivādaṃ akattha;
```

```
Mā vo tapī attakammāparādho, yathāpi te kimpurisekarattaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§210.</p>

```
Vividhaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0334" /> <note>vividha (sī. syā.)</note> adhimanā suṇomahaṃ, vacanapathaṃ tava atthasaṃhitaṃ;
```

```
Muñcaṃ <note>muñca (sī. pī.)</note> giraṃ nudaseva me daraṃ, samaṇa <pb ed="T" n="1.0443" /> sukhāvaha jīva me ciranti.
```

Bhallātiyajātakaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 505. Somanassajātakaṃ (9)

<p rend="hangnum">§211.</p>

```
Ko taṃ hiṃsati heṭheti, kiṃ <note>kinnu (pī. ka.)</note> dummano socasi appatīto;
```

```
Kassajja mātāpitaro rudantu, kvajja setu <note>ko nvejja seti (ka.), ko ajja setu (?)</note> nihato pathabyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§212.</p>

```
Tuṭṭhosmi deva tava dassanena, cirassaṃ passāmi taṃ bhūmipāla;
```

```
Ahiṃsako reṇumanuppavissa, puttena te heṭhayitosmi <note>pothayitosmi (ka.)</note> deva.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§213.</p>

```
Āyantu dovārikā khaggabandhā <note>khaggabaddhā (sī. pī.)</note>, kāsāviyā yantu <note>hantu (ka.)</note> antepurantaṃ;
```

```
Hantvāna taṃ somanassaṃ kumāraṃ, chetvāna sīsaṃ varamāharantu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§214.</p>

```
Pesitā rājino dūtā, kumāraṃ etadabravuṃ;
```

```
Issarena vitiṇṇosi, vadhaṃ pattosi khattiya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§215.</p>

```
Sa rājaputto paridevayanto, dasaṅguliṃ añjaliṃ paggahetvā;
```

```
Ahampi <pb ed="T" n="1.0444" /> icchāmi janinda daṭṭhuṃ, jīvaṃ maṃ netvā <note>jīvaṃ panetvā (sī. pī.)</note> paṭidassayetha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§216.</p>

```
Tassa taṃ vacanaṃ sutvā, rañño puttaṃ adassayuṃ;
```

```
Putto ca pitaraṃ disvā, dūratovajjhabhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§217.</p>

```
Āgacchuṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0335" /> <note>āgañchuṃ (sī.), āgañchu (pī.)</note> dovārikā khaggabandhā, kāsāviyā hantu mamaṃ janinda;
```

```
Akkhāhi me pucchito etamatthaṃ, aparādho ko nidha mamajja atthi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§218.</p>

```
Sāyañca pāto udakaṃ sajāti, aggiṃ sadā pāricaratappamatto;
```

```
Taṃ tādisaṃ saṃyataṃ brahmacāriṃ, kasmā tuvaṃ brūsi gahappatīti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§219.</p>

```
Tālā ca mūlā ca phalā ca deva, pariggahā vividhā santimassa;
```

```
Te rakkhati gopayatappamatto, <note>brāhmaṇo gahapati tena hoti (sī. syā. pī.)</note> tasmā ahaṃ brūmi gahappatīti <note>brāhmaṇo gahapati tena hoti (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§220.</p>

```
Saccaṃ kho etaṃ vadasi kumāra, pariggahā vividhā santimassa;
```

```
Te rakkhati gopayatappamatto, sa <note>natthi idaṃ sī. syā. pī. potthakesu</note> brāhmaṇo <pb ed="T" n="1.0445" /> gahapati tena hoti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§221.</p>

```
Suṇantu mayhaṃ parisā samāgatā, sanegamā jānapadā ca sabbe;
```

```
Bālāyaṃ bālassa vaco nisamma, ahetunā ghātayate maṃ <note>ghātayate (sī. pī.)</note> janindo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§222.</p>

```
Daḷhasmi <pb ed="V" n="1.0252" /> mūle visaṭe virūḷhe, dunnikkayo veḷu pasākhajāto;
```

```
Vandāmi pādāni tava <note>tavaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> janinda, anujāna maṃ pabbajissāmi deva.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§223.</p>

```
Bhuñjassu bhoge vipule kumāra, sabbañca te issariyaṃ dadāmi;
```

```
Ajjeva tvaṃ kurūnaṃ hohi rājā, mā pabbajī pabbajjā hi dukkhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§224.</p>

```
Kinnūdha <pb ed="M" n="1.0336" /> deva tavamatthi bhogā, pubbevahaṃ <note>pubbe cahaṃ (ka.)</note> devaloke ramissaṃ;
```

```
Rūpehi saddehi atho rasehi, gandhehi phassehi manoramehi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§225.</p>

```
Bhuttā ca me <note>bhuttā (sī. pī.)</note> bhogā tidivasmiṃ deva, parivāritā <note>paricāritā (ka.)</note> accharānaṃ gaṇena <note>accharāsaṃgaṇena (syā. pī. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Tuvañca <note>tavañca (sī. pī.)</note> bālaṃ paraneyyaṃ viditvā, na <pb ed="T" n="1.0446" /> tādise rājakule vaseyyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§226.</p>

```
Sacāhaṃ bālo paraneyyo asmi, ekāparādhaṃ <note>etāparādhaṃ (ka.)</note> khama putta mayhaṃ;
```

```
Punapi ce edisakaṃ bhaveyya, yathāmatiṃ somanassa karohi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§227.</p>

```
Anisamma kataṃ kammaṃ, anavatthāya cintitaṃ;
```

```
Bhesajjasseva vebhaṅgo, vipāko hoti pāpako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§228.</p>

```
Nisamma ca kataṃ kammaṃ, sammāvatthāya cintitaṃ;
```

```
Bhesajjasseva sampatti, vipāko hoti bhadrako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§229.</p>

```
Alaso gihī kāmabhogī na sādhu, asaññato pabbajito na sādhu;
```

```
Rājā na sādhu anisammakārī, yo paṇḍito kodhano taṃ na sādhu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§230.</p>

```
Nisamma khattiyo kayirā, nānisamma disampati;
```

```
Nisammakārino rāja, yaso kitti ca vaḍḍhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§231.</p>

```
Nisamma daṇḍaṃ paṇayeyya issaro, vegā kataṃ tappati bhūmipāla;
```

```
Sammāpaṇīdhī ca narassa atthā, anānutappā te bhavanti pacchā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§232.</p>

```
Anānutappāni <pb ed="M" n="1.0337" /> hi ye karonti, vibhajja <pb ed="T" n="1.0447" /> kammāyatanāni loke;
```

```
Viññuppasatthāni sukhudrayāni, bhavanti buddhānumatāni <note>vaddhānumatāni (sī. pī.)</note> tāni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§233.</p>

```
Āgacchuṃ dovārikā khaggabandhā, kāsāviyā hantu mamaṃ janinda;
```

```
Mātuñca <note>mātucca (pī.)</note> aṅkasmimahaṃ nisinno, ākaḍḍhito sahasā tehi deva.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§234.</p>

```
Kaṭukañhi sambādhaṃ sukicchaṃ <note>sukiccha (sī. pī.)</note> patto, madhurampi yaṃ jīvitaṃ laddha rāja;
```

```
Kicchenahaṃ ajja vadhā pamutto, pabbajjamevābhimanohamasmi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§235.</p>

```
Putto tavāyaṃ taruṇo sudhamme, anukampako somanasso kumāro;
```

```
Taṃ yācamāno na labhāmi svajja <note>sajja (sī. pī.)</note>, arahasi naṃ yācitave <note>yācituye (ka.)</note> tuvampi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§236.</p>

```
Ramassu <pb ed="V" n="1.0253" /> bhikkhācariyāya putta, nisamma dhammesu paribbajassu;
```

```
Sabbesu bhūtesu nidhāya daṇḍaṃ, anindito brahmamupehi ṭhānaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§237.</p>

```
Acchera <note>acchariya (sī. syā. pī.)</note> rūpaṃ vata yādisañca, dukkhitaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0448" /> maṃ dukkhāpayase sudhamme;
```

```
Yācassu puttaṃ iti vuccamānā, bhiyyova ussāhayase kumāraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§238.</p>

```
Ye vippamuttā anavajjabhogino <note>bhojino (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, parinibbutā lokamimaṃ caranti;
```

```
Tamariyamaggaṃ paṭipajjamānaṃ, na ussahe vārayituṃ kumāraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§239.</p>

```
Addhā <pb ed="M" n="1.0338" /> have sevitabbā sapaññā, bahussutā ye bahuṭhānacintino;
```

```
Yesāyaṃ sutvāna subhāsitāni, appossukkā vītasokā sudhammāti.
```

Somanassajātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 506. Campeyyajātakaṃ (10)

<p rend="hangnum">§240.</p>

```
Kā nu vijjurivābhāsi, osadhī viya tārakā;
```

```
Devatā nusi gandhabbī, na taṃ maññāmi mānusiṃ <note>mānusī (syā. ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§241.</p>

```
Namhi devī na gandhabbī, na mahārāja mānusī;
```

```
Nāgakaññāsmi bhaddante, atthenamhi idhāgatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§242.</p>

```
Vibbhantacittā kupitindriyāsi, nettehi te vārigaṇā savanti;
```

```
Kiṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0449" /> te naṭṭhaṃ kiṃ pana patthayānā, idhāgatā nāri tadiṅgha brūhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§243.</p>

```
Yamuggatejo uragoti cāhu, nāgoti naṃ āhu janā janinda;
```

```
Tamaggahī puriso jīvikattho, taṃ bandhanā muñca patī mameso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§244.</p>

```
Kathaṃ nvayaṃ balaviriyūpapanno, hatthatta <note>hatthattha (sī. syā. pī.)</note> māgacchi vanibbakassa;
```

```
Akkhāhi me nāgakaññe tamatthaṃ, kathaṃ vijānemu gahītanāgaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§245.</p>

```
Nagarampi nāgo bhasmaṃ kareyya, tathā hi so balaviriyūpapanno;
```

```
Dhammañca nāgo apacāyamāno, tasmā parakkamma tapo karoti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§246.</p>

```
Cātuddasiṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0339" /> pañcadasiṃ <note>pannarasiṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> ca rāja, catuppathe sammati nāgarājā;
```

```
Tamaggahī puriso jīvikattho, taṃ bandhanā muñca patī mameso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§247.</p>

```
Soḷasitthisahassāni, āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalā;
```

```
Vārigehasayā nārī <note>nāriyo (pī.)</note>, tāpi taṃ saraṇaṃ gatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§248.</p>

```
Dhammena <pb ed="T" n="1.0450" /> mocehi asāhasena, gāmena nikkhena gavaṃ satena;
```

```
Ossaṭṭhakāyo urago carātu, puññatthiko muñcatu bandhanasmā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§249.</p>

```
Dhammena <pb ed="V" n="1.0254" /> mocemi asāhasena, gāmena nikkhena gavaṃ satena;
```

```
Ossaṭṭhakāyo urago carātu, puññatthiko muñcatu bandhanasmā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§250.</p>

```
Dammi nikkhasataṃ ludda, thūlañca maṇikuṇḍalaṃ;
```

```
Catussadañca pallaṅkaṃ, umāpupphasarinnibhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§251.</p>

```
Dve ca sādisiyo bhariyā, usabhañca gavaṃ sataṃ;
```

```
Ossaṭṭhakāyo urago carātu, puññatthiko muñcatu bandhanasmā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§252.</p>

```
Vināpi dānā tava vacanaṃ janinda, muñcemu naṃ uragaṃ bandhanasmā;
```

```
Ossaṭṭhakāyo urago carātu, puññatthiko muñcatu bandhanasmā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§253.</p>

```
Mutto campeyyako nāgo, rājānaṃ etadabravi;
```

```
Namo te kāsirājatthu, namo te kāsivaḍḍhana;
```

```
Añjaliṃ te paggaṇhāmi, passeyyaṃ me nivesanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§254.</p>

```
Addhā <pb ed="T" n="1.0451" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0340" /> hi dubbissasametamāhu, yaṃ mānuso vissase amānusamhi;
```

```
Sace ca maṃ yācasi etamatthaṃ, dakkhemu te nāga nivesanāni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§255.</p>

```
Sacepi <note>sace hi (sī. pī. aṭṭha.)</note> vāto girimāvaheyya, cando ca suriyo ca chamā pateyyuṃ;
```

```
Sabbā ca najjo paṭisotaṃ vajeyyuṃ, na tvevahaṃ rāja musā bhaṇeyyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§256.</p>

```
Nabhaṃ phaleyya udadhīpi susse, saṃvaṭṭaye <note>saṃvaṭṭeyaṃ (sī. pī.), saṃvaṭṭeyya (syā. ka.)</note> bhūtadharā vasundharā;
```

```
Siluccayo meru samūlamuppate <note>mubbahe (sī. syā. pī. ka. aṭṭha.), muṭṭhahe (ka.)</note>, na tvevahaṃ rāja musā bhaṇeyyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§257.</p>

```
Addhā hi dubbissasametamāhu, yaṃ mānuso vissase amānusamhi;
```

```
Sace ca maṃ yācasi etamatthaṃ, dakkhemu te nāga nivesanāni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§258.</p>

```
Tumhe khottha ghoravisā uḷārā, mahātejā khippakopī ca hotha;
```

```
Maṃkāraṇā <note>mama kāraṇā (sī. syā. pī.)</note> bandhanasmā pamutto, arahasi no jānituye <note>jānitāye (sī.), jānitave (syā.), jānitaye (pī.)</note> katāni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§259.</p>

```
So <pb ed="T" n="1.0452" /> paccataṃ niraye ghorarūpe, mā kāyikaṃ sātamalattha kiñci;
```

```
Peḷāya baddho maraṇaṃ upetu, yo tādisaṃ kammakataṃ na jāne.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§260.</p>

```
Saccappaṭiññā <pb ed="M" n="1.0341" /> tavamesa hotu, akkodhano hohi anupanāhī;
```

```
Sabbañca te nāgakulaṃ supaṇṇā, aggiṃva gimhesu <note>gimhāsu (sī. syā. pī.)</note> vivajjayantu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§261.</p>

```
Anukampasī nāgakulaṃ janinda, mātā yathā suppiyaṃ ekaputtaṃ;
```

```
Ahañca te nāgakulena saddhiṃ, kāhāmi veyyāvaṭikaṃ uḷāraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§262.</p>

```
Yojentu ve rājarathe sucitte, kambojake assatare sudante;
```

```
Nāge ca yojentu suvaṇṇakappane, dakkhemu nāgassa nivesanāni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§263.</p>

```
Bherī <pb ed="V" n="1.0255" /> mudiṅgā <note>mutiṅgā (sī. pī.)</note> paṇavā ca saṅkhā, avajjayiṃsu uggasenassa rañño;
```

```
Pāyāsi rājā bahusobhamāno, purakkhato nārigaṇassa majjhe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§264.</p>

```
Suvaṇṇacitakaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0453" /> bhūmiṃ, addakkhi kāsivaḍḍhano;
```

```
Sovaṇṇamayapāsāde, veḷuriyaphalakatthate.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§265.</p>

```
Sa rājā pāvisi byamhaṃ, campeyyassa nivesanaṃ;
```

```
Ādiccavaṇṇasannibhaṃ, kaṃsavijju pabhassaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§266.</p>

```
Nānārukkhehi sañchannaṃ, nānāgandhasamīritaṃ;
```

```
So pāvekkhi kāsirājā, campeyyassa nivesanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§267.</p>

```
Paviṭṭhasmiṃ kāsiraññe, campeyyassa nivesanaṃ;
```

```
Dibbā tūriyā pavajjiṃsu, nāgakaññā ca naccisuṃ <note>naccayuṃ (sī. pī. ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§268.</p>

```
Taṃ nāgakaññā caritaṃ gaṇena, anvāruhī kāsirājā pasanno;
```

```
Nisīdi sovaṇṇamayamhi pīṭhe, sāpassaye <note>sopassaye (ka.)</note> candanasāralitte.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§269.</p>

```
So <pb ed="M" n="1.0342" /> tattha bhutvā ca atho ramitvā, campeyyakaṃ kāsirājā avoca;
```

```
Vimānaseṭṭhāni imāni tuyhaṃ, ādiccavaṇṇāni pabhassarāni;
```

```
Netādisaṃ atthi manussaloke, kiṃ patthayaṃ <note>kimatthiyaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> nāga tapo karosi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§270.</p>

```
Tā kambukāyūradharā suvatthā, vaṭṭaṅgulī tambatalūpapannā;
```

```
Paggayha <pb ed="T" n="1.0454" /> pāyenti anomavaṇṇā, netādisaṃ atthi manussaloke;
```

```
Kiṃ patthayaṃ nāga tapo karosi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§271.</p>

```
Najjo ca temā puthulomamacchā, āṭā <note>ādā (syā.), adā (pī.)</note> sakuntābhirudā sutitthā;
```

```
Netādisaṃ atthi manussaloke, kiṃ patthayaṃ nāga tapo karosi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§272.</p>

```
Koñcā mayūrā diviyā ca haṃsā, vaggussarā kokilā sampatanti;
```

```
Netādisaṃ atthi manussaloke, kiṃ patthayaṃ nāga tapo karosi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§273.</p>

```
Ambā ca sālā tilakā ca jambuyo, uddālakā pāṭaliyo ca phullā;
```

```
Netādisaṃ atthi manussaloke, kiṃ patthayaṃ nāga tapo karosi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§274.</p>

```
Imā ca te pokkharañño samantato, dibbā <note>dibyā (syā.), diviyā (pī.)</note> ca gandhā satataṃ pavāyanti;
```

```
Netādisaṃ atthi manussaloke, kiṃ patthayaṃ nāga tapo karosi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§275.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="M" n="1.0343" /> puttahetu na dhanassa hetu, na <pb ed="T" n="1.0455" /> āyuno cāpi <note>vāpi (sī. pī.)</note> janinda hetu;
```

```
Manussayoniṃ abhipatthayāno, tasmā parakkamma tapo karomi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§276.</p>

```
Tvaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0256" /> lohitakkho vihatantaraṃso, alaṅkato kappitakesamassu;
```

```
Surosito lohitacandanena, gandhabbarājāva disā pabhāsasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§277.</p>

```
Deviddhipattosi mahānubhāvo, sabbehi kāmehi samaṅgibhūto;
```

```
Pucchāmi taṃ nāgarājetamatthaṃ, seyyo ito kena manussaloko.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§278.</p>

```
Janinda nāññatra manussalokā, suddhī va saṃvijjati saṃyamo vā;
```

```
Ahañca laddhāna manussayoniṃ, kāhāmi jātimaraṇassa antaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§279.</p>

```
Addhā have sevitabbā sapaññā, bahussutā ye bahuṭhānacintino;
```

```
Nāriyo ca disvāna tuvañca nāga, kāhāmi puññāni anappakāni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§280.</p>

```
Addhā have sevitabbā sapaññā, bahussutā <pb ed="T" n="1.0456" /> ye bahuṭhānacintino;
```

```
Nāriyo ca disvāna mamañca rāja, karohi puññāni anappakāni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§281.</p>

```
Idañca me jātarūpaṃ pahūtaṃ, rāsī suvaṇṇassa ca tālamattā;
```

```
<note>ito haritvā sovaṇṇagharāni kāraya, rūpiyassa ca pākāraṃ karontu (sī. syā.) ito haritvā sovaṇṇagharāni, [kāraya] rūpiyassa ca pākāraṃ karontu (pī.)</note> Ito haritvāna suvaṇṇagharāni, karassu rūpiyapākāraṃ karontu <note>ito haritvā sovaṇṇagharāni kāraya, rūpiyassa ca pākāraṃ karontu (sī. syā.) ito haritvā sovaṇṇagharāni, [kāraya] rūpiyassa ca pākāraṃ karontu (pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§282.</p>

```
Muttā <pb ed="M" n="1.0344" /> ca <note>muttānañca (sī. syā.)</note> vāhasahassāni pañca, veḷuriyamissāni ito haritvā;
```

```
Antepure bhūmiyaṃ santharantu, nikkaddamā hehiti nīrajā ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§283.</p>

```
Etādisaṃ āvasa rājaseṭṭha, vimānaseṭṭhaṃ bahu sobhamānaṃ;
```

```
Bārāṇasiṃ nagaraṃ iddhaṃ phītaṃ, rajjañca kārehi anomapaññāti.
```

Campeyyajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

#### 507. Mahāpalobhanajātakaṃ (11)

<p rend="hangnum">§284.</p>

```
Brahmalokā cavitvāna, devaputto mahiddhiko;
```

```
Rañño putto udapādi, sabbakāmasamiddhisu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§285.</p>

```
Kāmā <pb ed="T" n="1.0457" /> vā kāmasaññā vā, brahmaloke na vijjati;
```

```
Svāssu <note>yvāssa (sī.)</note> tāyeva saññāya, kāmehi vijigucchatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§286.</p>

```
Tassa cantepure āsi, jhānāgāraṃ sumāpitaṃ;
```

```
So tattha paṭisallīno <note>paṭisallāno (ka.)</note>, eko rahasi jhāyatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§287.</p>

```
Sa rājā paridevesi, puttasokena aṭṭito;
```

```
Ekaputto cayaṃ mayhaṃ, na ca kāmāni bhuñjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§288.</p>

```
Ko nu khvettha <note>khettha (sī. pī.)</note> upāyo so, ko vā jānāti kiñcanaṃ;
```

```
Yo <note>ko (sī. pī.)</note> me puttaṃ palobheyya, yathā kāmāni patthaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§289.</p>

```
Ahu <pb ed="V" n="1.0257" /> kumārī tattheva, vaṇṇarūpasamāhitā;
```

```
Kusalā naccagītassa, vādite ca padakkhiṇā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§290.</p>

```
Sā tattha upasaṅkamma, rājānaṃ etadabravi;
```

```
Ahaṃ kho naṃ palobheyyaṃ, sace bhattā bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§291.</p>

```
Taṃ tathāvādiniṃ rājā, kumāriṃ etadabravi;
```

```
Tvaññeva naṃ palobhehi, tava bhattā bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§292.</p>

```
Sā <pb ed="M" n="1.0345" /> ca antepuraṃ gantvā, bahuṃ kāmupasaṃhitaṃ;
```

```
Hadayaṅgamā pemanīyā, citrā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§293.</p>

```
Tassā ca gāyamānāya, saddaṃ sutvāna nāriyā;
```

```
Kāmacchandassa uppajji, janaṃ so paripucchatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§294.</p>

```
Kasseso saddo ko vā so, bhaṇati uccāvacaṃ bahuṃ;
```

```
Hadayaṅgamaṃ pemanīyaṃ, aho <note>atho (sī. pī.)</note> kaṇṇasukhaṃ mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§295.</p>

```
Esā <pb ed="T" n="1.0458" /> kho pamadā deva, khiḍḍā esā anappikā <note>anappakā (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Sace tvaṃ kāme bhuñjeyya, bhiyyo bhiyyo chādeyyu taṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§296.</p>

```
Iṅgha āgacchatorena <note>āgacchatorenaṃ (ka.) āgacchatu + orena</note>, avidūramhi gāyatu;
```

```
Assamassa samīpamhi, santike mayhaṃ gāyatu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§297.</p>

```
Tirokuṭṭamhi gāyitvā, jhānāgāramhi pāvisi;
```

```
Bandhi naṃ <note>bhandhituṃ (syā. ka.)</note> anupubbena, āraññamiva kuñjaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§298.</p>

```
Tassa <note>tassā (syā.)</note> kāmarasaṃ ñatvā, issādhammo ajāyatha;
```

```
‘‘Ahameva kāme bhuñjeyyaṃ, mā añño puriso ahu’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§299.</p>

```
Tato asiṃ gahetvāna, purise hantuṃ upakkami;
```

```
Ahameveko bhuñjissaṃ, mā añño puriso siyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§300.</p>

```
Tato jānapadā sabbe, vikkandiṃsu samāgatā;
```

```
Putto tyāyaṃ mahārāja, janaṃ heṭhetyadūsakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§301.</p>

```
Tañca rājā vivāhesi <note>nivāhesi (syā.), vihāhesi (pī.)</note>, samhā raṭṭhā ca <note>raṭṭhāto (sī. pī.), raṭṭhato (ka.)</note> khattiyo;
```

```
Yāvatā vijitaṃ mayhaṃ, na te vatthabba <note>vattabba (sī. pī.)</note> tāvade.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§302.</p>

```
Tato so bhariyamādāya, samuddaṃ upasaṅkami;
```

```
Paṇṇasālaṃ karitvāna, vanamuñchāya pāvisi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§303.</p>

```
Athettha <pb ed="V" n="1.0258" /> isi māgacchi, samuddaṃ uparūpari;
```

```
So tassa gehaṃ pāvekkhi, bhattakāle upaṭṭhite.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§304.</p>

```
Tañca <pb ed="M" n="1.0346" /> bhariyā palobhesi, passa yāva sudāruṇaṃ;
```

```
Cuto so brahmacariyamhā, iddhiyā parihāyatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§305.</p>

```
Rājaputto <pb ed="T" n="1.0459" /> ca uñchāto, vanamūlaphalaṃ bahuṃ;
```

```
Sāyaṃ kājena <note>kācena (pī.)</note> ādāya, assamaṃ upasaṅkami.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§306.</p>

```
Isī ca khattiyaṃ disvā, samuddaṃ upasaṅkami;
```

```
‘‘Vehāyasaṃ gamissa’’nti, sīdate so mahaṇṇave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§307.</p>

```
Khattiyo ca isiṃ disvā, sīdamānaṃ mahaṇṇave;
```

```
Tasseva anukampāya, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§308.</p>

```
Abhijjamāne vārismiṃ, sayaṃ āgamma iddhiyā;
```

```
Missībhāvitthiyā gantvā, saṃsīdasi mahaṇṇave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§309.</p>

```
Āvaṭṭanī mahāmāyā, brahmacariyavikopanā;
```

```
Sīdanti naṃ viditvāna, ārakā parivajjaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§310.</p>

```
Analā mudusambhāsā, duppūrā tā nadīsamā;
```

```
Sīdanti naṃ viditvāna, ārakā parivajjaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§311.</p>

```
Yaṃ etā upasevanti, chandasā vā dhanena vā;
```

```
Jātavedova saṃ ṭhānaṃ, khippaṃ anudahanti naṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§312.</p>

```
Khattiyassa vaco sutvā, isissa nibbidā ahu;
```

```
Laddhā porāṇakaṃ maggaṃ, gacchate so vihāyasaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§313.</p>

```
Khattiyo ca isiṃ disvā, gacchamānaṃ vihāyasaṃ;
```

```
Saṃvegaṃ alabhī dhīro, pabbajjaṃ samarocayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§314.</p>

```
Tato so pabbajitvāna, kāmarāgaṃ virājayi;
```

```
Kāmarāgaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0460" /> virājetvā, brahmalokūpago ahūti.
```

Mahāpalobhanajātakaṃ ekādasamaṃ.

#### 508. Pañcapaṇḍitajātakaṃ (12)

<p rend="hangnum">§315.</p>

```
Pañca <pb ed="M" n="1.0347" /> paṇḍitā samāgatāttha, pañhā me paṭibhāti taṃ suṇātha;
```

```
Nindiyamatthaṃ pasaṃsiyaṃ vā, kassevāvikareyya <note>kassa vāvīkareyya (ka.)</note> guyhamatthaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§316.</p>

```
Tvaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0259" /> āvikarohi bhūmipāla, bhattā bhārasaho tuvaṃ vade taṃ;
```

```
Tava chandarucīni <note>chandañca ruciñca (sī. pī.)</note> sammasitvā, atha vakkhanti janinda pañca dhīrā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§317.</p>

```
Yā sīlavatī anaññatheyyā <note>anaññadheyyā (sī. pī.)</note>, bhattucchandavasānugā (piyā) <note>( ) natthi sī. pī. potthakesu</note> manāpā;
```

```
Nindiyamatthaṃ pasaṃsiyaṃ vā, bhariyāyāvikareyya <note>bhariyāya vāvīkareyya (ka.)</note> guyhamatthaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§318.</p>

```
Yo kicchagatassa āturassa, saraṇaṃ hoti gatī parāyanañca;
```

```
Nindiyamatthaṃ pasaṃsiyaṃ vā, sakhino vāvikareyya guyhamatthaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§319.</p>

```
Jeṭṭho <pb ed="T" n="1.0461" /> <note>yo jeṭṭho (syā.)</note> atha majjhimo kaniṭṭho, yo <note>so (sī. syā. pī.)</note> ce sīlasamāhito ṭhitatto;
```

```
Nindiyamatthaṃ pasaṃsiyaṃ vā, bhātu vāvīkareyya guyhamatthaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§320.</p>

```
Yo ve pituhadayassa paddhagū <note>patthagū (syā.), pattagū (ka.)</note>, anujāto pitaraṃ anomapañño;
```

```
Nindiyamatthaṃ pasaṃsiyaṃ vā, puttassāvikareyya <note>puttassa vāvīkareyya (ka.)</note> guyhamatthaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§321.</p>

```
Mātā <pb ed="M" n="1.0348" /> dvipadājanindaseṭṭha, yā naṃ <note>yo taṃ (sī. pī.)</note> poseti chandasā piyena;
```

```
Nindiyamatthaṃ pasaṃsiyaṃ vā, mātuyāvīkareyya <note>mātuyā vāvīkareyya (ka.)</note> guyhamatthaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§322.</p>

```
Guyhassa hi guyhameva sādhu, na hi guyhassa pasatthamāvikammaṃ;
```

```
Anipphannatā <note>anipphādāya (sī. pī.), anipphannatāya (syā.), ā nipphādā (?)</note> saheyya dhīro, nipphannova <note>nipphannattho (sī. pī.), nipphannatthova (syā.)</note> yathāsukhaṃ bhaṇeyya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§323.</p>

```
Kiṃ tvaṃ vimanosi rājaseṭṭha, dvipadajaninda <note>dipadinda (sī. syā. pī.)</note> vacanaṃ suṇoma metaṃ <note>netaṃ (sī. pī.), tetaṃ (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Kiṃ cintayamāno dummanosi, nūna deva aparādho atthi mayhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§324.</p>

```
‘‘Paṇhe <pb ed="T" n="1.0462" /> <note>pañño (sī. pī.), pañhe (syā.), panhe (ka.)</note> vajjho mahosadho’’ti, āṇatto me vadhāya bhūripañño;
```

```
Taṃ cintayamāno dummanosmi, na hi devī aparādho atthi tuyhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§325.</p>

```
Abhidosagato dāni ehisi, kiṃ sutvā kiṃ saṅkate mano te;
```

```
Ko te kimavoca bhūripañña, iṅgha vacanaṃ suṇoma brūhi metaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§326.</p>

```
‘‘Paṇhe vajjho mahosadho’’ti, yadi te mantayitaṃ janinda dosaṃ;
```

```
Bhariyāya rahogato asaṃsi, guyhaṃ pātukataṃ sutaṃ mametaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§327.</p>

```
Yaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0349" /> sālavanasmiṃ senako, pāpakammaṃ akāsi asabbhirūpaṃ;
```

```
Sakhinova rahogato asaṃsi, guyhaṃ pātukataṃ sutaṃ mametaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§328.</p>

```
Pukkusa <note>pakkusa (ka.) jā. 1.7.41 paṇṇajātake passitabbaṃ</note> purisassa te janinda, uppanno rogo arājayutto;
```

```
Bhātuñca <note>bhātucca (sī. pī.), bhātuva (syā.)</note> rahogato asaṃsi, guyhaṃ pātukataṃ sutaṃ mametaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§329.</p>

```
Ābādhoyaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0463" /> asabbhirūpo, kāmindo <note>kāvindo (sī. pī.)</note> naradevena phuṭṭho;
```

```
Puttassa rahogato asaṃsi, guyhaṃ pātukataṃ sutaṃ mametaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§330.</p>

```
Aṭṭhavaṅkaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0260" /> maṇiratanaṃ uḷāraṃ, sakko te adadā pitāmahassa;
```

```
Devindassa gataṃ tadajja hatthaṃ <note>devindassa tadajja hatthagataṃ (ka.)</note>, mātuñca rahogato asaṃsi;
```

```
Guyhaṃ pātukataṃ sutaṃ mametaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§331.</p>

```
Guyhassa hi guyhameva sādhu, na hi guyhassa pasatthamāvikammaṃ;
```

```
Anipphannatā saheyya dhīro, nipphannova yathāsukhaṃ bhaṇeyya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§332.</p>

```
Na guyhamatthaṃ vivareyya, rakkheyya naṃ yathā nidhiṃ;
```

```
Na hi pātukato sādhu, guyho attho pajānatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§333.</p>

```
Thiyā guyhaṃ na saṃseyya, amittassa ca paṇḍito;
```

```
Yo cāmisena saṃhīro, hadayattheno ca yo naro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§334.</p>

```
Guyhamatthaṃ asambuddhaṃ, sambodhayati yo naro;
```

```
Mantabhedabhayā tassa, dāsabhūto titikkhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§335.</p>

```
Yāvanto <pb ed="M" n="1.0350" /> purisassatthaṃ, guyhaṃ jānanti mantinaṃ;
```

```
Tāvanto <pb ed="T" n="1.0464" /> tassa ubbegā, tasmā guyhaṃ na vissaje.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§336.</p>

```
Vivicca bhāseyya divā rahassaṃ, rattiṃ giraṃ nātivelaṃ pamuñce;
```

```
Upassutikā hi suṇanti mantaṃ, tasmā manto khippamupeti bhedanti.
```

Pañcapaṇḍitajātakaṃ dvādasamaṃ.

#### 509. Hatthipālajātakaṃ (13)

<p rend="hangnum">§337.</p>

```
Cirassaṃ vata passāma, brāhmaṇaṃ devavaṇṇinaṃ;
```

```
Mahājaṭaṃ khāridharaṃ <note>bhāradharaṃ (pī.)</note>, paṅkadantaṃ rajassiraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§338.</p>

```
Cirassaṃ vata passāma, isiṃ dhammaguṇe rataṃ;
```

```
Kāsāyavatthavasanaṃ, vākacīraṃ paṭicchadaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§339.</p>

```
Āsanaṃ udakaṃ pajjaṃ, paṭigaṇhātu no bhavaṃ;
```

```
Agghe bhavantaṃ pucchāma, agghaṃ kurutu no bhavaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§340.</p>

```
Adhicca vede pariyesa vittaṃ, putte gahe <note>gehe (sī. syā. pī.)</note> tāta patiṭṭhapetvā;
```

```
Gandhe rase paccanubhuyya <note>paccanubhotva (syā.), paccanubhutva (pī.)</note> sabbaṃ, araññaṃ sādhu muni so pasattho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§341.</p>

```
Vedā na saccā na ca vittalābho, na puttalābhena jaraṃ vihanti;
```

```
Gandhe <pb ed="T" n="1.0465" /> rase muccana <note>muñcana (sī. ka.)</note> māhu santo, sakammunā <note>sakammanā (sī. pī.)</note> hoti phalūpapatti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§342.</p>

```
Addhā hi saccaṃ vacanaṃ tavetaṃ, sakammunā hoti phalūpapatti;
```

```
Jiṇṇā ca mātāpitaro tavīme <note>taveme (sī.), tava yime (syā. pī.)</note>, passeyyuṃ taṃ vassasataṃ arogaṃ <note>arogyaṃ (syā. ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§343.</p>

```
Yassassa <pb ed="V" n="1.0261" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0351" /> sakkhī maraṇena rāja, jarāya mettī naravīraseṭṭha;
```

```
Yo cāpi jaññā na marissaṃ kadāci, passeyyuṃ taṃ vassasataṃ arogaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§344.</p>

```
Yathāpi nāvaṃ puriso dakamhi, ereti ce naṃ upaneti tīraṃ;
```

```
Evampi byādhī satataṃ jarā ca, upaneti maccaṃ <note>maccu (syā. pī.)</note> vasamantakassa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§345.</p>

```
Paṅko ca kāmā palipo ca kāmā, manoharā duttarā maccudheyyā;
```

```
Etasmiṃ paṅke palipe byasannā <note>visannā (syā. ka.)</note>, hīnattarūpā na taranti pāraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§346.</p>

```
Ayaṃ pure luddamakāsi kammaṃ, svāyaṃ gahīto na hi mokkhito me;
```

```
Orundhiyā <pb ed="T" n="1.0466" /> naṃ parirakkhissāmi, māyaṃ puna luddamakāsi kammaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§347.</p>

```
Gavaṃva <note>gāvaṃva (sī.)</note> naṭṭhaṃ puriso yathā vane, anvesatī <note>pariyesatī (sī. pī.)</note> rāja apassamāno;
```

```
Evaṃ naṭṭho esukārī mamattho, sohaṃ kathaṃ na gaveseyyaṃ rāja.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§348.</p>

```
Hiyyoti hiyyati <note>hīyoti hīyati (sī.)</note> poso, pareti parihāyati;
```

```
Anāgataṃ netamatthīti ñatvā, uppannachandaṃ ko panudeyya dhīro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§349.</p>

```
Passāmi vohaṃ daharaṃ <note>daharī (syā. pī. ka.)</note> kumāriṃ, mattūpamaṃ ketakapupphanettaṃ;
```

```
Abhuttabhoge <note>abhutva bhoge (syā. ka. aṭṭha.), abhutva bhoge (pī.), bhoge atutvā (ka.)</note> paṭhame vayasmiṃ, ādāya maccu vajate kumāriṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§350.</p>

```
Yuvā <pb ed="M" n="1.0352" /> sujāto sumukho sudassano, sāmo kusumbhaparikiṇṇamassu;
```

```
Hitvāna kāme paṭikacca <note>paṭigacca (sī.), paṭigaccha (syā. pī.)</note> gehaṃ, anujāna maṃ pabbajissāmi deva.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§351.</p>

```
Sākhāhi rukkho labhate samaññaṃ, pahīnasākhaṃ pana khāṇumāhu;
```

```
Pahīnaputtassa mamajja bhoti, vāseṭṭhi <pb ed="T" n="1.0467" /> bhikkhācariyāya kālo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§352.</p>

```
Aghasmi koñcāva yathā himaccaye, katāni <note>tantāni (sī. pī.)</note> jālāni padāliya <note>padāleyya (sī.)</note> haṃsā;
```

Gacchanti puttā ca patī ca mayhaṃ, sāhaṃ kathaṃ nānuvaje pajānaṃ.

<p rend="hangnum">§353.</p>

```
Ete bhutvā vamitvā ca, pakkamanti vihaṅgamā;
```

```
Ye ca bhutvāna vamiṃsu, te me hatthatta <note>hatthattha (sī. syā. pī.)</note> māgatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§354.</p>

```
Avamī brāhmaṇo kāme, so <note>te (sī. pī.)</note> tvaṃ paccāvamissasi;
```

```
Vantādo puriso rāja, na so hoti pasaṃsiyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§355.</p>

```
Paṅke ca <note>paṅkeva (sī. pī.)</note> posaṃ palipe byasannaṃ, balī yathā dubbalamuddhareyya;
```

```
Evampi maṃ tvaṃ udatāri bhoti, pañcāli gāthāhi subhāsitāhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§356.</p>

```
Idaṃ vatvā mahārājā, esukārī disampati;
```

```
Raṭṭhaṃ hitvāna pabbaji, nāgo chetvāva bandhanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§357.</p>

```
Rājā <pb ed="V" n="1.0262" /> ca pabbajjamarocayittha, raṭṭhaṃ pahāya naravīraseṭṭho;
```

```
Tuvampi no hoti yatheva rājā, amhehi guttā anusāsa rajjaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§358.</p>

```
Rājā <pb ed="M" n="1.0353" /> ca pabbajjamarocayittha, raṭṭhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0468" /> pahāya naravīraseṭṭho;
```

```
Ahampi ekā <note>ekāva (sī.)</note> carissāmi loke, hitvāna kāmāni manoramāni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§359.</p>

```
Rājā ca pabbajjamarocayittha, raṭṭhaṃ pahāya naravīraseṭṭho;
```

```
Ahampi ekā carissāmi loke, hitvāna kāmāni yathodhikāni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§360.</p>

```
Accenti kālā tarayanti rattiyo, vayoguṇā anupubbaṃ jahanti;
```

```
Ahampi ekā carissāmi loke, hitvāna kāmāni manoramāni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§361.</p>

```
Accenti kālā tarayanti rattiyo, vayoguṇā anupubbaṃ jahanti;
```

```
Ahampi ekā carissāmi loke, hitvāna kāmāni yathodhikāni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§362.</p>

```
Accenti kālā tarayanti rattiyo, vayoguṇā anupubbaṃ jahanti;
```

```
Ahampi ekā carissāmi loke, sītibhūtā <note>sītībhūtā (sī.)</note> sabbamaticca saṅganti.
```

Hatthipālajātakaṃ terasamaṃ.

#### 510. Ayogharajātakaṃ (14)

<p rend="hangnum">§363.</p>

```
Yamekarattiṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0469" /> paṭhamaṃ, gabbhe vasati māṇavo;
```

```
Abbhuṭṭhitova so yāti <note>sayati (sī. pī.), sa yāti (katthaci)</note>, sagacchaṃ na nivattati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§364.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="M" n="1.0354" /> yujjhamānā na balenavassitā, narā na jīranti na cāpi miyyare;
```

```
Sabbaṃ hidaṃ <note>hi taṃ (sī. pī.)</note> jātijarāyupaddutaṃ, taṃ me matī hoti carāmi dhammaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§365.</p>

```
Caturaṅginiṃ senaṃ subhiṃsarūpaṃ, jayanti raṭṭhādhipatī pasayha;
```

```
Na maccuno jayitumussahanti, taṃ me matī hoti carāmi dhammaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§366.</p>

```
Hatthīhi assehi rathehi pattibhi, parivāritā muccare ekacceyyā <note>ekaceyyā (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Na maccuno <note>na maccuto (sī.)</note> muccitumussahanti, taṃ me matī hoti carāmi dhammaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§367.</p>

```
Hatthīhi assehi rathehi pattibhi, sūrā <note>purā (ka.)</note> pabhañjanti padhaṃsayanti;
```

```
Na maccuno bhañjitumussahanti, taṃ me matī hoti carāmi dhammaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§368.</p>

```
Mattā gajā bhinnagaḷā <note>pabhinnagalā (sī.)</note> pabhinnā, nagarāni <pb ed="T" n="1.0470" /> maddanti janaṃ hananti;
```

```
Na maccuno madditumussahanti, taṃ me matī hoti carāmi dhammaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§369.</p>

```
Issāsino katahatthāpi vīrā <note>vīrā (sī. pī.)</note>, dūrepātī <note>patī (ka.)</note> akkhaṇavedhinopi;
```

```
Na maccuno vijjhitumussahanti, taṃ me matī hoti carāmi dhammaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§370.</p>

```
Sarāni <pb ed="V" n="1.0263" /> khīyanti saselakānanā, sabbaṃ hidaṃ <note>hi taṃ (sī. pī.), pitaṃ (syā.)</note> khīyati dīghamantaraṃ;
```

```
Sabbaṃ hidaṃ <note>hi taṃ (sī. pī.), pitaṃ (syā.)</note> bhañjare kālapariyāyaṃ, taṃ me matī hoti carāmi dhammaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§371.</p>

```
Sabbe <pb ed="M" n="1.0355" /> samevaṃ hi narānanārinaṃ <note>narānarīnaṃ (pī.), nārī narānaṃ (syā.), naranārīnaṃ (ka.)</note>, calācalaṃ pāṇabhunodha jīvitaṃ;
```

```
Paṭova dhuttassa dumova kūlajo, taṃ me matī hoti carāmi dhammaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§372.</p>

```
Dumapphalāneva patanti māṇavā, daharā ca vuddhā ca sarīrabhedā;
```

```
Nāriyo narā majjhimaporisā ca, taṃ me matī hoti carāmi dhammaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§373.</p>

```
Nāyaṃ vayo tārakarājasannibho, yadabbhatītaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0471" /> gatameva dāni taṃ;
```

```
Jiṇṇassa hī natthi ratī kuto sukhaṃ, taṃ me matī hoti carāmi dhammaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§374.</p>

```
Yakkhā pisācā athavāpi petā, kupitāte <note>kupitāpi te (sī. pī.)</note> assasanti manusse;
```

```
Na maccuno assasitussahanti, taṃ me matī hoti carāmi dhammaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§375.</p>

```
Yakkhe pisāce athavāpi pete, kupitepi te nijjhapanaṃ karonti;
```

```
Na maccuno nijjhapanaṃ karonti, taṃ me matī hoti carāmi dhammaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§376.</p>

```
Aparādhake dūsake heṭhake ca, rājāno daṇḍenti viditvāna dosaṃ;
```

```
Na maccuno daṇḍayitussahanti, taṃ me matī hoti carāmi dhammaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§377.</p>

```
Aparādhakā dūsakā heṭṭhakā ca, labhanti te rājino nijjhapetuṃ;
```

```
Na maccuno nijjhapanaṃ karonti, taṃ me matī hoti carāmi dhammaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§378.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="M" n="1.0356" /> khattiyoti na ca brāhmaṇoti, na <pb ed="T" n="1.0472" /> aḍḍhakā balavā tejavāpi;
```

```
Na maccurājassa apekkhamatthi, taṃ me matī hoti carāmi dhammaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§379.</p>

```
Sīhā ca byagghā ca athopi dīpiyo, pasayha khādanti vipphandamānaṃ;
```

```
Na maccuno khāditumussahanti, taṃ me matī hoti carāmi dhammaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§380.</p>

```
Māyākārā raṅgamajjhe karontā, mohenti cakkhūni janassa tāvade;
```

```
Na maccuno mohayitussahanti, taṃ me matī hoti carāmi dhammaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§381.</p>

```
Āsīvisā kupitā uggatejā, ḍaṃsanti mārentipi te manusse;
```

```
Na maccuno ḍaṃsitumussahanti, taṃ me matī hoti carāmi dhammaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§382.</p>

```
Āsīvisā kupitā yaṃ ḍaṃsanti, tikicchakā tesa visaṃ hananti;
```

```
Na maccuno daṭṭhavisaṃ <note>daṭṭhassa visaṃ (ka.)</note> hananti, taṃ me matī hoti carāmi dhammaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§383.</p>

```
Dhammantarī vettaraṇī <note>vetaraṇī (sī. pī.)</note> ca bhojo, visāni <pb ed="T" n="1.0473" /> hantvāna bhujaṅgamānaṃ;
```

```
Suyyanti te kālakatā tatheva, taṃ me matī hoti carāmi dhammaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§384.</p>

```
Vijjādharā <pb ed="V" n="1.0264" /> ghoramadhīyamānā, adassanaṃ osadhehi vajanti;
```

```
Na maccurājassa vajantadassanaṃ <note>vajanti adassanaṃ (syā. ka.)</note>, taṃ me matī hoti carāmi dhammaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§385.</p>

```
Dhammo <pb ed="M" n="1.0357" /> have rakkhati dhammacāriṃ, dhammo suciṇṇo sukhamāvahāti;
```

```
Esānisaṃso dhamme suciṇṇe, na duggatiṃ gacchati dhammacārī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§386.</p>

```
Na hi dhammo adhammo ca, ubho samavipākino;
```

```
Adhammo nirayaṃ neti, dhammo pāpeti suggatinti.
```

Ayogharajātakaṃ cuddasamaṃ.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Mātaṅga sambhūta sivi sirimanto, rohaṇa haṃsa sattigumbo bhallātiya;
```

```
Somanassa campeyya brahma pañca-paṇḍita cirassaṃvata ayogharāti.
```

<trailer rend="centre">Vīsatinipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.</trailer>

### 16. Tiṃsanipāto

#### 511. Kiṃchandajātakaṃ (1)

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
Kiṃchando <pb ed="T" n="1.0474" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0265" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0358" /> kimadhippāyo, eko sammasi ghammani;
```

```
Kiṃ patthayāno kiṃ esaṃ, kena atthena brāhmaṇa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
Yathā mahā vāridharo, kumbho supariṇāhavā <note>supariṇāmavā (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Tathūpamaṃ ambapakkaṃ, vaṇṇagandharasuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
Taṃ vuyhamānaṃ sotena, disvānāmalamajjhime;
```

```
Pāṇīhi naṃ gahetvāna, agyāyatanamāhariṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
Tato kadalipattesu, nikkhipitvā sayaṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Satthena naṃ vikappetvā, khuppipāsaṃ ahāsi me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
Sohaṃ apetadaratho, byantībhūto <note>byantibhūto (sī. pī. ka.)</note> dukhakkhamo;
```

```
Assādaṃ nādhigacchāmi, phalesvaññesu kesuci <note>kesupi (ka. sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
Sosetvā nūna maraṇaṃ, taṃ mamaṃ āvahissati;
```

```
Ambaṃ yassa phalaṃ sādu, madhuraggaṃ manoramaṃ;
```

```
Yamuddhariṃ vuyhamānaṃ, udadhismā mahaṇṇave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
Akkhātaṃ te mayā sabbaṃ, yasmā upavasāmahaṃ;
```

```
Rammaṃ pati nisinnosmi, puthulomāyutā puthu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
Tvañca kho meva <note>me (sī.), mama (?)</note> akkhāhi, attānamapalāyini;
```

```
Kā vā tvamasi kalyāṇi, kissa vā tvaṃ sumajjhime.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
Ruppapaṭṭapalimaṭṭhīva <pb ed="T" n="1.0475" /> <note>ruppapaṭṭaplamaṭṭhīva (syā.), rūpapaṭṭapamaṭṭhīva (ka.)</note>, byagghīva girisānujā;
```

```
Yā santi nāriyo devesu, devānaṃ paricārikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
Yā ca manussalokasmiṃ, rūpenānvāgatitthiyo;
```

```
Rūpena te sadisī natthi, devesu gandhabbamanussaloke <note>devagandhabbamānuse (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Puṭṭhāsi me cārupubbaṅgi, brūhi nāmañca bandhave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
Yaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0266" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0359" /> tvaṃ pati nisinnosi, rammaṃ brāhmaṇa kosikiṃ;
```

```
Sāhaṃ bhusālayā vutthā, varavārivahoghasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
Nānādumagaṇākiṇṇā, bahukā girikandarā;
```

```
Mameva pamukhā honti, abhisandanti pāvuse.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
Atho bahū vanatodā, nīlavārivahindharā;
```

```
Bahukā nāgavittodā, abhisandanti vārinā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
Tā ambajambulabujā, nīpā tālā cudumbarā <note>tālamudumbarā (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Bahūni phalajātāni, āvahanti abhiṇhaso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
Yaṃ kiñci ubhato tīre, phalaṃ patati ambuni;
```

```
Asaṃsayaṃ taṃ sotassa, phalaṃ hoti vasānugaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
Etadaññāya medhāvi, puthupañña suṇohi me;
```

```
Mā rocaya mabhisaṅgaṃ, paṭisedha janādhipa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
Na vāhaṃ vaḍḍhavaṃ <note>vaddhavaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> maññe, yaṃ tvaṃ raṭṭhābhivaḍḍhana;
```

```
Āceyyamāno rājisi, maraṇaṃ abhikaṅkhasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
Tassa jānanti pitaro, gandhabbā ca sadevakā;
```

```
Ye <pb ed="T" n="1.0476" /> cāpi isayo loke, saññatattā tapassino;
```

```
Asaṃsayaṃ tepi <note>te (sī. pī.)</note> jānanti, paṭṭhabhūtā <note>vaddhabhūtā (sī. pī.)</note> yasassino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
Evaṃ viditvā vidū sabbadhammaṃ, viddhaṃsanaṃ cavanaṃ jīvitassa;
```

```
Na cīyatī tassa narassa pāpaṃ, sace na ceteti vadhāya tassa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
Isipūgasamaññāte, evaṃ lokyā viditā sati <note>pati (ka. syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Anariyaparisambhāse, pāpakammaṃ jigīsasi <note>jigiṃsasi (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
Sace ahaṃ marissāmi, tīre te puthusussoṇi;
```

```
Asaṃsayaṃ taṃ asiloko, mayi pete āgamissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
Tasmā <pb ed="M" n="1.0360" /> hi pāpakaṃ kammaṃ, rakkhasseva <note>rakkhassu ca (syā.)</note> sumajjhime;
```

```
Mā taṃ sabbo jano pacchā, pakuṭṭhāyi <note>pakatthāsi (sī. pī.), patvakkhāsi (syā.)</note> mayi mate.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
Aññātametaṃ avisayhasāhi, attānamambañca dadāmi te taṃ;
```

```
So duccaje kāmaguṇe pahāya, santiñca dhammañca adhiṭṭhitosi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
Yo hitvā pubbasaññogaṃ, pacchā saṃyojane ṭhito;
```

```
Adhammañceva carati, pāpañcassa pavaḍḍhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
Ehi <pb ed="V" n="1.0267" /> taṃ pāpayissāmi, kāmaṃ appossuko bhava;
```

```
Upānayāmi sītasmiṃ, viharāhi anussuko.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
Taṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0477" /> puppharasamattebhi, vakkaṅgehi arindama;
```

```
Koñcā mayūrā diviyā, kolaṭṭhimadhusāḷikā;
```

```
Kūjitā haṃsapūgehi, kokilettha pabodhare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
Ambettha vippasākhaggā <note>vippasūnaggā (sī. syā. pī.), vippaonaggā (ka.)</note>, palālakhalasannibhā;
```

```
Kosambasaḷalā <note>kosumbhasalalā (sī. syā. pī.)</note> nīpā, pakkatālavilambino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
Mālī tiriṭī kāyūrī, aṅgadī candanussado <note>candanassado (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Rattiṃ tvaṃ paricāresi, divā vedesi vedanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
Soḷasitthisahassāni, yā temā paricārikā;
```

```
Evaṃ mahānubhāvosi, abbhuto lomahaṃsano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
Kiṃ kammamakarī pubbe, pāpaṃ attadukhāvahaṃ;
```

```
Yaṃ karitvā manussesu, piṭṭhimaṃsāni khādasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
Ajjhenāni paṭiggayha, kāmesu gadhito <note>gathito (sī. pī.), giddhito (syā. ka.), giddhiko (ka. aṭṭha.)</note> ahaṃ;
```

```
Acariṃ dīghamaddhānaṃ, paresaṃ ahitāyahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
Yo piṭṭhimaṃsiko hoti, evaṃ ukkacca khādati;
```

```
Yathāhaṃ ajja khādāmi, piṭṭhimaṃsāni attanoti.
```

Kiṃchandajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 512. Kumbhajātakaṃ (2)

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
Ko <pb ed="M" n="1.0361" /> pāturāsī tidivā nabhamhi, obhāsayaṃ saṃvariṃ candimāva;
```

```
Gattehi <pb ed="T" n="1.0478" /> te rasmiyo niccharanti, sateratā <note>sateritā (sī. syā. ka.)</note> vijjurivantalikkhe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
So chinnavātaṃ kamasī aghamhi, vehāyasaṃ gacchasi tiṭṭhasī ca;
```

```
Iddhī nu te vatthukatā subhāvitā, anaddhagūnaṃ api devatānaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
Vehāyasaṃ gammamāgamma <note>kamamāgamma (sī. syā.)</note> tiṭṭhasi, kumbhaṃ kiṇāthāti yametamatthaṃ;
```

```
Ko vā tuvaṃ kissa vā tāya kumbho, akkhāhi me brāhmaṇa etamatthaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
Na sappikumbho napi telakumbho, na phāṇitassa na madhussa kumbho;
```

```
Kumbhassa vajjāni anappakāni, dose bahū kumbhagate suṇātha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
Gaḷeyya <pb ed="V" n="1.0268" /> yaṃ pitvā <note>pītvā (sī. pī.)</note> pate papātaṃ, sobbhaṃ guhaṃ candaniyoḷigallaṃ;
```

```
Bahumpi bhuñjeyya abhojaneyyaṃ, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
Yaṃ pitvā <note>yaṃ ve pītvā (sī.)</note> cittasmimanesamāno, āhiṇḍatī goriva bhakkhasārī <note>bhakkhasādī (sī. syā. aṭṭha.)</note>;
```

```
Anāthamāno <pb ed="T" n="1.0479" /> upagāyati naccati ca, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
Yaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0362" /> ve pivitvā acelova naggo, careyya gāme visikhantarāni;
```

```
Sammūḷhacitto ativelasāyī, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
Yaṃ pitvā uṭṭhāya pavedhamāno, sīsañca bāhuñca <note>bāhañca (pī.)</note> pacālayanto;
```

```
So naccatī dārukaṭallakova, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
Yaṃ ve pivitvā aggidaḍḍhā sayanti, atho sigālehipi khāditāse;
```

```
Bandhaṃ vadhaṃ bhogajāniñcupenti, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
Yaṃ pitvā bhāseyya ābhāsaneyyaṃ, sabhāyamāsīno apetavattho;
```

```
Sammakkhito <note>samakkhito (sī.)</note> vantagato byasanno, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
Yaṃ ve pivitvā ukkaṭṭho āvilakkho, mameva sabbā pathavīti maññe <note>maññati (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Na <pb ed="T" n="1.0480" /> me samo cāturantopi rājā, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
Mānātimānā kalahāni pesuṇī, dubbaṇṇinī naggayinī palāyinī;
```

```
Corāna dhuttāna gatī niketo, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
Iddhāni phītāni kulāni assu, anekasāhassadhanāni loke;
```

```
Ucchinnadāyajjakatānimāya, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
Dhaññaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0363" /> dhanaṃ rajataṃ jātarūpaṃ, khettaṃ gavaṃ yattha vināsayanti;
```

```
Ucchedanī vittavataṃ <note>ucchedanī vittagataṃ (syā.), ucchedanivittagataṃ (ka.)</note> kulānaṃ, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
Yaṃ ve pitvā dittarūpova <note>duṭṭharūpova (sī.)</note> poso, akkosati mātaraṃ pitarañca;
```

```
Sassumpi gaṇheyya athopi suṇhaṃ, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
Yaṃ ve pitvā dittarūpāva nārī, akkosati sasuraṃ sāmikañca;
```

```
Dāsampi <pb ed="T" n="1.0481" /> gaṇhe paricārakampi, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
Yaṃ ve pivitvāna <note>yañce pītvāna (pī.)</note> haneyya poso, dhamme ṭhitaṃ samaṇaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ vā;
```

```
Gacche apāyampi tatonidānaṃ, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
Yaṃ ve pivitvā duccaritaṃ caranti, kāyena vācāya ca cetasā ca;
```

```
Nirayaṃ vajanti duccaritaṃ caritvā, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
Yaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0269" /> yācamānā na labhanti pubbe, bahuṃ hiraññampi pariccajantā;
```

```
So taṃ pivitvā alikaṃ bhaṇāti, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
Yaṃ ve pitvā pesane pesiyanto, accāyike karaṇīyamhi jāte;
```

```
Atthampi so nappajānāti vutto, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
Hirīmanāpi <pb ed="M" n="1.0364" /> ahirīkabhāvaṃ, pātuṃ karonti madanāya <note>madirāya (pī.)</note> mattā;
```

```
Dhīrāpi <pb ed="T" n="1.0482" /> santā bahukaṃ bhaṇanti, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
Yaṃ ve pitvā ekathūpā sayanti, anāsakā thaṇḍiladukkhaseyyaṃ;
```

```
Dubbaṇṇiyaṃ āyasakyañcupenti, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
Yaṃ ve pitvā pattakhandhā sayanti, gāvo kuṭahatāva na hi vāruṇiyā;
```

```
<note>yaṃ ve pitvā pattakkhandhā, sayanti gāvo kūṭahatāriva; na hi vāruṇiyā vego, narena sussahoriva; (sī.)</note> Vego narena susahoriva <note>yaṃ ve pitvā pattakkhandhā, sayanti gāvo kūṭahatāriva; na hi vāruṇiyā vego, narena sussahoriva; (sī.)</note>, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
Yaṃ manussā vivajjenti, sappaṃ ghoravisaṃ miva <note>visamiva (syā.), visaṃ iva (ka.), visāmiva (?)</note>;
```

```
Taṃ loke visasamānaṃ, ko naro pātumarahati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
Yaṃ ve pitvā andhakaveṇḍaputtā, samuddatīre paricārayantā <note>andhakaveṇhuputtā (sī. pī.), aṇḍakaveṇḍaputtā (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Upakkamuṃ musalehaññamaññaṃ, tassā puṇṇaṃ kumbhamimaṃ kiṇātha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
Yaṃ ve pitvā pubbadevā pamattā, tidivā cutā sassatiyā samāya;
```

```
Taṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0483" /> tādisaṃ majjamimaṃ niratthakaṃ, jānaṃ mahārāja kathaṃ piveyya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
Nayimasmiṃ kumbhasmiṃ dadhi vā madhu vā, evaṃ abhiññāya kiṇāhi rāja;
```

```
Evañhimaṃ kumbhagatā mayā te, akkhātarūpaṃ tava sabbamitta.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="M" n="1.0365" /> me pitā vā athavāpi mātā, etādisā yādisako tuvaṃsi;
```

```
Hitānukampī paramatthakāmo, sohaṃ karissaṃ vacanaṃ tavajja.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
Dadāmi te gāmavarāni pañca, dāsīsataṃ satta gavaṃ satāni;
```

```
Ājaññayutte ca rathe dasa ime, ācariyo hosi mamatthakāmo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
Taveva dāsīsatamatthu rāja, gāmā ca gāvo ca taveva hontu;
```

```
Ājaññayuttā ca rathā taveva, sakkohamasmī tidasānamindo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
Maṃsodanaṃ sappipāyāsaṃ <note>sappipāyañca (sī.)</note> bhuñja, khādassu ca tvaṃ madhumāsapūve;
```

```
Evaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0484" /> tuvaṃ dhammarato janinda, anindito saggamupehi ṭhānanti.
```

Kumbhajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 513. Jayaddisajātakaṃ (3)

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
Cirassaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0270" /> vata me udapādi ajja, bhakkho mahā sattamibhattakāle;
```

```
Kutosi ko vāsi tadiṅgha brūhi, ācikkha jātiṃ vidito yathāsi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
Pañcālarājā migavaṃ paviṭṭho, jayaddiso nāma yadissuto te;
```

```
Carāmi kacchāni vanāni cāhaṃ, pasadaṃ imaṃ khāda mamajja muñca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
Seneva <pb ed="M" n="1.0366" /> tvaṃ paṇasi sassamāno <note>sayhamāno (syā. ka.)</note>, mamesa bhakkho pasado yaṃ vadesi;
```

```
Taṃ khādiyāna pasadaṃ jighaññaṃ <note>jighacchaṃ (?)</note>, khādissaṃ pacchā na vilāpakālo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
Na catthi mokkho mama nikkayena <note>vikkayena (sī.)</note>, gantvāna paccāgamanāya paṇhe;
```

```
Taṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0485" /> saṅkaraṃ <note>saṅgaraṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> brāhmaṇassappadāya, saccānurakkhī punarāvajissaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
Kiṃ kammajātaṃ anutappate tvaṃ <note>anutappatī taṃ (sī. pī.)</note>, pattaṃ samīpaṃ maraṇassa rāja;
```

```
Ācikkha me taṃ api sakkuṇemu, anujānituṃ āgamanāya paṇhe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
Katā mayā brāhmaṇassa dhanāsā, taṃ saṅkaraṃ paṭimukkaṃ na muttaṃ;
```

```
Taṃ saṅkaraṃ brāhmaṇassappadāya, saccānurakkhī punarāvajissaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
Yā te katā brāhmaṇassa dhanāsā, taṃ saṅkaraṃ paṭimukkaṃ na muttaṃ;
```

```
Taṃ saṅkaraṃ brāhmaṇassappadāya, saccānurakkhī punarāvajassu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
Mutto ca so porisādassa <note>purisādassa (pī.)</note> hatthā, gantvā sakaṃ mandiraṃ kāmakāmī;
```

```
Taṃ saṅkaraṃ brāhmaṇassappadāya, āmantayī puttamalīnasattaṃ <note>sattuṃ (syā. pī. ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
Ajjeva <pb ed="M" n="1.0367" /> rajjaṃ abhisiñcayassu, dhammaṃ cara sesu paresu cāpi;
```

```
Adhammakāro <pb ed="T" n="1.0486" /> ca te māhu raṭṭhe, gacchāmahaṃ porisādassa ñatte <note>ñante (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
Kiṃ kamma kubbaṃ tava deva pāva <note>devapāde (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, nārādhayī taṃ tadicchāmi sotuṃ;
```

```
Yamajja rajjamhi udassaye tuvaṃ, rajjampi niccheyyaṃ tayā vināhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
Na kammunā vā vacasā va tāta, aparādhitohaṃ tuviyaṃ sarāmi;
```

```
Sandhiñca <note>saddhiṃ ca (ka.)</note> katvā purisādakena, saccānurakkhī punāhaṃ gamissaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
Ahaṃ gamissāmi idheva hohi, natthi tato jīvato vippamokkho;
```

```
Sace tuvaṃ gacchasiyeva rāja, ahampi gacchāmi ubho na homa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
Addhā hi tāta satānesa dhammo, maraṇā ca me dukkhataraṃ tadassa;
```

```
Kammāsapādo taṃ yadā pacitvā, pasayha khāde bhidā rukkhasūle.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
Pāṇena te pāṇamahaṃ nimissaṃ, mā tvaṃ agā porisādassa ñatte;
```

```
Etañca <pb ed="T" n="1.0487" /> te pāṇamahaṃ nimissaṃ, tasmā mataṃ jīvitassa vaṇṇemi <note>varemi (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
Tato <pb ed="V" n="1.0271" /> have dhitimā rājaputto, vanditvā mātu ca pitu ca <note>vandittha mātucca pitucca (sī. pī.)</note> pāde;
```

```
Dukhinissa mātā nipatā <note>nipatī (sī. pī.)</note> pathabyā, pitāssa paggayha bhujāni kandati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
Taṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0368" /> gacchantaṃ tāva pitā viditvā, parammukho vandati pañjalīko;
```

```
Somo ca rājā varuṇo ca rājā, pajāpatī candimā sūriyo ca;
```

```
Etehi gutto purisādakamhā, anuññāto sotthi paccehi tāta.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
Yaṃ daṇḍakirañño gatassa <note>yaṃ daṇḍakāraññagatassa (pī.)</note> mātā, rāmassakāsi sotthānaṃ suguttā;
```

```
Taṃ te ahaṃ sotthānaṃ karomi, etena saccena sarantu devā;
```

```
Anuññāto sotthi paccehi putta.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
Āvī raho vāpī manopadosaṃ, nāhaṃ sare jātu malīnasatte;
```

```
Etena saccena sarantu devā, anuññāto sotthi paccehi bhātika <note>bhāta (sī.), bhātā (syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
Yasmā ca me anadhimanosi sāmi, na cāpi me manasā appiyosi;
```

```
Etena saccena sarantu devā, anuññāto <pb ed="T" n="1.0488" /> sotthi paccehi sāmi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
Brahā ujū cārumukho kutosi, na maṃ pajānāsi vane vasantaṃ;
```

```
Luddaṃ maṃ ñatvā ‘‘purisādako’’ti, ko sotthi mājānamidhā’vajeyya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
Jānāmi ludda purisādako tvaṃ, na taṃ na jānāmi vane vasantaṃ;
```

```
Ahañca puttosmi jayaddisassa, mamajja khāda pituno pamokkhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
Jānāmi <pb ed="M" n="1.0369" /> puttoti <note>puttosi (syā. ka.)</note> jayaddisassa, tathā hi vo mukhavaṇṇo ubhinnaṃ;
```

```
Sudukkaraññeva <note>sudukkarañceva (syā. pī. ka.)</note> kataṃ tavedaṃ, yo mattumicche pituno pamokkhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
Na dukkaraṃ kiñci mahettha maññe, yo mattumicche pituno pamokkhā;
```

```
Mātu ca <note>mātucca (sī.)</note> hetu paraloka gantvā <note>gamyā (sī. syā.), gamya (pī.)</note>, sukhena <pb ed="T" n="1.0489" /> saggena ca sampayutto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
Ahañca kho attano pāpakiriyaṃ, āvī raho vāpi sare na jātu;
```

```
Saṅkhātajātīmaraṇohamasmi, yatheva me idha tathā parattha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
Khādajja maṃ dāni mahānubhāva, karassu kiccāni imaṃ sarīraṃ;
```

```
Rukkhassa vā te papatāmi aggā, chādayamāno mayhaṃ tvamadesi maṃsaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
Idañca te ruccati rājaputta, cajesi <note>cajāsi (sī. pī.)</note> pāṇaṃ pituno pamokkhā;
```

```
Tasmā hi so <note>tasmātiha (sī. syā.)</note> tvaṃ taramānarūpo, sambhañja kaṭṭhāni jalehi aggiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
Tato have dhitimā rājaputto, dāruṃ samāhatvā mahantamaggiṃ;
```

```
Sandīpayitvā paṭivedayittha, ādīpito dāni mahāyamaggi <note>mayā yakkhamaggi (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
Khādajja <pb ed="V" n="1.0272" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0370" /> maṃ dāni pasayhakārī, kiṃ maṃ muhuṃ pekkhasi haṭṭhalomo;
```

```
Tathā tathā tuyhamahaṃ karomi, yathā <pb ed="T" n="1.0490" /> yathā maṃ chādayamāno adesi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
Ko tādisaṃ arahati khāditāye, dhamme ṭhitaṃ saccavādiṃ vadaññuṃ;
```

```
Muddhāpi tassa viphaleyya sattadhā, yo tādisaṃ saccavādiṃ adeyya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§93.</p>

```
Idañhi so brāhmaṇaṃ maññamāno, saso avāsesi sake sarīre;
```

```
Teneva so candimā devaputto, sasatthuto <note>sasaṭṭhako (syā.)</note> kāmaduhajja <note>kāmaruhajja (ka.)</note> yakkha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§94.</p>

```
Cando yathā rāhumukhā pamutto, virocate pannaraseva bhāṇumā <note>bhānumā (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Evaṃ tuvaṃ porisādā pamutto, viroca kapile <note>kampilla (sī. pī.), kapille (syā.)</note> mahānubhāva;
```

```
Āmodayaṃ pitaraṃ mātarañca, sabbo ca te nandatu ñātipakkho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§95.</p>

```
Tato have dhitimā rājaputto, katañjalī pariyāya <note>pariyagā (sī.), paggayha (syā. pī.)</note> porisādaṃ;
```

```
Anuññāto sotthi sukhī arogo, paccāgamā <note>paccāga (pī.)</note> kapilamalīnasattā <note>kampilla’malīnasatto (sī. pī.), kapila’malīnasattā (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§96.</p>

```
Taṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0491" /> negamā jānapadā ca sabbe, hatthārohā rathikā pattikā ca;
```

```
Namassamānā pañjalikā upāgamuṃ, namatthu te dukkarakārakosīti.
```

Jayaddisajātakaṃ <note>jayadisajātakaṃ (ka.)</note> tatiyaṃ.

#### 514. Chaddantajātakaṃ (4)

<p rend="hangnum">§97.</p>

```
Kiṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0371" /> nu socasinuccaṅgi, paṇḍūsi varavaṇṇini;
```

```
Milāyasi visālakkhi, mālāva parimadditā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§98.</p>

```
Dohaḷo me mahārāja, supinantenupajjhagā <note>nu’paccagā (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Na so sulabharūpova, yādiso mama dohaḷo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§99.</p>

```
Ye keci mānusā kāmā, idha lokasmi nandane;
```

```
Sabbe te pacurā mayhaṃ, ahaṃ te dammi dohaḷaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§100.</p>

```
Luddā deva samāyantu, ye keci vijite tava;
```

```
Etesaṃ ahamakkhissaṃ, yādiso mama dohaḷo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§101.</p>

```
Ime te luddakā devi, katahatthā visāradā;
```

```
Vanaññū ca migaññū ca, mamatthe <note>mama te (pī.)</note> cattajīvitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§102.</p>

```
Luddaputtā nisāmetha, yāvantettha samāgatā;
```

```
Chabbisāṇaṃ gajaṃ setaṃ, addasaṃ supine ahaṃ;
```

```
Tassa dantehi me attho, alābhe natthi jīvitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§103.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="T" n="1.0492" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0273" /> no pitūnaṃ na pitāmahānaṃ, diṭṭho suto kuñjaro chabbisāṇo;
```

```
Yamaddasā supine rājaputtī, akkhāhi no yādiso hatthināgo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§104.</p>

```
Disā catasso vidisā catasso, uddhaṃ adho dasa disā imāyo;
```

```
Katamaṃ disaṃ tiṭṭhati nāgarājā, yamaddasā supine chabbisāṇaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§105.</p>

```
Ito ujuṃ uttariyaṃ disāyaṃ, atikkamma so sattagirī brahante;
```

```
Suvaṇṇapasso nāma girī uḷāro, supupphito <note>sampupphito (syā.)</note> kimpurisānuciṇṇo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§106.</p>

```
Āruyha <pb ed="M" n="1.0372" /> selaṃ bhavanaṃ kinnarānaṃ, olokaya pabbatapādamūlaṃ;
```

```
Atha dakkhasī meghasamānavaṇṇaṃ, nigrodharājaṃ atha sahassapādaṃ <note>poraṃ (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§107.</p>

```
Tatthacchatī kuñjaro chabbisāṇo, sabbaseto duppasaho parebhi;
```

```
Rakkhanti naṃ aṭṭhasahassanāgā, īsādantā vātajavappahārino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§108.</p>

```
Tiṭṭhanti <pb ed="T" n="1.0493" /> te tumūlaṃ <note>tumūla (syā.), bhimūla (pī. ka.)</note> passasantā, kuppanti vātassapi eritassa;
```

```
Manussabhūtaṃ pana tattha disvā, bhasmaṃ kareyyuṃ nāssa rajopi tassa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§109.</p>

```
Bahū hime rājakulamhi santi, piḷandhanā jātarūpassa devī;
```

```
Muttāmaṇīveḷuriyāmayā ca, kiṃ kāhasi dantapiḷandhanena;
```

```
Māretukāmā kuñjaraṃ chabbisāṇaṃ, udāhu ghātessasi luddaputte.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§110.</p>

```
Sā issitā dukkhitā casmi ludda, uddhañca sussāmi anussarantī;
```

```
Karohi me luddaka etamatthaṃ, dassāmi te gāmavarāni pañca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§111.</p>

```
Katthacchatī katthamupeti ṭhānaṃ, vīthissa kā nhāna <note>nahāna (sī. pī.)</note> gatassa hoti;
```

```
Kathañhi so nhāyati <note>nahāyati (sī. pī.)</note> nāgarājā, kathaṃ vijānemu gatiṃ gajassa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§112.</p>

```
Tattheva <pb ed="M" n="1.0373" /> sā pokkharaṇī adūre <note>avidūre (syā. ka.)</note>, rammā sutitthā ca mahodikā <note>mahodakā (syā. ka.)</note> ca;
```

```
Sampupphitā <pb ed="T" n="1.0494" /> bhamaragaṇānuciṇṇā <note>kiṇṇā (katthaci)</note>, ettha hi so nhāyati nāgarājā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§113.</p>

```
Sīsaṃ nahātuppala <note>nahāto uppala (sī. syā. pī.)</note> mālabhārī, sabbaseto puṇḍarīkattacaṅgī;
```

```
Āmodamāno gacchati sanniketaṃ, purakkhatvā mahesiṃ sabbabhaddaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§114.</p>

```
Tattheva so uggahetvāna vākyaṃ, ādāya tūṇiñca dhanuñca luddo;
```

```
Vituriyati <note>vituriya so (sī. aṭṭha.)</note> sattagirī brahante, suvaṇṇapassaṃ nāma giriṃ uḷāraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§115.</p>

```
Āruyha selaṃ bhavanaṃ kinnarānaṃ, olokayī pabbatapādamūlaṃ;
```

```
Tatthaddasā meghasamānavaṇṇaṃ, nigrodharājaṃ aṭṭhasahassapādaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§116.</p>

```
Tatthaddasā kuñjaraṃ chabbisāṇaṃ, sabbasetaṃ duppasahaṃ parebhi;
```

```
Rakkhanti naṃ aṭṭhasahassanāgā, īsādantā vātajavappahārino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§117.</p>

```
Tatthaddasā <pb ed="V" n="1.0274" /> pokkharaṇiṃ adūre, rammaṃ sutitthañca mahodikañca;
```

```
Sampupphitaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0495" /> bhamaragaṇānuciṇṇaṃ, yattha hi so nhāyati nāgarājā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§118.</p>

```
Disvāna nāgassa gatiṃ ṭhitiñca, vīthissa yā nhānagatassa hoti;
```

```
Opātamāgacchi anariyarūpo, payojito cittavasānugāya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§119.</p>

```
Khaṇitvāna <pb ed="M" n="1.0374" /> kāsuṃ phalakehi chādayi, attānamodhāya dhanuñca luddo;
```

```
Passāgataṃ puthusallena nāgaṃ, samappayī dukkaṭakammakārī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§120.</p>

```
Viddho ca nāgo koñcamanādi ghoraṃ, sabbe ca <note>sabbeva (sī. syā. pī.)</note> nāgā ninnaduṃ <note>ninnādu (syā.), ninnādaṃ (ka.)</note> ghorarūpaṃ;
```

```
Tiṇañca kaṭṭhañca raṇaṃ <note>cuṇṇaṃ (ka. sī. pī.)</note> karontā, dhāviṃsu te aṭṭhadisā samantato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§121.</p>

```
Vadhissametanti <note>vadhissamenanti (syā.)</note> parāmasanto, kāsāvamaddakkhi dhajaṃ isīnaṃ;
```

```
Dukkhena phuṭṭhassudapādi saññā, arahaddhajo sabbhi avajjharūpo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§122.</p>

```
Anikkasāvo kāsāvaṃ, yo vatthaṃ paridahissati <note>paridahessati (sī. pī.), paridhassati (katthaci)</note>;
```

```
Apeto damasaccena, na so kāsāvamarahati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§123.</p>

```
Yo <pb ed="T" n="1.0496" /> ca vantakasāvassa, sīlesu susamāhito;
```

```
Upeto damasaccena, sa ve kāsāvamarahati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§124.</p>

```
Samappito puthusallena nāgo, aduṭṭhacitto luddakamajjhabhāsi;
```

```
Kimatthayaṃ kissa vā samma hetu, mamaṃ vadhī kassa vāyaṃ payogo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§125.</p>

```
Kāsissa rañño mahesī bhadante, sā pūjitā rājakule subhaddā;
```

```
Taṃ addasā sā ca mamaṃ asaṃsi, dantehi atthoti ca maṃ <note>atthoti mamaṃ (syā. ka.)</note> avoca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§126.</p>

```
Bahū <pb ed="M" n="1.0375" /> hi me dantayugā uḷārā, ye me pitūnañca <note>pitunnampi (pī.)</note> pitāmahānaṃ;
```

```
Jānāti sā kodhanā rājaputtī, vadhatthikā veramakāsi bālā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§127.</p>

```
Uṭṭhehi tvaṃ ludda kharaṃ gahetvā, dante ime chinda purā marāmi;
```

```
Vajjāsi taṃ kodhanaṃ rājaputtiṃ, ‘‘nāgo hato handa imassa dantā’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§128.</p>

```
Uṭṭhāya so luddo kharaṃ gahetvā, chetvāna <pb ed="T" n="1.0497" /> dantāni gajuttamassa;
```

```
Vaggū subhe appaṭime pathabyā, ādāya pakkāmi tato hi khippaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§129.</p>

```
Bhayaṭṭitā <note>bhayadditā (sī. pī.)</note> nāgavadhena aṭṭā, ye te nāgā aṭṭha disā vidhāvuṃ;
```

```
Adisvāna <note>adisva (sī. pī.)</note> posaṃ gajapaccamittaṃ, paccāgamuṃ yena so nāgarājā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§130.</p>

```
Te tattha kanditvā roditvāna <note>roditva (sī. pī.)</note> nāgā, sīse sake paṃsukaṃ okiritvā;
```

```
Agamaṃsu te sabbe sakaṃ niketaṃ, purakkhatvā mahesiṃ sabbabhaddaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§131.</p>

```
Ādāya <pb ed="V" n="1.0275" /> dantāni gajuttamassa, vaggū subhe appaṭime pathabyā;
```

```
Suvaṇṇarājīhi samantamodare, so luddako kāsipuraṃ upāgami;
```

```
Upanesi so rājakaññāya dante, nāgo hato handa imassa dantā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§132.</p>

```
Disvāna <pb ed="M" n="1.0376" /> dantāni gajuttamassa, bhattuppiyassa purimāya jātiyā;
```

```
Tattheva tassā hadayaṃ aphāli, teneva <pb ed="T" n="1.0498" /> sā kālamakāsi bālā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§133.</p>

```
Sambodhipatto sa <note>ca (sī. syā.), va (pī.)</note> mahānubhāvo, sitaṃ akāsi parisāya majjhe;
```

```
Pucchiṃsu bhikkhū suvimuttacittā, nākāraṇe pātukaronti buddhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§134.</p>

```
Yamaddasātha dahariṃ kumāriṃ, kāsāyavatthaṃ anagāriyaṃ carantiṃ;
```

```
Sā kho tadā rājakaññā ahosi, ahaṃ tadā nāgarājā ahosiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§135.</p>

```
Ādāya dantāni gajuttamassa, vaggū subhe appaṭime pathabyā;
```

```
Yo luddako kāsipuraṃ upāgami, so kho tadā devadatto ahosi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§136.</p>

```
Anāvasūraṃ cirarattasaṃsitaṃ, uccāvacaṃ <note>ucaṃ nīcaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> caritamidaṃ purāṇaṃ;
```

```
Vītaddaro vītasoko visallo, sayaṃ abhiññāya abhāsi buddho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§137.</p>

```
Ahaṃ vo tena kālena, ahosiṃ tattha bhikkhavo;
```

```
Nāgarājā tadā homi <note>hosiṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, evaṃ dhāretha jātakanti.
```

Chaddantajātakaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 515. Sambhavajātakaṃ (5)

<p rend="hangnum">§138.</p>

```
Rajjañca <pb ed="T" n="1.0499" /> paṭipannāsma, ādhipaccaṃ sucīrata;
```

```
Mahattaṃ pattumicchāmi, vijetuṃ pathaviṃ imaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§139.</p>

```
Dhammena no adhammena, adhammo me na ruccati;
```

```
Kiccova dhammo carito, rañño hoti sucīrata.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§140.</p>

```
Idha <pb ed="M" n="1.0377" /> cevāninditā yena, pecca yena aninditā;
```

```
Yasaṃ devamanussesu, yena pappomu <note>pappemu (sī. aṭṭha.)</note> brāhmaṇa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§141.</p>

```
Yohaṃ atthañca dhammañca, kattumicchāmi brāhmaṇa;
```

```
Taṃ tvaṃ atthañca dhammañca, brāhmaṇakkhāhi pucchito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§142.</p>

```
Nāññatra vidhurā rāja, etadakkhātumarahati;
```

```
Yaṃ tvaṃ atthañca dhammañca, kattumicchasi khattiya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§143.</p>

```
Ehi <pb ed="V" n="1.0276" /> kho pahito gaccha, vidhurassa upantikaṃ;
```

```
Nikkhañcimaṃ <note>nikkhaṃ ratta (sī.), nikkhamimaṃ (pī.)</note> suvaṇṇassa, haraṃ gaccha sucīrata;
```

```
Abhihāraṃ imaṃ dajjā, atthadhammānusiṭṭhiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§144.</p>

```
Svādhippāgā bhāradvājo, vidhurassa upantikaṃ;
```

```
Tamaddasa mahābrahmā, asamānaṃ sake ghare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§145.</p>

```
Raññohaṃ pahito dūto, korabyassa yasassino;
```

```
‘‘Atthaṃ dhammañca pucchesi’’, iccabravi yudhiṭṭhilo;
```

```
Taṃ tvaṃ atthañca dhammañca, vidhurakkhāhi pucchito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§146.</p>

```
Gaṅgaṃ me pidahissanti, na taṃ sakkomi brāhmaṇa;
```

```
Apidhetuṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0500" /> mahāsindhuṃ, taṃ kathaṃ so bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§147.</p>

```
Na te sakkomi akkhātuṃ, atthaṃ dhammañca pucchito;
```

```
