```
Bhadrakāro ca me putto, oraso mama atrajo;
```

```
Taṃ tvaṃ atthañca dhammañca, gantvā pucchassu brāhmaṇa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§148.</p>

```
Svādhippāgā bhāradvājo, bhadrakārassupantikaṃ <note>bhadrakārassa santikaṃ (sī. syā.)</note>;
```

```
Tamaddasa mahābrahmā, nisinnaṃ samhi vesmani.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§149.</p>

```
Raññohaṃ pahito dūto, korabyassa yasassino;
```

```
‘‘Atthaṃ dhammañca pucchesi’’, iccabravi yudhiṭṭhilo;
```

```
Taṃ tvaṃ atthañca dhammañca, bhadrakāra pabrūhi <note>bravīhi (sī. pī.)</note> me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§150.</p>

```
Maṃsakājaṃ <note>maṃsakācaṃ (pī.)</note> avahāya, godhaṃ anupatāmahaṃ;
```

```
Na te sakkomi akkhātuṃ, atthaṃ dhammañca pucchito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§151.</p>

```
Sañcayo <pb ed="M" n="1.0378" /> <note>sañjayo (sī. syā. pī.)</note> nāma me bhātā, kaniṭṭho me sucīrata;
```

```
Taṃ tvaṃ atthañca dhammañca, gantvā pucchassu brāhmaṇa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§152.</p>

```
Svādhippāgā bhāradvājo, sañcayassa upantikaṃ;
```

```
Tamaddasa mahābrahmā, nisinnaṃ samhi vesmani <note>parisati (syā.), parīsati (pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§153.</p>

```
Raññohaṃ pahito dūto, korabyassa yasassino;
```

```
‘‘Atthaṃ dhammañca pucchesi’’, iccabravi yudhiṭṭhilo;
```

```
Taṃ tvaṃ atthañca dhammañca, sañcayakkhāhi pucchito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§154.</p>

```
Sadā maṃ gilate <note>gilatī (sī.), gilati (pī.)</note> maccu, sāyaṃ pāto sucīrata;
```

```
Na te sakkomi akkhātuṃ, atthaṃ dhammañca pucchito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§155.</p>

```
Sambhavo <pb ed="T" n="1.0501" /><pb ed="V" n="1.0277" /> nāma me bhātā, kaniṭṭho me sucīrata;
```

```
Taṃ tvaṃ atthañca dhammañca, gantvā pucchassu brāhmaṇa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§156.</p>

```
Abbhuto vata bho dhammo, nāyaṃ asmāka ruccati;
```

```
Tayo janā pitāputtā, tesu paññāya no vidū.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§157.</p>

```
Na taṃ sakkotha akkhātuṃ, atthaṃ dhammañca pucchitā;
```

```
Kathaṃ nu daharo jaññā, atthaṃ dhammañca pucchito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§158.</p>

```
Mā naṃ daharoti uññāsi <note>maññāsi (syā. ka.)</note>, apucchitvāna sambhavaṃ;
```

```
Pucchitvā sambhavaṃ jaññā, atthaṃ dhammañca brāhmaṇa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§159.</p>

```
Yathāpi cando vimalo, gacchaṃ ākāsadhātuyā;
```

```
Sabbe tārāgaṇe loke, ābhāya atirocati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§160.</p>

```
Evampi daharūpeto, paññāyogena sambhavo;
```

```
Mā naṃ daharoti uññāsi, apucchitvāna sambhavaṃ;
```

```
Pucchitvā sambhavaṃ jaññā, atthaṃ dhammañca brāhmaṇa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§161.</p>

```
Yathāpi rammako māso, gimhānaṃ hoti brāhmaṇa;
```

```
Atevaññehi māsehi, dumapupphehi sobhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§162.</p>

```
Evampi <pb ed="M" n="1.0379" /> daharūpeto, paññāyogena sambhavo;
```

```
Mā naṃ daharoti uññāsi, apucchitvāna sambhavaṃ;
```

```
Pucchitvā sambhavaṃ jaññā, atthaṃ dhammañca brāhmaṇa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§163.</p>

```
Yathāpi himavā brahme, pabbato gandhamādano;
```

```
Nānārukkhehi sañchanno, mahābhūtagaṇālayo;
```

```
Osadhehi <pb ed="T" n="1.0502" /> ca dibbehi, disā bhāti pavāti ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§164.</p>

```
Evampi daharūpeto, paññāyogena sambhavo;
```

```
Mā naṃ daharoti uññāsi, apucchitvāna sambhavaṃ;
```

```
Pucchitvā sambhavaṃ jaññā, atthaṃ dhammañca brāhmaṇa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§165.</p>

```
Yathāpi pāvako brahme, accimālī yasassimā;
```

```
Jalamāno vane gacche <note>caraṃ kacche (pī.)</note>, analo kaṇhavattanī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§166.</p>

```
Ghatāsano dhūmaketu, uttamāhevanandaho;
```

```
Nisīthe <note>nissīve (syā.), nisive (ka.)</note> pabbataggasmiṃ, pahūtedho <note>bahutejo (syā. ka.)</note> virocati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§167.</p>

```
Evampi <pb ed="V" n="1.0278" /> daharūpeto, paññāyogena sambhavo;
```

```
Mā naṃ daharoti uññāsi, apucchitvāna sambhavaṃ;
```

```
Pucchitvā sambhavaṃ jaññā, atthaṃ dhammañca brāhmaṇa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§168.</p>

```
Javena bhadraṃ jānanti, balibaddañca <note>balivaddañca (sī. pī.)</note> vāhiye;
```

```
Dohena dhenuṃ jānanti, bhāsamānañca paṇḍitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§169.</p>

```
Evampi daharūpeto, paññāyogena sambhavo;
```

```
Mā naṃ daharoti uññāsi, apucchitvāna sambhavaṃ;
```

```
Pucchitvā sambhavaṃ jaññā, atthaṃ dhammañca brāhmaṇa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§170.</p>

```
Svādhippāgā bhāradvājo, sambhavassa upantikaṃ;
```

```
Tamaddasa mahābrahmā, kīḷamānaṃ bahīpure.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§171.</p>

```
Raññohaṃ pahito dūto, korabyassa yasassino;
```

```
‘‘Atthaṃ dhammañca pucchesi’’, iccabravi yudhiṭṭhilo;
```

```
Taṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0503" /> tvaṃ atthañca dhammañca, sambhavakkhāhi pucchito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§172.</p>

```
Taggha <pb ed="M" n="1.0380" /> te ahamakkhissaṃ, yathāpi kusalo tathā;
```

```
Rājā ca kho taṃ jānāti, yadi kāhati vā na vā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§173.</p>

```
‘‘Ajja suve’’ti saṃseyya, raññā puṭṭho sucīrata;
```

```
Mā katvā avasī rājā, atthe jāte yudhiṭṭhilo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§174.</p>

```
Ajjhattaññeva saṃseyya, raññā puṭṭho sucīrata;
```

```
Kummaggaṃ na niveseyya, yathā mūḷho acetaso <note>acetano (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§175.</p>

```
Attānaṃ nātivatteyya, adhammaṃ na samācare;
```

```
Atitthe nappatāreyya, anatthe na yuto siyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§176.</p>

```
Yo ca etāni ṭhānāni, kattuṃ jānāti khattiyo;
```

```
Sadā so vaḍḍhate rājā, sukkapakkheva candimā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§177.</p>

```
Ñātīnañca piyo hoti, mittesu ca virocati;
```

```
Kāyassa bhedā sappañño, saggaṃ so upapajjatīti.
```

Sambhavajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 516. Mahākapijātakaṃ (6)

<p rend="hangnum">§178.</p>

```
Bārāṇasyaṃ <note>bārāṇassaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> ahū rājā, kāsīnaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhano;
```

```
Mittāmaccaparibyūḷho, agamāsi migājinaṃ <note>migājiraṃ (sī.), migāciraṃ (pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§179.</p>

```
Tattha <pb ed="V" n="1.0279" /> brāhmaṇamaddakkhi, setaṃ citraṃ kilāsinaṃ;
```

```
Viddhastaṃ koviḷāraṃva, kisaṃ dhamanisanthataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§180.</p>

```
Paramakāruññataṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0504" /> pattaṃ, disvā kicchagataṃ naraṃ;
```

```
Avaca byamhito rājā, ‘‘yakkhānaṃ katamo nusi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§181.</p>

```
‘‘Hatthapādā ca te setā, tato setataraṃ <note>setataro (pī.)</note> siro;
```

```
Gattaṃ kammāsavaṇṇaṃ te, kilāsabahulo casi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§182.</p>

```
‘‘Vaṭṭanāvaḷi <note>vaṭṭhanāvali (pī.)</note> saṅkāsā, piṭṭhi te ninnatunnatā;
```

```
Kāḷapabbāva <note>kāḷapabbā ca (syā.), kāḷā pabbā ca (pī.)</note> te aṅgā, nāññaṃ passāmi edisaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§183.</p>

```
‘‘Ugghaṭṭapādo <pb ed="M" n="1.0381" /> tasito, kiso dhamanisanthato;
```

```
Chāto ātattarūposi <note>ādittarūposi (ka.), atittarūposi (syā. ka. aṭṭha.)</note>, kutosi kattha gacchasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§184.</p>

```
‘‘Duddasī appakārosi, dubbaṇṇo bhīmadassano;
```

```
Janetti yāpi te mātā, na taṃ iccheyya passituṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§185.</p>

```
‘‘Kiṃ kammamakaraṃ <note>kammamakarā (sī. syā. pī.)</note> pubbe, kaṃ avajjhaṃ aghātayi;
```

```
Kibbisaṃ yaṃ karitvāna, idaṃ dukkhaṃ upāgami’’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§186.</p>

```
Taggha te ahamakkhissaṃ, yathāpi kusalo tathā;
```

```
Saccavādiñhi lokasmiṃ, pasaṃsantīdha paṇḍitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§187.</p>

```
Eko caraṃ gogaveso, mūḷho accasariṃ vane;
```

```
Araññe irīṇe <note>īriṇe (sī. syā. pī.)</note> vivane, nānākuñjarasevite.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§188.</p>

```
Vāḷamigānucarite, vippanaṭṭhosmi kānane;
```

```
Acariṃ tattha sattāhaṃ, khuppipāsa <note>khuppipāsā (sī. pī.)</note> samappito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§189.</p>

```
Tattha tindukamaddakkhiṃ, visamaṭṭhaṃ bubhukkhito;
```

```
Papātamabhilambantaṃ, sampannaphaladhārinaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§190.</p>

```
Vātassitāni <pb ed="T" n="1.0505" /> bhakkhesiṃ, tāni rucciṃsu me bhusaṃ;
```

```
Atitto rukkhamārūhiṃ <note>māruyha (sī. syā.)</note>, tattha hessāmi āsito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§191.</p>

```
Ekaṃ me bhakkhitaṃ āsi, dutiyaṃ abhipatthitaṃ;
```

```
Tato sā bhañjatha sākhā, chinnā pharasunā viya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§192.</p>

```
Sohaṃ sahāva sākhāhi, uddhaṃpādo avaṃsiro;
```

```
Appatiṭṭhe anālambe, giriduggasmi pāpataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§193.</p>

```
Yasmā ca vāri gambhīraṃ, tasmā na samapajjisaṃ <note>samapajjasiṃ (sī.), samabhajjisaṃ (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Tattha sesiṃ nirānando, anūnā <note>anātho (sī.)</note> dasa rattiyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§194.</p>

```
Athettha <pb ed="V" n="1.0280" /> kapi māgañchi <note>māgacchi (syā. ka.)</note>, gonaṅgulo darīcaro;
```

```
Sākhāhi sākhaṃ vicaranto, khādamāno dumapphalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§195.</p>

```
So <pb ed="M" n="1.0382" /> maṃ disvā kisaṃ paṇḍuṃ, kāruññamakaraṃ mayi;
```

```
Ambho ko nāma so ettha, evaṃ dukkhena aṭṭito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§196.</p>

```
Manusso amanusso vā, attānaṃ me pavedaya;
```

```
Tassañjaliṃ paṇāmetvā, idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§197.</p>

```
Manussohaṃ byasampatto <note>vasampatto (syā. ka.)</note>, sā me natthi ito gati;
```

```
Taṃ vo vadāmi bhaddaṃ vo, tvañca me saraṇaṃ bhava.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§198.</p>

```
Garuṃ <note>garu (sī. pī.)</note> silaṃ gahetvāna, vicarī <note>vicari (pī.)</note> pabbate kapi;
```

```
Silāya yoggaṃ katvāna, nisabho etadabravi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§199.</p>

```
Ehi me piṭṭhimāruyha, gīvaṃ gaṇhāhi bāhubhi;
```

```
Ahaṃ taṃ uddharissāmi, giriduggata vegasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§200.</p>

```
Tassa <pb ed="T" n="1.0506" /> taṃ vacanaṃ sutvā, vānarindassa sirīmato;
```

```
Piṭṭhimāruyha dhīrassa, gīvaṃ bāhāhi aggahiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§201.</p>

```
So maṃ tato samuṭṭhāsi, tejassī <note>tejasī (syā. pī. ka.)</note> balavā kapi;
```

```
Vihaññamāno kicchena, giriduggata vegasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§202.</p>

```
Uddharitvāna maṃ santo, nisabho etadabravi;
```

```
Iṅgha maṃ samma rakkhassu, passupissaṃ muhuttakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§203.</p>

```
Sīhā byagghā ca dīpī ca, acchakokataracchayo;
```

```
Te maṃ pamattaṃ hiṃseyyuṃ, te tvaṃ disvā nivāraya <note>disvāna vāraya (pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§204.</p>

```
Evaṃ me parittātūna <note>parittātuna (ka.)</note>, passupi so muhuttakaṃ;
```

```
Tadāhaṃ pāpikaṃ diṭṭhiṃ, paṭilacchiṃ ayoniso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§205.</p>

```
Bhakkho ayaṃ manussānaṃ, yathā caññe vane migā;
```

```
Yaṃ nūnimaṃ vadhitvāna, chāto khādeyya vānaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§206.</p>

```
Asito <note>āsiko (pī.)</note> ca gamissāmi, maṃsamādāya sambalaṃ;
```

```
Kantāraṃ nittharissāmi, pātheyyaṃ me bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§207.</p>

```
Tato silaṃ gahetvāna, matthakaṃ sannitāḷayiṃ;
```

```
Mama gatta <note>bhatta (sī. syā.), hattha (pī.)</note> kilantassa, pahāro dubbalo ahu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§208.</p>

```
So <pb ed="V" n="1.0281" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0383" /> ca vegenudappatto, kapi ruhira <note>rudhira (sī.)</note> makkhito;
```

```
Assupuṇṇehi nettehi, rodanto maṃ udikkhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§209.</p>

```
Māyyomaṃ kari bhaddante, tvañca nāmedisaṃ kari;
```

```
Tvañca kho nāma dīghāvu <note>dīghāyu (pī.)</note>, aññe <note>aññaṃ (pī.)</note> vāretumarahasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§210.</p>

```
Aho <pb ed="T" n="1.0507" /> vata re purisa, tāva dukkarakāraka;
```

```
Edisā visamā duggā, papātā uddhato <note>uddhaṭo (pī.)</note> mayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§211.</p>

```
Ānīto paralokāva, dubbheyyaṃ maṃ amaññatha;
```

```
Taṃ tena pāpadhammena, pāpaṃ pāpena cintitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§212.</p>

```
Mā heva tvaṃ adhammaṭṭha, vedanaṃ kaṭukaṃ phusi;
```

```
Mā heva pāpakammaṃ taṃ, phalaṃ veḷuṃva taṃ vadhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§213.</p>

```
Tayime natthi vissāso, pāpadhamma asaññata <note>pāpadhammaṃ amaññatha (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Ehi me piṭṭhito gaccha, dissamānova santike.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§214.</p>

```
Muttosi hatthā vāḷānaṃ, pattosi mānusiṃ padaṃ;
```

```
Esa maggo adhammaṭṭha, tena gaccha yathāsukhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§215.</p>

```
Idaṃ vatvā giricaro, rahade <note>ruhiraṃ (syā. ka.)</note> pakkhalya matthakaṃ;
```

```
Assūni sampamajjitvā, tato pabbatamāruhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§216.</p>

```
Sohaṃ tenābhisattosmi, pariḷāhena aṭṭito;
```

```
Ḍayhamānena gattena, vāriṃ pātuṃ upāgamiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§217.</p>

```
Agginā viya santatto, rahado ruhiramakkhito;
```

```
Pubbalohitasaṅkāso, sabbo me samapajjatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§218.</p>

```
Yāvanto udabindūni, kāyasmiṃ nipatiṃsu me;
```

```
Tāvanto gaṇḍa <note>gaṇḍū (sī. pī.), gaṇḍu (syā.)</note> jāyetha, addhabeluvasādisā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§219.</p>

```
Pabhinnā pagghariṃsu me, kuṇapā pubbalohitā;
```

```
Yena yeneva gacchāmi, gāmesu nigamesu ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§220.</p>

```
Daṇḍahatthā <pb ed="T" n="1.0508" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0384" /> nivārenti, itthiyo purisā ca maṃ;
```

```
Okkitā <note>okiṇṇā (sī.)</note> pūtigandhena, māssu orena āgamā <note>māgamā (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§221.</p>

```
Etādisaṃ idaṃ dukkhaṃ, satta vassāni dāni me;
```

```
Anubhomi sakaṃ kammaṃ, pubbe dukkaṭamattano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§222.</p>

```
Taṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0282" /> vo vadāmi bhaddante <note>bhaddaṃ vo (sī. pī.)</note>, yāvantettha samāgatā;
```

```
Māssu mittāna <note>mittānaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> dubbhittho, mittadubbho hi pāpako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§223.</p>

```
Kuṭṭhī kilāsī bhavati, yo mittānidha dubbhati <note>yo mittānaṃ idhaddubhi (sī. aṭṭha.), yo mittānaṃ idha dubbhati (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Kāyassa bhedā mittaddu <note>mittadubbhī (syā. ka.)</note>, nirayaṃ sopapajjatīti <note>so upapajjatīti (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

Mahākapijātakaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 517. Dakarakkhasajātakaṃ (7)

<p rend="hangnum">§224.</p>

```
Sace vo vuyhamānānaṃ, sattannaṃ udakaṇṇave;
```

```
Manussabalimesāno, nāvaṃ gaṇheyya rakkhaso;
```

```
Anupubbaṃ kathaṃ datvā, muñcesi dakarakkhasā <note>dakarakkhato (pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§225.</p>

```
Mātaraṃ paṭhamaṃ dajjaṃ, bhariyaṃ datvāna bhātaraṃ;
```

```
Tato sahāyaṃ datvāna, pañcamaṃ dajjaṃ <note>dajja (syā.)</note> brāhmaṇaṃ;
```

```
Chaṭṭhāhaṃ dajjamattānaṃ, neva dajjaṃ mahosadhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§226.</p>

```
Posetā te janettī ca, dīgharattānukampikā;
```

```
Chabbhī tayi padussati <note>paduṭṭhasmiṃ (sī. syā.)</note>, paṇḍitā atthadassinī;
```

```
Aññaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0509" /> upanisaṃ katvā, vadhā taṃ parimocayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§227.</p>

```
Taṃ tādisiṃ <note>tādisaṃ (ka.)</note> pāṇadadiṃ, orasaṃ gabbhadhāriniṃ <note>gabbhadhāriṇiṃ (sī. syā.)</note>;
```

```
Mātaraṃ kena dosena, dajjāsi dakarakkhino <note>dakarakkhato (pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§228.</p>

```
Daharā viyalaṅkāraṃ, dhāreti apiḷandhanaṃ;
```

```
Dovārike anīkaṭṭhe, ativelaṃ pajagghati <note>sañjagghati (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§229.</p>

```
Athopi <pb ed="M" n="1.0385" /> paṭirājūnaṃ, sayaṃ dūtāni sāsati;
```

```
Mātaraṃ tena dosena, dajjāhaṃ dakarakkhino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§230.</p>

```
Itthigumbassa pavarā, accantaṃ piyabhāṇinī <note>accantapiyavādinī (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Anuggatā <note>anubbatā (syā.), anupubbatā (ka.)</note> sīlavatī, chāyāva anapāyinī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§231.</p>

```
Akkodhanā puññavatī <note>paññavatī (sī. pī.)</note>, paṇḍitā atthadassinī;
```

```
Ubbariṃ <note>uppariṃ (sī.)</note> kena dosena, dajjāsi dakarakkhino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§232.</p>

```
Khiḍḍāratisamāpannaṃ, anatthavasamāgataṃ;
```

```
Sā maṃ sakāna puttānaṃ, ayācaṃ yācate dhanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§233.</p>

```
Sohaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0283" /> dadāmi sāratto <note>sārato (syā.)</note>, bahuṃ uccāvacaṃ dhanaṃ;
```

```
Suduccajaṃ cajitvāna, pacchā socāmi dummano;
```

```
Ubbariṃ tena dosena, dajjāhaṃ dakarakkhino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§234.</p>

```
Yenocitā janapadā <note>jānapadā (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, ānītā ca paṭiggahaṃ;
```

```
Ābhataṃ pararajjebhi, abhiṭṭhāya bahuṃ dhanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§235.</p>

```
Dhanuggahānaṃ pavaraṃ, sūraṃ tikhiṇamantinaṃ;
```

```
Bhātaraṃ kena dosena, dajjāsi dakarakkhino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§236.</p>

```
Yenocitā <pb ed="T" n="1.0510" /> <note>mayocitā (sī.), mayācitā (pī.)</note> janapadā, ānītā ca paṭiggahaṃ;
```

```
Ābhataṃ pararajjebhi, abhiṭṭhāya bahuṃ dhanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§237.</p>

```
Dhanuggahānaṃ pavaro, sūro tikhiṇamanti ca <note>tikhiṇamantino (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Mayāyaṃ <note>mayā so (sī. pī.)</note> sukhito rājā, atimaññati dārako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§238.</p>

```
Upaṭṭhānampi me ayye, na so eti yathā pure;
```

```
Bhātaraṃ tena dosena, dajjāhaṃ dakarakkhino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§239.</p>

```
Ekarattena ubhayo, tvañceva dhanusekha ca <note>dhanusekhavā (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Ubho jātettha pañcālā, sahāyā susamāvayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§240.</p>

```
Cariyā <pb ed="M" n="1.0386" /> taṃ anubandhittho <note>anubandho (ka.)</note>, ekadukkhasukho tava;
```

```
Ussukko te divārattiṃ, sabbakiccesu byāvaṭo;
```

```
Sahāyaṃ kena dosena, dajjāsi dakarakkhino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§241.</p>

```
Cariyā maṃ ayaṃ <note>cariyāya ayaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> ayye, pajagghittho <note>sañjagghittho (syā.)</note> mayā saha;
```

```
Ajjāpi tena vaṇṇena, ativelaṃ pajagghati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§242.</p>

```
Ubbariyāpihaṃ ayye, mantayāmi rahogato;
```

```
Anāmanto <note>anāmantā (sī.)</note> pavisati, pubbe appaṭivedito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§243.</p>

```
Laddhadvāro <note>laddhavāro (sī. pī.)</note> katokāso, ahirikaṃ anādaraṃ;
```

```
Sahāyaṃ tena dosena, dajjāhaṃ dakarakkhino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§244.</p>

```
Kusalo sabbanimittānaṃ, rutaññū <note>rudaññū (sī. syā. pī.)</note> āgatāgamo;
```

```
Uppāte supine yutto, niyyāne ca pavesane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§245.</p>

```
Paṭṭho <note>paddho (sī. pī.)</note> bhūmantalikkhasmiṃ, nakkhattapadakovido;
```

```
Brāhmaṇaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0511" /> kena dosena, dajjāsi dakarakkhino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§246.</p>

```
Parisāyampi me ayye, ummīlitvā udikkhati;
```

```
Tasmā accabhamuṃ luddaṃ, dajjāhaṃ dakarakkhino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§247.</p>

```
Sasamuddapariyāyaṃ<pb ed="V" n="1.0284" />, mahiṃ sāgarakuṇḍalaṃ;
```

```
Vasundharaṃ āvasasi, amaccaparivārito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§248.</p>

```
Cāturanto mahāraṭṭho, vijitāvī mahabbalo;
```

```
Pathabyā ekarājāsi, yaso te vipulaṃ gato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§249.</p>

```
Soḷasitthisahassāni, āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalā;
```

```
Nānājanapadā nārī, devakaññūpamā subhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§250.</p>

```
Evaṃ sabbaṅgasampannaṃ, sabbakāmasamiddhinaṃ;
```

```
Sukhitānaṃ piyaṃ dīghaṃ, jīvitaṃ āhu khattiya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§251.</p>

```
Atha tvaṃ kena vaṇṇena, kena vā pana hetunā;
```

```
Paṇḍitaṃ anurakkhanto, pāṇaṃ cajasi duccajaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§252.</p>

```
Yatopi <pb ed="M" n="1.0387" /> āgato ayye, mama hatthaṃ mahosadho;
```

```
Nābhijānāmi dhīrassa, anumattampi dukkaṭaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§253.</p>

```
Sace ca kismici kāle, maraṇaṃ me pure siyā;
```

```
So me putte <note>putte ca me (sī. syā. pī.</note> paputte ca, sukhāpeyya mahosadho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§254.</p>

```
Anāgataṃ paccuppannaṃ, sabbamatthampi passati <note>sabbamatthaṃ vipassati (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Anāparādhakammantaṃ, na dajjaṃ dakarakkhino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§255.</p>

```
Idaṃ suṇātha pañcālā, cūḷaneyyassa <note>cūḷanīyassa (sī.)</note> bhāsitaṃ;
```

```
Paṇḍitaṃ <pb ed="T" n="1.0512" /> anurakkhanto, pāṇaṃ cajati duccajaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§256.</p>

```
Mātu bhariyāya bhātucca, sakhino brāhmaṇassa ca;
```

```
Attano cāpi pañcālo, channaṃ cajati jīvitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§257.</p>

```
Evaṃ mahatthikā <note>khahiddhiyā (syā.), mahiddhikā (ka.)</note> paññā, nipuṇā sādhucintinī;
```

```
Diṭṭhadhammahitatthāya, samparāyasukhāya cāti.
```

Dakarakkhasajātakaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 518. Paṇḍaranāgarājajātakaṃ (8)

<p rend="hangnum">§258.</p>

```
Vikiṇṇavācaṃ aniguyha <note>anigūḷha (pī.)</note> mantaṃ, asaññataṃ aparicakkhitāraṃ <note>aparirakkhitāraṃ (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Bhayaṃ tamanveti sayaṃ abodhaṃ, nāgaṃ yathā paṇḍarakaṃ supaṇṇo <note>suvaṇṇo (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§259.</p>

```
Yo guyhamantaṃ parirakkhaneyyaṃ, mohā naro saṃsati hāsamāno <note>bhāsamāno (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Taṃ bhinnamantaṃ bhayamanveti khippaṃ, nāgaṃ yathā paṇḍarakaṃ supaṇṇo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§260.</p>

```
Nānumitto <pb ed="V" n="1.0285" /> garuṃ atthaṃ, guyhaṃ veditumarahati;
```

```
Sumitto ca asambuddhaṃ, sambuddhaṃ vā anattha vā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§261.</p>

```
Vissāsamāpajjimahaṃ <pb ed="M" n="1.0388" /> acelaṃ <note>acelo (sī. pī.)</note>, samaṇo <pb ed="T" n="1.0513" /> ayaṃ sammato bhāvitatto;
```

```
Tassāhamakkhiṃ vivariṃ <note>vivaraṃ (sī.)</note> guyhamatthaṃ, atītamattho kapaṇaṃ <note>kapaṇo (pī.)</note> rudāmi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§262.</p>

```
Tassāhaṃ paramaṃ <note>purimaṃ (sī.)</note> brahme guyhaṃ, vācañhi maṃ nāsakkhiṃ <note>nāsakkhi (pī.)</note> saṃyametuṃ;
```

```
Tappakkhato hi bhayamāgataṃ mamaṃ, atītamattho kapaṇaṃ rudāmi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§263.</p>

```
Yo ve naro suhadaṃ maññamāno, guyhamatthaṃ saṃsati dukkulīne;
```

```
Dosā bhayā athavā rāgarattā <note>rāgaratto (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, pallatthito <note>pallittho (pī.), pallattito (ka.)</note> bālo asaṃsayaṃ so.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§264.</p>

```
Tirokkhavāco asataṃ paviṭṭho, yo saṅgatīsu mudīreti vākyaṃ;
```

```
Āsīviso dummukhotyāhu taṃ naraṃ, ārā ārā <note>ārā arā (pī.)</note> saṃyame tādisamhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§265.</p>

```
Annaṃ pānaṃ kāsika <note>kāsikaṃ (pī.)</note> candanañca, manāpitthiyo mālamucchādanañca;
```

```
Ohāya gacchāmase sabbakāme, supaṇṇa pāṇūpagatāva tyamhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§266.</p>

```
Ko nīdha tiṇṇaṃ garahaṃ upeti, asmiṃdha <pb ed="T" n="1.0514" /> loke pāṇabhū nāgarāja;
```

```
Samaṇo supaṇṇo atha vā tvameva, kiṃ kāraṇā paṇḍarakaggahīto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§267.</p>

```
Samaṇoti <pb ed="M" n="1.0389" /> me sammatatto ahosi, piyo ca me manasā bhāvitatto;
```

```
Tassāhamakkhiṃ vivariṃ guyhamatthaṃ, atītamattho kapaṇaṃ rudāmi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§268.</p>

```
Na catthi satto amaro pathabyā, paññāvidhā natthi na ninditabbā;
```

Saccena dhammena dhitiyā <note>dhiyā (sī. pī.)</note> damena, alabbhamabyāharatī naro idha.

<p rend="hangnum">§269.</p>

```
Mātāpitā paramā bandhavānaṃ, nāssa tatiyo anukampakatthi;
```

```
Tesampi guyhaṃ paramaṃ na saṃse, mantassa bhedaṃ parisaṅkamāno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§270.</p>

```
Mātāpitā bhaginī bhātaro ca, sahāyā vā yassa honti sapakkhā;
```

```
Tesampi guyhaṃ paramaṃ na saṃse, mantassa bhedaṃ parisaṅkamāno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§271.</p>

```
Bhariyā ce purisaṃ vajjā, komārī piyabhāṇinī;
```

```
Puttarūpayasūpetā<pb ed="T" n="1.0515" />, ñātisaṅghapurakkhatā, tassāpi guyhaṃ paramaṃ na saṃse;
```

```
Mantassa bhedaṃ parisaṅkamāno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§272.</p>

```
Na guyhamatthaṃ <note>guyhatthaṃ (ka.)</note> vivareyya, rakkheyya naṃ yathā nidhiṃ;
```

```
Na hi pātukato sādhu, guyho attho pajānatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§273.</p>

```
Thiyā guyhaṃ na saṃseyya, amittassa ca paṇḍito;
```

```
Yo cāmisena saṃhīro, hadayattheno ca yo naro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§274.</p>

```
Guyhamatthaṃ <pb ed="V" n="1.0286" /> asambuddhaṃ, sambodhayati yo naro;
```

```
Mantabhedabhayā tassa, dāsabhūto titikkhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§275.</p>

```
Yāvanto <pb ed="M" n="1.0390" /> purisassatthaṃ, guyhaṃ jānanti mantinaṃ;
```

```
Tāvanto tassa ubbegā, tasmā guyhaṃ na vissaje.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§276.</p>

```
Vivicca bhāseyya divā rahassaṃ, rattiṃ giraṃ nātivelaṃ pamuñce;
```

```
Upassutikā hi suṇanti mantaṃ, tasmā manto khippamupeti bhedaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§277.</p>

```
Yathāpi assa <note>ayo (syā.), aya (ka.)</note> nagaraṃ mahantaṃ, advārakaṃ <note>āḷārakaṃ (pī.)</note> āyasaṃ bhaddasālaṃ;
```

```
Samantakhātāparikhāupetaṃ, evampi me te idha guyhamantā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§278.</p>

```
Ye guyhamantā avikiṇṇavācā, daḷhā <pb ed="T" n="1.0516" /> sadatthesu narā dujivha <note>dujivhā (syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Ārā amittā byavajanti tehi, āsīvisā vā riva sattusaṅghā <note>sattasaṅghā (sī. syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§279.</p>

```
Hitvā gharaṃ pabbajito acelo, naggo muṇḍo carati ghāsahetu;
```

```
Tamhi <note>tamhī (pī.)</note> nu kho vivariṃ guyhamatthaṃ, atthā ca dhammā ca apaggatamhā <note>apāgatamhā (sī.), apagatamhā (syā.), avāgatamhā (pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§280.</p>

```
Kathaṃkaro hoti supaṇṇarāja, kiṃsīlo kena vatena vattaṃ;
```

```
Samaṇo caraṃ hitvā mamāyitāni, kathaṃkaro saggamupeti ṭhānaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§281.</p>

```
Hiriyā titikkhāya damenupeto <note>damena khantiyā (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, akkodhano pesuṇiyaṃ pahāya;
```

```
Samaṇo caraṃ hitvā mamāyitāni, evaṃkaro saggamupeti ṭhānaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§282.</p>

```
Mātāva <pb ed="M" n="1.0391" /> puttaṃ taruṇaṃ tanujjaṃ <note>tanūjaṃ (sī.)</note>, samphassatā <note>sampassa taṃ (sī. pī.)</note> sabbagattaṃ phareti;
```

```
Evampi me tvaṃ pāturahu dijinda, mātāva puttaṃ anukampamāno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§283.</p>

```
Handajja <pb ed="T" n="1.0517" /> tvaṃ muñca <note>mucca (sī.)</note> vadhā dujivha, tayo hi puttā na hi añño atthi;
```

```
Antevāsī dinnako atrajo ca, rajjassu <note>rajassu (sī. syā. pī.)</note> puttaññataro me ahosi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§284.</p>

```
Icceva vākyaṃ visajjī supaṇṇo, bhumyaṃ patiṭṭhāya dijo dujivhaṃ;
```

```
Muttajja tvaṃ sabbabhayātivatto, thalūdake hohi mayābhigutto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§285.</p>

```
Ātaṅkinaṃ yathā kusalo bhisakko, pipāsitānaṃ rahadova sīto;
```

```
Vesmaṃ yathā himasītaṭṭitānaṃ <note>himasisiraṭṭitānaṃ (pī.)</note>, evampi te saraṇamahaṃ bhavāmi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§286.</p>

```
Sandhiṃ katvā amittena, aṇḍajena jalābuja;
```

```
Vivariya dāṭhaṃ sesi, kuto taṃ bhayamāgataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§287.</p>

```
Saṅketheva amittasmiṃ, mittasmimpi na vissase;
```

```
Abhayā bhayamuppannaṃ, api mūlāni kantati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§288.</p>

```
Kathaṃ nu vissase tyamhi, yenāsi kalaho kato;
```

```
Niccayattena ṭhātabbaṃ, so disabbhi <note>so disamhi (pī.)</note> na rajjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§289.</p>

```
Vissāsaye <pb ed="V" n="1.0287" /> na ca taṃ <note>naṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> vissayeyya, asaṅkito saṅkito ca <note>asaṅkito ca saṅkito (sī. pī.)</note> bhaveyya;
```

```
Tathā <pb ed="T" n="1.0518" /> tathā viññū parakkameyya, yathā yathā bhāvaṃ paro na jaññā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§290.</p>

```
Te <pb ed="M" n="1.0392" /> devavaṇṇā <note>devavaṇṇī (pī.)</note> sukhumālarūpā, ubho samā sujayā <note>sujayo (sī. syā. pī.)</note> puññakhandhā <note>puññagandhā (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Upāgamuṃ karampiyaṃ <note>kādambiyaṃ (sī.), kārambiyaṃ (pī.)</note> acelaṃ, missībhūtā assavāhāva nāgā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§291.</p>

```
Tato have paṇḍarako acelaṃ, sayamevupāgamma idaṃ avoca;
```

```
Muttajjahaṃ sabbabhayātivatto, na hi <note>ha (pī.)</note> nūna tuyhaṃ manaso piyamhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§292.</p>

```
Piyo hi me āsi supaṇṇarājā, asaṃsayaṃ paṇḍarakena saccaṃ;
```

```
So rāgarattova akāsimetaṃ, pāpakammaṃ <note>pāpaṃ kammaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> sampajāno na mohā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§293.</p>

```
Na me piyaṃ appiyaṃ vāpi hoti, sampassato lokamimaṃ parañca;
```

```
Susaññatānañhi viyañjanena, asaññato lokamimaṃ carāsi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§294.</p>

```
Ariyāvakāsosi anariyovāsi <note>anariyo cāsi (sī. pī.)</note>, asaññato saññatasannikāso;
```

```
Kaṇhābhijātikosi <pb ed="T" n="1.0519" /> anariyarūpo, pāpaṃ bahuṃ duccaritaṃ acāri.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§295.</p>

```
Aduṭṭhassa tuvaṃ dubbhi, dubbhī <note>dūbhi, dūbhī (pī.)</note> ca pisuṇo casi;
```

```
Etena saccavajjena, muddhā te phalatu sattadhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§296.</p>

```
Tasmā hi mittānaṃ na dubbhitabbaṃ, mittadubbhā <note>mittadubbhā hi (syā.)</note> pāpiyo natthi añño;
```

```
Āsittasatto nihato pathabyā, indassa vākyena hi saṃvaro hatoti.
```

Paṇḍaranāgarājajātakaṃ <note>paṇḍarakajātakaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 519. Sambulājātakaṃ (9)

<p rend="hangnum">§297.</p>

```
Kā <pb ed="M" n="1.0393" /> vedhamānā girikandarāyaṃ, ekā tuvaṃ tiṭṭhasi saṃhitūru <note>saññatūra (sī. pī.), sañcitūru (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Puṭṭhāsi me pāṇipameyyamajjhe, akkhāhi me nāmañca bandhave ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§298.</p>

```
Obhāsayaṃ vanaṃ rammaṃ, sīhabyagghanisevitaṃ;
```

```
Kā vā tvamasi kalyāṇi, kassa vā tvaṃ sumajjhime;
```

```
Abhivādemi taṃ bhadde, dānavāhaṃ namatthu te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§299.</p>

```
Yo putto kāsirājassa, sotthisenoti taṃ vidū;
```

```
Tassāhaṃ sambulā bhariyā, evaṃ jānāhi dānava;
```

```
Abhivādemi <pb ed="T" n="1.0520" /> taṃ bhante <note>bhaddante (sī. syā.)</note>, sambulāhaṃ namatthu te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§300.</p>

```
Vedehaputto <pb ed="V" n="1.0288" /> bhaddante, vane vasati āturo;
```

```
Tamahaṃ rogasammattaṃ, ekā ekaṃ upaṭṭhahaṃ <note>upaṭṭhahiṃ (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§301.</p>

```
Ahañca vanamuñchāya, madhumaṃsaṃ migābilaṃ <note>migāvilaṃ (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Yadā harāmi taṃ bhakkho, tassa nūnajja nādhati <note>nāthati (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§302.</p>

```
Kiṃ vane rājaputtena, āturena karissasi;
```

```
Sambule pariciṇṇena, ahaṃ bhattā bhavāmi te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§303.</p>

```
Sokaṭṭāya durattāya, kiṃ rūpaṃ vijjate mama;
```

```
Aññaṃ pariyesa bhaddante, abhirūpataraṃ mayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§304.</p>

```
Ehimaṃ girimāruyha, bhariyā me <note>mayhaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> catussatā;
```

```
Tāsaṃ tvaṃ pavarā hohi, sabbakāmasamiddhinī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§305.</p>

```
Nūna <note>nanu (sī. syā. pī. ka.)</note> tārakavaṇṇābhe <note>hāṭakavaṇṇābhe (pī.)</note>, yaṃ kiñci manasicchasi;
```

```
Sabbaṃ taṃ pacuraṃ mayhaṃ, ramassvajja <note>ramasujja (sī. syā.)</note> mayā saha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§306.</p>

```
No ce tuvaṃ maheseyyaṃ, sambule kārayissasi;
```

```
Alaṃ tvaṃ pātarāsāya, paṇhe <note>maññe (sī. pī.)</note> bhakkhā bhavissasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§307.</p>

```
Tañca <pb ed="M" n="1.0394" /> sattajaṭo luddo, kaḷāro purisādako;
```

```
Vane nāthaṃ apassantiṃ, sambulaṃ aggahī bhuje.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§308.</p>

```
Adhipannā pisācena, luddenāmisacakkhunā;
```

```
Sā ca sattuvasampattā, patimevānusocati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§309.</p>

```
Na me idaṃ tathā dukkhaṃ, yaṃ maṃ khādeyya rakkhaso;
```

```
Yañca <pb ed="T" n="1.0521" /> me ayyaputtassa, mano hessati aññathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§310.</p>

```
Na santi devā pavasanti nūna, na hi nūna santi idha lokapālā;
```

```
Sahasā karontānamasaññatānaṃ, na hi nūna santi paṭisedhitāro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§311.</p>

```
Itthīnamesā pavarā yasassinī, santā samā aggirivuggatejā;
```

```
Tañce tuvaṃ rakkhasādesi kaññaṃ, muddhā ca hi sattadhā te phaleyya;
```

```
Mā tvaṃ dahī <note>jahī (pī.)</note> muñca patibbatāya <note>patibbatā sā (sī.), patibbatā yā (pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§312.</p>

```
Sā ca assamamāgacchi, pamuttā purisādakā;
```

```
Nīḷaṃ <note>niḍḍaṃ (syā. ka.)</note> paḷinaṃ sakuṇīva <note>phalinasakuṇīva (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, gatasiṅgaṃva ālayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§313.</p>

```
Sā tattha paridevesi, rājaputtī yasassinī;
```

```
Sambulā utumattakkhā, vane nāthaṃ apassantī <note>apassatī (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§314.</p>

```
Samaṇe <pb ed="V" n="1.0289" /> brāhmaṇe vande, sampannacaraṇe ise;
```

```
Rājaputtaṃ apassantī, tumhaṃmhi <note>tumhaṃ hi (pī.)</note> saraṇaṃ gatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§315.</p>

```
Vande sīhe ca byagghe ca, ye ca aññe vane migā;
```

```
Rājaputtaṃ apassantī, tumhaṃmhi saraṇaṃ gatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§316.</p>

```
Tiṇā <note>tiṇa (pī.)</note> latāni osadhyo, pabbatāni vanāni ca;
```

```
Rājaputtaṃ apassantī, tumhaṃmhi saraṇaṃ gatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§317.</p>

```
Vande <pb ed="T" n="1.0522" /><pb ed="M" n="1.0395" /> indīvarīsāmaṃ, rattiṃ nakkhattamāliniṃ;
```

```
Rājaputtaṃ apassantī, tumhaṃmhi saraṇaṃ gatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§318.</p>

```
Vande bhāgīrathiṃ gaṅgaṃ, savantīnaṃ paṭiggahaṃ;
```

```
Rājaputtaṃ apassantī, tumhaṃmhi saraṇaṃ gatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§319.</p>

```
Vande ahaṃ pabbatarājaseṭṭhaṃ, himavantaṃ siluccayaṃ;
```

```
Rājaputtaṃ apassantī, tumhaṃmhi saraṇaṃ gatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§320.</p>

```
Atisāyaṃ vatāgacchi, rājaputti yasassini;
```

```
Kena nujja samāgacchi <note>samāgacchi (sī. pī.)</note>, ko te piyataro mayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§321.</p>

```
Idaṃ khohaṃ tadāvocaṃ <note>tadavocaṃ (sī. syā.)</note>, gahitā tena sattunā;
```

```
Na me idaṃ tathā dukkhaṃ, yaṃ maṃ khādeyya rakkhaso;
```

```
Yañca me ayyaputtassa, mano hessati aññathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§322.</p>

```
Corīnaṃ bahubuddhīnaṃ, yāsu saccaṃ sudullabhaṃ;
```

```
Thīnaṃ bhāvo durājāno, macchassevodake gataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§323.</p>

```
Tathā maṃ saccaṃ pāletu, pālayissati ce mamaṃ;
```

```
Yathāhaṃ nābhijānāmi, aññaṃ piyataraṃ tayā;
```

```
Etena saccavajjena, byādhi te vūpasammatu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§324.</p>

```
Ye kuñjarā sattasatā uḷārā, rakkhanti rattindivamuyyutāvudhā;
```

```
Dhanuggahānañca satāni soḷasa, kathaṃvidhe passasi bhadde sattavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§325.</p>

```
Alaṅkatāyo <pb ed="T" n="1.0523" /> padumuttarattacā, virāgitā passati haṃsagaggarā;
```

```
Tāsaṃ suṇitvā mitagītavāditaṃ <note>mitagītavādinaṃ (pī.)</note>, na dāni me tāta tathā yathā pure.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§326.</p>

```
Suvaṇṇasaṃkaccadharā <pb ed="M" n="1.0396" /> suviggahā, alaṅkatā mānusiyaccharūpamā;
```

```
Senopiyā <note>senūpiyā (pī.)</note> tāta aninditaṅgiyo, khattiyakaññā paṭilobhayanti <note>paṭilābhayanti (pī.)</note> naṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§327.</p>

```
Sace ahaṃ tāta tathā yathā pure, patiṃ tamuñchāya punā vane bhare;
```

```
Sammānaye maṃ na ca maṃ vimānaye, itopi me tāta tato varaṃ siyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§328.</p>

```
Yamannapāne <pb ed="V" n="1.0290" /> vipulasmi ohite, nārī vimaṭṭhābharaṇā alaṅkatā;
```

```
Sabbaṅgupetā <note>pañcaṅgupetā (sī. syā. pī.)</note> patino ca appiyā, abajjha <note>avajjha (syā.), ābajjha (pī.)</note> tassā maraṇaṃ tato varaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§329.</p>

```
Api ce daliddā kapaṇā anāḷhiyā, kaṭādutīyā patino ca sā piyā;
```

```
Sabbaṅgupetāyapi appiyāya, ayameva <pb ed="T" n="1.0524" /> seyyā <note>seyyo (syā. ka.)</note> kapaṇāpi yā piyā <note>kapaṇāpi yā (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§330.</p>

```
Sudullabhitthī purisassa yā hitā, bhattitthiyā dullabho yo hito ca;
```

```
Hitā ca te sīlavatī ca bhariyā, janinda dhammaṃ cara sambulāya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§331.</p>

```
Sace tuvaṃ vipule laddhabhoge, issāvatiṇṇā maraṇaṃ upesi;
```

```
Ahañca te bhadde imā rājakaññā <note>imā ca kaññā (pī.)</note>, sabbe <note>sabbeva (sī. syā. pī.)</note> te vacanakarā bhavāmāti.
```

Sambulājātakaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 520. Gandhatindukajātakaṃ (10)

<p rend="hangnum">§332.</p>

```
Appamādo <pb ed="M" n="1.0397" /> amataṃ padaṃ <note>amatapadaṃ (sī. pī.)</note>, pamādo maccuno padaṃ;
```

```
Appamattā na mīyanti, ye pamattā yathā matā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§333.</p>

```
Madā pamādo jāyetha, pamādā jāyate khayo;
```

```
Khayā padosā <note>khayā ca dosā (sī.)</note> jāyanti, mā pamādo <note>mā mado (sī. syā. pī.)</note> bharatūsabha <note>bhāradhūsabha (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§334.</p>

```
Bahū hi khattiyā jīnā, atthaṃ raṭṭhaṃ pamādino;
```

```
Athopi gāmino gāmā, anagārā agārino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§335.</p>

```
Khattiyassa pamattassa, raṭṭhasmiṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhana;
```

```
Sabbe bhogā vinassanti, rañño taṃ vuccate aghaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§336.</p>

```
Nesa <pb ed="T" n="1.0525" /> dhammo mahārāja, ativelaṃ pamajjasi;
```

```
Iddhaṃ phītaṃ janapadaṃ, corā viddhaṃsayanti naṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§337.</p>

```
Na te puttā bhavissanti, na hiraññaṃ na dhāniyaṃ <note>na hiraññanidhāniyā (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Raṭṭhe viluppamānamhi, sabbabhogehi jiyyasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§338.</p>

```
Sabbabhogā parijiṇṇaṃ, rājānaṃ vāpi khattiyaṃ <note>khattiya (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Ñātimittā suhajjā ca, na taṃ maññanti māniyaṃ <note>mantiyaṃ (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§339.</p>

```
Hatthārohā anīkaṭṭhā, rathikā pattikārakā;
```

```
Tamevamupajīvantā, na taṃ maññanti māniyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§340.</p>

```
Asaṃvihitakammantaṃ, bālaṃ dummantimantinaṃ;
```

```
Sirī jahati dummedhaṃ, jiṇṇaṃva urago tacaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§341.</p>

```
Susaṃvihitakammantaṃ<pb ed="V" n="1.0291" />, kāluṭṭhāyiṃ atanditaṃ;
```

```
Sabbe bhogābhivaḍḍhanti, gāvo sausabhāmiva.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§342.</p>

```
Upassutiṃ mahārāja, raṭṭhe janapade cara;
```

```
Tattha disvā ca sutvā ca, tato taṃ <note>tvaṃ (ka.)</note> paṭipajjasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§343.</p>

```
Evaṃ vedetu pañcālo, saṅgāme saramappito <note>samappito (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Yathāhamajja vedemi, kaṇṭakena samappito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§344.</p>

```
Jiṇṇo <pb ed="M" n="1.0398" /> dubbalacakkhūsi, na rūpaṃ sādhu passasi;
```

```
Kiṃ tattha brahmadattassa, yaṃ taṃ maggeyya <note>maggheyya (pī.)</note> kaṇṭako <note>kaṇḍako (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§345.</p>

```
Bahvettha brahmadattassa, sohaṃ <note>yohaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> maggasmi <note>maggosmi (pī.)</note> brāhmaṇa;
```

```
Arakkhitā <pb ed="T" n="1.0526" /> jānapadā, adhammabalinā hatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§346.</p>

```
Rattiñhi <note>rattiñca (sī.)</note> corā khādanti, divā khādanti tuṇḍiyā;
```

```
Raṭṭhasmiṃ kūṭarājassa, bahu adhammiko jano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§347.</p>

```
Etādise bhaye jāte <note>tāta (sī. pī.)</note>, bhayaṭṭā tāta <note>tāva (sī. pī.)</note> māṇavā;
```

```
Nillenakāni kubbanti, vane āhatva kaṇṭakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§348.</p>

```
Kadāssu nāmayaṃ rājā, brahmadatto marissati;
```

```
Yassa raṭṭhamhi jiyyanti, appatikā kumārikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§349.</p>

```
Dubbhāsitañhi te jammi, anatthapadakovide;
```

```
Kuhiṃ rājā kumārīnaṃ, bhattāraṃ pariyesati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§350.</p>

```
Na me dubbhāsitaṃ brahme, kovidatthapadā ahaṃ;
```

```
Arakkhitā jānapadā, adhammabalinā hatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§351.</p>

```
Rattiñhi <pb ed="T" n="1.0527" /> corā khādanti, divā khādanti tuṇḍiyā;
```

```
Raṭṭhasmiṃ kūṭarājassa, bahu adhammiko jano;
```

```
Dujjīve dubbhare dāre, kuto bhattā kumāriyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§352.</p>

```
Evaṃ sayatu pañcālo, saṅgāme sattiyā hato;
```

```
Yathāyaṃ kapaṇo seti, hato phālena sāliyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§353.</p>

```
Adhammena tuvaṃ jamma, brahmadattassa kujjhasi;
```

```
Yo tvaṃ sapasi rājānaṃ, aparajjhitvāna attano <note>attanā (pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§354.</p>

```
Dhammena brahmadattassa, ahaṃ kujjhāmi brāhmaṇa;
```

```
Arakkhitā jānapadā, adhammabalinā hatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§355.</p>

```
Rattiñhi <pb ed="V" n="1.0292" /> corā khādanti, divā khādanti tuṇḍiyā;
```

```
Raṭṭhasmiṃ kūṭarājassa, bahu adhammiko jano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§356.</p>

```
Sā <pb ed="M" n="1.0399" /> nūna puna re pakkā, vikāle bhattamāhari;
```

```
Bhattahāriṃ apekkhanto, hato phālena sāliyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§357.</p>

```
Evaṃ haññatu pañcālo, saṅgāme asinā hato <note>daḷhaṃ (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Yathāhamajja pahato, khīrañca me pavaṭṭitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§358.</p>

```
Yaṃ pasu khīraṃ chaḍḍeti, pasupālaṃ vihiṃsati <note>pasupālañca hiṃsati (sī.), pasu phālañca hiṃsati (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Kiṃ tattha brahmadattassa, yaṃ no garahate <note>garahato (pī.)</note> bhavaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§359.</p>

```
Gārayho brahme pañcālo, brahmadattassa rājino;
```

```
Arakkhitā jānapadā, adhammabalinā hatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§360.</p>

```
Rattiñhi <pb ed="T" n="1.0528" /> corā khādanti, divā khādanti tuṇḍiyā;
```

```
Raṭṭhasmiṃ kūṭarājassa, bahu adhammiko jano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§361.</p>

```
Caṇḍā aṭanakā <note>aṭanaka (pī.), akaṭanā (ka.)</note> gāvī, yaṃ pure na duhāmase;
```

```
Taṃ dāni ajja dohāma, khīrakāmehupaddutā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§362.</p>

```
Evaṃ kandatu pañcālo, viputto vippasukkhatu;
```

```
Yathāyaṃ kapaṇā gāvī, viputtā paridhāvati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§363.</p>

```
Yaṃ pasu pasupālassa, sambhameyya <note>pabbhameyya (sī. pī.)</note> raveyya vā;
```

```
Ko nīdha aparādhatthi, brahmadattassa rājino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§364.</p>

```
Aparādho mahābrahme, brahmadattassa rājino;
```

```
Arakkhitā jānapadā, adhammabalinā hatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§365.</p>

```
Rattiñhi corā khādanti, divā khādanti tuṇḍiyā;
```

```
Raṭṭhasmiṃ kūṭarājassa, bahu adhammiko jano;
```

```
Kathaṃ no asikosatthā, khīrapā haññate pajā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§366.</p>

```
Evaṃ khajjatu pañcālo, hato yuddhe saputtako;
```

```
Yathāhamajja khajjāmi, gāmikehi <note>gāmakehi (sī. pī.)</note> araññajo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§367.</p>

```
Na <pb ed="M" n="1.0400" /> sabbabhūtesu vidhenti <note>vidhanti (ka.)</note> rakkhaṃ, rājāno maṇḍūka manussaloke;
```

```
Nettāvatā rājā adhammacārī, yaṃ tādisaṃ jīvamadeyyu dhaṅkā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§368.</p>

```
Adhammarūpo vata brahmacārī, anuppiyaṃ bhāsasi khattiyassa;
```

```
Viluppamānāya puthuppajāya, pūjesi rājaṃ paramappamādaṃ <note>rājaṃ paramappavādaṃ (sī.), rājā paramappavādiṃ (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§369.</p>

```
Sace <pb ed="V" n="1.0293" /> imaṃ brahme surajjakaṃ siyā, phītaṃ raṭṭhaṃ muditaṃ <note>pūritaṃ (ka.)</note> vippasannaṃ;
```

```
Bhutvā baliṃ aggapiṇḍañca kākā, na mādisaṃ jīvamadeyyu dhaṅkāti.
```

Gandhatindukajātakaṃ dasamaṃ.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Kiṃchanda <pb ed="T" n="1.0529" /> kumbha jayaddisa chaddanta, atha paṇḍitasambhava sirakapi;
```

```
Dakarakkhasa paṇḍaranāgavaro, atha sambula tindukadevasutoti.
```

Tiṃsanipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

<trailer rend="centre">Jātakapāḷiyā paṭhamo bhāgo niṭṭhito.</trailer>
